BhG 1


atha arjuna-viShAda-yogo nAma
prathamo 'dhyAyaH |

==============================

bhagavat-shaN^karAcArya-kR^ita-bhAShyam

upodghATaH

om
nArAyaNaH paro 'vyaktAd aNDam avyakta-sambhavam |
aNDasyAntas tv ime lokAH sapta-dvIpA ca medinI ||

sa bhagavAn sR^iShTvedam jagat | tasya ca sthitim cikIrShuH marIchyAdIn agre sR^iShTvA prajApatIn pravR^itti-lakShaNam dharmam grAhayAmAsa vedoktam | tato 'nyAn ca sanaka-sanandanAdIn utpAdya nivR^itti-lakShaNam dharmam j~nAna-vairAgya-lakShaNam grAhayAmAsa | dvividho hi vedokto dharmaH pravR^itti-lakShaNo nivR^itti-lakShaNash ca | jagataH sthiti-kAraNam | prANinAm sAkShAd abhyudaya-niHshreyasa-hetur yaH sa dharmo brAhmaNAdyair varNibhir Ashramibhish ca shreyo 'rthibhir anuShThIyamAnaH | dIrgheNa kAlena anuShThAtÌNAm kAmodbhavAd dhIyamAna-viveka-j~nAna-hetukena adharmeNa abhibhUyamAne dharme, pravardhamAne ca adharme, jagataH sthitim paripipAlayiShuH sa Adi-kartA nArAyaNAkhyo viShNur bhaumasya brahmaNo brAhmaNatvasya cAbhirakShaNArtham devakyAm vasudevAd amshena kR^iShNaH kila sambabhUva | brAhmaNatvasya hi rakShaNena rakShitaH syAd vaidiko dharmaH tad-adhInatvAd varNAshrama-bhedAnAm | 

sa ca bhagavAn j~nAnaishvarya-shakti-bala-vIrya-tejobhiH sadA sampannas triguNAtmikAm vaiShNavIm svAm mAyAm mUla-prakR^itim vashIkR^itya, ajo 'vyayo bhUtAnAm Ishvaro nitya-shuddha-buddha-mukta-svabhAvo 'pi san, sva-mAyayA dehavAn iva jAta iva ca lokAnugraham kurvan lakShyate | sva-prayojanAbhAve 'pi bhUtAnujighR^ikShayA vaidikam hi dharma-dvayam arjunAya shoka-moha-mahodadhau nimagnAya upadidesha guNAdhikair hi gR^ihIto 'nuShThIyamAnash ca dharmaH pracayam gamiShyatIti | tam dharmam bhagavatA yathopadiShTam veda-vyAsaH sarvaj~no bhagavAn gItAkhyaiH saptabhiH shloka-shatair upanibabandha |

tad idam gItA-shAstram samasta-vedArtha-sAra-saN^graha-bhUtam durvij~nayArtham tad-arthAviShkaraNAya anekair vivR^ita-pada-padArtha-vAkya-vAkyArtha-nyAyam api atyanta-viruddhAnekArthatvena laukikair gR^ihyamANam upalabhyAham vivekato 'rtha-nirdhAraNArtham samkShepato vivaraNam kariShyAmi | 

tasya asya gItA-shAstrasya samkShepataH prayojanam param niHshreyasam sa-hetukasya samsArasya atyantoparama-lakShaNam | tac ca sarva-karma-sannyAsa-pUrvakAd Atma-j~nAna-niShThA-rUpAd dharmAd bhavati | tathA imam eva gItArtha-dharmam uddishya bhagavataivoktam | sa hi dharmaH suparyApto brahmaNaH pada-vedane [Mbh 14.16.12] ity anugItAsu | tatraiva coktam - naiva dharmI na cAdharmI na caiva hi shubhAshubhI [Mbh 14.19.7], yaH syAd ekAyane lInas tUShNIm kimcid acintayan [Mbh 14.19.1], j~nAnam samnyAsa-lakShaNam [Mbh 14.43.26] iti ca | ihApi cAnte uktam arjunAya - sarva-dharmAn parityajya mAm ekam sharaNam vraja [GItA 18.66] iti | 

abhyudayArtho 'pi yaH pravR^itti-lakShaNo dharmo varNAn AshramAmsh coddishya vihitaH sa devAdi-sthAna-prApti-hetur api san, IshvarArpaNa-buddhyAnuShThIyamAnaH sattva-shuddhaye bhavati phalAbhisandhi-varjitaH | shuddha-sattvasya ca j~nAna-niShThAyogyatA-prApti-dvAreNa j~nAnotpatti-hetutvena ca niHshreyasa-hetutvam api pratipadyate | tathA cemam evArtham abhisandhAya vakShyati brahmaNy AdhAya karmANi [GItA 5.10], yoginaH karma kurvanti saN^gam tyaktvAtma-shuddhaye [GItA 5.11] iti | 

imam dviprakAram dharmam niHshreyasa-prayojanam | paramArtha-tattvam ca vAsudevAkhyam para-brahmAbhidheya-bhUtam visheShataH abhivya¤jayad vishiShTa-prayojana-sambandhAbhidheyavad gItA-shAstram | yatas tad-artha-vij~nAnena samasta-puruShArtha-siddhiH | ataH tad-vivaraNe yatnaH kriyate mayA ||


BhG 1


dharma-kShetre kuru-kShetre samavetA yuyutsavaH |
mAmakAH pANDavAsh caiva kim akurvata samjaya ||BhG_1.1||

samjaya uvAca
dR^iShTvA tu pANDavAnIkam vyUDham duryodhanas tadA |
AcAryam upasamgamya rAjA vacanam abravIt ||BhG_1.2||
pashyaitAm pANDu-putrANAm AcArya mahatIm camUm |
vyUDhAm drupada-putreNa tava shiShyeNa dhImatA ||BhG_1.3||
atra shUrA maheShvAsA bhImArjuna-samA yudhi |
yuyudhAno virATash ca drupadash ca mahArathaH ||BhG_1.4||
dhR^iShTaketush cekitAnaH kAshirAjash ca vIryavAn |
purujit kuntibhojash ca shaibyash ca nara-pumgavaH ||BhG_1.5||
yudhAmanyush ca vikrAnta uttamaujAsh ca vIryavAn |
saubhadro draupadeyAsh ca sarva eva mahA-rathAH ||BhG_1.6||
asmAkam tu vishiShTA ye tAn nibodha dvijottama |
nAyakA mama sainyasya samj~nArtham tAn bravImi te ||BhG_1.7||
bhavAn bhIShmash ca karNash ca kR^ipash ca samitimjayaH |
ashvatthAmA vikarNash ca saumadattir jayadrathaH ||BhG_1.8||
anye ca bahavaH shUrA mad-arthe tyakta-jIvitAH |
nAnA-shastra-praharaNAH sarve yuddha-vishAradAH ||BhG_1.9||
aparyAptam tad asmAkam balam bhIShmAbhirakShitam |
paryAptam tv idam eteShAm balam bhImAbhirakShitam ||BhG_1.10||
ayaneShu ca sarveShu yathA-bhAgam avasthitAH |
bhIShmam evAbhirakShantu bhavantaH sarva eva hi ||BhG_1.11||
tasya samjanayan harSham kuru-vR^iddhaH pitAmahaH |
simha-nAdam vinadyoccaiH shaN^kham dadhmau pratApavAn ||BhG_1.12||
tataH shaN^khAsh ca bheryash ca paNavAnaka-gomukhAH |
sahasaivAbhyahanyanta sa shabdas tumulo 'bhavat ||BhG_1.13||
tataH shvetair hayair yukte mahati syandane sthitau |
mAdhavaH pANDavash caiva divyau shaN^khau pradadhmatuH ||BhG_1.14||
pAJNcajanyam hR^iShIkesho devadattam dhanamjayaH |
pauNDram dadhmau mahA-shaN^kham bhIma-karmA vR^ikodaraH ||BhG_1.15||
ananta-vijayam rAjA kuntI-putro yudhiShThiraH |
nakulaH sahadevash ca sughoSha-maNipuShpakau ||BhG_1.16||
kAshyash ca parameShvAsaH shikhaNDI ca mahA-rathaH |
dhR^iShTadyumno virATash ca sAtyakish cAparAjitaH ||BhG_1.17||
drupado draupadeyAsh ca sarvashaH pR^ithivI-pate |
saubhadrash ca mahAbAhuH shaN^khAn dadhmuH pR^ithak pR^ithak ||BhG_1.18||
sa ghoSho dhArtarAShTrANAm hR^idayAni vyadArayat |
nabhash ca pR^ithivIm caiva tumulo vyanunAdayan ||BhG_1.19||
atha vyavasthitAn dR^iShTvA dhArtarAShTrAn kapi-dhvajaH |
pravR^itte shastra-sampAte dhanur udyamya pANDavaH ||BhG_1.20||
hR^iShIkesham tadA vAkyam idam Aha mahI-pate |
senayor ubhayor madhye ratham sthApaya me 'cyuta ||BhG_1.21||
yAvad etAn nirIkShe 'ham yoddhu-kAmAn avasthitAn |
kair mayA saha yoddhavyam asmin raNa-samudyame ||BhG_1.22||
yotsyamAnAn avekShe 'ham ya ete 'tra samAgatAH |
dhArtarAShTrasya durbuddher yuddhe priya-cikIrShavaH ||BhG_1.23||
evam ukto hR^iShIkesho guDAkeshena bhArata |
senayor ubhayor madhye sthApayitvA rathottamam ||BhG_1.24||
bhIShma-droNa-pramukhataH sarveShAm ca mahIkShitAm |
uvAca pArtha pashyaitAn samavetAn kurUn iti ||BhG_1.25||
tatrApashyat sthitAn pArthaH pitÌn atha pitAmahAn |
AcAryAn mAtulAn bhrAtÌn putrAn pautrAn sakhIms tathA ||BhG_1.26||
shvashurAn suhR^idash caiva senayor ubhayor api |
tAn samIkShya sa kaunteyaH sarvAn bandhUn avasthitAn ||BhG_1.27||
kR^ipayA parayAviShTo viShIdann idam abravIt |
dR^iShTvemam svajanam kR^iShNa yuyutsum samupasthitam ||BhG_1.28||
sIdanti mama gAtrANi mukham ca parishuShyati |
vepathush ca sharIre me romaharShash ca jAyate ||BhG_1.29||
gANDIvam sramsate hastAt tvak caiva paridahyate |
na ca shaknomy avasthAtum bhramatIva ca me manaH ||BhG_1.30||
nimittAni ca pashyAmi viparItAni keshava |
na ca shreyo 'nupashyAmi hatvA svajanam Ahave ||BhG_1.31||
na kAN^kShe vijayam kR^iShNa na ca rAjyam sukhAni ca |
kim no rAjyena govinda kim bhogair jIvitena vA ||BhG_1.32||
yeShAm arthe kAN^kShitam no rAjyam bhogAH sukhAni ca |
ta ime 'vasthitA yuddhe prANAms tyaktvA dhanAni ca ||BhG_1.33||
AcAryAH pitaraH putrAs tathaiva ca pitAmahAH |
mAtulAH shvashurAH pautrAH shyAlAH sambandhinas tathA ||BhG_1.34||
etAn na hantum icchAmi ghnato 'pi madhusUdana |
api trailokya-rAjyasya hetoH kim nu mahI-kR^ite ||BhG_1.35||
nihatya dhArtarAShTrAn naH kA prItiH syAj janArdana |
pApam evAshrayed asmAn hatvaitAn AtatAyinaH ||BhG_1.36||
tasmAn nArhA vayam hantum dhArtarAShTrAn sva-bAndhavAn |
svajanam hi katham hatvA sukhinaH syAma mAdhava ||BhG_1.37||
yady apy ete na pashyanti lobhopahata-cetasaH |
kula-kShaya-kR^itam doSham mitra-drohe ca pAtakam ||BhG_1.38||
katham na j~neyam asmAbhiH pApAd asmAn nivartitum |
kula-kShaya-kR^itam doSham prapashyadbhir janArdana ||BhG_1.39||
kula-kShaye praNashyanti kula-dharmAH sanAtanAH |
dharme naShTe kulam kR^itsnam adharmo 'bhibhavaty uta ||BhG_1.40||
adharmAbhibhavAt kR^iShNa praduShyanti kula-striyaH |
strIShu duShTAsu vArShNeya jAyate varNa-samkaraH ||BhG_1.41||
samkaro narakAyaiva kula-ghnAnAm kulasya ca |
patanti pitaro hy eShAm lupta-piNDodaka-kriyAH ||BhG_1.42||
doShair etaiH kula-ghnAnAm varNa-samkara-kArakaiH |
utsAdyante jAti-dharmAH kula-dharmAsh ca shAshvatAH ||BhG_1.43||
utsanna-kula-dharmANAm manuShyANAm janArdana |
narake niyatam vAso bhavatIty anushushruma ||BhG_1.44||
aho bata mahat pApam kartum vyavasitA vayam |
yad rAjya-sukha-lobhena hantum svajanam udyatAH ||BhG_1.45||
yadi mAm apratIkAram ashastram shastra-pANayaH |
dhArtarAShTrA raNe hanyus tan me kShemataram bhavet ||BhG_1.46||
evam uktvArjunaH samkhye rathopastha upAvishat |
visR^ijya sasharam cApam shoka-samvigna-mAnasaH ||BhG_1.47||

iti shaN^karAcArya-kR^ite gItA-bhAShye prathamo 'dhyAyaH 
||1||

BhG 2

dvitIyo 'dhyAyaH 

samjaya uvAca
tam tathA kR^ipayAviShTam ashrupUrNAkulekShaNam |
viShIdantam idam vAkyam uvAca madhusUdanaH ||BhG_2.1||
kutas tvA kashmalam idam viShame samupasthitam |
anArya-juShTam asvargyam akIrti-karam arjuna ||BhG_2.2||
klaibyam mA sma gamaH pArtha naitat tvayy upapadyate |
kShudram hR^idaya-daurbalyam tyaktvottiShTha paramtapa ||BhG_2.3||
katham bhIShmam aham samkhye droNam ca madhusUdana |
iShubhiH pratiyotsyAmi pUjArhAv arisUdana ||BhG_2.4||

gurUn ahatvA hi mahAnubhAvA¤
shreyo bhoktum bhaikShyam apIha loke |
hatvArtha-kAmAms tu gurUn ihaiva
bhu¤jIya bhogAn rudhira-pradigdhAn ||BhG_2.5||

na caitad vidmaH kataran no garIyo
yad vA jayema yadi vA no jayeyuH |
yAn eva hatvA na jijIviShAmas
te 'vasthitAH pramukhe dhArtarAShTrAH ||BhG_2.6||

kArpaNya-doShopahata-svabhAvaH
pR^icchAmi tvAm dharma-sammUDha-cetAH |
yac chreyaH syAn nishcitam brUhi tan me
shiShyas te 'ham shAdhi mAm tvAm prapannam ||BhG_2.7||

na hi prapashyAmi mamApanudyAd
yac chokam ucchoShaNam indriyANAm |
avApya bhUmAv asapatnam R^iddham
rAjyam surANAm api cAdhipatyam ||BhG_2.8||

samjaya uvAca
evam uktvA hR^iShIkesham guDAkeshaH parantapaH |
na yotsya iti govindam uktvA tUShNIm babhUva ha ||BhG_2.9||
tam uvAca hR^iShIkeshaH prahasann iva bhArata |
senayor ubhayor madhye viShIdantam idam vacaH ||BhG_2.10||

atra ca dR^iShTvA tu pANDavAnIkam ity Arabhya yAvat na yotsya iti govindam uktvA tUShNIm babhUva ha ity etad-antaH prANinAm shoka-mohAdi-samsAra-bIja-bhUta-doShodbhava-kAraNa-pradarshanArthatvena vyAkhyeyo granthaH | tathA hi -- arjunena rAjya-guru-putra-mitra-suhR^it-svajana-sambandhi-bAndhaveShu aham eteShAm mamaite ity evam bhrAnti-pratyaya-nimitta-sneha-vicchedAdi-nimittau AtmanaH shoka-mohau pradarshitau | katham bhIShmam aham samkhye ity AdinA | shoka-mohAbhyAm hy abhibhUta-viveka-vij~nAnaH svata eva kShatra-dharme yuddhe pravR^itto 'pi tasmAd yuddhAd upararAma | para-dharmam ca bhikShA-jIvanAdikam kartum pravavR^ite | tathA ca sarva-prANinAm shoka-mohAdi-doShAviShTa-cetasAm svabhAvata eva svadharma-parityAgaH pratiShiddha-sevA ca syAt | sva-dharme pravR^ittAnAm api teShAm vAN^-manaH-kAyAdInAm pravR^ittiH phalAbhisamdhi-pUrvikaiva sAhamkArA ca bhavati | tatraivam sati dharmAdharmopacayAd iShTAniShTa-janma-sukha-duHkhAdi-prApti-lakShaNaH samsAro 'nuparato bhavati | ity ataH samsAra-bIja-bhUtau shoka-mohau | tayosh ca sarva-karma-samnyAsa-pUrvakAd Atma-j~nAnAt nAnyato nivR^ittir iti tad-upadidikShuH sarva-lokAnugrahArtham arjunam nimittIkR^itya Aha bhagavAn vAsudevaH--- ashocyAn ityAdi |

atra kecid AhuH-sarva-karma-samnyAsa-pUrvakAd Atma-j~nAna-niShThA-mAtrAd eva kevalAt kaivalyam na prApyata eva | kim tarhi ? agnihotrAdi-shrauta-smArta-karma-sahitAt j~nAnAt kaivalya-prAptir iti sarvAsu gItAsu nishcito 'rtha iti | j~nApakam cAhur asyArthasya -- 
atha cet tvam imam dharmyam samgrAmam na kariShyasi [GItA 2.33] karmaNy evAdhikAras te [GItA 2.47], kuru karmaiva tasmAt tvam [GItA 4.15] ity Adi | himsAdi-yuktatvAt vaidikam karma adharmAya itIyam apy AshaN^kA na kAryA | katham ? kShAtram karma yuddha-lakShaNam guru-bhrAtR^i-putrAdi-himsA-lakShaNam atyantam krUram api sva-dharma iti kR^itvA nAdharmAya | tad-akaraNe ca tataH sva-dharmam kIrtim ca hitvA pApam avApsyasi [GItA 2.33] iti bruvatA yAvaj jIvAdi-shruti-coditAnAm pashv-Adi-himsA-lakShaNAnAm ca karmaNAm prAg eva nAdharmatvam iti sunishcitam uktam bhavati -- iti |

tad asat | j~nAna-karma-niShThayor vibhAga-vacanAd buddhi-dvayAshrayayoH | ashocyAn ity AdinA bhagavatA yAvat svadharmam api cAvekShya ity etad-antena granthena yat-paramArthAtma-tattva-nirUpaNam kR^itam, tat sAmkhyam | tad-viShayA buddhir Atmano janmAdi-ShaD-vikriyAbhAvAd akartA Atmeti prakaraNArtha-nirUpaNAd yA jAyate, sA sAmkhya-buddhiH | sA yeShAm j~nAninAm ucitA bhavati, te sAmkhyAH | etasyA buddher janmanaH prAk Atmano dehAdivyatiriktatvakartR^itvabhoktR^itvabhoktR^itvAdyapekSho dharmAdharma-viveka-pUrvako mokSha-sAdhanAnuShThAna-lakShaNo yogaH | tad-viShayA buddhiH yoga-buddhiH | sA yeShAm karmiNAm ucitA bhavati te yoginaH | tathA ca bhagavatA vibhakte dve buddhI nirdiShTe eShA te 'bhihitA sAmkhye buddhir yoge tv imAm shR^iNu iti | tayosh ca sAmkhya-buddhy-AshrayAm j~nAna-yogena niShThAm sAmkhyAnAm vibhaktAm vakShyati purA vedAtmanA mayA proktA iti | tathA ca yoga-buddhy-AshrayAm karma-yogena niShThAm vibhaktAm vakShyati - karma-yogena yoginAm iti | evam sAmkhya-buddhim yoga-buddhim ca Ashritya dve niShThe vibhakte bhagavataiva ukte j~nAna-karmaNoH kartR^itvAkartR^itvaikatvAnekatva-buddhy-AshrayayoH yugapad-eka-puruShAshrayatvAsambhavam pashyatA | yathA etad-vibhAga-vacanam tathaiva darshitam shAtapathIye brAhmaNe - etam eva pravrAjino lokam icchanto brAhmaNAH pravrajanti [BAU 4.4.22] iti sarva-karma-samnyAsam vidhAya tac-cheSheNa kim prajayA kariShyAmo yeShAm no 'yam AtmAyam lokaH [BAU 4.4.22] iti | tatraiva ca prAg dAra-parigrahAt puruSha Atmo prAkR^ito dharma-jij~nAsottara-kAlam loka-traya-sAdhanam | putram, dvi-prakAram ca vittam mAnuSham dvi-prakAram ca | tatra mAnuSham karma-rUpam pitR^i-loka-prApti-sAdhanam vidyAm ca daivam vittam deva-loka-prApti-sAdhanam | so 'kAmayata [BAU 1.4.17] iti avidyA-kAmavata eva sarvANi karmANi shrautAdIni darshitAni | tebhyo vyutthAya, pravrajanti [BAU 4.4.22] iti vyutthAnam AtmAnam eva lokam icchato 'kAmasya vihitam | tad etad vibhAga-vacanam anupapannam syAd yadi shrauta-karma-j~nAnayoH samuccayo 'bhipretaH syAd bhagavataH |

na cArjunasya prashna upapanno bhavati jyAyasI cet karmaNas te [GItA 3.1] ity AdiH | eka-puruShAnuShTheyatvAsambhavam buddhi-karmaNoH bhagavatA pUrvam anuktam katham arjuno 'shrutam buddhA ca karmaNo jyAyastvam bhagavaty adhyAropayen mR^iShaiva jyAyasI cet karmaNas te matA buddhiH iti |

kim ca -- yadi buddhi-karmaNoH sarveShAm samuccaya uktaH syAt arjunasyApi sa ukta eveti, yac chrAya etayor ekam tan me brUhi sunishcitam iti katham ubhayor upadeshe sati anyatara-viShaya eva prashnaH syAt ? na hi pitta-prashamanArthinaH vaidyena madhuram shItalam ca bhoktavyam ity upadiShTe tayor anyatarat-pitta-prashamana-kAraNam brUhi iti prashnaH sambhavati |

athArjunasya bhagavad-ukta-vacanArtha-vivekAnavadhAraNa-nimittaH prashnaH kalpyeta, tathApi bhagavatA prashnAnurUpam prativacanam deyam -- mayA buddhi-karmaNoH samuccaya uktaH kim artham ittham tvam bhrAnto 'si -- iti | na tu punaH prativacanam ananurUpam pR^iShTAd anyad eva dve niShThA mayA purA proktA iti vaktum yuktam |

nApi smArtenaiva karmaNA buddheH samuccaye abhiprete vibhAga-vacanAdi sarvam upapananam | kim ca -- kShatriyasya yuddham smArtam karma sva-dharma iti jAnataH tat kim karmaNi ghoro mAm niyojayasi ity upAlambho 'nupapannaH |

tasmAd gItA-shAstre IShan-mAtreNApi shrautena smArtena vA karmaNA Atma-j~nAnasya samuccayo na kenacid darshayitum shakyaH | yasya tv aj~nAnAt rAgAdi-doShato vA karmaNi pravR^ittasya yaj~nena dAnena tapasA vA vishuddha-sattvasya j~nAnam utpannam paramArtha-tattva-viShayam ekam evedam sarvam brahma akartR^i ca iti, tasya karmaNi karma-prayojane ca nivR^itte 'pi loka-samgrahArtham yatna-pUrvam yathA pravR^ittiH, tathaiva pravR^ittasya yat pravR^itti-rUpam dR^ishyate na tat karma yena buddheH samuccayaH syAt | yathA bhagavato vAsudevasya kShatra-dharma-ceShTitam na j~nAnena samuccIyate puruShArtha-siddhaye, tadvat tat-phalAbhisamdhy-ahamkArAbhAvasya tulyatvAd viduShaH | tattvavin nAham karomIti manyate, na ca tat-phalam abhisandhatte | yathA ca svargAdi-kAmArthino 'gnihotrAdi-karma-lakShaNa-dharmAnuShThAnAya AhitAgneH kAmye eva agnihotrAdau pravR^ittasya sAmi kR^ite vinaShTA 'pi kAme tad eva agnihotrAdy-anutiShThato 'pi na tat-kAmyam agnihotrAdi bhavati | tathA ca darshayati bhagavAn - kurvann api na lipyate na karoti na lipyate iti tatra tatra || 

yac ca pUrvaiH pUrvataram kR^itam karmaNaiva hi samsiddhim AsthitA janakAdayaH iti, tat tu pravibhajya vij~neyam | tat katham ? yadi tAvat pUrve janakAdayaH tattva-vido 'pi pravR^itta-karmANaH syuH, te loka-samgrahArtham guNA guNeShu vartante iti j~nAnenaiva samsiddhim AsthitAH, karma-samnyAse prApte 'pi karmaNA sahaiva samsiddhim AsthitAH, na karma-samnyAsam kR^itavanta ity arthaH | 

atha na te tattva-vidaH | Ishvara-samarpitena karmaNA sAdhana-bhUtena samsiddhim sattva-shuddhim, j~nAnotpatti-lakShaNAm vA samsiddhim, AsthitA janakAdaya iti vyAkhyeyam | etam evArtham vakShyati bhagavAn sattva-shuddhaye karma kurvanti iti | sva-karmaNA tam abhyarcya siddhim vindati mAnavaH ity uktvA siddhim prAptasya punar-j~nAna-niShThAm vakShyati -- siddhim prApto yathA brahma ity AdinA || 

tasmAd gItA-shAstre kevalAd eva tattva-j~nAnAn mokSha-prAptiH na karma-samuccitAt iti nishcito 'rthaH | yathA cAyam arthaH, tathA prakaraNasho vibhajya tatra tatra darshayiShyAmaH || 

tatraiva dharma-sammUDha-cetaso mithyA-j~nAnavato mahati shoka-sAgare nimagnasya arjunasya anyatrAtma-j~nAnAd uddharaNam apashyan bhagavAn vAsudevaH tataH kR^ipayA arjunam uddidhArayiShuH Atma-j~nAnAyAvatArayann Aha - 

shrI-bhagavAn uvAca
ashocyAn anvashocas tvam praj~nA-vAdAmsh ca bhAShase |
gatAsUn agatAsUmsh ca nAnushocanti paNDitAH ||BhG_2.11||

na shocyA ashocyAH bhIShma-droNAdayaH | sad-vR^ittatvAt paramArtha-svarUpeNa ca nityatvAt, tAn ashocyAn anvashoco 'nushocitavAn asi te mriyante man-nimittam, aham tair vinAbhUtaH kim kariShyAmi rAjya-sukhAdinA iti | tvam praj~nA-vAdAn praj~nAvatAm buddhimatAm vAdAmsh ca vacanAni ca bhAShase | tad etat mauDhyam pANDityam ca viruddham Atmani darshayasi unmatta iva ity abhiprAyaH | yasmAt gatAsUn gata-prANAn mR^itAn, agatAsUn agata-prANAn jIvatash ca 
nAnushocanti paNDitAH Atmaj~nAH | paNDA Atma-viShayA buddhir yeShAm te hi paNDitAH, pANDityam nirvidya [BAU 3.5.1] iti shruteH | paramArthatas tu tAn nityAn ashocyAn anushocasi, ato mUDho 'si ity abhiprAyaH ||BhGS_2.11||

==============================

kutas te ashocyAH ? yato nityAH | katham ? 

na tv evAham jAtu nAsam na tvam neme janAdhipAH |
na caiva na bhaviShyAmaH sarve vayam ataH param ||BhG_2.12||

na tv eva jAtu kadAcid aham nAsam kintv Asam eva | atIteShu dehotpatti-vinAsheShu ghaTAdiShu viyad iva nitya eva aham Asam ity abhiprAyaH | tathA na tvam nAsIH, kintv AsIr eva | tathA neme janAdhipA Asan kintv Asann eva | tathA na caiva na bhaviShyAmaH, kintu bhaviShyAma eva, sarve vayam ato 'smAd deha-vinAshAt param uttara-kAle 'pi | triShv api kAleShu nityA Atma-svarUpeNa ity arthaH | dehAbhedAnuvR^ittyA bahu-vacanam, nAtma-bhedAbhiprAyeNa ||BhGS_2.12||

==============================

tatra katham iva nitya Atmeti dR^iShTAntam Aha -

dehino 'smin yathA dehe kaumAram yauvanam jarA |
tathA dehAntara-prAptir dhIras tatra na muhyati ||BhG_2.13||

deho 'sya astIti dehI, tasya dehino dehavataH Atmano 'smin vartamAne dehA yathA yena prakAreNa kaumAram kumAra-bhAvo bAlyAvasthA, yauvanam yUno bhAvo madhyamAvasthA, jarA vayo-hAniH jIrNAvasthA, ity etAH tisro 'vasthAH anyonya-vilakShaNAH | tAsAm prathamAvasthA-nAshe na nAshaH, dvitIyAvasthopajane na upajana AtmanaH | kim tarhi ?avikriyasyaiva dvitIya-tR^itIyAvasthA-prAptiH Atmano dR^iShTA | tathA tadvad eva dehAd anyo deho dehAntaram, tasya prAptiH dehAntara-prAptiH avikriyasyaiva Atmana ity arthaH | dhIro dhImAn tatraivam sati na muhyati na moham Apadyate ||BhGS_2.13||

==============================

yadyapy Atma-vinAsha-nimitto moho na sambhavati nitya AtmA iti vijAnataH, tathApi shItoShNa-sukha-duHkha-prApti-nimitto moho laukiko dR^ishyate, sukha-viyoga-nimitto moho duHkha-samyoga-nimitta ca shokaH | ity etad arjunasya vacanam AshaN^kaya bhagavAn Aha -

mAtrA-sparshAs tu kaunteya shItoShNa-sukha-duHkhadAH |
AgamApAyino 'nityAs tAms titikShasva bhArata ||BhG_2.14||

mAtrA AbhiH mIyante shabdAdaya iti shrotrAdIni indriyANi | mAtrANAm sparshAH shabdAdibhiH samyogAH | te shItoShNasukha-duHkha-dAH shItam uShNam sukham duHkham ca prayacchantIti | athavA spR^ishyanta iti sparshA viShayAH shabdAdayaH | mAtrAsh ca sparshAsh ca shItoShNa-sukha-duHkha-dAH | shItam kadAcit sukham kadAcit duHkham | tathA uShNam api aniyata-svarUpam | sukha-duHkhe punaH niyata-rUpe yato na vyabhicarataH | atas tAbhyAm pR^ithak shItoShNayoH grahaNam | yasmAt te mAtrA-sparshAdayaH AgamApAyinaH AgamApAyashIlAH tasmAt anityAH | ataH tAn shItoShNAdIn titikShasva prasahasva | teShu harSham viShAdam vA mA kArShIH ity arthaH ||BhGS_2.14|| 

==============================

shItoShNAdIn sahataH kim syAd iti shR^iNu ---

yam hi na vyathayanty ete puruSham puruSharShabha |
sama-duHkha-sukham dhIram so 'mR^itatvAya kalpate ||BhG_2.15||

yam hi puruSham same duHkha-sukhe yasya tam sama-duHkha-sukham sukha-duHkha-prAptau harSha-viShAda-rahitam dhIram dhImantam na vyathayanti na cAlayanti nityAtma-darshanAt ete yathoktAH shItoShNAdayaH, sa nityAtma-svarUpa-darsha-niShTho dvandva-sahiShNuH amR^itatvAya amR^ita-bhAvAya mokShAyety arthaH kalpate samartho bhavati ||BhGS_2.15||

==============================

itash ca shoka-mohau akR^itvA shItoShNAdi-sahanam yuktam, yasmAt ---

nAsato vidyate bhAvo nAbhAvo vidyate sataH |
ubhayor api dR^iShTo 'ntas tv anayos tattva-darshibhiH ||BhG_2.16||

na asato  'vidyamAnasya shItoShNAdeH sa-kAraNasya na vidyate nAsti bhAvo bhavanam astitA || 
na hi shItoShNAdi sa-kAraNam pramANair nirUpyamANam vastu sambhavati | vikAro hi saH, vikArash ca vyabhicarati | yathA ghaTAdi-samsthAnam cakShuShA nirUpyamANam mR^id-vyatirekeNAnupalabdher asat | tathA sarvo vikAraH kAraNa-vyatirekeNAnupalabdher asat | janma-pradhvamsAbhyAm prAg Urdhvam cAnupalabdheH | kAryasya ghaTAdeH mR^id-Adi-kAraNasya ca tat-kAraNa-vyatirekeNAnupalabdher asattvam || 

tad-asattve sarvAbhAva-prasaN^ga iti cet, na | sarvatra buddhi-dvayopalabdheH, sad-buddhir asad-buddhir iti | yad-viShayA buddhir na vyabhicarati, tat sat | yad-viShayA vyabhicarati, tad asat | iti sad-asad-vibhAge buddhi-tantre sthite | sarvatra dve buddhI sarvair upalabhyete samAnAdhikaraNe na nIlotpalavat, san ghaTaH san paTaH, san hastI iti | evam sarvatra | tayor buddhyoH ghaTAdi-buddhir vyabhicarati | tathA ca darshitam | na tu sad-buddhiH | tasmAt ghaTAdi-buddhi-viShayo 'san, vyabhicArAt | na tu sad-buddhi-viShayaH, avyabhicArAt || 
ghaTe vinaShTe ghaTa-buddhau vyabhicarantyAm sad-buddhir api vyabhicaratIti cet na | paTAd evapi sad-buddhi-darshanAt | visheShaNa-viShayaiva sA sad-buddhiH |

sad-buddhivat ghaTa-buddhir api ghaTAntarA dR^ishyata iti cet, na | paTAdau adarshanAt || 

sad-buddhir api naShTe ghaTe na dR^ishyata iti cet, na | visheShyAbhAvAt | sad-buddhir visheShaNa-viShayA satI visheShyAbhAve visheShaNAnupapattau kim-viShayA syAt ? na tu punaH sad-buddheH viShayAbhAvAt || 

ekAdhikaraNatvam ghaTAdi-visheShyAbhAve na yuktam iti cet, na | idam udakam iti marIcy-Adau anyatarAbhAve 'pi sAmAnAdhikaraNya-darshanAt || 

tasmAd dehAder dvandvasya ca sa-kAraNasya asato na vidyate bhAva iti | tathA satash ca Atmano 'bhAvo 'vidyamAnatA na vidyate, sarvatrAvyabhicArAt ity avocAma || 

evam AtmAnAtmanoH sad-asatoH ubhayor api dR^iShTaH upalabdho 'nto nirNayaH sat sad eva, asat asad eveti, tv anayoH yathoktayoH tattva-darshibhiH | tad iti sarva-nAma sarvam ca brahma, tasya nAma tad iti, tad-bhAvas tattvam, brahmaNo yAthAtmyam | tad draShTum shIlam yeShAm te tattva-darshinaH, tais tattva-darshibhiH | tvam api tattva-darshinAm dR^iShTim Ashritya shokam moham ca hitvA shItoShNAdIni niyatAniyata-rUpANi dvandvAni vikAro 'yam asann eva marIci-jalavan mithyAvabhAsate iti manasi nishcitya titikShasva ity abhiprAyaH ||BhGS_2.16||


==============================


kim punas tat yat sad eva sarvadaiva astIti | ucyate ---

avinAshi tu tad viddhi yena sarvam idam tatam |
vinAsham avyayasyAsya na kashcit kartum arhati ||BhG_2.17||

avinAshi na vinaShTum shIlam yasyeti | tu-shabdo 'sato visheShaNArthaH | tat viddhi vijAnIhi | kim ? yena sarvam idam jagat tatam vyAptam sad-Akhyena brahmaNA sAkAsham, AkAshenaiva ghaTAdayaH | vinAsham adarshanam abhAvam | avyayasya na vyeti upacayApacayau na yAti iti avyayam tasya avyayasya | naitat sadAkhyam brahma svena rUpeNa vyeti vyabhicarati, niravayavatvAt, dehAdivat | nApy AtmIyena, AtmIyAbhAvAt | yathA devadatto dhana-hAnyA vyeti, na tu evam brahma vyeti | ato 'vyayasya asya brahmaNaH vinAsham na kashcit kartum arhati, na kashcit atmAnam vinAshayitum shaknoti Ishvaro 'pi | AtmA hi brahma, svAtmani ca kriyAvirodhAt ||BhGS_2.17|| 

==============================

kim punas tad asat yat svAtma-sattAm vyabhicaratIti, ucyate -

antavanta ime dehA nityasyoktAH sharIriNaH |
anAshino 'prameyasya tasmAd yudhyasva bhArata ||BhG_2.18||

antaH vinAshaH vidyate yeShAm te antavantaH | yathA mR^igatR^iShNikAdau sad-buddhiH anuvR^ittA pramANanirUpaNAnte vicchidyate, sa tasya antaH | tathA ime dehAH svapnamAyAdehAdivaca antavantaH nityasya sharIriNaH sharIravato 'nAshino 'prameyarya Atmano 'ntavanta iti uktAH vivekibhirity arthaH | nityasya anAshinaH iti na punaruktam | nityatvasya dvividhatvAt lokA, nAshasya ca | yathA deho bhasmIbhUto 'darshanam gato naShTa ucyate | vidyamAno 'pi yathA anyathA pariNato vyAdhyAdi-yukto jAto naShTa ucyate | tatra nityasya Th anAshinaH iti dvividhenApi nAshena asambandho 'syety arthaH | anyathA pR^ithivyAdivad api nityatvam syAt AtmanaH | tat mA bhUditi nityasya anAshinaH ityAha | aprameyamya na prameyasya pratyakShAdi-pramANaiH aparicchAdyasyety arthaH || 

nanu Agamena AtmA paricchidyate, pratyakShAdinA ca pUrvam | na | AtmanaH svataHsiddhatvAt | sirA hi Atmani pramAtari pramitsoH pramANAnveShaNA bhavati | na hi pUrvam itthamaham iti AtmAnamapramAya pa cAt prameyaparicchAdAya pravartate | na hi AtmA nAma kasyacit aprasiddho bhavati | shAstram tu antyam pramANam atad-dharmAdhyAropaNa-mAtra-nivartakatvena pramANatvam AtmanaH pratipadyate, na hy aj~nAtArthaj~nApakatvena | tathA ca shrutiH --- yat sAkShAd aparokShAd brahma ya AtmA sarvAntaraH [BAU 3.4.1] iti | yasmAd evam nityo 'vikriyash cAtmA tasmAd yudhyasva, yuddhAd uparamam mA kArShIH ity arthaH |

na hy atra yuddha-kartavyatA vidhIyate, yuddhe pravR^itta eva hi asau shoka-moha-pratibaddhaH tUShNIm Aste | ataH tasya pratibandhApanayana-mAtram bhagavatA kriyate | tasmAd yudhyasva iti anuvAda-mAtram, na vidhiH ||BhGS_2.18||

==============================

shoka-mohAdi-samsAra-kAraNa-nivR^itty-artham gItA-shAstram, na pravartakam ity etasyArthasya sAkShi-bhUte R^icau AninAya bhagavAn | yat tu manyase yuddhA bhIShmAdayo mayA hanyante aham eva teShAm hantA iti, eShA buddhir mR^iShaiva te | katham ?

ya enam vetti hantAram yash cainam manyate hatam |
ubhau tau na vijAnIto nAyam hanti na hanyate ||BhG_2.19||

ya enam prakR^itam dehinam vetti vijAnAti hantAram hanana-kriyAyAH kartAram ya ca enam anyo manyate hatam deha-hananena hato 'ham iti hanana-kriyAyAH karma-bhUtam | tau ubhau na vijAnItaH na j~nAtavantau avivekena AtmAnam | hantA aham, hato 'smy aham iti deha-hananena AtmAnam aham pratyaya-viShayam yau vijAnItaH tau Atma-svarUpAnabhij~nau ity arthaH | yasmAt na ayam atmA hanti na hanana-kriyAyAH kartA bhavati, na ca hanyate na ca karma bhavatIty arthaH, avikriyatvAt ||BhGS_2.19|| 

==============================

katham avikriya Atmeti dvitIyo mantraH -- 

na jAyate mriyate vA kadAcin
nAyam bhUtvA bhavitA vA na bhUyaH |
ajo nityaH shAshvato 'yam purANo
na hanyate hanyamAne sharIre ||BhG_2.20||

na jAyate notpadyate, jani-lakShaNA vastu-vikriyA na Atmano vidyate ity arthaH | tathA na mriyate vA | vA-shabdaH cArthe | na mriyate ca iti antyA vinAsha-lakShaNA vikriyA pratiShidhyate | kadAcic chabdaH sarva-vikriyA-pratiShedhaiH sambadhyate -- na kadAcit jAyate, na kadAcit mriyate, ity evam | yasmAt ayam AtmA bhUtvA bhavana-kriyAm anubhUya pashcAt abhavitA abhAvam gantA na bhUyaH punaH, tasmAt na mriyate | yo hi bhUtvA na bhavitA sa mriyata ity ucyate lokA | vA-shabdAt na-shabdAc ca ayam AtmA abhUtvA vA bhavitA dehavat na bhUyaH | tasmAt na jAyate | yo hi abhUtvA bhavitA sa jAyata ity ucyate | naivam AtmA | ato na jAyate | yasmAd evam tasmAt ajaH, yasmAt na mriyate tasmAt nityash ca | 

yadyapi Ady-antayor vikriyayoH pratiShedhe sarvA vikriyAH pratiShiddhA bhavanti, tathApi madhya-bhAvinInAm vikriyANAm sva-shabdair eva pratiShedhaH kartavyo 'nuktAnAm api yauvanAdi-samasta-vikriyANAm pratiShedho yathA syAt ity Aha-- shAshvata ity AdinA | shAshvata iti apakShaya-lakShaNA vikriyA pratiShidhyate | shashvad-bhavaH shAshvataH | na apakShIyate svarUpeNa, niravayavatvAt | nApi guNa-kShayeNa apakShayaH, nirguNatvAt | apakShaya-viparItApi vR^iddhi-lakShaNA vikriyA pratiShidhyate --- purANa iti | yo hi avayavAgamena upacIyate sa vardhate abhinava iti ca ucyate | ayam tu AtmA niravayavatvAt purApi nava eveti purANaH na vardhate ity arthaH | tathA na hanyate | hantiH atra vipariNAmArthe draShTavyo 'punaruktatAyai | na vipariNamyate ity arthaH | 

hanyamAne vipariNamyamAne 'pi sharIrAH | asmin mantre ShaD-bhAva-vikArA laukika-vastu-vikriyA Atmani pratiShidhyante | sarva-prakAra-vikriyA-rahita AtmA iti vAkyArthaH | yasmAd evam tasmAt ubhau tau na vijAnItaH iti pUrveNa mantreNa asya sambandhaH ||BhGS_2.20|| 

==============================

ya enam vetti hantAram ityanena mantreNa hanana-kriyAyAH kartA karma ca na bhavati iti pratij~nAya, na jAyate ity anena avikriyatvam hetum uktvA pratij~nAtArtham upasamharati-- 

vedAvinAshinam nityam ya enam ajam avyayam |
katham sa puruShaH pArtha kam ghAtayati hanti kam ||BhG_2.21||

veda vijAnAti avinAshinam antya-bhAva-vikAra-rahitam nityam vipariNAma-rahitam yo veda iti sambandhaH | enam pUrveNa matreNokta-lakShaNam ajam janma-rahitam avyayam apakShaya-rahitam katham kena prakAreNa sa vidvAn puruSho 'dhikR^itaH hanti hanana-kriyAm karoti, katham vA ghAtayati hantAram prayojayati | na kathamcit kamcit hanti, na kathamcit kamcit ghAtayati iti ubhayatra AkShepaH evArthaH prashnArthAsambhavAt | hetv-arthasya ca avikriyatvasya tulyatvAt viduShaH sarva-karma-pratiShedha eva prakaraNArtho 'bhipreto bhagavatA | hantes tu AkShepaH udAharaNArthatvena kathitaH | viduShaH kam karmAsambhave hetu-visheSham pashyan karmANy AkShipati bhagavAn katham sa puruShaH iti | 

nanu ukta evAtmano 'vikriyatvam sarva-karmAsambhava-kAraNa-visheShaH | satyam uktaH | na tu sa kAraNa-visheShaH, anyatvAt viduSho 'vikriyAd AtmanaH | na hi avikriyam sthANum viditavataH karma na sambhavati iti cet, na | viduShaH AtmatvAt | na dehAdi-samghAtasya vidvattA | ataH pArisheShyAt asamhata AtmA vidvAn avikriyaH iti tasya viduShaH karmAsambhavAt AkShepo yuktaH katham sa puruShaH iti | yathA buddhyAdy AhR^itasya shabdAdy-arthasya avikriya eva san buddhi-vR^itty-aviveka-vij~nAnena avidyayA upalabdhA AtmA kalpyate, evam eva AtmAnAtma-viveka-j~nAnena buddhi-vR^ittyA vidyA asatya-rUpayaiva paramArthato 'vikriya eva AtmA vidvAn ucyate | viduShaH karmAsambhava-vacanAt yAni karmANi shAstreNa vidhIyante tAni aviduSho vihitAni iti bhagavato nishcayo 'vagamyate || 

nanu vidyApi aviduSha eva vidhIyate, vidita-vidyasya piShTa-peShaNavat vidyA-vidhAnAnarthakyAt | tatra aviduShaH karmANi vidhIyante na viduShaH iti visheSho nopapadyate iti cet, na | anuShTheyasya bhAvAbhAva-visheShopapatteH | agnihotrAdi-vidhy-artha-j~nAnottara-kAlam agnihotrAdi-karma aneka-sAdhanopasamhAra-pUrvakam anuShTheyam kartA aham, mama kartavyam ity evam prakAra-vij~nAnavato 'viduShaH yathA anuShTheyam bhavati, na tu tathA na jAyate ity Ady Atma-svarupa-vidhy-artha-j~nAnottara-kAla-bhAvi kimcid anuShTheyam bhavati | kintu nAham kartA, nAham bhoktA ity Ady AtmaikatvAkartR^itvAdi-viShaya-j~nAnAt nAnyad utpadyate iti eSha visheSha upapadyate | yaH punaH kartA aham iti vetti AtmAnam, tasya mama idam kartavyam iti avashyambhAvinI buddhiH syAt | tad-apekShayA so 'dhikriyate iti tam prati karmANi sambhavanti | sa ca avidvAn ubhau tau na vijAnItaH iti vacanAt visheShitasya ca viduShaH karmAkShepa-vacanAt katham sa puruShaH iti | 

tasmAt visheShitasya avikriyAtma-darshinaH viduShaH mumukSho ca sarva-karma-samnyAse eva adhikAraH | ata eva bhagavAn nArAyaNaH sAmkhyAn viduSho 'viduSha ca karmiNaH pravibhajya dve niShThe grAhayati-j~nAna-yogena sAmkhyAnAm karma-yogena yoginAm iti | tathA ca putrAya Aha bhagavAn vyAsaH - dvAv imAv atha panthAnau [MahAÁA 241.6] ity Adi | tathA ca kriyA-pathash caiva purastAt pashcAt samnyAsash ca iti | etam eva vibhAgam punaH punar darshayiShyati bhagavAn --- atattvavit ahamkAra-vimUDhAtmA kartAham iti manyate, tattvavit tu, nAham karomi iti | tathA ca sarva-karmANi manasA samnyasyAste ityAdi || 

tatra kecit paNDitam-manyA vadanti --- janmAdi-ShaD-bhAva-vikriyA-rahito 'vikriyo 'kartA eko 'ham AtmA iti na kasyacit j~nAnam utpadyate, yasmin sati sarva-karma-samnyAsaH upadishyate iti | tan na | na jAyate ityAdi shAstropadeshAnarthakya-prasaN^gAt | yathA ca shAstropadesha-sAmarthyAt dharmAdharmAstitva-vij~nAnam kartush ca dehAntara-sambandha-vij~nAnam utpadyate, tathA shAstrAt tasyaiva Atmano 'vikriyatvAkartR^itvaikatvAdi-vij~nAnam kasmAt notpadyate iti praShTavyAH te | karaNAgocaratvAt iti cet, na | manasaivAnudraShTavyam [BAU 4.4.19] iti shruteH | shAstrAcAryopadesha-shama-damAdi-samskR^itam mana Atma-darshane karaNam | tathA ca tad adhigamAya anumAne Agame ca sati j~nAnam notpadyata iti sAhasa-mAtram etat | j~nAnam ca utpadyamAnam tad-viparItam aj~nAnam avashyam bAdhate ity abhyupagantavyam | tac ca aj~nAnam darshitam hantA aham, hato 'smi iti ubhau tau na vijAnIta iti | atra ca AtmanaH hanana-kriyAyAH kartR^itvam karmatvam hetu-kartR^itvam ca aj~nAna-kR^itam darshitam | tac ca sarva-kriyAsv api samAnam kartR^itvAdeH avidyA-kR^itatvam avikriyatvAt AtmanaH | vikriyAvAn hi kartA AtmanaH karma-bhUtam anyam prayojayati kuru iti | 

tad etat avisheSheNa viduShaH sarva-kriyAsu kartR^itvam hetu-kartR^itvam ca pratiShedhati bhagavAn vAsudevo viduShaH karmAdhikArAbhAva-pradarshanArtham vedAvinAshinam, katham sa puruShaH ity AdinA | kva punaH viduSho 'dhikAra iti etad uktam pUrvam eva j~nAna-yogena sAmkhyAnAm iti | tathA ca sarva-karma-samnyAsam vakShyati sarva-karmANi manasA ity AdinA || 

nanu manasA iti vacanAt na vAcikAnAm kAyikAnA ca samnyAsaH iti cet, na | sarva-karmANi iti visheShitatvAt | mAnasAnAm eva sarva-karmaNAm iti cet, na | mano-vyApAra-pUrvakatvAd vAk-kAya-vyApArANAm mano-vyApArAbhAve tad-anupapatteH | shAstrIyANAm vAk-kAya-karmaNAm kAraNAni mAnasAni karmANi varjayitvA anyAni sarva-karmANi manasA samnyasyed iti cet, na | naiva kurvan na kArayan iti visheShaNAt | sarva-karma-samnyAso 'yam bhagavatA uktaH mariShyato na jIvata iti cet, na | nava-dvAre pure dehI Aste iti visheNAnupapatteH | na hi sarva-karma-samnyAsena mR^itasya tad-dehe Asanam sambhavati | 

akurvato 'kArayata ca dehe samnyasya iti sambandho na dehe Aste iti cet, na | sarvatra Atmano 'vikriyatvAvadhAraNAt | Asana-kriyAyAsh cAdhikaraNApekShatvAt | tad-anapekShatvAc ca samnyAsasya | sampUrvas tu nyAsa-shabdo 'tra tyAgArthaH, na nikShepArthaH | tasmAt gItA-shAstre Atma-j~nAnavataH samnyAsa eva adhikAro na karmaNIti tatra tatra upariShTAt Atma-j~nAna-prakaraNe darshayiShyAmaH ||BhGS_2.21|| 

==============================

prakR^itam tu vakShyAmaH | tatra Atmano 'vinAshitvam pratij~nAtam | tat kim iveti, ucyate - 

vAsAmsi jIrNAni yathA vihAya
navAni gR^ihNAti naro 'parANi |
tathA sharIrANi vihAya jIrNAni
anyAni samyAti navAni dehI ||BhG_2.22||

vAsAmsi vastrANi jIrNAni durbalatAm gatAni yathA loke vihAya parityajya navAni abhinavAni gR^ihNAti upAdatte naraH puruSho 'parANi anyAni, tathA tadvad eva sharIrANi vihAya jIrNAni anyAni samyAti samgacchati navAni dehI AtmA puruShavat avikriya evety arthaH ||BhGS_2.22|| 

==============================

kasmAt avikriya eveti, Aha --- 

nainam chindanti shastrANi nainam dahati pAvakaH |
na cainam kledayanty Apo na shoShayati mArutaH ||BhG_2.23||

enam prakR^itam dehinam na chindanti shastrANi, niravayavatvAt nAvayava-vibhAgam kurvanti | shastrANi asy-AdIni | tathA nainam dahati pAvakaH, agnir api na bhasmIkaroti | tathA na cainam kledayanti ApaH | apAm hi sAvayavasya vastuna AdrIbhAva-karaNena avayava-vishleShApAdane sAmarthyam | tan na niravayave Atmani sambhavati | tathA snehavat dravyam sneha-shoShaNena nAshayati vAyuH | enam tv AtmAnam na shoShayati mAruto 'pi ||BhGS_2.23|| 

==============================

yata evam tasmAt -- 

acchedyo 'yam adAhyo 'yam akledyo 'shoShya eva ca |
nityaH sarva-gataH sthANur acalo 'yam sanAtanaH ||BhG_2.24||

yasmAt anyonya-nAsha-hetu-bhUtAni enam AtmAnam nAshayitum notsahante asyAdIni tasmAt nityaH | nityatvAt sarvagataH | sarva-gatatvAt sthANur iva, sthira ity etat | sthiratvAt acalo 'yam AtmA | ataH sanAtanash cirantanaH, na kAraNAt kutashcin niShpannaH, abhinava ity arthaH | 

naiteShAm lokAnAm paunaruktyam codanIyam, yataH ekenaiva lokAn AtmanaH nityatvam avikriyatvam coktam na jAyate mriyate vA ity AdinA | tatra yad eva Atma-viShayam kimcid ucyate, tad etasmAt lokArthAn nAtiricyate | kimcic chabdataH punaruktam, kimcid arthataH iti | durbodhatvAt Atma-vastunaH punaH punaH prasaN^gam ApAdya shabdAntareNa tad eva vastu nirUpayati bhagavAn vAsudevaH katham nu nAma samsAriNAm asamsAritva-buddhi-gocaratAm Apannam sat avyaktam tattvam samsAra-nivR^ittaye syAt iti ||BhGS_2.24||

==============================
kim ca-- 

avyakto 'yam acintyo 'yam avikAryo 'yam ucyate |
tasmAd evam viditvainam nAnushocitum arhasi ||BhG_2.25||

avyaktaH sarva-karaNAviShayatvAt na vyajyata iti avyakto 'yam AtmA | ataeva acintyo 'yam | yad dhi indriya-gocaras tac cintA-viShayatvam Apadyate | ayam tv AtmA anindriya-gocaratvAt acintyaH | ataeva avikAryaH, yathA kShIram dadhyAtaJNcanAdinA vikAri na tathA ayam AtmA | niravayavatvAc cAvikriyaH | na hi niravayavam kimcit vikriyAtmakam dR^iShTAm | avikriyatvAt avikAryo 'yam AtmA ucyate | tasmAt evam yathokta-prakAreNa enam AtmAnam viditvA tvam na anushocitum arhasi hantAham eShAm, mayaite hanyanta iti ||BhGS_2.25|| 

==============================

Atmano 'nityatvam abhyupagamya idam ucyate --- 

atha cainam nityajAtam nityam vA manyase mR^itam |
tathApi tvam mahAbAho naivam shocitum arhasi ||BhG_2.26||

atha ca iti abhyupagamArthaH | enam prakR^itam AtmAnam nitya-jAtam loka-prasiddhayA praty aneka-sharIrotpatti jAto jAta iti manyase | tathA prati-tat-tad-vinAsham nityam vA manyase mR^itam mR^ito mR^ita iti | tathApi tathAbhAve 'py Atmani tvam mahAbAho, na evam shocitum arhasi, janmavato nAsho nAshavato janma cety etAv avashyambhAvinAv iti ||BhGS_2.26|| 

==============================

tathA ca sati-- 

jAtasya hi dhruvo mR^ityur dhruvam janma mR^itasya ca |
tasmAd aparihArye 'rthe na tvam shocitum arhasi ||BhG_2.27||

jAtasya hi labdha-janmanaH dhruvo 'vyabhicArI mR^ityur maraNam dhruva janma mR^itasya ca | tasmAd aparihAryo 'yam janma-maraNa-lakShaNo 'rthaH | tasminn aparihArye 'rthe na tvam shocitum arhasi ||BhGS_2.27|| 


==============================

kArya-karaNa-samghAtAtma-kAnyapi bhUtAny uddishya shoko na yuktaH kartum, yataH-

avyaktAdIni bhUtAni vyakta-madhyAni bhArata |
avyakta-nidhanAny eva tatra kA paridevanA ||BhG_2.28||

avyaktAdIny avyaktam adarshanam anupalabdhiH Adir yeShAm bhUtAnAm putra-mitrAdi-kArya-karaNa-samghAtAtmakAnAm tAni avyaktadIni bhUtAni prAg-utpatteH, utpannAni ca prAN^-maraNAt vyakta-madhyAni | avyakta-nidhanAny eva punar avyaktam adarshanam nidhanam maraNam yeShAm tAni avyakta-nidhanAni | maraNAd Urdhvam apy avyaktatAm eva pratipadyante ity arthaH | tathA coktam --- 

adarshanAd ApatitaH punash cAdarshanam gataH | 
nAsau tava na tasya tvam vR^ithA kA paridevanA || [MahA. StrI. 2.13] iti | 

tatra kA paridevanA ko vA pralApo 'dR^iShTa-dR^iShTa-pranaShTa-bhrAnti-bhUteShu bhUteShv ity arthaH ||BhGS_2.28||

==============================

durvij~neyo 'tham prakR^ita AtmA | kim tvAmevaikamupAlabhe sAdhAraNe bhrAntinimitte | katham durvij~neyo 'yamAtmA ityata Aha --- 

Ashcaryavat pashyati kashcid enam
Ashcaryavad vadati tathaiva cAnyaH |
Ashcaryavac cainam anyaH shR^iNoti
shrutvApy enam veda na caiva kashcit ||BhG_2.29||


Ashcaryavat Ashcaryam adR^iShTa-pUrvam adbhutam akasmAd dR^ishyamAnam tena tulyam Ashcaryavat Ashcaryam iva enam AtmAnam pashyati kashcit | Ashcaryavad enam vadati tathaiva cAnyaH | Ashcaryavac ca enam anyaH sR^iNoti | shrutvA dR^iShTvA uktvApi enam AtmAnam veda na caiva kashcit | athavA yo 'yam AtmAnam pashyati sa Ashcarya-tulyaH, yo vadati ya ca sR^iNoti so 'neka-sahasreShu kashcid eva bhavati | ato durbodha AtmA ity abhiprAyaH ||BhGS_2.29|| 

==============================

athedAnIm prakaraNArtham upasamharan brUte - 

dehI nityam avadhyo 'yam dehe sarvasya bhArata |
tasmAt sarvANi bhUtAni na tvam shocitum arhasi ||BhG_2.30||

dehI sharIrI nityam sarvadA sarvAvasthAsu avadhyaH niravayavatvAn nityatvAc ca | tatra avadhyo 'yam dehe sharIre sarvasya sarva-gatatvAt sthAvarAdiShu sthito 'pi sarvasya prANi-jAtasya dehe vadhyamAne 'py ayam dehI na vadhyo yasmAt, tasmAd bhIShmAdIni sarvANi bhUtAni uddishya na tvam shocitum arhasi ||BhGS_2.30|| 

==============================

iha paramArtha-tattvApekShAyAm shoko moho vA na sambhavatIty uktam | na kevalam paramArtha-tattvApekShAyAm eva, kim tu --- 

sva-dharmam api cAvekShya na vikampitum arhasi |
dharmyAd dhi yuddhAc chreyo 'nyat kShatriyasya na vidyate ||BhG_2.31||

svadharmam api svo dharmaH kShatriyasya yuddham tam api avekShya tvam na vikampitum pracalitum nArhasi kShatriyasya svAbhAvikAd dharmAd Atma-svAbhAvyAd ity abhiprAyaH | tac ca yuddham pR^ithivI-jaya-dvAreNa dharmArtham prajA-rakShaNArtham ceti dharmAd anapetam param dharmyam | tasmAd dharmyAd yuddhAc chreyo 'nyat kShatriyasya na vidyate hi yasmAt ||BhGS_2.31||

==============================

kutash ca tat yuddham kartavyam iti, ucyate --- 

yadR^icchayA copapannam svarga-dvAram apAvR^itam |
sukhinaH kShatriyAH pArtha labhante yuddham IdR^isham ||BhG_2.32||

yadR^icchayA ca aprArthitatayA upapannam Agatam svarga-dvAram apAvR^itam udghATitam ya etad IdR^isham yuddham labhante kShatriyAH he pArtha, kim na sukhinas te ? ||BhGS_2.32|| 

==============================
etam kartavyatA-prAptam api - 

atha cet tvam imam dharmyam samgrAmam na kariShyasi |
tataH sva-dharmam kIrtim ca hitvA pApam avApsyasi ||BhG_2.33||

atha cet tvam imam dharmyam dharmAd anapetam vihitam samgrAmam yuddham na kariShyasi cet, tataH tad-akaraNAt svadharmam kIrtim ca mahA-devAdi-samAgama-nimittAm hitvA kevalam pApam avApsyasi ||BhGS_2.33|| 

==============================

na kevalam svadharma-kIrti-parityAgaH - 

akIrtim cApi bhUtAni kathayiShyanti te 'vyayAm |
sambhAvitasya cAkIrtir maraNAd atiricyate ||BhG_2.34||

akIrtim cApi yuddhA bhUtAni kathayiShyanti te tava avyayAm dIrgha-kAlAm | dharmAtmA shUra ity evam AdibhiH guNaiH sambhAvitasya ca akIrtiH maraNAt atiricyate, sambhAvitasya ca akIrteH varam maraNam ity arthaH ||BhGS_2.34|| 

==============================

kim ca-- 

bhayAd raNAd uparatam mamsyante tvAm mahArathAH |
yeShAm ca tvam bahumato bhUtvA yAsyasi lAghavam ||BhG_2.35||

bhayAt karNAdibhyaH raNAt yuddhAt uparatam nivR^ittam mamsyante cintayiShyanti na kR^ipayeti tvAm mahArathAH duryodhana-prabhR^itayaH | yeShAm ca tvam duryodhanAdInAm bahu-mato bahubhir guNair yuktaH ity evam mataH bahumato bhUtvA punar yAsyasi lAghavam laghu-bhAvam ||BhGS_2.35|| 

==============================
kim ca -- 

avAcya-vAdAmsh ca bahUn vadiShyanti tavAhitAH |
nindantas tava sAmarthyam tato duHkhataram nu kim ||BhG_2.36||

avAcya-vAdAn avaktavya-vAdAmsh ca bahUn aneka-prakArAn vadiShyanti tavAhitAH shatravaH nindantaH kutsayantaH tava tvadIyam sAmarthyam nivAta-kavacAdi-yuddha-nimittam | tatas tasmAt nindA-prApter duHkhAt duHkhataram nu kim ? tataH kaShTataram duHkham nAstIty arthaH ||BhGS_2.36|| 

==============================

yurA punaH kriyamANe karNAdibhiH-

hato vA prApsyasi svargam jitvA vA bhokShyase mahIm |
tasmAd uttiShTha kaunteya yuddhAya kR^ita-nishcayaH ||BhG_2.37||

hato vA prApsyasi svargam, hataH san svargam prApsyasi | jitvA vA karNAdIn shUrAn bhokShyase mahIm | ubhayathApi tava lAbha evety abhiprAyaH | yata evam tasmAt uttiShTha kaunteya yuddhAya kR^itAni ca yaH jeShyAmi shatrUn, mariShyAmi vA iti nishcayam kR^itvety arthaH ||BhGS_2.37|| 

==============================

tatra yuddham svadharma ity evam yudhyamAnasyopadesham imam sR^iNu - 

sukha-duHkhe same kR^itvA lAbhAlAbhau jayAjayau |
tato yuddhAya yujyasva naivam pApam avApsyasi ||BhG_2.38||

sukha-duHkhe same tulye kR^itvA, rAga-dveShAv apy akR^itvety etat | tathA lAbhAlAbhau jayAjayau ca samau kR^itvA tato yuddhAya yujyasva ghaTAsva | na evam yuddham kurvan pApam avApsyasi | ity eSha upadeshaH prAsaN^gikaH ||BhGS_2.38|| 
 
==============================

shoka-mohApanayanAya laukiko nyAyaH svadharmam api cAvekShya ity AdyaiH lokair uktaH, na tu tAtparyeNa | paramArtha-darshanam iha prakR^itam | tac coktam upasamhriyate -- eShA te 'bhihitA iti shAstra-viShaya-vibhAga-pradarshanAya | iha hi pradarshite punaH shAstra-viShaya-vibhAge upariShTAt j~nAna-yogena sAmkhyAnAm karma-yogena yoginAm iti niShThA-dvaya-viShayam shAstram sukham pravartiShyate, shrotArash ca viShaya-vibhAgena sukham grahIShyanti ity ata Aha --- 

eShA te 'bhihitA sAmkhye buddhir yoge tv imAm shR^iNu |
buddhyA yukto yayA pArtha karmabandham prahAsyasi ||BhG_2.39||

eShA te tubhyam abhihitA uktA sAmkhye paramArtha-vastu-viveka-viShaye buddhir j~nAnam sAkShAt shoka-mohAdi-samsAra-hetu-doSha-nivR^itti-kAraNam | yoge tu tat-prApty-upAye niHsaN^gatayA dvandva-prahANa-pUrvakam IshvarArAdhanArthe karma-yoge karmAnuShThAne samAdhi-yoge cemAm anantaram evocyamAnAm buddhim shR^iNu | tAm ca buddhim stauti prarocanArtham -- buddhyA yayA yoga-viShayayA yuktaH | he pArtha, karma-bandham karmaiva dharmAdharmAkhyo bandhaH karma-bandhas tam prahAsyasi Ishvara-prasAda-nimitta-j~nAna-prApter ity abhiprAyaH ||BhGS_2.39|| 

==============================

kim cAnyat -- 

nehAbhikrama-nAsho 'sti pratyavAyo na vidyate |
svalpam apy asya dharmasya trAyate mahato bhayAt ||BhG_2.40||


neha mokSha-mArge karma-yoge abhikrama-nAsho 'bhikramaNam abhikramaH prArambhas tasya nAsho nAsti yathA kR^iShyAdeH | yoga-viShaye prArambhasya na anaikAntika-phalatvam ity arthaH | kim ca nApi cikitsAvat pratyavAyo vidyate bhavati | kim tu svalpam api asya dharmasya yoga-dharmasya anuShThitam trAyate rakShati mahataH bhayAt samsAra-bhayAt janma-maraNAdi-lakShaNAt ||BhGS_2.40|| 

==============================

yeyam sAmkhye buddhir uktA yoge ca, vakShyamANa-lakShaNA sA - 

vyavasAyAtmikA buddhir ekeha kuru-nandana |
bahu-shAkhA hy anantAsh ca buddhayo 'vyavasAyinAm ||BhG_2.41||

vyavasAyAtmikA nishcaya-svabhAvA ekA eva buddhir itara-viparIta-buddhi-shAkhA-bhedasya vAdhikA, samyak-pramANa-janitatvAt, iha shreyo-mArge | he kurunandana ! yAH punar itarA viparIta-buddhayaH, yAsAm shAkhA-bheda-pracAra-vashAt ananto 'pAro 'nuparataH 
samsAro nitya-pratato vistIrNo bhavati, pramANa-janita-viveka-buddhi-nimitta-vashAc ca uparatAsv ananta-bheda-buddhiShu samsAro 'py uparamate tA buddhayo bahu-shAkhAH bahvvayaH shAkhAH yAsAm tAH bahu-shAkhAH, bahu-bhedA ity etat | pratishAkhA-bhedena hy anantA ca buddhayaH | keShAm ? avyavasAyinAm pramANa-janita-viveka-buddhi-rahitAnAm ity arthaH ||BhGS_2.41|| 

==============================

yeShAm vyavasAyAtmikA buddhir nAsti te-- 

yAm imAm puShpitAm vAcam pravadanty avipashcitaH |
veda-vAda-ratAH pArtha nAnyad astIti vAdinaH ||BhG_2.42||

yAm imAm vakShyamANAm puShpitAm puShpita iva vR^ikShaH shobhamAnAm shrUyamANa-ramaNIyAm vAcam vAkya-lakShaNAm pravadanti | ke ? avipashcito 'medhaso 'vivekina ity arthaH | veda-vAda-ratAH bahvy-artha-vAda-phala-sAdhana-prakAshakeShu veda-vAkyeShu ratAH he pArtha, na anyat svarga-prApty-Adi-phala-sAdhanebhyaH karmabhyo 'sti ity evam vAdinaH vadana-shIlAH ||BhGS_2.42|| 

==============================
 
te ca -- 

kAmAtmAnaH svarga-parA janma-karma-phala-pradAm |
kriyA-visheSha-bahulAm bhogaishvarya-gatim prati ||BhG_2.43||

kAmAtmAnaH kAmasvabhAvAH, kAmaparA ity arthaH | svarga-parAH svargaH paraH puruShArthaH yeShAm te svarga-parAH svarga-pradhAnAH | janma-karma-phala-pradAm karmaNaH phalam karma-phalam janmaiva karma-phalam janma-karma-phalam tat pradadAtIti janma-karma-phala-pradA, tAm vAcam | pravadanti ity anuShajyate | kriyA-visheSha-bahulAm kriyANAm visheShAH kriyA-visheShAH te bahulA yasyAm vAci tAm svarga-pashu-putrAdy-arthAH yayA vAcA bAhulyena prakAshyante | bhogaishvarya-gatim prati bhogash ca aishvaryam ca bhogaishvarye, tayor gatiH prAptiH bhogaishvarya-gatiH, tAm prati sAdhana-bhUtAH ye kriyA-visheShAH tad-bahulAm tAm vAcam pravadantaH mUDhAH samsAre parivartante ity abhiprAyaH ||BhGS_2.43|| 

==============================

teShAm ca - 

bhogaishvarya-prasaktAnAm tayApahR^ita-cetasAm |
vyavasAyAtmikA buddhiH samAdhau na vidhIyate ||BhG_2.44||

bhogaishvarya-prasaktAnAm bhogaH kartavyaH caishvaryam ca iti bhogaishvaryayor eva praNayavatAm tad-Atma-bhUtAnAm | tayA kriyA-visheSha-bahulayA vAcA apahR^ita-cetasAm AcchAdita-viveka-praj~nAnAm vyavasAyAtmikA sAmkhye yoge vA buddhiH samAdhau samAdhIyate asmin puruShopabhogAya sarvam iti samAdhiH antaHkaraNam buddhiH tasmin samAdhau, na vidhIyate na bhavati ity arthaH ||BhGS_2.44||

==============================

ya evam viveka-buddhi-rahitAH teShAm kAmAtmanAm yat phalam tad Aha - 

traiguNya-viShayA vedA nistraiguNyo bhavArjuna |
nirdvandvo nitya-sattva-stho niryoga-kShema AtmavAn ||BhG_2.45||

traiguNya-viShayAH traiguNyam samsAro viShayaH prakAshayitavyaH yeShAm te vedAH traiguNya-viShayAH | tvam tu nistraiguNyo bhava arjuna, niShkAmo bhava ity arthaH | nirdvandvaH sukha-duHkha-hetU sa-pratipakShau padArthau dvandva-shabda-vAcyau | tataH nirgataH nirdvandvo bhava | nitya-sattva-sthaH sadA sattva-guNAshrito bhava | tathA niryoga-kShemo 'nupAttasya upAdAnam yogaH, upAttasya rakShaNam kShemaH, yoga-kShema-pradhAnasya shreyasi pravR^ittir duShkarA ity ataH niryoga-kShemo bhava | AtmavAn apramattash ca bhava | eSha tava upadeshaH sva-dharmam anutiShThataH ||BhGS_2.45|| 

==============================

sarveShu vedokteShu karmasu yAny uktAny anantAni phalAni tAni nApekShyante cet, kim artham tAni IshvarAyety anuShThIyante ity ucyate | sR^iNu - 

yAvAn artha udapAne sarvataH samplutodake |
tAvAn sarveShu vedeShu brAhmaNasya vijAnataH ||BhG_2.46||

yathA loke kUpa-taDAgAdy-anekasmin udapAne paricchinnodake yAvAn yAvat-parimANaH snAna-pAnAdir arthaH phalam prayojanam sa sarvo 'rthaH sarvataH samplutodake 'pi yo 'rthaH tAvAn eva sampadyate, tatra antarbhavatIty arthaH | evam tAvAn tAvat-parimANa eva sampadyate sarveShu vedeShu vedokteShu karmasu yo 'rthaH yat karma-phalam so 'rthaH brAhmaNasya samnyAsinaH paramArtha-tattvam vijAnataH yo 'rthaH yat vij~nAna-phalam sarvataH samplutodaka-sthAnIyam tasmin tAvAn eva sampadyate tatraivAntarbhavatIty arthaH | yathA kR^itAya vijitAyAdhareyAH samyanty evam enam sarvam tad abhisameti yat kimcit prajAH sAdhu kurvanti yas tad veda yat sa veda [ChAU 4.1.2] iti shruteH | sarvam karmAkhilam iti ca vakShyati | tasmAt prAk j~nAna-niShThAdhikAra-prApteH karmaNy adhikR^itena kUpa-taDAgAdy-artha-sthAnIyam api karma kartavyam ||BhGS_2.46|| 

==============================

tava ca - 

karmaNy evAdhikAras te mA phaleShu kadAcana |
mA karma-phala-hetur bhUr mA te saN^go 'stv akarmaNi ||BhG_2.47||

karmaNy evAdhikAro na j~nAna-niShThAyAm te tava | tatra ca karma kurvataH mA phaleShu adhikAro 'stu, karma-phala-tR^iShNA mA bhUt kadAcana kasyAmcid apy avasthAyAm ity arthaH | yadA karma-phale tR^iShNA te syAt tadA karma-phala-prApter hetuH syAH, evam mA karma-phala-hetuH bhUH | yadA hi karma-phala-tR^iShNA-prayuktaH karmaNi pravartate tadA karma-phalasyaiva janmano hetur bhavet | yadi karma-phalam neShyate, kim karmaNA duHkha-rUpeNa ? iti mA te tava saN^go 'stv akarmaNi akaraNe prItir mA bhUt ||BhGS_2.47||

==============================


yadi karma-phala-prayuktena na kartavyam karma, katham tarhi kartavyam iti | ucyate -

yogasthaH kuru karmANi saN^gam tyaktvA dhanamjaya |
siddhy-asiddhyoH samo bhUtvA samatvam yoga ucyate ||BhG_2.48||

yoga-sthaH san kuru karmANi kevalam IshvarArtham | tatrApIshvaro me tuShyatu iti saN^gam tyaktvA dhanamjaya | phala-tR^iShNA-shUnyena kriyamANe karmaNi sattva-shuddhijA j~nAna-prApti-lakShaNA siddhiH, tad-viparyayajA asiddhiH, tayoH siddhy-asiddhyor api samaH tulyo bhUtvA kuru karmANi | ko 'sau yogo yatra-sthaH kuru ity uktam ? idam eva tat --- siddhy-asiddhyoH samatvam yoga ucyate ||BhGS_2.48||

==============================


yat punaH samatva-buddhi-yuktam IshvarArAdhanArtham karmoktam, etasmAt karmaNaH -- 

dUreNa hy avaram karma buddhi-yogAd dhanamjaya |
buddhau sharaNam anviccha kR^ipaNAH phala-hetavaH ||BhG_2.49||

dUreNa ativiprakarSheNa atyantam eva hy avaram adhamam nikR^iShTam karma phalArthinA kriyamANam buddhi-yogAt samatva-buddhi-yuktAt karmaNaH, janma-maraNAdi-hetutvAt | he dhanamjaya, yata evam tataH yoga-viShayAyAm buddhau tat-paripAka-jAyAm vA sAmkhya-buddhau sharaNam Ashrayam abhaya-prApti-kAraNam anviccha prArthayasva, paramArtha-j~nAna-sharaNo bhavety arthaH | yato 'varam karma kurvANAH kR^ipaNAH dInAH phala-hetavaH phala-tR^iShNA-prayuktAH santaH, yo vA etad akSharam gArgy aviditvAsmAl lokAt praiti sa kR^ipaNaH [BAU 3.8.10] iti shruteH ||BhGS_2.49||

==============================

samatva-buddhi-yuktaH san svadharmam anutiShThan yat phalam prApnoti tac chR^iNu -- 

buddhi-yukto jahAtIha ubhe sukR^ita-duShkR^ite |
tasmAd yogAya yujyasva yogaH karmasu kaushalam ||BhG_2.50||

buddhi-yuktaH karma-samatva-viShayayA buddhyA yukto buddhi-yuktaH saH jahAti parityajati iha asmin loke ubhe sukR^ita-duShkR^ite puNya-pApe sattva-shuddhi-j~nAna-prApti-dvAreNa yataH, tasmAt samatva-buddhi-yogAya yujyasva ghaTAsva | yogo hi karmasu kaushalam sva-dharmAkhyeShu karmasu vartamAnasya yA siddhy-asiddhyoH samatva-buddhir IshvarArpita-cetastayA tat kaushalam kushala-bhAvaH | tad dhi kaushalam yad bandhana-svabhAvAny api karmANi samatva-buddhyA svabhAvAn nivartante | tasmAt samatva-buddhi-yukto bhava tvam ||BhGS_2.50|| 

==============================

yasmAt - 
karmajam buddhi-yuktA hi phalam tyaktvA manIShiNaH |
janma-bandha-vinirmuktAH padam gacchanty anAmayam ||BhG_2.51||

karmajam phalam tyaktvA iti vyavahitena sambandhaH | iShTAniShTa-deha-prAptiH karmajam phalam karmabhyo jAtam buddhi-yuktAH samatva-buddhi-yuktAH santaH hi yasmAt phalam tyaktvA parityajya manIShiNaH j~nAnino bhUtvA, janma-bandha-vinirmuktAH janmaiva bandhaH janma-bandhaH tena vinirmuktAH jIvanta eva janma-bandhAt vinirmuktAH santaH, padam paramam viShNoH mokShAkhyam gacchanti anAmayam sarvopadrava-rahitam ity arthaH | athavA buddhi-yogAd dhanamjaya ity Arabhya paramArtha-darshana-lakShaNaiva sarvataH samplutodaka-sthAnIyA karma-yogaja-sattva-shuddha-janitA buddhir darshitA, sAkShAt-sukR^ita-duShkR^ita-prahANAdi-hetutva-shravaNAt ||BhGS_2.51|| 

==============================

yogAnuShThAna-janita-sattva-shuddhajA buddhiH kadA prApsyate ity ucyate --- 

yadA te moha-kalilam buddhir vyatitariShyati |
tadA gantAsi nirvedam shrotavyasya shrutasya ca ||BhG_2.52||


yadA yasmin kAle te tava moha-kalilam mohAtmakam aviveka-rUpam kAluShyam yena AtmAnAtma-viveka-bodham kaluShIkR^itya viShayam pratyantaH-karaNam pravartate, tat tava buddhiH vyatitariShyati vyatikramiShyati, atishuddha-bhAvam ApAtryate ity arthaH | tadA tasmin kAle gantAsi prApsyasi nirvedam vairAgyam shrotavyasya shrutasya ca, tadA shrotavyam shrutam ca te niShphalam pratibhAtIty abhiprAyaH ||BhGS_2.52|| 

==============================

moha-kalilAtyaya-dvAreNa labdhAtma-vivekaja-praj~naH kadA karma-yogajam phalam paramArtha-yogam avApsyAmIti cet, tat sR^iNu -- 

shruti-vipratipannA te yadA sthAsyati nishcalA |
samAdhAv acalA buddhis tadA yogam avApsyasyi ||BhG_2.53||

shruti-vipratinnA aneka-sAdhya-sAdhana-sambandha-prakAshana-shrutibhiH shravaNaiH pravR^itti-nivR^itti-lakShaNaiH vipratipannA nAnA-pratinnA vikShiptA satI te tava buddhir yadA yasmin kAle sthAsyati sthirIbhUtA bhaviShyati nishcalA vikShepa-calana-varjitA satI samAdhau, samAdhIyate cittam asminn iti samAdhir AtmA, tasmin Atmani ity etat | acalA tatrApi vikalpa-varjitA ity etat | buddhir antaHkaraNam | tadA tasmin kAle yogam avApsyasi viveka-praj~nAm samAdhim prApsyasi ||BhGS_2.53||

==============================

prashnabIjam pratilabhya arjuna uvAcalabdhasamAdhipraj~nasya lakShaNabubhutsayA --- 
arjuna uvAca-

arjuna uvAca
sthita-praj~nasya kA bhAShA samAdhi-sthasya keshava |
sthita-dhIH kim prabhASheta kim AsIta vrajeta kim ||BhG_2.54||

sthitA pratiShThitA aham asmi param brahma iti praj~nA yasya saH sthita-praj~nas tasya sthita-praj~nasya kA bhAShA kim bhAShaNam vacanam katham asau parair bhAShyate samAdhi-sthasya samAdhau sthitasya he keshava | sthita-dhIH sthita-praj~naH svayam vA kim prabhASheta | kim AsIta vrajeta kim Asanam vrajanam vA tasya katham ity arthaH | sthita-praj~nasya lakShaNam anena lokena pR^icchayate ||BhGS_2.54||

==============================

yo hy Adita eva samnyasya karmANi j~nAna-yoga-niShThAyAm pravR^ittaH, yash ca karma-yogena, tayoH prajahAti ity Arabhya A adhyAya-parisamApteH sthita-praj~na-lakShaNam sAdhanam copadishyate | sarvatraiva hi adhyAtma-shAstre kR^itArtha-lakShaNAni yAni tAny eva sAdhanAni upadishyante, yatna-sAdhyatvAt | yAni yatna-sAdhyAni sAdhanAni lakShaNAni ca bhavanti tAni shrI-bhagavAn uvAca-- 
prajahAti yadA kAmAn sarvAn pArtha mano-gatAn |
Atmany evAtmanA tuShTaH sthita-praj~nas tadocyate ||BhG_2.55||

prajahAti prakarSheNa jahAti parityajati yadA yasmin kAle sarvAn samastAn kAmAn icchA-bhedAn he pArtha, mano-gatAn manasi praviShTAan hR^idi praviShTAn | sarva-kAma-parityAge tuShTi-kAraNAbhAvAt sharIra-dhAraNa-nimitta-sheShe ca sati unmatta-pramattasyeva pravR^ittiH prAptA, ity ata ucyate --- Atmany eva pratyag-Atma-svarUpe eva AtmanA svenaiva bAhya-lAbha-nirapekShas tuShTAH paramArtha-darshanAmR^ita-rasa-lAbhena anyasmAd alam-pratyayavAn sthita-praj~naH sthitA pratiShThitA AtmAnAtma-vivekajA praj~nA yasya saH sthita-praj~naH vidvAn tadA ucyate | tyakta-putra-vitta-lokaiShaNaH samnyAsI AtmArAma Atma-krIDAH sthita-praj~na ity arthaH ||BhGS_2.55|| 

==============================

kim ca -- 

duHkheShv anudvigna-manAH sukheShu vigata-spR^ihaH |
vIta-rAga-bhaya-krodhaH sthita-dhIr munir ucyate ||BhG_2.56||

duHkheShv AdhyAtmikAdiShu prApteShu na udvignam na prakShubhitam duHkha-prAptau mano yasya so 'yam anudvigna-manAH | tathA sukheShu prApteShu vigatA spR^ihA tR^iShNA yasya, na agnir iva indhanAdy-AdhAne sukhAny anu vivardhate sa vigata-spR^ihaH | vIta-rAga-bhaya-krodhaH rAga ca bhayam ca krodha ca vItA vigatA yasmAt sa vIta-rAga-bhaya-krodhaH | sthita-dhIH sthita-praj~no muniH samnyAsI tadA ucyate ||BhGS_2.56|| 

==============================

kim ca-- 

yaH sarvatrAnabhisnehas tat tat prApya shubhAshubham |
nAbhinandati na dveShTi tasya praj~nA pratiShThitA ||BhG_2.57||

yaH muniH sarvatra deha-jIvitAdiShv api anabhisneho 'bhisneha-varjitas tat tat prApya shubhAshubham tat tat shubham ashubham vA labdhvA nAbhinandati na dveShTi shubham prApya na tuShyati na hR^iShyati, ashubham ca prApya na dveShTi ity arthaH | tasya evam harSha-viShAda-varjitasya vivekajA praj~nA pratiShThitA bhavati ||BhGS_2.57|| 

==============================

kim ca -- 

yadA samharate cAyam kUrmo 'N^gAnIva sarvashaH |
indriyANIndriyArthebhyas tasya praj~nA pratiShThitA ||BhG_2.58||

yadA samharate samyag upasamharate cAyam j~nAna-niShThAyAm pravR^itto yatiH kUrmo 'N^gAni iva yathA kUrmo bhayAt svAny aN^gAni upasamharati sarvashaH sarvataH, evam j~nAna-niShThaH indriyANi indriyArthebhyaH sarva-viShayebhya upasamharate | tasya praj~nA pratiShThitA ity uktArtham vAkyam ||BhGS_2.58||


==============================

tatra viShayAn anAharataH AturasyApi indriyANi kUrmAN^gAnIva samhriyante na tu tad-viShayo rAgaH sa katham samhriyate ity ucyate - 

viShayA vinivartante nirAhArasya dehinaH |
rasa-varjam raso 'py asya param dR^iShTvA nivartate ||BhG_2.59||

yadyapi viShayAH viShayopalakShitAni viShaya-shabda-vAcyAni indriyANi nirAhArasya anAhriyamANa-viShayasya kaShTe tapasi sthitasya mUrkhasyApi vinivartante dehino dehavataH rasa-varjam raso rAgo viShayeShu yas tam varjayitvA | rasa-shabdo rAge prasiddhaH, sva-rasena pravR^ittaH rasikaH rasaj~naH, ity Adi-darshanAt | so 'pi raso ra¤jana-rUpaH sUkShmo 'sya yateH param paramArtha-tattvam brahma dR^iShTvA upalabhya aham eva tat iti vartamAnasya nivartate nirbIjam viShaya-vij~nAnam sampadyate ity arthaH | nAsati samyag-darshane rasasya ucchedaH | tasmAt samyag-darshanAtmikAyAH praj~nAyAH sthairyam kartavyam ity abhiprAyaH ||BhGS_2.59|| 

==============================

samyag-darshana-lakShaNa-praj~nA-sthairyam cikIrShatA Adau indriyANi sva-vashe sthApayitavyAni, yasmAt tad-anavasthApane doSham Aha --- 

yatato hy api kaunteya puruShasya vipashcitaH |
indriyANi pramAthIni haranti prasabham manaH ||BhG_2.60||

yatataH prayatnam kurvataH hi yasmAt kaunteya puruShasya vipashcitaH medhAvino 'pi iti vyavahitena sambandhaH | indriyANi pramAthIni pramathana-shIlAni viShayAbhimukham hi puruSham vikShobhayanti AkulIkurvanti, AkulIkR^itya ca haranti prasabham prasahya prakAsham eva pashyato viveka-vij~nAna-yuktam manaH ||BhGS_2.60||

==============================

yatas tasmAt-- 

tAni sarvANi samyamya yukta AsIta mat-paraH |
vashe hi yasyendriyANi tasya praj~nA pratiShThitA ||BhG_2.61||

tAni sarvANi samyamya samyamanam vashIkaraNam kR^itvA yuktaH samAhitaH san AsIta mat-paro 'ham vAsudevaH sarva-pratyag-AtmA paro yasya sa mat-paraH, nAnyo 'ham tasmAt ity AsIta ity arthaH | evam AsInasya yater vashe hi yasyendriyANi vartante abhyAsa-balAt tasya praj~nA pratiShThitA ||BhGS_2.61||

==============================

athedAnIm parAbhaviShyataH sarvAnartha-mUlam idam ucyate -- 

dhyAyato viShayAn pumsaH saN^gas teShUpajAyate |
saN^gAt samjAyate kAmaH kAmAt krodho 'bhijAyate ||BhG_2.62||
krodhAd bhavati sammohaH sammohAt smR^iti-vibhramaH |
smR^iti-bhramshAd buddhi-nAsho buddhi-nAshAt praNashyati ||BhG_2.63||

dhyAyatash cintayato viShayAt shabdAdIn viShaya-visheShAn AlocayataH pumsaH puruShasya saN^gaH AsaktiH prItis teShu viShayeShu upajAyate utpadyate | saN^gAt prIteH samjAyate samutpadyate kAmas tR^iShNA | kAmAt kutashcit pratihatAt krodho 'bhijAyate |

krodhAd bhavati sammoho 'vivekaH kAryAkArya-viShayaH | kruddho hi sammUDhaH san gurum apy Akroshati | sammohAt smR^iti-vibhramaH shAstrAcAryopadeshAhita-samskAra-janitAyAH smR^ite syAt vibhramo bhramshaH smR^ity-utpatti-nimitta-prAptau anutpattiH | tataH smR^iti-bhramshAt buddhi-nAshaH buddhi-nAshaH | kAryAkArya-viShaya-vivekAyogyatA antaH-karaNasya buddher nAsha ucyate | buddher nAshAt praNashyati | tAvad eva hi puruShaH yAvad antaHkaraNam tadIyam kAryAkArya-viShaya-viveka-yogyam | tad-ayogyatve naShTa eva puruSho bhavati | ataH tasyAntaH-karaNasya buddher nAshAt praNashyati puruShArthAyogyo bhavatIty arthaH ||BhGS_2.62-63|| 
 
==============================

sarvAnarthasya mUlamuktam viShayAbhidhyAnam | atha idAnIm mokShakAraNamidamucyate -- 

rAga-dveSha-viyuktais tu viShayAn indriyaish caran |
Atma-vashyair vidheyAtmA prasAdam adhigacchati ||BhG_2.64||

rAga-dveSha-viyuktai rAgash ca dveShash ca rAga-dveShau, tat-puraHsarA hi indriyANAm pravR^ittiH svAbhAvikI, tatra yo mumukShuH bhavati saH tAbhyAm viyuktaiH shrotrAdibhir indriyair viShayAn avarjanIyAn caran upalabhamAnaH Atma-vashyair Atmano vashyAni vashIbhUtAni indriyANi tair Atma-vashyair vidheyAtmA icchAtaH vidheya AtmA antaH-karaNam yasya so 'yam prasAdam adhigacchati | prasAdaH prasannatA svAsthyam ||BhGS_2.64||

==============================

prasAde sati kim syAt ity ucyate -
 
prasAde sarva-duHkhAnAm hAnir asyopajAyate |
prasanna-cetaso hy Ashu buddhiH paryavatiShThate ||BhG_2.65||

prasAde sarva-duHkhAnAm AdhyAtmikAdInAm hAnir vinAsho 'sya yater upajAyate | kim ca - prasanna-cetasaH svasthAntaH-karaNasya hi yasmAt Ashu shIghram buddhiH paryavatiShThate AkAsham iva pari samantAt avatiShThate, Atma-svarUpeNaiva nishcalIbhavatIty arthaH | 
evam prasanna-cetaso 'vasthita-buddhiH kR^ita-kR^ityatA yataH, tasmAt rAga-dveSha-viyuktair indriyaiH shAstrA-viruddheShu avarjanIyeShu yuktaH samAcaret iti vAkyArthaH ||BhGS_2.65|| 

==============================

seyam prasannatA stUyate -- 

nAsti buddhirayuktasya na cAyuktasya bhAvanA |
na cAbhAvayataH shAntir ashAntasya kutaH sukham ||BhG_2.66||

nAsti na vidyate na bhavatIty arthaH, buddhiH Atma-svarUpa-viShayA ayuktasya asamAhitAntaH-karaNasya | na ca asti ayuktasya bhAvanA Atma-j~nAnAbhiniveshaH | tathA -- na cAsty abhAvayata Atma-j~nAnAbhinivesham akurvataH shAntir upashamaH | ashAntasya kutaH sukham ? indriyANAm hi viShaya-sevA-tR^iShNAtaH nivR^ittir yA tat-sukham, na viShaya-viShayA tR^iShNA | duHkham eva hi sA | na tR^iShNAyAm satyAm sukhasya gandha-mAtram apy upapadyate ity arthaH ||BhGS_2.66|| 

==============================

ayuktasya kasmAd buddhir nAsti ity ucyate -

indriyANAm hi caratAm yan mano 'nuvidhIyate |
tad asya harati praj~nAm vAyur nAvam ivAmbhasi ||BhG_2.67||

indriyANAm hi yasmAt caratAm sva-sva-viShayeShu pravartamAnAnAm yat mano 'nuvidhIyate anupravartate tat indriya-viShaya-vikalpanena pravR^ittam mano 'sya yateH harati praj~nAm AtmAnAtma-vivekajAm nAshayati | katham ? vAyuH nAvam iva ambhasi udake jigamiShatAm mArgAduddhR^itya unmArge yathA vAyuH nAvam pravartayati, evam Atma-viShayAm praj~nAm hR^itvA mano viShaya-viShayAm karoti ||BhGS_2.67||

==============================

yatato hi ity upanyastasyArthasya anekadhA upapattim uktvA tam cArtham upapAdya upasamharati --- 

tasmAd yasya mahAbAho nigR^ihItAni sarvashaH |
indriyANIndriyArthebhyas tasya praj~nA pratiShThitA ||BhG_2.68||

indriyANAm pravR^ittau doSha upapAdito yasmAt tasmAt yasya yateH he mahAbAho, nigR^ihItAni sarvashaH sarva-prakAraiH mAnasAdi-bhedaiH indriyANi indriyArthebhyaH shabdAdibhyas tasya praj~nA pratiShThitA ||BhGS_2.68|| 

==============================

yo 'yam laukiko vaidika ca vyavahAraH sa utpanna-viveka-j~nAnasya sthita-praj~nasya avidyAkAryatvAt avidyA-nivR^ittau nivartate, avidyAyA ca vidyA-virodhAt nivR^ittiH, ity etam artham sphuTIkurvann Aha --- 

yA nishA sarva-bhUtAnAm tasyAm jAgarti samyamI |
yasyAm jAgrati bhUtAni sA nishA pashyato muneH ||BhG_2.69||

yA nishA rAtriH sarva-padArthAnAm aviveka-karI tamaH-svabhAvatvAt sarva-bhUtAnAm sarveShAm bhUtAnAm | kim tat paramArtha-tattvam sthita-praj~nasya viShayaH | yathA naktam-carANAm ahar eva sad anyeShAm nishA bhavati, tadvat naktam-cara-sthAnIyAnAm aj~nAnAm sarva-bhUtAnAm nisheva nishA paramArtha-tattvam, agocaratvAd atad-buddhInAm | tasyAm paramArtha-tattva-lakShaNAyAm aj~nAna-nidrAyAH prabuddho jAgarti samyamI samyamavAn, jitendriyo yogIty arthaH | yasyAm grAhya-grAhaka-bheda-lakShaNAyAm avidyA-nishAyAm prasuptAny eva bhUtAni jAgrati iti ucyante, yasyAm nishAyAm prasuptA iva svapna-dR^ishaH, sA nishA avidyA-rUpatvAt paramArtha-tattvam pashyato muneH |

ataH karmANi avidyAvasthAyAm eva codyante, na vidyAvasthAyAm | vidyAyAm hi satyAm udite savitari shArvaram iva tamaH praNAsham upagacchati avidyA | prAk vidyotpatteH avidyA pramANa-buddhyA gR^ihyamANA kriyA-kAraka-phala-bheda-rUpA satI sarva-karma-hetutvam pratipadyate | na apramANa-buddhyA gR^ihyamANAyAH karma-hetutvopapattiH, pramANa-bhUtena vedena mama coditam kartavyam karma iti hi karmaNi kartA pravartate, na avidyA-mAtram idam sarvam bheda-jAtam iti j~nAnam tasya Atmaj~nasya sarva-karma-samnyAse eva adhikAro na pravR^ittau | tathA ca darshayiShyati --- tad-buddhayas tad-AtmAnaH ity AdinA j~nAna-niShThAyAm eva tasya adhikAram |

tatrApi pravartaka-pramANAbhAve pravR^itty-anupapattiH iti cet, na | svAtma-viShayatvAd Atma-vij~nAnasya | na hy AtmanaH svAtmani pravartaka-pramANApekShatA, AtmatvAd eva | tad-antatvAc ca sarva-pramANAnAm pramANatvasya | na hy Atma-svarUpAdhigame sati punaH pramANa-prameya-vyavahAraH sambhavati | pramAtR^itvam hy AtmanaH nivartayati antyam pramANam | nivartayad eva cApramANIbhavati, svapna-kAla-pramANam iva prabodhe | loke ca vastv-adhigame pravR^itti-hetutvAdarshanAt pramANasya | tasmAn nAtma-vidaH karmaNy adhikAra iti siddham ||BhGS_2.69||

==============================

viduShas tyaktaiShaNasya sthita-praj~nasya yater eva mokSha-prAptiH, na tu asamnyAsinaH kAma-kAminaH ity etam artham dR^iShTAntena pratipAdayiShyan Aha -

ApUryamANam acala-pratiShTham
samudram ApaH pravishanti yadvat |
tadvat kAmA yam pravishanti sarve
sa shAntim Apnoti na kAma-kAmI ||BhG_2.70||

ApUryamANam adbhir acala-pratiShTham acalatayA pratiShThA avasthitiH yasya tam acala-pratiShTham samudram ApaH sarvato gatAH pravishanti svAtmastham avikriyam eva santam yadvat, tadvat kAmAH viShaya-samnidhAv api sarvataH icchA-visheShAH yam puruSham --- samudram iva ApaH -- avikurvantaH pravishanti sarve Atmany eva pralIyante na svAtma-vasham kurvanti, sa shAntir mokSham Apnoti, netaraH kAma-kAmI, kAmyanta iti kAmAH viShayAH tAn kAmayitum shIlam yasya saH kAma-kAmI, naiva prApnotIty arthaH ||BhGS_2.70|| 

==============================

yasmAd evam tasmAt - 

vihAya kAmAn yaH sarvAn pumAmsh carati niHspR^ihaH |
nirmamo nirahamkAraH sa shAntim adhigacchati ||BhG_2.71||

vihAya parityajya kAmAn yaH samnyAsI pumAn sarvAn asheShataH kArtsnyena carati, jIvana-mAtra-ceShTAsheShaH paryaTatIty arthaH | niHspR^ihaH sharIra-jIvana-mAtre 'pi nirgatA spR^ihA yasya saH niHspR^ihaH san nirmamaH sharIra-jIvana-mAtrAkShipta-parigrahe 'pi mamedam ity abhinivesha-varjitaH, nirahamkAraH vidyAvattvAdi-nimittAtma-sambhAvanA-rahitaH ity etat | sa evambhUtaH sthita-praj~naH brahmavit shAntim sarva-samsAra-duHkhoparama-lakShaNAm nirvANAkhyAm adhigacchati prApnoti brahma-bhUto bhavati ity arthaH ||BhGS_2.71||

==============================

saiShA j~nAna-niShThA stUyate -

eShA brAhmI sthitiH pArtha nainAm prApya vimuhyati |
sthitvAsyAm anta-kAle 'pi brahma-nirvANam R^icchati ||BhG_2.72||

eShA yathoktA brAhmI brahmaNi bhavA iyam sthitiH sarvam karma samnyasya brahma-rUpeNaiva avasthAnam ity etat | he pArtha, nainAm sthitim prApya labdhvA na vimuhyati na moham prApnoti | sthitvAsyAm sthitau brAhmyAm yathoktAyAm anta-kAle 'pi antye vayasy api brahma-nirvANam brahma-nirvR^itim mokSham R^icchati gacchati | kim u vaktavyam brahmacaryAd eva samnyasya yAvaj jIvam yo brahmaNy eva avatiShThate sa brahma-nirvANam R^icchati iti ||BhGS_2.72|| 

iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrI-govinda-bhagavat-pUjya-pAda-shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^itau shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye dvitIyo 'dhyAyaH || 


__________________________________________________________

BhG 3

tR^itIyo 'dhyAyaH shaN^kara-bhAShyam 

shAstrasya pravR^itti-nivR^itti-viShaya-bhUte dve buddhI bhagavatA nirdiShTe, sAN^khye buddhir yoge buddhir iti ca | tatra prajahAti yadA kAmAn ity Arabhya A adhyAya-parisamApteH sAN^khya-buddhy-AshritAnAm samnyAsam kartavyam uktvA teShAm tan-niShThatayaiva ca kR^itArthatA uktA eShA brAhmI sthitiH iti | arjunAya ca karmaNy evAdhikAras te, mA saN^go 'stv akarmaNi iti karma eva kartavyam uktavAn yoga-buddhim Ashritya, na tata eva shreyaH-prAptim uktavAn | tad etad AlakShya paryAkulIbhUta-buddhir arjuna uvAca - katham bhaktAya shreyo 'rthine yat sAkShAt shreyaH-sAdhanam sAN^khya-buddhi-niShThAm shrAvayitvA mAm karmaNi dR^iShTAnekAnartha-yukte pAramparyeNApi anaikAntika-shreyaH-prApti-phale niyu¤jyAd iti yuktaH paryAkulIbhAvo 'rjunasya | tad-anurUpa-prashnaH jyAyasI cet ity AdiH | prashnApAkaraNa-vAkyam ca bhagavatA uktam yathokta-vibhAga-viShaye shAstre | 

kecit tu arjunasya prashnArtham anyathA kalpayitvA tat-pratikUlam bhagavataH prativacanam varNayanti | yathA ca AtmanA sambandha-granthe gItArtho nirUpitas tat-pratikUlam ceha punaH prashna-prativacanayor artham nirUpayanti | katham ? tatra sambandha-granthe tAvat sarveShAm AshramiNAm j~nAna-karmaNoH samuccayo gItA-shAstre nirUpito 'rtha ity uktam | punaH visheShitam ca yAvaj-jIva-shruti-coditAni karmANi parityajya kevalAd eva j~nAnAn mokShaH prApyata ity etad ekAntenaiva pratiShiddham iti | 

iha tv Ashrama-vikalpam darshayatA yAvaj-jIva-shruti-coditAnAm eva karmaNAm parityAga uktaH | tat katham IdR^isham viruddham artham arjunAya brUyAd bhagavAn, shrotA vA katham viruddham artham avadhArayet | tatraitat syAd gR^ihasthAnAm eva shrauta-karma-parityAgena kevalAd eva j~nAnAn mokShaH pratiShidhyate na tv AshramAntarANAm iti | 

etad api pUrvottar-viruddham eva | katham, sarvAshramiNAm j~nAna-karmaNoH samuccayo gItA-shAstre nishcito 'rtha iti pratij~nAya iha katham tad-viruddham kevalAd eva j~nAnAn mokSham brUyAd AshramAntarANAm |

atha matam shrauta-karmApekShayaitad-vacanam kevalAd eva j~nAnAt shrauta-karma-rahitAd gR^ihasthAnAm mokShaH pratiShidhyate iti | tatra gR^ihasthAnAm vidyamAnam api smArtam karmAvidyamAnavad upekShya j~nAnAd eva kevalAn na mokSha ity ucyata iti | etad api viruddham | katham ? gR^ihasthasyaiva smArta-karmaNA samuccitAd j~nAnAn mokShaH pratiShidhyate na tu AshramAntarANAm iti katham vivekibhiH shakyam avadhArayitum |

kim ca, yadi mokSha-sAdhanatvena smArtAni karmANi Urdhva-retasAm samuccIyante tathA gR^ihasthasyApi iShyatAm smArtair eva samuccayo na shrautaiH | 

atha shrautaiH smArtaish ca gR^ihasthasyaiva samuccayo mokShAya Urdhva-retasAm tu smArta-karma-mAtra-samuccitAj j~nAnAn mokSha iti | tatraivam sati gR^ihasthasyAyAsa-bAhulyam shrautam smArtam ca bahu-duHkha-rUpam karma shirasi aropitam syAt | 

atha gR^ihasthasyaivAyAsa-bAhulya-kAraNAn mokShaH syAn nAshramAntarANAm shrauta-nitya-karma-rahitatvAd iti | tad apy asat | sarvopaniShatsu itihAsa-purANa-yoga-shAstre ca j~nAnAN^gatvena mumukShoH sarva-karma-samnyAsa-vidhAnAd Ashrama-vikalpa-samuccaya-vidhAnAc ca shruti-smR^ityoH | 

siddhas tarhi sarvAshramiNAm j~nAna-karmaNoH samuccayaH ? na, mumukShoH sarva-karma-samnyAsa-vidhAnAt | vyutthAyAtha bhikShAcaryam caranti [BAU 3.5.1], tasmAt samnyAsam eShAm tapasAm atiriktam AhuH [NAU 2.79], nyAsa evAtyarecayet [NAU 2.78], iti | na karmaNA na prajayA dhanena tyAgenaike 'mR^itatvam AnashuH [NAU 2.12] iti ca | brahmacaryAd eva pravrajet [JAvAU 4] ity AdyAH shrutayaH |

tyaja dharmam adharmam ca ubhe satyAnR^ite tyaja |
ubhe satyAnR^ite tyaktvA yena tyajasi tat tyaja ||
samsAram eva niHsAram dR^iShTvA sAra-didR^ikShayA |
pravrajanty akR^itodvAhAH param vairAgyam AshritAH || iti bR^ihaspatir api kacam prati | 

   karmaNA badhyate jantur vidyayA ca vimucyate |
tasmAt karma na kurvanti yatayaH pAra-darshinaH || [Mbh 12.241.7] iti shukAnushAsanam |

ihApi sarva-karmANi manasA samnyasya ity Adi | mokShasya cAkAryatvAn mumukShoH karmAnarthakyam | nityAni pratyavAya-parihArArtham anuShTheyAni iti cet, na | asamnyAsi-viShayatvAt pratyavAya-prApteH | na hi agnikAryAdy-akaraNAt samnyAsinaH pratyavAyaH kalpayitum shakyo yathA brahmacAriNAm asamnyAsinAm api karmiNAm | na tavan nityAnAm karmaNAm abhAvAd eva bhAva-rUpasya pratyavAyasya utpattiH kalpayitum shakyA katham asataH sajjAyate [ChAU 6.2.2] iti asataH sajjanmAsambhava-shruteH | 

yadi vihitAkaraNAd asambhAvyam api pratyavAyam brUyAd vedas tadA anartha-karo vedaH apramANam ity uktam syAt | vihitasya karaNAkaraNayoH duHkha-mAtra-phalatvAt | tathA ca kArakam shAstram na j~nApakam iti anupapannArtham kalpitam syAt | na caitad iShTam | tasmAn na samnyAsinAm karmANi ato j~nAna-karmaNoH samuccayAnupapattiH | jyAyasI cet karmaNas te matA buddhir iti | arjunasya prashnAnupapattesh ca |

yadi hi bhagavatA dvitIye adhyAye j~nAnam karma ca samuccayena tvayAnuShTheyam ity uktam syAt tato 'rjunasya prashno 'nupapanno jyAyasI cet karmaNas te matA buddhir janArdana iti | arjunAya ced buddhi-karmaNI tvayAnuShTheye iti ukte yA karmaNo jyAyasI buddhiH sA apy uktA eveti tat kim karmaNi ghore mAm niyojayasi keshava iti prashno na kathamcana upapadyate |

na cArjunasyaiva jyAyasI buddhir nAnuShTheyeti bhagavatoktam pUrvam iti kalpayitum yuktam, yena jyAyasI ced iti prashnaH syAt | yadi punar ekasya puruShasya j~nAna-karmaNor virodhAd yugapad anuShThAnam na sambhavatIti bhinna-puruShAnuShTheyatvam bhagavatA pUrvam uktam syAt tato 'yam prashna upapannaH jyAyasI ced ity AdiH |

avivekataH prashna-kalpanAyAm api bhinna-puruShAnuShTheyatvena bhagavataH prativacanam nopapadyate | na cAj~nAna-nimittam bhagavat-prativacanam kalpyam | asmAc ca bhinna-puruShAnuShTheyatvena j~nAna-karma-niShThayor bhagavataH prativacana-darshanAt, j~nAna-karmaNoH samuccayAnupapattiH | tasmAt kevalAd eva j~nAnAn mokSha ity eSho 'rtho nishcito gItAsu sarvopaniShatsu ca | j~nAna-karmaNor ekam vada nishcitya iti ca eka-viShayaiva prArthanAnupapannobhayoH samuccaya-sambhave | 

kuru karmaiva tasmAt tvam iti ca j~nAna-niShThA-sambhavam arjunasyAvadhAraNena darshayiShyati | 

arjuna uvAca
jyAyasI cet karmaNas te matA buddhir janArdana |
tat kim karmaNi ghore mAm niyojayasi keshava ||BhG_3.1||

jyAyasI shreyasI cet yadi karmaNaH sakAshAt te tava matA abhipretA buddhir j~nAnam | he janArdana ! yadi buddhi-karmaNI samuccite iShTe tadaikam shreyaH-sAdhanam iti karmaNo jyAyasI buddhir iti karmaNo 'tirikta-karaNam buddher anupapannam arjunena kR^itam syAt | na hi tad eva tasmAt phalato 'tiriktam syAt | tathA ca, karmaNaH shreyaskarI bhagavatoktA buddhiH | ashreyaskaram ca karma kurv iti mAm pratipAdayati, tat kim nu kAraNam iti bhagavata upAlambham iva kurvan tat kim kasmAt karmaNi ghore krUre himsA-lakShaNe mAm niyojayasi keshava iti ca yad Aha, tac ca nopapadyate | atha smArtenaiva karmaNA samuccayaH sarveShAm bhagavatokto 'rjunena cAvadhArita cet, tat kim karmaNi ghore mAm niyojayasi ity Adi katham yuktam vacanam ||BhGS_3.1||

==============================

kim ca - 

vyAmishreNeva vAkyena buddhim mohayasIva me |
tad ekam vada nishcitya yena shreyo 'ham ApnuyAm ||BhG_3.2||

vyAmishreNeva, yadyapi vivaktAbhidhAyI bhagavAn, tathApi mama manda-buddher vyAmishram iva bhagavad-vAkyam pratibhAti | tena mama buddhim mohayasIva, mama buddhi-vyAmohApanayAya hi pravR^ittas tvam tu katham mohayasi ? ataH bravImi | buddhim mohayasi iva me mama iti | tvam tu bhinna-kartR^ikayoH j~nAna-karmaNor eka-puruShAnuShThAnAsambhavam yadi manyase, tatraivam sati tat tayor ekam buddhim karma vA idam evArjunasya yogyam buddhi-shakty-avasthAnurUpam iti nishcitya vada brUhi, yena j~nAnena karmaNA vA anyatareNa shreyo 'ham ApnuyAm prApnuyAm | 

yadi hi karma-niShThAyAm guNa-bhUtam api j~nAnam bhagavatoktam syAt | tat katham tayor ekam vada ity eka-viShayaivArjunasya shushrUShA syAt | na hi bhagavatA pUrvam uktam anyatarad eva j~nAna-karmaNoH vakShyAmi, naiva dvayam iti, yena ubhaya-prApty-asambhavam Atmano manyamAna ekam eva prArthayet ||BhGS_3.2|| 

==============================

prashnAnurUpam eva prativacanam -

shrI-bhagavAn uvAca
loke 'smin dvividhA niShThA purA proktA mayAnagha |
j~nAna-yogena sAmkhyAnAm karma-yogena yoginAm ||BhG_3.3||
