loke 'smin shAstrArthAnuShThAnAdhikR^itAnAm traivarNikAnAm dvi-vidhA dvi-prakArA niShThA sthitiH anuShTheya-tAtparyam purA pUrvam sargAdau prajAH sR^iShTvA tAsAm abhyudaya-niHshreyasa-prApti-sAdhanam vedArtha-sampradAyam AviShkurvatA proktA mayA sarvaj~nena IshvareNa he anaghApApa | tatra kA sA dvividhA niShThA ity Aha - tatra j~nAna-yogena j~nAnam eva yogas tena sAmkhyAnAm AtmAnAtma-viShaya-viveka-vij~nAnavatAm brahmacaryAshramAd eva kR^ita-samnyAsAnAm vedAnta-vij~nAna-sunishcitArthAnAm paramahamsa-parivrAjakAnAm brahmaNy evAvasthitAnAm niShThA proktA | karma-yogena karma eva yogaH karma-yogas tena karma-yogena yoginAm karmiNAm niShThA proktA ity arthaH | 

yadi caikena puruSheNa ekasmai puruShArthAya j~nAnam karma ca samuccityAnuShTheyam bhagavatA iShTam uktam vakShyamANam vA gItAsu vedeShu coktam, katham ihArjunAya upasannAya priyAya vishiShTAbhinna-puruSha-kartR^ike eva j~nAna-karma-niShThe brUyAt ? yadi punar arjuno j~nAnam karma ca dvayam shrutvA svayam evAnuShThAsyati anyeShAm tu bhinna-puruShAnuShTheyatAm vakShyAmi iti matam bhagavataH kalpyeta, tadA rAga-dveShavAn apramANa-bhUto bhagavAn kalpitaH syAt | tac cAyuktam | tasmAt kayApi yuktyA na samuccayo j~nAna-karmaNoH || 

yad arjunenoktam karmaNo jyAyastvam buddhes tac ca sthitam anirAkaraNAt | tasyAsh ca j~nAna-niShThAyAH samnyAsinAm evAnuShTheyatvam , bhinna-puruShAnuShTheyatva-vacanAt | bhagavata evam evAnumatam iti gamyate ||BhGS_3.3||

==============================

mAm ca bandha-kAraNe karmaNy eva niyojayasi iti viShaNNa-manasam arjunam karma nArabhe ity evam manvAnam AlakShya Aha bhagavAn - na karmaNAman ArambhAd iti | athavA - j~nAna-karma-niShThayoH paraspara-virodhAd ekena puruSheNa yugapad anuShThAtum ashakyatve sati itaretarAnapekShayor eva puruShArtha-hetutve prApte karma-niShThAyA j~nAna-niShThA-prApti-hetutvena puruShArtha-hetutvam, na svAtantryeNa | j~nAna-niShThA tu karma-niShThopAya-labdhAtmikA satI svAtantryeNa puruShArtha-hetuH anyAnapekShA, ity etam artham pradarshayiShyan Aha bhagavAn - 

na karmaNAm anArambhAn naiShkarmyam puruSho 'shnute |
na ca samnyasanAd eva siddhim samadhigacchati ||BhG_3.4 ||

na karmaNA kriyANAm yaj~nAdInAm iha janmani janmAntare vA anuShThitAnAm upAtta-durita-kShaya-hetutvena sattva-shuddhi-kAraNAnAm tat-kAraNatvena ca j~nAnotpatti-dvAreNa j~nAna-niShThA-hetUnAm, 

j~nAnam utpadyate pumsAm kShayAt pApasya karmaNaH | 
yathAdarshatala-prakhye pashyaty AtmAnam Atmani || [Mbh 12 208.8] ity Adi smaraNAt | 

anArambhAd ananuShThAnAt naiShkarmyam niShkarma-bhAvam karma-shUnyatAm j~nAna-yogena niShThAm niShkriyAtma-svarUpeNaivAvasthAnam iti yAvat | puruSho nAshnute na prApnotIty arthaH |
karmaNAm anArambhAn naiShkarmyam nAshnuta iti vacanAt tad-viparyayAt teShAm ArambhAn naiShkarmyam ashnuta iti gamyate | kasmAt punaH kAraNAt karmaNAm anArambhAn naiShkarmyam nAshnute iti ? ucyate, karmArambhasyaiva naiShkarmyopAyatvAt | na hy upAyam antareNa upeya-prAptir asti | karma-yogopAyatvam ca naiShkarmya-lakShaNasya j~nAna-yogasya, shrutau iha ca pratipAdanAt | shrutau tAvat prakR^itasyAtma-lokasya vedyasya vedanopAyatvena tam etam vedAnuvacanena brAhmaNA vividiShanti yaj~nena [BAU 4.4.22] ity AdinA karma-yogasya j~nAna-yogopAyatvam pratipAditam | ihApi ca - samnyAsas tu mahAbAho duHkham Aptum ayogataH [kraItA 5.6], yoginaH karma kurvanti saN^gam tyaktvAtmashuddhaye [kraItA 5.11], yaj~no dAnam tapash caiva pAvanAni manIShiNAm [kraItA 18.5] ity Adi pratipAdayiShyati | 

nanu cAbhayam sarva-bhUtebhyo dattvA naiShkarmyam Acaret ity Adau kartavya-karma-samnyAsAd api naiShkarmya-prAptim darshayati | loke ca karmaNAm anArambhAn naiShkarmyam iti prasiddhataram | atash ca naiShkarmyArthinaH kim karmArambheNa ? iti prAptam | ata Aha- na ca samnyasanAd eveti | nApi samnyasanAd eva kevalAt karma-parityAga-mAtrAd eva j~nAna-rahitAt siddhim naiShkarmya-lakShaNAm j~nAna-yogena niShThAm samadhigacchati na prApnoti ||BhGS_3.4|| 

==============================

kasmAt punaH kAraNAt karma-samnyAsa-mAtrAd eva kevalAt j~nAna-rahitAt siddhim naiShkarmya-lakShaNAm puruSho nAdhigacchati iti hetv-AkAN^kShAyAm Aha - 

na hi kashcit kShaNam api jAtu tiShThaty akarmakR^it |
kAryate hy avashaH karma sarvaH prakR^itijair guNaiH ||BhG_3.5||

na hi yasmAt kShaNam api kAlam jAtu kadAcit kashcit tiShThaty akarma-kR^it san | kasmAt ? kAryate pravartyate hi yasmAd avasha evAsvatantra eva karma sarvaH prANI prakR^iti-jaiH prakR^itito jAtaiH sattva-rajas-tamobhiH guNaiH | aj~na iti vAkya-sheShaH, yato vakShyati guNair yo na vicAlyate iti | sAmkhyAnAm pR^ithak-karaNAt aj~nAnAm eva hi karma-yogaH, na j~nAninAm | j~nAninAm tu guNair acAlyamAnAnAm svatash calanAbhAvAt karma-yogo nopapadyate | tathA ca vyAkhyAtam vedAvinAshinam [kraItA 2.21] ity atra ||BhGS_3.5|| 

==============================

yat tv anAtmaj~naH coditam karma nArabhate iti tad asad evety Aha - 

karmendriyANi samyamya ya Aste manasA smaran |
indriyArthAn vimUDhAtmA mithyAcAraH sa ucyate ||BhG_3.6||

karmendriyANi hastAdIni samyamya samhR^itya ya Aste tiShThati manasA smaran cintayan indriyArthAn viShayAn vimUDhAtmA vimUDhAntaH-araNo mithyAcAro mR^iShAcAraH pApAcAraH sa ucyate ||BhGS_3.6|| 

==============================

yas tv indriyANi manasA niyamyArabhate 'rjuna |
karmendriyaiH karma-yogam asaktaH sa vishiShyate ||BhG_3.7||

yas tu punaH karmaNy adhikR^ito 'j~naH buddhIndriyANi manasA niyamya Arabhate arjuna karmendriyaiH vAk-pANy-AdibhiH | kim Arabhate ity Aha-karma-yogam asaktaH san phalAbhisandhi-varjitaH sa vishiShyate itarasmAt mithyAcArAt ||BhGS_3.7|| 

==============================

yataH evam ataH-

niyatam kuru karma tvam karma jyAyo hy akarmaNaH |
sharIrayAtrApi ca te na prasidhyed akarmaNaH ||BhG_3.8||

niyatam nityam shAstropadiShTam | yo yasmin karmaNy adhikR^itaH phalAya cAshrutam tan niyatam karma, tat kuru tvam he arjuna ! yataH karma jyAyo 'dhikataram phalataH | hi yasmAd akarmaNo 'karaNAt anArambhAt | katham ? sharIra-yAtrA sharIra-sthitir api ca te tava na prasidhyet prasiddhim na gacchet akarmaNo 'karaNAt | ato dR^iShTaH karmAkarmaNor visheSho loke ||BhGS_3.8||

==============================

yac ca manyase bandhArthatvAt karma na kartavyam iti tad apy asat | katham ?

yaj~nArthAt karmaNo 'nyatra loko 'yam karma-bandhanaH |
tad artham karma kaunteya muktasaN^gaH samAcara ||BhG_3.9||

yaj~no vai viShNuH [TaittS 1.7.4] iti shruter yaj~na IshvaraH | tad-artham yat kriyate tat yaj~nArtham karma | tasmAt karmaNo 'nyatrAnyena karmaNA loko 'yam adhikR^itaH karma-kR^it karma-bandhanaH [Taitt.BhA. 3.1.6] karma bandhanam yasya so 'yam karma-bandhano lokaH, na tu yaj~nArthAt | atas tad-artham yaj~nArtham karma kaunteya, mukta-saN^gaH karma-phala-saN^ga-varjitaH san samAcAra nirvartaya ||BhGS_3.9||

==============================

itash cAdhikR^itena karma kartavyam - 

saha-yaj~nAH prajAH sR^iShTvA purovAca prajApatiH |
anena prasaviShyadhvam eSha vo 'stv iShTa-kAma-dhuk ||BhG_3.10||

saha-yaj~nAH yaj~na-sahitAH prajAs trayo varNAs tAH sR^iShTvotpAdya purA pUrvam sargAdAv uvAca uktavAn prajApatiH prajAnAm srAShTA | anena yaj~nena prasaviShyadhvam prasavo vR^iddhir utpattis tAm kurudhvam | eSha yaj~no vo yuShmAkam astu bhavatu iShTa-kAma-dhuk | iShTAn abhipretAn kAmAn phala-visheShAn dogdhIti iShTa-kAma-dhuk ||BhGS_3.10||

==============================

katham ?

devAn bhAvayatAnena te devA bhAvayantu vaH |
parasparam bhAvayantaH shreyaH param avApsyatha ||BhG_3.11||

devAn indrAdIn bhAvayata vardhayatAnena yaj~nena | te devA bhAvayantu ApyAyayantu vR^iShTy-AdinA vo yuShmAn | evam parasparam anyonyam bhAvayantaH shreyaH param mokSha-lakShaNam vij~nAna-prApti-krameNAvApsyatha | svargam vA param shreyo 'vApsyatha ||BhGS_3.11|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

iShTAn bhogAn hi vo devA dAsyante yaj~na-bhAvitAH |
tair dattAn apradAyaibhyo yo bhuN^kte stena eva saH ||BhG_3.12||

iShTAn abhipretAn bhogAn hi vo yuShmabhyam devA dAsyante vitariShyanti | strI-pashu-putrAdIn yaj~na-bhAvitA yaj~nair vardhitAs toShitA ity arthaH | tair devair dattAn bhogAn apradAyAdattvA, AnR^iNyam akR^itvety arthaH | ebhyo devebhyaH | yo bhuN^kte sva-dehendriyANy eva tarpayati stena eva taskara eva sa devAdi-svApahArI ||BhGS_3.12||

==============================

ye punaH- 

yaj~na-shiShTAshinaH santo mucyante sarva-kilbiShaiH |
bhu¤jate te tv agham pApA ye pacanty Atma-kAraNAt ||BhG_3.13||

deva-yaj~nAdIn nirvartya tac-chiShTam ashanam amR^itAkhyam ashitum shIlam yeShAm te yaj~na-shiShTAshinaH santo mucyante sarva-kilbiShaiH sarva-pApaish cully-Adi-paJNca-sUnAkR^itaiH pramAda-kR^ita-himsAdi-janitaish cAnyaiH | ye tv Atmambharayo bhu¤jate te tv agham pApam svayam api pApA ye pacanti pAkam nirvartayanti Atma-kAraNAt Atma-hetoH ||BhGS_3.13||

==============================

itash cAdhikR^itena karma kartavyam | jagac-cakra-pravR^itti-hetur hi karma | katham ? ity ucyate - 

annAd bhavanti bhUtAni parjanyAd anna-sambhavaH |
yaj~nAd bhavati parjanyo yaj~naH karma-samudbhavaH ||BhG_3.14||

annAd bhuktAl lohita-retaH-pariNatAt pratyakSham bhavanti jAyante bhUtAni | parjanyAd vR^iShTer annasya sambhavo 'nna-sambhavaH | yaj~nAd bhavati parjanyaH | 

agnau prAstAhutiH samyag Adityam upatiShThate |
AdityAj jAyate vR^iShTir vR^iShTer annam tataH prajAH || [Manu 3.76] iti smR^iteH | 

yaj~no 'pUrvam | sa ca yaj~naH karma-samudbhavaH | R^itvig-yajamAnayosh ca vyApAraH karma, tad-samudbhavo yasya yaj~nasyApUrvasya sa yaj~naH karma-samudbhavaH ||BhGS_3.14||

==============================

tac caivamvidham karma kuto jAtam ity Aha - 

karma brahmodbhavam viddhi brahmAkShara-samudbhavam |
tasmAt sarva-gatam brahma nityam yaj~ne pratiShThitam ||BhG_3.15||

karma brahmodbhavam | brahma vedaH | sa udbhavaH kAraNam prakAshako yasya tat karma brahmodbhavam viddhi vijAnIhi | brahma punaH vedAkhyam akShara-samudbhavam akSharam brahma paramAtmA samudbhavo yasya tat akShara-samudbhavam | brahma veda ity arthaH | yasmAt sAkShAt paramAtmAkhyAd akSharAt puruSha-niHshvAsavat samudbhUtam brahma tasmAt sarvArtha-prakAshakatvAt sarva-gatam | sarva-gatam api sat nityam sadA yaj~na-vidhi-pradhAnatvAt yaj~ne pratiShThitam ||BhGS_3.15|| 

==============================

evam pravartitam cakram nAnuvartayatIha yaH |
aghAyur indriyArAmo mogham pArtha sa jIvati ||BhG_3.16||

evam ittham IshvareNa veda-yaj~na-pUrvakam jagac-cakram pravartitam nAnuvartayatIha loke yaH karmaNy adhikR^itaH sann aghAyur agham pApam Ayur jIvanam yasya so 'ghAyuH pApa-jIvana iti yAvat | indriyArAmaH indriyair ArAmaH AramaNam AkrIDA viShayeShu yasya sa indriyArAmo mogham vR^ithA he pArtha, sa jIvati | tasmAd aj~nenAdhikR^itena kartavyam eva karmeti prakaraNArthaH | prAg Atma-j~nAna-niShThA-yogyatA-prAptes tAdarthyena karma-yogAnuShThAnam adhikR^itenAnAtmaj~nena kartavyam evety etan na karmaNAm anArambhAd [GItA 3.4] ity ata Arabhya sharIra-yAtrApi ca te na prasidhyed akarmaNa [GItA 3.8] ity evam antena pratipAdya, yaj~nArthAt karmaNo 'nyatra [GItA 3.9] ity AdinA mogham pArtha sa jIvati ity evam antenApi granthena prAsaN^gikam adhikR^itasyAnAtmavidaH karmAnuShThAne bahu kAraNam uktam | tad-akaraNe ca doSha-samkIrtanam kR^itam ||BhGS_3.16||

==============================

evam sthite kim evam pravartitam caktram sarveNAnuvartanIyam ? Aho svit pUrvokta-karma-yogAnuShThAnopAya-prApyAm anAtma-vidA j~nAna-yogenaiva niShThAm Atma-vidbhiH sAmkhyair anuShTheyAm aprAptenaiva ? ity evam artham arjunasya prashnam AshaN^kaya svayam eva vA shAstrArthasya viveka-pratipatty-artham etam vai tam AtmAnam viditvA nivR^itta-mithyA-j~nAnAH santo brAhmaNA mithyA-j~nAnavadbhyo 'vashyam kartavyebhyaH putraiShaNAdibhyo vyutthAyAtha bhikShA-caryam sharIra-sthiti-mAtra-prayuktam caranti | na teShAm Atma-j~nAna-niShThA-vyatirekeNAnyat kAryam asti [BAU 3.5.1] ity evam shruty-artham iha gItA-shAstre pratipipAdayiShitam AviShkurvann Aha bhagavAn - 

yas tv Atma-ratir eva syAd Atma-tR^iptash ca mAnavaH |
Atmany eva ca samtuShTas tasya kAryam na vidyate ||BhG_3.17||

yas tu sAmkhya Atma-j~nAna-niShTha Atma-ratiH Atmany eva ratir na viShayeShu yasya sa Atma-ratir eva syAd bhaved Atma-tR^iptash cAtmanaiva tR^ipto nAnna-rasAdinA sa mAnavo manuShyaH samnyAsI Atmany eva ca santuShTaH | santoSho hi bAhyArtha-lAbhe sarvasya bhavati, tam anapekShya Atmany eva ca santuShTaH sarvato vIta-tR^iShNa ity etat | ya IdR^ishaH Atma-vit tasya kAryam karaNIyam na vidyate nAstIty arthaH ||BhGS_3.17||

==============================

kim ca - 

naiva tasya kR^itenArtho nAkR^iteneha kashcana |
na cAsya sarva-bhUteShu kashcid artha-vyapAshrayaH ||BhG_3.18||

naiva tasya paramAtma-rateH kR^itena karmaNArthaH prayojanam asti | astu tarhy akR^itenAkaraNena pratyavAyAkhyo 'narthaH | nAkR^iteneha loke kashcana kashcid api pratyavAya-prApti-rUpaH Atma-hAni-lakShaNo vA naivAsti | na cAsya sarva-bhUteShu brahmAdi-sthAvarAnteShu bhUteShu kashcid artha-vyapAshrayaH prayojana-nimitta-kriyA-sAdhyo vyapAshrayaH | vyapAshrayaNam Alambanam kamcit bhUta-visheSham Ashritya na sAdhyaH kashcid artho 'sti, yena tad-arthA kriyA anuShTheyA syAt | na tvam etasmin sarvataH samplutodaka-sthAnIye samyag-darshane vartase ||BhGS_3.18|| 

==============================

yataH evam - 

tasmAd asaktaH satatam kAryam karma samAcara |
asakto hy Acaran karma param Apnoti pUruShaH ||BhG_3.19||

tasmAt asaktaH saN^gavarjitaH satatam sarvadA kAryam kartavyam nityam karma samAcara nirvartaya | asakto hi yasmAt samAcaran IshvarArtham karma kurvan param mokSham Apnoti pUruShaH sattvashuddhidvAreNa ity arthaH ||BhGS_3.19|| 

==============================

yasmAc ca - 

karmaNaiva hi samsiddhim AsthitA janakAdayaH |
loka-samgraham evApi sampashyan kartum arhasi ||BhG_3.20||

karmaNaiva hi yasmAt pUrve kShatriyAH vidvAmsaH samsiddhim mokSham gantum AsthitAH pravR^ittAH | ke ? janakAdayaH janakA vapatiprabhR^itayaH | yadi te prAptasamyagdarshanAH, tataH lokasamgrahArtham prArabdhakarmatvAt karmaNA sahaivAsamnyasyaiva karma samsiddhimAsthitA ity arthaH | athAprAptasamyagadarshanAH janakAdayaH, tadA karmaNA sattvashuddhisAdhanabhUtena ktrameNa samsiddhimAsthitA iti vyAkhyeyaH lokaH | atha manyase pUrverapi janakAdibhiH ajAnadbhireva kartavyam karma kR^itam | tAvatA nAvashyamanyena kartavyam samyagdarshanavatA kR^itAtheneti | tathApi prArabdhakarmAyattaH tvam lokasamgraham evApi lokasya unmArgapravR^ittinivAraNam lokasamgrahaH, tamevApi prayojanam sampashyan kartum arhasi ||BhGS_3.20||
==============================

loka-samgrahaH kim artham kartavya ity ucyate - 

yad yad Acarati shreShThas tat tad evetaro janaH |
sa yat pramANam kurute lokas tad anuvartate ||BhG_3.21||

yadyat karma Acarati karoti shreShThaH pradhAnaH tattadeva karma Acarati itaro 'nyaH janaH tadanugataH | kim ca saH shreShThaH yat pramANam kurute laukikam vaidikam vA lokaH tat anuvartate tadeva pramANIkaroti ity arthaH ||BhGS_3.21||

==============================

yady atra te loka-samgraha-kartavyatAyAm vipratipattis tarhi mAm kim na pashyasi ? 

na me pArthAsti kartavyam triShu lokeShu kimcana |
nAnavAptam avAptavyam vartaiva ca karmaNi ||BhG_3.22||

na me mama pArtha nAsti na vidyate kartavyam triShv api lokeShu kimcana kimcid api | kasmAt ? nAnavAptam aprAptam avAptavyam prApaNIyam | tathApi varta eva ca karmaNy aham ||BhGS_3.22|| 

==============================

yadi hy aham na varteyam jAtu karmaNy atandritaH |
mama vartmAnuvartante manuShyAH pArtha sarvashaH ||BhG_3.23||

yadi hi punar aham na varteya jAtu kadAcit karmaNy atandrito 'nalasaH san mama shreShThasya sato vatrma mArgam anuvartante manuShyAH | he pArtha ! sarvashaH sarva-prakAraiH ||BhGS_3.23||

==============================

utsIdeyur ime lokA na kuryAm karma ced aham |
samkarasya ca kartA syAm upahanyAm imAH prajAH ||BhG_3.24||

utsIdeyur vinashyeyur ime sarve lokAH loka-sthiti-nimittasya karmaNo 'bhAvAt na kuryAm karma ced aham | kim ca, samkarasya ca kartA syAm | tena kAraNena upahanyAm imAH prajAH | prajAnAm anugrahAya pravR^itta upahatim upahananam kuryAm ity arthaH | mama IshvarasyAnanurUpam Apadyate ||BhGS_3.24||

==============================

yadi punar aham iva tvam kR^itArtha-buddhiH, Atmavid anyo vA, tasyApi AtmanaH kartavyAbhAve 'pi parAnugraha eva kartavya ity Aha - 

saktAH karmaNy avidvAmso yathA kurvanti bhArata |
kuryAd vidvAms tathAsaktash cikIrShur loka-samgraham ||BhG_3.25||

saktAH karmaNy asya karmaNaH phalam mama bhaviShyatIti kecid avidvAmso yathA kurvanti bhArata, kuryAd vidvAn Atmavit tathAsaktaH san | tadvat kim artham karoti ? tat sR^iNu - cikIrShuH kartum icchuH loka-samgraham ||BhGS_3.25|| 

==============================

evam loka-samgraham cikIrSher na mamAtma-vidaH kartavyam asti anyasya vA loka-samgraham muktvA | tatas tasya Atma-vidaH idam upadishyate - 

na buddhi-bhedam janayed aj~nAnAm karma-saN^ginAm |
joShayet sarva-karmANi vidvAn yuktaH samAcaran ||BhG_3.26||

buddhi-bhedo buddhi-bhedo mayA idam kartavyam bhoktavyam cAsya karmaNaH phalam iti nishcaya-rUpAyA buddher bhedanam cAlanam buddhi-bhedas tam na janayen notpAdayed aj~nAnAm avivekinAm karma-saN^ginAm karmaNy AsaktAnAm AsaN^gavatAm | kim nu kuryAt ? joShayet kArayet sarva-karmANi vidvAn svayam tad evAviduShAm karma yukto 'bhiyuktaH samAcaran ||BhGS_3.26|| 

==============================

avidvAn aj~naH katham karmasu sajjate ? ity Aha - 

prakR^iteH kriyamANAni guNaiH karmANi sarvashaH |
ahamkAra-vimUDhAtmA kartAham iti manyate ||BhG_3.27||

prakR^iteH prakR^itiH pradhAnam sattva-rajas-tamasAm guNAnAm sAmyAvasthA | tasyAH prakR^iteH guNaiH vikAraiH kArya-karaNa-rUpaiH kriyamANAni karmANi laukikAni shAstrIyANi ca sarvashaH sarva-prakArair ahamkAra-vimUDhAtmA kArya-karaNa-samghAtAtma-pratyayo 'hamkAras tena vividham nAnAvidham mUDha AtmA antaH-karaNam yasya so 'yam kArya-karaNa-dharmA kArya-karaNAbhimAnI avidyayA karmANi Atmani manyamAnaH tat-tat-karmaNAm aham karteti manyate ||BhGS_3.27|| 

==============================

yaH punar vidvAn - 

tattvavit tu mahAbAho guNa-karma-vibhAgayoH |
guNA guNeShu vartanta iti matvA na sajjate ||BhG_3.28||

tattvavit tu mahAbAho | kasya tattvavit ? guNakarmavibhAgayoH guNavibhAgasya karmavibhAgasya ca tattvavit ity arthaH | guNAH karaNAtmakAH guNeShu viShayAtmakeShu vartante na AtmA iti matvA na sajjate saktim na karoti ||BhGS_3.28|| 

==============================
 
ye punaH - 

prakR^iter guNa-sammUDhAH sajjante guNa-karmasu |
tAn akR^itsna-vido mandAn kR^itsnavin na vicAlayet ||BhG_3.29||

prakR^iteH guNaiH samyak mUDhAH sammohitAH santaH sajjante guNAnAm karmasu guNa-karmasu vayam karma kurmaH phalAya iti | tAn karma-saN^gino 'kR^itsna-vidaH karma-phala-mAtra-darshino mandAn manda-praj~nAn kR^itsna-vit Atma-vit svayam na vicAlayet buddhi-bheda-karaNam eva cAlanam tan na kuryAt ity arthaH ||BhGS_3.29|| 

==============================
 
katham punaH karmaNy adhikR^itenAj~nena mumukShuNA karma kartavyam iti, ucyate -- 

mayi sarvANi karmANi samnyasyAdhyAtma-cetasA |
nirAshIr nirmamo bhUtvA yudhyasva vigata-jvaraH ||BhG_3.30||

mayi vAsudeve parameshvare sarvaj~ne sarvAtmani sarvANi karmANi samnyasya nikShipyAdhyAtma-cetasA viveka-buddhyA, aham kartA IshvarAya bhR^ityavat karomi ity anayA buddhyA | kim ca, nirAshIs tyaktAshIH nirmamo mama-bhAvash ca nirgato yasya tava sa tvam nirmamo bhUtvA yudhyasva vigata-jvaro vigata-santApo vigata-shokaH sann ity arthaH ||BhGS_3.30|| 

==============================
 
yad etan mama matam karma kartavyam iti sa-pramANam uktam tat tathA - 

ye me matam idam nityam anutiShThanti mAnavAH |
shraddhAvanto 'nasUyanto mucyante te 'pi karmabhiH ||BhG_3.31||

ye me madIyam idam matam nityam anutiShThanti anuvartante mAnavA manuShyAH shraddhAvantaH shraddadhAnA anasUyanto 'sUyAm ca mayi parama-gurau vAsudeve 'kurvanto, mucyante te 'py evambhUtAH karmabhir dharmAdharmAkhyaiH ||BhGS_3.31|| 

==============================

ye tv etad abhyasUyanto nAnutiShThanti me matam |
sarva-j~nAna-vimUDhAms tAn viddhi naShTAn acetasaH ||BhG_3.32||

ye tu tad-viparItA etan mama matam abhyasUyanto nindanto nAnutiShThanti nAnuvartante me matam | sarveShu j~nAneShu vividham mUDhAs te | sarva-j~nAna-vimUDhAms tAn viddhi jAnIhi naShTAn nAsham gatAn acetaso 'vivekinaH ||BhGS_3.32|| 

==============================

kasmAt punaH kAraNAt tvadIyam matam nAnutiShThantaH para-dharmAn anutiShThanti ? sva-dharmam ca nAnuvartante ? tvat-pratikUlAH katham na bibhyati tvac-chAsanAtikrama-doShAt ? tatrAha - 

sadR^isham ceShTate svasyAH prakR^iter j~nAnavAn api |
prakR^itim yAnti bhUtAni nigrahaH kim kariShyati ||BhG_3.33||

sadR^isham anurUpam ceShTate ceShTAm karoti | kasyAH ? svasyAH svakIyAyAH prakR^iteH | prakR^itir nAma pUrva-kR^ita-dharmAdharmAdi-samskArA vartamAna-janmAdAv abhivyaktAH | sA prakR^itiH | tasyAH sadR^isham eva sarvo jantur j~nAnavAn api ceShTate, kim punar mUrkhaH ? tasmAt prakR^itim yAnty anugacchanti bhUtAni prANinaH | nigraho niShedha-rUpaH kim kariShyati mama vAnyasya vA ? durnigrahA prakR^itir iti vAkya-sheShaH ||BhGS_3.33||

==============================

yadi sarvo jantur AtmanaH prakR^iti-sadR^isham eva ceShTate, na ca prakR^iti-shUnyaH kashcid asti, tataH puruShakArasya viShayAnupapatteH shAstrAnarthakya-prAptAv idam ucyate - 

indriyasyendriyasyArthe rAga-dveShau vyavasthitau |
tayor na vasham Agacchet tau hy asya paripanthinau ||BhG_3.34||

indriyasyendriyasyArthe sarvendriyANAm arthe shabdAdi-viShaye iShTe rAgo 'niShTe dveSha ity evam pratIndriyArtham rAgadveShAv avashyambhAvinau tatrAyam puruShakArasya shAstrArthasya ca viShaya ucyate | shAstrArthe pravR^ittaH pUrvam eva rAga-dveShayor vasham nAgacchet | yA hi puruShasya prakR^itiH sA rAga-dveSha-puraHsaraiva sva-kArye puruSham pravartayati | tadA svadharma-parityAgaH para-dharmAnuShThAnam ca bhavati | yadA punA rAga-dveShau tat-pratipakSheNa niyamayati tadA shAstra-dR^iShTir eva puruSho bhavati, na prakR^iti-vashaH | tasmAt tayo rAga-dveShayor vasham nAgacchet | yatas tau hy asya puruShasya paripanthinau shreyo-mArgasya vighna-kartArau taskarAv iva pathIty arthaH ||BhGS_3.34|| 

==============================

tatra rAga-dveSha-prayukto manyate shAsrArtham apy anyathA para-dharmo 'pi dharmatvAd anuShTheya eva iti, tad asat - 

shreyAn sva-dharmo viguNaH para-dharmAt svanuShThitAt |
sva-dharme nidhanam shreyaH para-dharmo bhayAvahaH ||BhG_3.35||

shreyAn prashasyataraH svo dharmaH svadharmo viguNo 'pi vigata-guNo 'pi anuShThIyamAnaH para-dharmAt svanuShThitAt sAdguNyena sampAditAd api | sva-dharme sthitasya nidhanam maraNam api shreyaH para-dharme sthitasya jIvitAt | kasmAt ? para-dharmaH bhayAvahaH narakAdi-lakShaNam bhayam AvahatIti yataH ||BhGS_3.35|| 

==============================

yadyapi anartha-mUlam dhyAyato viShayAn pumsa [GItA 2.62] iti rAga-dveShau hy asya paripanthinau [GItA 3.34] iti coktam | vikShiptam anavadhAritam ca tad uktam | tat samkShiptam nishcitam ca idam eveti j~nAtum icchan arjuna uvAca j~nAte hi tasmin tad-ucchedAya yatnam kuryAm iti arjuna uvAca- 

atha kena prayukto 'yam pApam carati pUruShaH |
anicchann api vArShNeya balAd iva niyojitaH ||BhG_3.36||

atha kena hetu-bhUtena prayuktaH san rAj~neva bhR^ityo 'yam pApam karma carati Acarati pUruShaH puruShaH svayam anicchann api he vArShNeya vR^iShNi-kula-prasUta ! balAd iva niyojito rAj~nevety ukto dR^iShTAntaH ||BhGS_3.36|| 

==============================

shR^iNu tvam tam vairiNam sarvAnartha-karam yam tvam pR^icchasIti bhagavAn uvAca - 

kAma eSha krodha eSha rajo-guNa-samudbhavaH |
mahAshano mahA-pApmA viddhy enam iha vairiNam ||BhG_3.37||

aishvaryasya samagrasya dharmasya yashasaH shriyaH | 
vairAgyasyAtha mokShasya ShaNNAm bhaga itIN^ganA || [ViP 6.5.74] 

ity aishvaryAdi-ShaTkam yasmin vAsudeve nityam apratibaddhatvena sAmastyena ca vartate, 

utpattim pralayam caiva bhUtAnAm Agatim gatim | 
vetti vidyAm avidyAm ca sa vAcyo bhagavAn iti || [ViP 6.5.78] 

utpatty-Adi-viShayam ca vij~nAnam yasya sa vAsudevo vAcyo bhagavAn iti | 

kAma iti | kAma eSha sarva-loka-shatrur yan-nimittA sarvAnartha-prAptiH prANinAm | sa eSha kAmaH pratihataH kenacit krodhatvena pariNamate | ataH krodho 'py eSha eva rajo-guNa-samudbhavo rajash ca tad-guNash ca rajo-guNaH sa samudbhavo yasya sa kAmo rajo-guNa-samudbhavaH | rajo-guNasya vA samudbhavaH | kAmo hy udbhUto rajaH pravartayan puruSham pravartayati | tR^iShNayA hy ahamkArita iti duHkhinAm rajaH-kArye sevAdau pravR^ittAnAm pralApaH shrUyate | mahAshano mahad ashanam asyeti mahAshanaH | ataeva mahA-pApmA | kAmena hi prerito jantuH pApam karoti | ato viddhy enam kAmam iha samsAre vairiNam ||BhGS_3.37|| 

==============================

katham vairI ? iti dR^iShTAntaiH pratyAyayati - 

dhUmenAvriyate vahnir yathAdarsho malena ca |
yatholbenAvR^ito garbhas tathA tenedam AvR^itam ||BhG_3.38||

dhUmena sahajenAvriyate vahniH prakAshAtmako 'prakAshAtmakena, yathA vA Adarsho malena ca, yatholbena ca jarAyuNA garbha-veShTanena cAvR^ita AcchAdito garbhas tathA tenedam AvR^itam ||BhGS_3.38|| 

==============================

kim punas tad idam-shabda-vAcyam yat kAmenAvR^itam ity ucyate - 

AvR^itam j~nAnam etena j~nAnino nitya-vairiNA |
kAma-rUpeNa kaunteya duShpUreNAnalena ca ||BhG_3.39||

AvR^itam etena j~nAnam j~nAnino nitya-vairiNA, j~nAnI hi jAnAty anenAham anarthe prayuktaH pUrvam eveti | duHkhI ca bhavati nityam eva | ato 'sau j~nAnino nitya-vairI, na tu mUrkhasya | sa hi kAmam tR^iShNA-kAle mitram iva pashyan tat-kArye duHkhe prApte jAnAti tR^iShNayAham duHkhitvam ApAdita iti, na pUrvam eva | ato j~nAnina eva nitya-vairI | kim-rUpeNa ? kAma-rUpeNa kAma icchaiva rUpam asyeti kAmarUpas tena duShpUreNa duHkhena pUraNam asyeti duShpUras tenAnalena nAsyAlam paryAptir vidyata ity analas tena ca ||BhGS_3.39|| 

==============================

kim adhiShThAnaH punaH kAmo j~nAnasyAvaraNatvena vairI sarvasya lokasya ? ity apekShAyAm Aha, j~nAte hi shatror adhiShThAne sukhena nibarhaNam kartum shakyata iti- 

indriyANi mano buddhir asyAdhiShThAnam ucyate |
etair vimohayaty eSha j~nAnam AvR^itya dehinam ||BhG_3.40||

indriyANi mano buddhish cAsya kAmasyAdhiShThAnam Ashraya ucyate | etair indriyAdibhir Ashrayair vimohayati vividham mohayaty eSha kAmo j~nAnam AvR^itya AcchAdya dehinam sharIriNam ||BhGS_3.40|| 

==============================

yata evam - 

tasmAt tvam indriyANy Adau niyamya bharatarShabha |
pApmAnam prajahi hy enam j~nAna-vij~nAna-nAshanam ||BhG_3.41||

tasmAt tvam indriyANy Adau pUrvam eva niyamya vashIkR^itya bharatarShabha pApmAnam pApAcAram kAmam prajahihi parityaja enam prakR^itam vairiNam j~nAna-vij~nAna-nAshanam j~nAnam shAstrata AcAryatash cAtmAdInAm avabodhaH | vij~nAnam visheShatas tad-anubhavas tayor j~nAna-vij~nAnayoH shreyaH-prApti-hetvor nAshanam nAsha-karam prajahihi AtmanaH parityajety arthaH ||BhGS_3.41|| 

==============================
 
indriyANy Adau niyamya kAmam shatrum jahihi ity uktam | tatra kim AshrayaH kAmam jahyAt ity ucyate -- 

indriyANi parANy Ahur indriyebhyaH param manaH |
manasas tu parA buddhir yo buddheH paratas tu saH ||BhG_3.42||

indriyANi shrotrAdIni paJNca | deham sthUlam bAhyam paricchinnam cApekShya saukShmyAntaratva-vyApitvAdy-apekShayA parANi prakR^iShTAny AhuH paNDitAH | tathA indriyebhyaH param manaH samkalpa-vikalpAtmakam | tathA manasas tu parA buddhir nishcayAtmikA | tathA yaH sarva-dR^ishyebhyo buddhy-antebhyo 'bhyantaro yam dehinam indriyAdibhir Ashrayair yuktaH kAmo j~nAnAvaraNa-dvAreNa mohayatIty uktam | buddheH paratas tu sa | sa buddher draShTA | para AtmA ||BhGS_3.42|| 

==============================
 
tataH kim -- 

evam buddheH param buddhvA samstabhyAtmAnam AtmanA |
jahi shatrum mahAbAho kAma-rUpam durAsadam ||BhG_3.43||

evam buddheH param AtmAnam buddhvA j~nAtvA samstabhya samyak stambhanam kR^itvAtmAnam svenaivAtmanA samskR^itena manasA samyak samAdhAyety arthaH | jahy enam shatrum he mahAbAho ! kAma-rUpam durAsadam duHkhenAsada AsAdanam prAptir yasya tam durAsadam durvij~neyAneka-visheSham iti ||BhGS_3.43|| 

iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrI-govinda-bhagavat-pUjya-pAda- 
shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^itau shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye 
tR^itIyo 'dhyAyaH 
||3|| 


__________________________________________________________

BhG 4

atha caturtho 'dhyAyaH
(shaN^kara-bhAShyaH)

yo 'yam yogo 'dhyAya-dvayenokto j~nAna-niShThA-lakShaNaH sa sannyAsaH karma-yogopAyaH | yasmin vedArthaH parisamAptaH pravR^itti-lakShaNo nivR^itti-lakShaNash ca gItAsu ca sarvAsv ayam eva yogo vivakShito bhagavatA | ataeva parisamAptaH pravR^ittim vedArtham manvAnas tam vamsha-kathanena stauti shrI-bhagavAn | 

shrI-bhagavAn uvAca
imam vivasvate yogam proktavAn aham avyayam |
vivasvAn manave prAha manur ikShvAkave 'bravIt ||BhG_4.1||

imam adhyAya-dvayenoktam yogam vivasvate AdityAya sargAdau proktavAn aham | jagat-paripAlayitÌNAm kShatriyANAm balAdhAnAya | tena yoga-balena yuktAH samarthA bhavanti brahma parirakShitum, brahma-kShatre paripAlite jagat paripAlayitum alam | avyayam avyaya-phalatvAt | na hy asya samyag darshana-niShThA-lakShaNasya mokShAkhyam phalam vyeti | sa ca vivasvAn manave prAha | manur ikShvAkave sva-putrAyAdirAjAyAbravIt ||BhGS_4.1||

==============================

evam paramparA-prAptam imam rAjarShayo viduH |
sa kAleneha mahatA yogo naShTaH parantapa ||BhG_4.2||

evam kShatriya-paramparA-prAptam imam rAjarShayo rAjAnash ca te R^iShayash ca rAjarShayo vidur imam yogam | sa yogaH kAleneha mahatA dIrgheNa naShTo vicchinna-sampradAyaH samvR^itto he parantapa ! Atmano vipakSha-bhUtAH para ucyante tAn shaurya-tejo-gabhastibhir bhAnur iva tApayatIti parantapaH shatru-tApana ity arthaH ||BhGS_4.2||

==============================

durlabhAn ajitendriyAn prApya naShTam yogam imam upalabhya lokam cApuruShArtha-sambandhinam - 

sa evAyam mayA te 'dya yogaH proktaH purAtanaH |
bhakto 'si me sakhA ceti rahasyam hy etad uttamam ||BhG_4.3||

sa evAyam mayA te tubhyam adya idAnIm yogaH proktaH purAtanaH | bhakto 'si me sakhA cAsIti | rahasyam hi yasmAd etad uttamam yogo j~nAnam ity arthaH ||BhGS_4.3||
 
==============================

bhagavatA vipratiShiddham uktam iti mA bhUt kasyacid buddhir iti parihArArtham codyam iva kurvann arjuna uvAca -

aparam bhavato janma param janma vivasvataH |
katham etad vijAnIyAm tvam Adau proktavAn iti ||BhG_4.4||

aparam arvAg vasudeva-gR^ihe bhavato janma param pUrvam sargAdau janma utpattiH vivasvata Adityasya | tat katham etad vijAnIyAm aviruddhArthatayA yas tvam evAdau proktavAn imam yogam | sa eva tvam idAnIm mahyam proktavAn asIti ||BhGS_4.4||

==============================

yA vAsudeve anIshvarAsarvaj~nAshaN^kA mUrkhANAm tAm pariharan shrI-bhagavAn uvAca padartho hy arjunasya prashnaH -

bahUni me vyatItAni janmAni tava cArjuna |
tAny aham veda sarvANi na tvam vettha parantapa ||BhG_4.5||

bahUni me mama vyatItAni atikrAntAni janmAni tava ca he arjuna tAny aham veda jAne sarvANi na tvam vettha jAnIShe | dharmAdharmAdi-pratibaddha-j~nAna-shaktitvAt | aham punar nitya-shuddha-buddha-mukta-svabhAvatvAd anAvaraNa-j~nAna-shaktir iti vedAham | he parantapa ||BhGS_4.5||

==============================

katham tarhi tava nityeshvarasya dharmAdharmAbhAve 'pi janma ? ity ucyate - 

ajo 'pi sann avyayAtmA bhUtAnAm Ishvaro 'pi san |
prakR^itim svAm adhiShThAya sambhavAmy Atma-mAyayA ||BhG_4.6||

ajo 'pi janma-rahito 'pi san, tathAvyayAtmAkShINa-j~nAna-shakti-svabhAvo 'pi san, tathA bhUtAnAm brahmAdi-stamba-paryantAnAm Ishvara Ishana-shIlo 'pi san | prakR^itim svAm mama vaiShNavIm mAyAm triguNAtmikAm yasyA vashe sarvam idam jagad vartate | yayA mohitam jagat sat svam AtmAnam vAsudevam na jAnAti | tAm prakR^itim svAm adhiShThAya vashIkR^itya sambhavAmi dehavAn iva bhavAmi jAta ivAtma-mAyayAtmano mAyayA, na paramArthato lokavat ||BhGS_4.6|| 

==============================

tac ca janma kadA kim-artham ca ? ity ucyate - 

yadA yadA hi dharmasya glAnir bhavati bhArata |
abhyutthAnam adharmasya tadAtmAnam sR^ijAmy aham ||BhG_4.7||

yadA yadA hi dharmasya glAnir hAnir varNAshramAdi-lakShaNasya prANinAm abhyudaya-niHshreyasa-sAdhanasya bhavati | bhArata ! abhyutthAnam udbhavo 'dharmasya tadAtmAnam sR^ijAmy aham mAyayA ||BhGS_4.7||
 
==============================

kim-artham ? 

paritrANAya sAdhUnAm vinAshAya ca duShkR^itAm |
dharma-samsthApanArthAya sambhavAmi yuge yuge ||BhG_4.8||

paritrANAya parirakShaNAya sAdhUnAm san-mArga-sthAnAm | vinAshAya ca duShkR^itAm pApa-kAriNAm | kim ca dharma-samsthApanArthAya dharmasya samyak-sthApanam tad-artham sambhavAmi | yuge yuge pratiyugam ||BhGS_4.8||
 
==============================

janma karma ca me divyam evam yo vetti tattvataH |
tyaktvA deham punar janma naiti mAm eti so 'rjuna ||BhG_4.9||

taj-janma mAyA-rUpam, karma ca sAdhu-paritrANAdi, me mama divyam aprAkR^itam aishvaram evam yathoktam yo vetti tattvatas tattvena yathAvat tyaktvA deham imam punar janma punar utpattim naiti na prApnoti, mAm ety Agacchati, sa mucyate he 'rjuna ||BhGS_4.9||

==============================

naiSha mokSha-mArga idAnIm pravR^ittaH | kim tarhi ? pUrvam api - 

vIta-rAga-bhaya-krodhA man-mayA mAm upAshritAH |
bahavo j~nAna-tapasA pUtA mad-bhAvam AgatAH ||BhG_4.10||

vIta-rAga-bhaya-krodhAH - rAgash ca bhayam ca krodhash ca rAga-bhaya-krodhAH, vItA vigatA rAga-bhaya-krodhA yebhyas te vIta-rAga-bhaya-krodhAH | man-mayA brahma-vida IshvarAbheda-darshinaH | mAm eva parameshvaram upAshritAH | kevala-j~nAna-niShThA ity arthaH | bahavo 'neke j~nAna-tapasA j~nAnam eva ca paramAtma-viShayam tapaH | tena j~nAna-tapasA | pUtAH parAm shuddhim gatAH santaH | mad-bhAvam Ishvara-bhAvam mokSham AgatAH samanuprAptAH | itara-tapo-nirapekShA j~nAna-niShThA ity asya liN^gam j~nAna-tapaseti visheShaNam ||BhGS_4.10||

==============================

tava tarhi rAga-dveShau staH | yena kebhyashcit evAtma-bhAvam prayacchasi, na sarvebhyaH | ity ucyate - 

ye yathA mAm prapadyante tAms tathaiva bhajAmy aham |
mama vartmAnuvartante manuShyAH pArtha sarvashaH ||BhG_4.11||

ye yathA yena prakAreNa yena prayojanena yat-phalArthitayA mAm prapadyante tAms tathaiva tat-phala-dAnena bhajAmy anugR^ihNAmy aham ity etat | teShAm mokSham pratyanarthitvAt | na hy ekasya mumukShutvam phalArthitvam ca yugapat sambhavati | ato ye yat-phalArthinas tAms tat-phala-pradAnena, ye yathokta-kAriNas tv aphalArthino mumukShavash ca tAn j~nAna-pradAnena | ye j~nAninaH sannyAsino mumukShavash ca tAn mokSha-pradAnena, tathArtAnArti-haraNena ity evam yathA prapadyante ye tAms tathaiva bhajAmIty arthaH | na punAr rAga-dveSha-nimittam moha-nimittam vA kamcid bhajAmi | sarvathApi sarvAvasthasya mameshvarasya vartma mArgam anuvartante manuShyAH | yat-phalArthitayA yasmin karmaNy adhikR^itA ye prayatante te manuShyA atra ucyante he pArtha sarvashaH sarva-prakAraiH ||BhGS_4.11||

==============================

yadi taveshvarasya rAgAdi-doShAbhAvAt sarva-prANiShv anujighR^ikShAyAm tulyAyAm sarva-phala-pradAna-samarthe ca tvayi sati vAsudevaH sarvam [GItA 7.19] iti j~nAnenaiva mumukShavaH santaH kasmAt tvAm eva sarve na pratipadyante ? iti shR^iNu tatra kAraNam -

kAN^kShantaH karmaNAm siddhim yajanta iha devatAH |
kShipram hi mAnuShe loke siddhir bhavati karmajA ||BhG_4.12||

kAN^kShanto 'bhIpsantaH karmaNAm siddhim phala-niShpattim prArthayanto yajanta ihAsmin loke devatA indrAdgny-AdyAH | atha yo 'nyAm devatAm upAste 'nyo 'sAv anyo 'ham asmIti na sa veda, yathA pashuH | evam sa devAnAm [BAU 1.4.10] iti shruteH | teShAm hi bhinna-devatAyAjinAm phalAkAN^kShiNAm kShipram shIghram hi yasmAn mAnuShe loke | manuShya-loke hi shAstrAdhikAraH | kShipram hi mAnuShe loke iti visheShaNAt | anyeShv api karma-phala-siddhim darshayati bhagavAn | mAnuShe loke varNAshramAdi-karmAdhikAra iti visheShaH | teShAm ca varNAshramAdhikAriNAm karmiNAm phala-siddhiH kShipram bhavati karmajA karmaNo jAtA ||BhGS_4.12||

==============================

mAnuSha eva loke varNAshramAdi-karmAdhikAraH | nAnyeShu lokeShv iti niyamaH kim-nimittaH ? iti | athavA varNAshramAdi-pravibhAgopetA manuShyA mama vartmAnuvartante sarvasha [GItA 4.11] ity uktam kasmAt punaH kAraNAn niyamena tavaiva vartmAnuvartante, nAnyasya kim ? ucyate - 

cAtur-varNyam mayA sR^iShTam guNa-karma-vibhAgashaH |
tasya kartAram api mAm viddhy akartAram avyayam ||BhG_4.13||

cAturvarNyam catvAra eva varNAsh cAturvarNyam mayeshvareNa sR^iShTam utpAditam brAhmaNo 'sya mukham AsIt [ãk 8.4.19.2, YajuH 32.11] ity Adi shruteH | guNa-karma-vibhAgasho guNa-vibhAgashaH karma-vibhAgashash ca | guNAH sattva-rajas-tamAmsi | tatra sAttvikasya sattva-pradhAnasya brAhmaNasya shamo damas tapaH [GItA 18.42] ity AdIni karmANi | sattvopa-sarjana-rajaH-pradhAnasya kShatriyasya shaurya-tejaH-prabhR^itIni karmANi | tama-upasarjana-rajaH-pradhAnasya vaishyasya kR^iShy-AdIni karmANi | raja-upasarjana-tamaH-pradhAnasya shUdrasya shushrUShaiva karma | ity evam guNa-karma-vibhAgashash cAturguNyam mayA sR^iShTam ity arthaH | tac cedam cAturvarNyam nAnyeShu lokeShu | ato mAnuShe loke iti visheShaNam | hanta tarhi cAturvarNya-sargAdeH karmaNaH kartR^itvAt tat-phalena yujyase 'to na tvam nitya-mukto nityeshvarash ceti | ucyate - yadyapi mAyA-samvyavahAreNa tasya karmaNaH kartAram api santam mAm paramArthato viddhy akartAram, ataevAvyayam asamsAriNam ca mAm viddhi ||BhGS_4.13||

==============================

yeShAm tu karmaNAm kartAram mAm manyase paramArthatas teShAm akartaivAham | yato -

na mAm karmANi limpanti na me karma-phale spR^ihA |
iti mAm yo 'bhijAnAti karmabhir na sa badhyate ||BhG_4.14||

na mAm tAni karmANi limpanti dehAdy-ArambhakatvenAhaN^kArAbhAvAt | na ca teShAm karmaNAm phale me mama spR^ihA tR^iShNA | yeShAm tu samsAriNAm aham kartety AbhimAnaH karmasu spR^ihA tat-phaleShu ca tAn karmANi limpantIti yuktam | tad-abhAvAn na mAm karmANi limpantIti | evam yo 'nye 'pi mAm AtmatvenAbhijAnAti nAham kartA na me karma-phale spR^iheti na karmabhir na badhyate | tasyApi na dehAdy-ArambhakAni karmANi bhavantIty arthaH ||BhGS_4.14||

==============================

nAham kartA, na me karma-phale spR^iheti -

evam j~nAtvA kR^itam karma pUrvair api mumukShubhiH |
kuru karmaiva tasmAt tvam pUrvaiH pUrvataram kR^itam ||BhG_4.15||

evam j~nAtvA kR^itam karma pUrvair apy atikrAntair mumukShubhiH | kuru tena karmaiva tvam | na tuShNIm Asanam nApi samnyAsaH kartavyaH | tasmAt tvat-pUrvair apy anuShThitatvAd yady anAtmaj~nas tvam tad Atma-shuddhy-artham | tattvavic cet loka-samgrahArtham | pUrve janakAdibhiH pUrvataram kR^itam | nAdhunAtana-kR^itam nivartitam ||BhGS_4.15||

==============================

tatra karma cet kartavyam tvad-vacanAd eva karomy aham | kim visheShitena ? pUrvaiH pUrvataram kR^itam [GItA 4.15] iti | ucyate -- yasmAn mahad vaiShamyam karmaNi | katham ? 

kim karma kim akarmeti kavayo 'py atra mohitAH |
tat te karma pravakShyAmi yaj j~nAtvA mokShyase 'shubhAt ||BhG_4.16||

kim karma kim cAkarmeti kavayo medhAvino 'py atrAsmin karmAdi-viShaye mohitA moham gatAH | atas te tubhyam aham karmAkarma ca pravakShyAmi yaj j~nAtvA viditvA karmAdi mokShyase 'shubhAt samsArAt ||BhGS_4.16||

==============================

na caitat tvayA mantavyam, karma nAma dehAdi-ceShTA loka-prasiddham, akarma nAma tad-akriyA tUShNIm Asanam | kim tatra boddhavyam ? iti | kasmAt ? ucyate -

karmaNo hy api boddhavyam boddhavyam ca vikarmaNaH |
akarmaNash ca boddhavyam gahanA karmaNo gatiH ||BhG_4.17||

karmaNaH shAstra-vihitasya hi yasmAd apy asti boddhavyam | boddhavyam cAsty eva vikarmaNaH pratiShiddhasya | tathAkarmaNash ca tUShNImbhAvasya boddhavyam astIti triShv apy adhyAhAraH kartavyaH | yasmAd gahanA viShamA durj~nAnA karmaNa ity upalakShaNArtham karmAdInAm karmAkarma-vikarmaNAm gatir yAthAtmyam tattvam ity arthaH ||BhGS_4.17||

==============================

kim punas tattvam karmAder yad boddhavyam vakShyAmIti pratij~nAtam ? ucyate -- 

karmaNy akarma yaH pashyed akarmaNi ca karma yaH |
sa buddhimAn manuShyeShu sa yuktaH kR^itsna-karma-kR^it ||BhG_4.18||

karmaNi | karma kriyata iti karma vyApAra-mAtram, tasmin karmaNy akarma karmAbhAvam yaH pashyet | akarmaNi ca karmAbhAve kartR^i-tantratvAt pravR^itti-nivR^ittyor vastv aprApyaiva hi sarva eva kriyAkArakAdi-vyavahAro 'vidyAbhUmAv eva karma yaH pashyet pashyati | sa buddhimAn manuShyeShu, sa yukto yogI ca kR^itsna-karma-kR^it samasta-karma-kR^ic ca sa iti stUyate karmAkarmaNor itaretara-darshI |

nanu kim idam viruddham ucyate karmaNy akarma yaH pashyed iti | akarmaNi ca karma iti | na hi karmAkarma syAd akarma vA karma, tatra viruddham katham pashyed draShTA ? na | akarmaiva paramArthataH sat-karmavad avabhAsate mUDha-dR^iShTer lokasya, tathA karmaivAkarmavat | tatra yathAbhUta-darshanArtham Aha bhagavAn karmaNy akarma yaH pashyed ity Adi | ato na viruddham buddhimattvAdy-upapattesh ca | boddhavyam iti ca yathAbhUta-darshanam ucyate | na ca viparIta-j~nAnAd ashubhAn mokShaNam syAt yaj j~nAtvA mokShyase 'shubhAt [GItA 4.16] iti coktam | tasmAt karmAkarmaNI viparyayeNa gR^ihIte prANibhis tad-viparyaya-grahaNa-nivR^itty-artham bhagavato vacanam karmaNy akarma yaH ity Adi | 

na cAtra karmAdhikaraNa-karmAsti, kuNDe badarANIva | nApy akarmAdhikaraNam karmAsti karmAbhAvatvAd akarmaNaH | ato viparIta-gR^ihIte eva karmAkarmaNI laukikaiH, yathA mR^igatR^iShNikAyAm udakam shuktikAyAm vA rajatam | 

nanu karma karmaiva sarveShAm na kvacid vyabhicarati | tan na nau-sthasya nAvi gacchantyAm taTasthesv agatiShu nageShu pratikUla-gati-darshanAt | dUreShu cakShuShAsannikR^iShTeShu gacchatsu gaty-abhAva-darshanAt | evam ihApy akarmaNy aham karomIti karma-darshanam karmaNi cAkarma-darshanam viparIta-darshanam yena, tan-nirAkaraNArtham ucyate karmaNy akarma yaH pashyet ity Adi |

tad etad ukta-prativacanam apy asakR^id atyanta-viparIta-darshana-bhAvitatayA momuhyamAno lokaH shrutam apy asakR^it tattvam vismR^itya vismR^itya mithyA-prasaN^gam avatAryAvatArya codayatIti punaH punar uttaram Aha bhagavAn | durvij~neyatvam cAlakShya vastunaH | avyakto 'yam acintyo 'yam [GItA 2.25], na jAyate mriyate [GItA 2.27] ity AdinAtmani karmAbhAvaH shruti-smR^iti-nyAya-prasiddha ukto vakShyamANash ca | tasminn Atmani karmAbhAve 'karmaNi karma-viparIta-darshanam atyanta-nirUDham | yataH kim karma kim akarmeti kavayo 'py atra mohitAH [GItA 4.16] dehAdy-Ashrayam karmAtmany adhyAropya | aham kartA mamaitat karma, mayAsya karmaNaH phalam bhoktavyam iti ca | tathA aham tUShNIm bhavAmi, yenAham nirAyAso 'karmA sukhI syAm iti kArya-karaNAshraya-vyApAroparamam tat-kR^itam casukhitvam Atmany adhyAropya na karomi kimcit tUShNIm sukham Asam ity abhimanyate lokaH | tatredam lokasya viparIta-darshanApanayanAyAha bhagavAn karmaNy akarma yaH pashyed ity Adi |

atra ca karma karmaiva sat kArya-karaNAshrayam karma-rahito 'vikriya Atmani sarvair adhyastam | yataH paNDito 'py aham karomIti manyate | atha Atma-samavetatayA sarva-loka-prasiddhe karmaNi nadI-kula-stheShv iva gatiH pratilaumyena | ato 'karma karmAbhAvam yathA-bhUtam gaty-abhAvam iva vR^ikSheShu yaH pashyet | akarmaNi ca kArya-karaNa-vyApAroparame karmavad Atmany adhyAropite tUShNIm akurvan sukham Ase ity ahaN^kArAbhisandhi-hetutvAt tasminn akarmaNi ca karma yaH pashyet | ya evam karmAkarma-vibhAgaj~naH sa buddhimAn paNDito manuShyeShu | sa yukto yogI kR^itsna-karma-kR^ic ca | so 'shubhAn mokShitaH kR^ita-kR^ityo bhavatIty arthaH |

ayam shloko 'nyathA vyAkhyAtaH kaishcit | katham ? nityAnAm kila karmaNAm IshvarArthe 'nuShThIyamAnAnAm tat-phalAbhAvAd akarmANi tAny ucyante gauNyA vR^ittyA | teShAm cAkaraNam akarma | tac ca pratyavAya-phalatvAt karmocyate gauNyaiva vR^ittyA | tatra nitye karmaNy akarma yaH pashyet phalAbhAvAt | yathA dhenur api gaur agaur ucyate kShIrAkhyam phalam na prayacchatIti tadvat | tathA nityAkaraNe tv akarmaNi karmaH Ashyen narakAdi-pratyavAya-phalam prayacchatIti | naitad yuktam vyAkhyAnam | evam-j~nAnAd ashubhAn mokShAnupapatteH | yaj j~nAtvA mokShyase 'shubhAt [GItA 4.16] iti bhagavatoktam vacanam bodhyeta | katham ? nityAnAm anuShThAnAd ashubhAt syAn nAma mokShaNam | na tu teShAm phalAbhAva-j~nAnAt | na hi nityAnAm phalAbhAva-j~nAnam ashubha-mukti-phalatvena coditam nitya-karma-j~nAnam vA | na ca bhagavativehoktam | 

etenAkarmaNi karma-darshanam pratyuktam | na hy akarmaNi karmeti darshanam kartavyatayeha codyate, nityasya tu kartavyatA-mAtram | na cAkaraNAn nityasya pratyavAyo bhavatIti vij~nAnAt kimcit phalam syAt | nApi nityAkaraNam j~neyatvena coditam | nApi karmAkarmeti mithA-darshanAd ashubhAn mokShaNam | buddhimattvam, yuktatA, kR^itsna-karma-kR^ittvAdi ca phalam upapadyate stutir vA | mithyA-j~nAnam eva hi sAkShAd ashubha-rUpam kuto 'nyasmAd ashubhAn mokShaNam ? na hi tamas tamaso nivartakam bhavati | 

nanu karmaNi yad akarma-darshanam akarmaNi vA karma-darshanam, na tan-mithyA-j~nAnam | kim tarhi gauNam phala-bhAvAbhAva-nimittam ? na, karmAkarma-vij~nAnAd api gauNAt phalasyAshravaNAt | nApi shruta-hAnya-shruta-parikalpanayA kashcid visheSho labhyate | sva-shabdenApi shakyam vaktum nitya-karmaNAm phalam nAsty akaraNAc ca teShAm naraka-pAtaH syAd iti | tatra vyAjena para-vyAmoha-rUpeNa karmaNy akarma yaH pashyed ity AdinA kim ? tatraiva vyAcakShANena bhagavatoktam vAkyam loka-vyAmohArtham iti vyaktam kalpitam syAt | na caitac chadma-rUpeNa vAkyena rakShaNIyam vastu, nApi shabdAntareNa punaH punar ucyamAnam subodham syAd ity evam vaktum yuktam | karmaNy evAdhikAras te [GItA 2.47] ity atra hi sphuTatara ukto 'rtho na punar vaktavyo bhavati | sarvatra ca prashastam boddhavyam ca kartavyam eva, na niShprayojanam boddhavyam ity ucyate |

na ca mithyA-j~nAnam boddhavyam bhavati tat-pratyupasthApitam vA vastv-AbhAsam | nApi nityAnAm akaraNAd abhAvAt prayavAya-bhAvotpattiH | nAsato vidyate bhAvo [GItA 2.16] iti vacanAt | tat-katham asataH saj jAyate [ChAU 6.2.2] iti ca darshitam | asataH saj-janma-pratiShedhAd asataH sad-utpattim bruvatA 'sad eva sad bhavet | sac cAsad bhaved ity uktam syAt | tac cAyuktam, sarva-pramANa-virodhAt | na ca niShphalam vidadhyAt karma shAstram duHkha-svarUpatvAt | duHkhasya ca buddhi-pUrvakatayA kAryatvAnupapatteH | tad-akaraNe ca naraka-pAtAbhyupagame 'narthAyaiva | ubhayathApi karaNe 'karaNe ca shAstram niShphalam kalpitam syAt | svAbhyupagama-virodhash ca nityam niShphalam karmety abhyupagamya mokSha-phalAyeti bruvataH | tasmAd yathA-shruta evArthaH karmaNy akarma ya ity AdeH | tathA ca vyAkhyAto 'smAbhiH shlokaH ||BhGS_4.18||

==============================

tad etat karmaNy akarmAdi-darshanam stUyate - 

yasya sarve samArambhAH kAma-samkalpa-varjitAH |
j~nAnAgni-dagdha-karmANam tam AhuH paNDitam budhAH ||BhG_4.19||

yasya yathokta-darshinaH sarve yAvantaH samArambhAH karmANi samArabhyanta iti samArambhAH | kAma-samkalpa-varjitAH kAmaistat-kAraNaish ca saN^kalpa-varjitA mudhaiva ceShTA-mAtrA anuShThIyante | pravR^ittena cel loka-saN^grahArtham, nivR^ittena cej jIvana-mAtrArtham, tam j~nAnAgni-dagdha-karmANam karmAdAv akarmAdi-darshanam j~nAnam, tad evAgnis tena j~nAnAgninA dagdhAni shubhAshubha-lakShaNAni karmANi yasya | tam AhuH paramArthataH paNDitam budhAH brahma-vidaH ||BhGS_4.19||

==============================

yas tu karmAdAv akarmAdi-darshI so 'karmAdi-darshanAd eva niShkarmA sannyAsI jIvana-mAtrArtha-ceShTaH san karmaNi na pravartate, yadyapi prAg-vivekataH pravR^ittaH | yas tu prArabdha-karmA sann uttara-kAlam utpannAtma-samyag-darshanaH syAt, sa sarva-karmaNi prayojanam apashyan sa-sAdhanam karma pariyajaty eva | sa kutashcin nimittAt karma-parityAgAsambhave sati karmaNi tat-phale ca saN^ga-rahitatayA sva-prayojanAbhAvAl loka-saN^grahArtham pUrvavat karmaNi pravR^itto 'pi naiva kimcit karoti j~nAnAgni-dagdha-karmatvAt tadIyam karmAkarmaiva sampadyata ity etam artham darshayiShyann Aha - 

tyaktvA karma-phalAsaN^gam nitya-tR^ipto nirAshrayaH |
karmaNy abhipravR^itto 'pi naiva kimcit karoti saH ||BhG_4.20||

tyaktvA karmasv abhimAnam phalAsaN^gam ca yathoktena j~nAnena nitya-tR^ipto nirAkAN^kSho viShayeShv ity arthaH | nirAshraya Ashraya-rahitaH | Ashrayo nAma yad Ashritya puruShArtham sisAdhayiShati | dR^iShTAdR^iShTa-phala-sAdhanAshraya-rahita ity arthaH | viduShA kriyamANam karma paramArthato 'karmaiva | tasya niShkriyAtma-darshana-sampannatvAt | tenaivambhUtena sva-prayojanAbhAvAt sa-sAdhanam karma parityaktavyam eveti prApte, tato nirgamAsambhavAl loka-saN^graha-cikIrShayA shiShTa-vigarhaNAparijihIrShayA vA pUrvavat karmaNy-abhipravR^itto 'pi niShkryAtma-darshana-sampannatvAn naiva kimcit karoti saH ||BhGS_4.20||

==============================

yaH punaH pUrvokta-viparItaH prAg eva karmAmbhAd brahmaNi sarvAntare pratyag-Atmani niShkriye samjAtAtma-darshanaH, sa dR^iShTAdR^iShTeShTa-viShayAshIr vivarjitatayA dR^iShTAdR^iShTArthe karmaNi prayojanam apyashyan sa-sAdhanam karma samnyasya sharIra-yAtrA-mAtra-ceShTo yatir j~nAna-niShTho mucyata iti | etad artham darshayitum Aha- 

nirAshIr yata-cittAtmA tyakta-sarva-parigrahaH |
shArIram kevalam karma kurvan nApnoti kilbiSham ||BhG_4.21||

nirAshIr nirgatA AshiSho yasmAt sa nirAshIH | yata-cittAtmA cittam antaH-karaNam | AtmA bAhyaH kArya-karaNa-samghAtaH | tAv ubhAv api yatau samyatau yasya sa yata-cittAtmA | tyakta-sarva-parigrahaH - tyaktaH sarvaH parigraho yena sa tyakta-sarva-parigrahaH | shArIram sharIra-sthiti-mAtra-prayojanam kevalam tatrApi abhimAna-varjitam karma kurvan | nApnoti na prApnoti kilbiSham aniShTa-rUpam pApam dharmam ca | dharmo 'pi mumukShor aniShTa-rUpam kilbiSham eva | bandhApAdakatvAt | tasmAt tAbhyAm mukto bhavati, samsArAn mukto bhavatIty arthaH | 

kim ca shArIram kevalam karmety atra kim sharIra-nirvartyam shArIram karmAbhipretam ? Aho svic charIra-sthiti-mAtra-prayojanam shArIram karma ? iti | kim cAto yadi sharIra-nirvartyam shArIram karma yadi vA sharIra-sthiti-mAtra-prayojanam sharIram ? iti | ucyate -- yadA sharIra-nirvartyam karma shArIram abhipretam syAt tadA dR^iShTAdR^iShTa-prayojanam karma pratiShiddham api sharIreNa kurvan nApnoti kilbiSham iti bruvato viruddhAbhidhAnam prasajyeta | shAstrIyam ca karma dR^iShTAdR^iShTa-prayojanam sharIreNa kurvan nApnoti kilbiSham ity api bruvato 'prApta-pratiShedha-prasaN^gaH | shArIram karma kurvan iti visheShaNAt kevala-shabda-prayogAc ca vAN^-manasa-nirvartyam karma vidhi-pratiShedha-viShayam dharmAdharma-shabda-vAcyam kurvan prApnoti kilbiSham ity uktam syAt |

tatrApi vAN^-manasAbhyAm vihitAnuShThAna-pakShe kilbiSha-prApti-vacanam viruddham Apadyeta | pratiShiddha-sevi-pakShe 'pi bhUtArthAnuvAda-mAtram anarthakam syAt | yadA tu sharIra-sthiti-mAtra-prayojanam shArIram karmAbhipretam bhavet, tadA dR^iShTAdR^iShTa-prayojanam karma vidhi-pratiShedha-gamyam sharIra-vAN^-manasa-nirvartyam anyad akruvams tair eva sharIrAdibhiH sharIra-sthiti-mAtra-prayojanam kevala-shabda-prayogAt aham karomi ity abhimAna-varjitaH sharIrAdi-ceShTA-mAtram loka-dR^iShTyA kurvan nApnoti kilbiSham | evambhUtasya pApa-shabda-vAcya-kilbiSha-prApty-asambhavAt kilbiSham samsAram nApnoti | j~nAnAgni-dagdha-sarva-karmatvAd apratibandhena mucyate eveti pUrvokta-samyag-darshana-phalAnuvAda evaiShaH | evam sharIram kevalam karma ity asyArthasya parigrahe niravadyam bhavati ||BhGS_4.21||

==============================

tyakta-sarva-parigrahasya yater annAdeH sharIra-sthiti-hetorH parigrahasyAbhAvAd yAcanAdinA sharIra-sthitau kartavyatAyAm prAptAyAm ayAcitam asamk ptam upapannam yadR^icchayA [Mbh 14.46.19; Baudhayana-dharma-sUtra 21.8.12] ity AdinA vacanenAnuj~nAtam yateH sharIra-sthiti-hetor annAdeH prApti-dvAram AviShkurvann Aha -

yadR^icchA-lAbha-santuShTo dvandvAtIto vimatsaraH |
samaH siddhAv asiddhau ca kR^itvApi na nibadhyate ||BhG_4.22||

yadR^icchA-lAbha-santuShTaH prArthitopanato lAbho yadR^icchA-lAbhaH, tena santuShTaH samjAtAlam-pratyayaH | dvandvAtIto dvandvaiH shItoShNAdibhir hanyamAno 'py aviShaNNa-citto dvandvAtIta ucyate | vimatsaro vigata-matsaro nirvaira-buddhiH | samas tulyo yadR^icchA-lAbhasya siddhAv asiddhau ca, ya evambhUto yatir annAdeH sharIra-sthiti-hetor lAbhAlAbhayoH samo harSha-viShAda-varjitaH, karmAdAv akarmAdi-darshI, yathA-bhUtAtma-darshana-niShThaH san sharIra-sthiti-mAtra-prayojane bhikShATanAdi-karmaNi sharIrAdi-nirvartye naiva kimcit karomIti [GItA 5.8] guNA guNeShu vartanta [GItA 3.28] ity evam sadA samparicakShANa AtmanaH kartR^itvAbhAvam pashyann eva kimcid bhikShATanAdikam karma karoti | loka-vyavahAra-sAmAnya-darshanena tu laukikair Aropita-kartR^itve bhikShATanAdau karmaNi kartA bhavati | svAnubhavena tu shAstra-pramANAdi-janitenAkartraiva | sa evam parAdhyAropita-kartR^itvam sharIra-sthiti-mAtra-prayojanam bhikShATanAdikam karma kR^itvApi na nibadhyate, bandha-hetoH karmaNaH sahetukasya j~nAnAgninA dagdhatvAd ity uktAnuvAda evaiShaH ||BhGS_4.22||

==============================

tyaktvA karma-phalAsaN^gam [GItA 4.20] ity anena shlokena yaH prArabdha-karmA san yadA niShkriya-brahmAtma-darshana-sampannaH syAt tadA tasyAtmanaH kartR^i-karma-prayojanAbhAva-darshinaH karma-parityAge prApte kutashcin nimittAt tad-asambhave sati pUrvavat tasmin karmaNy abhipravR^ittasyApi naiva kimcit karoti sa [GItA 4.20] itikarmAbhAvaH pradarshitaH | yasyaivam karmAbhAvo darshitas tasyaiva -

gata-saN^gasya muktasya j~nAnAvasthita-cetasaH |
yaj~nAyAcarataH karma samagram pravilIyate ||BhG_4.23||

gata-saN^gasya sarvato nivR^ittAsakter muktasya nivR^itta-dharmAdharmAdi-bandhanasya, j~nAnAvasthita-cetaso j~nAna evAvasthitam ceto yasya so 'yam j~nAnAvasthita-cetAH | tasya yaj~nAya yaj~na-nirvR^itty-artham Acarato nirvartayataH karma samagram sahAgreNa phalena vartata iti samagram karma tat-samagram pravilIyate vinashyatIty arthaH ||BhGS_4.23||

==============================

kasmAt punaH kAraNAt kriyamANam karma svakAryArambham akurvat samagram pravilIyata ity ucyate ? yataH -

brahmArpaNam brahma havir brahmAgnau brahmaNA hutam |
brahmaiva tena gantavyam brahma-karma-samAdhinA ||BhG_4.24||

brahmArpaNam yena karaNena brahmavid havir agnAv arpayati | tad brahmaiveti pashyati tasyAtma-vyatirekeNAbhAvam pashyati | yathA shuktikAyAm rajatAbhAvam pashyati tad ucyate brahmaivArpaNam iti | yathA yad rajatam tac chuktikaiveti | brahma arpaNam ity asamaste pade yad-arpaNa-buddhyA gR^ihyate loke tad asya brahma-vido brahmaivety arthaH |

brahma havis tathA yad dhavir buddhyA gR^ihyamANam tad brahmaivAsay | tathA brahmAgnau iti samastam padam | agnir api brahmaiva | yatra hUyate brahmaNA kartrA brahmaiva kartety arthaH | yat tena hutam havana-kriyA tad brahmaiva | yat tena gantavyam phalam tad api brahmaiva | brahma-karma-samAdhinA brahmaiva karma brahma-karma tasmin samAdhir yasya sa brahma-karma-samAdhis tena brahma-karma-samAdhinA brahmaiva gantavyam | 

evam loka-saN^graham cikIrShuNApi kriyamANam karam, paramArthato 'karma brahma-buddhy-upamR^iditvAt | evam sati nivR^itta-karmaNo 'pi sarva-karma-sannyAsinaH samyag-darshana-stuty-artham yaj~natva-sampAdanam j~nAnasya sutarAm upapadyate | yad-arpaNAdy-adhiyaj~ne prasiddham tad asyAdhyAtmam brahmaiva paramArtha-darshina iti | anyathA sarvasya brahmatve 'rpaNAdInAm eva visheShato brahmatvAbhidhAnam anarthakam syAt | tasmAd brahmaivedam sarvam ity abhijAnato viduShaH sarva-karmAbhAvaH |

kAraka-buddhy-abhAvAc ca | nahi kAraka-buddhi-rahitam yaj~nAkhyam karma dR^iShTam | sarvam evAgni-hotrAdikam karma shabda-samarpita-devatA-visheSha-sampradAnAdi-kAraka-buddhimat-kartr-abhimAna-phalAbhisandhimac ca dR^iShTam | nopamR^idita-kriyAkAraka-phala-bheda-buddhimat kartR^itvAbhimAna-phalAbhisandhi-rahitam vA | idam tu brahma-buddhy-upamR^iditArpaNAdi-kAraka-kriyA-phala-bheda-buddhi karmAto 'karmaiva tat | 

tathA ca darshitam karmaNy akarma yaH pashyet [GItA 4.18], karmaNy abhipravR^itto 'pi naiva kimcit karoti saH [GItA 4.20], guNA guNeShu vartante [GItA 3.28], naiva kimcit karomIti yukto manyeta tattvavit [GItA 5.8] ity AdibhiH | tathA ca darshayams tatra tatra kriyA-kAraka-phala-bheda-buddhy-upamardam karoti | dR^iShTA ca kAmyAgnihotrAdau kAmopamardena kAmyAgnihotrAdi-hAniH | tathA mati-pUrvakAm atipUrvakAdInAm karmaNAm kArya-visheShasyArambhakatvam dR^iShTam | tathehApi brahma-buddhy-upamR^iditArpaNAdi-kAraka-kriyA-phala-bheda-buddher bAhya-ceShTA-mAtreNa karmApi viduSho 'karma sampadyate | ata uktam samagram pravilIyate [GItA 4.23] iti |

atra kecid AhuH - yad brahma tad arpaNAdIni | brahmaiva kilArpaNAdinA paJNca-vidhena kArakAtmanA vyavasthitam sat tad eva karma karoti | tatra nArpaNAdi-buddhir nivartyate | kintv arpaNAdiShu brahma-buddhir AdhIyate | yathA pratimAdau viShNv-Adi-buddhiH, yathA vA nAmAdau brahma-buddhir iti | satyam evam api syAd yadi j~nAna-yaj~na-stuty-artham prakaraNam na syAt | atra tu samyag-darshanam j~nAna-yaj~na-shabditam anekAn yaj~na-shabditAn kriyA-visheShAn upanyasya shreyAn dravya-mayAd yaj~nAj j~nAna-yaj~naH parantapa [GItA 4.33] iti j~nAnam stauti | atra ca samartham idam vacanam brahmArpaNam ity Adi j~nAnasya yaj~natva-sampAdane, anyathA sarvasya brahmatve 'rpaNAdInAm eva visheShato brahmatvAbhidhAnam anarthakam syAt | ye tv arpaNAdiShu pratimAyAm viShNu-dR^iShTivad brahma-dR^iShTiH kShipyate | nAmAdiShv iva ceti bruvate, na teShAm brahma-vidyokteha vivakShitA syAt | arpaNAdi-viShayatvAj j~nAnasya | na ca dR^iShTi-sampAdana-j~nAnena mokSha-phalam prApyate | brahmaiva tena gantavyam iti cocyate |

viruddham ca samyag-darshanam antareNa mokSha-phalam prApyata iti | prakR^iti-virodhash ca | samyag-darshanam ca prakR^itam karmaNy akarma yaH pashyet [GItA 4.18] ity atrAnte ca samyag-darshanam tasyaivopasamhArAt | shreyAn dravya-mayAd yaj~nAj j~nAna-yaj~naH parantapa [GItA 4.33] j~nAnam labdhvA parAm shAntim [GItA 4.39] ity AdinA samyag-darshana-stutim eva kurvann upakShINo 'dhyAyaH | tatrAkasmAd arpaNAdau brahma-dR^iShTir aprakaraNe pratimAyAm iva viShNu-dR^iShTir ucyata ity anupapannam | tasmAd yathA-vyAkhyAtArtha evAyam shlokaH ||BhGS_4.24||

==============================

tatrAdhunA samyag-darshanasya yaj~natvam sampAdya tat-stuty-artham anye 'pi yaj~nA upakShipyante -

daivam evApare yaj~nam yoginaH paryupAsate |
brahmAgnAv apare yaj~nam yaj~nenaivopajuhvati ||BhG_4.25||

daivam eva devA ijyante yena yaj~nenAsau daivo yaj~nas tam evApare yaj~nam yoginaH karmiNaH paryupAsate, kurvantIty arthaH | brahmAgnau satyam j~nAnam anantam brahma [TaittU 2.1] vij~nAnam Anandam brahma [BAU 3.9.28], yat sAkShAd aparokShAd brahma ya AtmA sarvAntaraH [BAU 3.4.1], ity Adi vacanoktam ashanAyApipAsAdi-sarva-samsAra-dharma-varjitam neti neti [BAU 4.4.22] iti nirastAsheSha-visheSham brahma-shabdenocyate | brahma ca tad-agnish ca sa homAdhikaraNatva-vivakShayA brahmAgnis tasmin brahmAgnAv apare 'nye brahma-vido yaj~nam yaj~na-shabda-vAcya AtmA Atma-nAmasu yaj~na-shabdasya pAThAt [Nirukti 14.11] tam AtmAnam yaj~nam paramArthataH param eva brahma santam buddhyAdy-upAdhi-samyuktam adhyasta-sarvopAdhi-dharmakam Ahuti-rUpam yajNinaivAtmanaivokta-lakShaNopajuhvati prakShipanti, sopAdhikasyAtmano nirupAdhikena para-brahma-svarUpeNaiva yad darshanam, sa tasmin homas tam kurvanti, brahmAtmaikatva-darshana-niShThAH sannyAsina ity arthaH | so 'yam samyag-darshana-lakShaNo yaj~no daiva-yaj~nAdiShu yaj~neShUpakShipyante brahmArpaNam ity Ad-shlokaiH prastutaH shreyAn dravya-mayAd yaj~nAj j~nAna-yaj~naH parantapa [GItA 4.33] ity AdinA stuty-artham ||BhGS_4.25||

==============================

shrotrAdInIndriyANy anye samyamAgniShu juhvati |
shabdAdIn viShayAn anya indriyAgniShu juhvati ||BhG_4.26||

shrotrAdInIndriyANy anye yoginaH samyamAgniShu pratIndriyam samyamo bhidyata iti bahu-vacanam | samyamA evAgnayas teShu juhvati | indriya-samyamam eva kurvantIty arthaH | shabdAdIn viShayAn anya indriyAgniShu juhvati, indriyANy evAgnayas teShv indriyAgniShu juhvati shrotrAdibhir aviruddha-viShaya-grahaNam homam manyante ||BhGS_4.26||

==============================

kim ca -
sarvANIndriya-karmANi prANa-karmANi cApare |
Atma-samyama-yogAgnau juhvati j~nAna-dIpite ||BhG_4.27||

sarvANIndriya-karmANi indriyANAm karmANIndriya-karmANi | tathA prANa-karmANi prANo vAyur AdhyAtmikas tat-karmANy AkuJNcana-prasAraNAdIni tAni cApara Atma-samyama-yogAgnau, Atmani samyama Atma-samyamaH | sa eva yogAgnis tasminn Atma-samyama-yogAgnau juhvati prakShipanti | j~nAna-dIpite sneheneva pradIpite viveka-vij~nAnenojjvala-bhAvam ApAdite pravilApayantIty arthaH ||BhGS_4.27||

==============================

dravya-yaj~nAs tapo-yaj~nA yoga-yaj~nAs tathApare |
svAdhyAya-j~nAna-yaj~nAsh ca yatayaH samshita-vratAH ||BhG_4.28||

dravya-yaj~nAs tIrtheShu dravya-viniyogam yaj~na-buddhyA kurvanti ye te dravya-yaj~nAH | tapo-yaj~nAs tapo yaj~no yeShAm tapasvinAm te tapo-yaj~nAH | yoga-yaj~nAH prANAyAma-pratyAhArAdi-lakShaNo yogo yaj~no yeShAm te yoga-yaj~nAH | tathApare svAdhyAya-j~nAna-yaj~nAsh ca svAdhyAyo yathA-vidhi R^ig-Ady-abhyAso yaj~no yeShAm te svAdhyAya-yaj~nAH | j~nAna-yaj~nA j~nAnam shAstrArtha-parij~nAnam yaj~no yeShAm te j~nAna-yaj~nAH | svAdhyAya-yaj~nA j~nAna-yaj~nAsh ca yatayo yatana-shIlAH | shamsita-vratAH samyak shitAni tanUkR^itAni tIkShNIkR^itAni vratAni yeShAm te samshita-vratAH ||BhGS_4.28||

==============================

kim ca -
apAne juhvati prANam prANe 'pAnam tathApare |
prANApAna-gatI ruddhvA prANAyAma-parAyaNAH ||BhG_4.29||

apAne 'pAna-vR^ittau juhvati pratikShipanti prANam prANa-vR^ittim, pUrakAkhyam prANAyAmam kurvantIty arthaH | prANe 'pAnam tathApare juhvati | recakAkhyam ca prANAyAmam kurvantIty etat | prANApAna-gatI mukhya-nAsikAbhyAm vAyor nirgamanam prANasya gatis tad-viparyayeNAdho-gamanam apAnasya gatis, te prANApAna-gatI | ete ruddhvA nirudhya prANAyAma-parAyaNAH prANAyAma-tat-parAH kumbhakAkhyam prANAyAmam kurvantIty arthaH ||BhGS_4.29|| 

==============================

kim ca -

apare niyatAhArAH prANAn prANeShu juhvati |
sarve 'py ete yaj~na-vido yaj~na-kShapita-kalmaShAH ||BhG_4.30||

apare niyatAhArA niyataH parimita AhAro yeShAm te niyatAhArAH santaH, prANAn vAyu-bhedAn prANeShv eva juhvati | yasya yasya vAyor jayaH kriyata itarAn vAyu-bhedAn tasmin tasmin juhvati, te tatra praviShTA iva bhavanti | sarve 'py ete yaj~na-vido yaj~na-kShapitakalmaShA yaj~nair yathoktaiH kShapito nAshitaH kalmaSho yeShAm te yaj~na-kShapita-kalmaShAH ||BhGS_4.30|| 

==============================

evam yathoktAn yaj~nAn nirvatrya --- 

yaj~na-shiShTAmR^ita-bhujo yAnti brahma sanAtanam |
nAyam loko 'sty ayaj~nasya kuto 'nyaH kurusattama ||BhG_4.31||

yaj~na-shiShTAmR^ita-bhujo yaj~nAnAm shiShTam yaj~na-shiShTam yaj~na-shiShTam ca tad amR^itam ca yaj~na-shiShTAmR^itam tad bhu¤jata iti yaj~na-shiShTAmR^ita-bhujaH | yathoktAn yaj~nAn kR^itvA tac-chiShTena kAlena yathA-vidhi-coditam annam amR^itAkhyam bhu¤jate iti yaj~na-shiShTAmR^ita-bhujo yAnti gacchanti brahma sanAtanam cirantanam mumukShavash cet | kAlAtikramApekShayeti sAmarthyAd gamyate | nAyam lokaH sarva-prANi-sAdhAraNo 'py asti yathoktAnAm yaj~nAnAm eko 'pi yaj~no yasya nAsti so 'yaj~nas tasya | kuto 'nyo vishiShTa-sAdhana-sAdhyaH kuru-sattama ||BhGS_4.31||

==============================

evam bahu-vidhA yaj~nA vitatA brahmaNo mukhe |
karmajAn viddhi tAn sarvAn evam j~nAtvA vimokShyase ||BhG_4.32||

evam yathoktA bahu-vidhA bahu-prakArA yaj~nA vitatA vistIrNA brahmaNo vedasya mukhe dvAre veda-dvAreNa avagamyamAnA brahmaNo mukhe vitatA ucyante | tad yathA vAci hi prANam juhumaH ity AdayaH | karmajAn kAyika-vAcika-mAnasa-karmodbhavAn viddhi tAn sarvAn anAtmajAn, nirvyApAro hy AtmA | ata evam j~nAtvA vimokShyase 'shubhAt | na mad-vyApArA ime, nirvyApAro 'ham udAsIna ity evam j~nAtvAsmAt samyag-darshanAn mokShyase samsAra-bandhanAd ity arthaH ||BhGS_4.32|| 

==============================

brahmArpaNam [GItA 4.24] ity Adi lokena samyag-darshanasya yaj~natvam sampAditam | yaj~nAsh cAneka upadiShTAH | taiH siddha-puruShArtha-prayojanair j~nAnam stUyate | katham ? --- 

shreyAn dravya-mayAd yaj~nAj j~nAna-yaj~naH parantapa |
sarvam karmAkhilam pArtha j~nAne parisamApyate ||BhG_4.33||

shreyAn dravya-mayAt dravya-sAdhana-sAdhyAd yaj~nAj j~nAna-yaj~no he paramtapa | dravya-mayo hi yaj~naH phalasyArambhakaH, j~nAna-yaj~no na phalArambhakaH, ataH shreyAn prashasyataraH | katham ? yataH sarvam karma samastam akhilam apratibaddham pArtha j~nAne mokSha-sAdhane sarvataH samplutodaka-sthAnIye parisamApyate antarbhavatIty arthaH | yathA kR^itAya vijitAyAdhareyAH samyanty evam enam sarvam tad abhisameti yat kimcit prajAH sAdhu kurvanti yas tad veda yat sa veda [ChAU 4.1.4] iti shruteH ||BhGS_4.33||

==============================

tad etad vishiShTAm j~nAnam tarhi kena prApyata ity ucyate --- 

tad viddhi praNipAtena pariprashnena sevayA |
upadekShyanti te j~nAnam j~nAninas tattva-darshinaH ||BhG_4.34||

tat viddhi vijAnIhi yena vidhinA prApyate iti | AcAryAn abhigamya, praNipAtena prakarSheNa nIcaiH patanam praNipAto dIrgha-namaskAras tena | katham bandhaH ? katham mokShaH ? kA vidyA ? kA cAvidyA ? iti pariprashnena, sevayA guru-shushrUShayA evam AdinA | prashrayeNAvarjitA AcAryA upadekShyanti kathayiShyanti te j~nAnam yathokta-visheShaNam j~nAninaH | j~nAnavanto 'pi kecid yathAvat tattva-darshana-shIlAH, apare na | ato vishinaShTi tattva-darshina iti | ye samyag-darshinas tair upadiShTam j~nAnam kArya-kShamam bhavati | netarad iti bhagavato matam ||BhGS_4.34||

==============================

tathA ca satIdamapi samartham vacanam -- 

yaj j~nAtvA na punar moham evam yAsyasi pANDava |
yena bhUtAny asheSheNa drakShyasy Atmany atho mayi ||BhG_4.35||

yaj j~nAtvA yaj j~nAnam tair upadiShTam adhigamya prApya punar bhUyo moham evam yathedAnIm moham gato 'si punar evam na yAsyasi he pANDAva | kim ca ---- yena j~nAnena bhUtAny asheSheNa brahmAdIni stamba-paryantAni drakShyasi sAkShAd Atmani pratyag Atmani mat-samsthAnImAni bhUtAnIty atho api mayi vAsudeve parameshvare cemAnIti | kShetraj~neshvaraikatvam sarvopaniShat-prasiddham drakShyasIty arthaH ||BhGS_4.35|| 

==============================

kim caitasya j~nAnasya mAhAtmyam --- 

api ced asi pApebhyaH sarvebhyaH pApa-kR^ittamaH |
sarvam j~nAna-plavenaiva vR^ijinam santariShyasi ||BhG_4.36||

api ced asi pApebhyaH pApa-kR^idbhyaH sarvebhyo 'tishayena pApa-kR^it pApa-kR^ittamaH sarvam j~nAna-plavenaiva j~nAnam eva plavam kR^itvA vR^ijinam vR^ijinArNavam pApa-samudram samtariShyasi | dharmo 'pIha mumukShoH pApam ucyate ||BhGS_4.36|| 

==============================

j~nAnam katham nAshayati pApam ? iti sa-dR^iShTAntam ucyate --- 

yathaidhAmsi samiddho 'gnir bhasmasAt kurute 'rjuna |
j~nAnAgniH sarva-karmANi bhasmasAt kurute tathA ||BhG_4.37||

yathaidhAmsi kAShThAni samiddhaH samyag iddho dIpto 'gnir bhasmasAt bhasmIbhAvam kurute he arjuna, j~nAnam eva agnir j~nAnAgniH sarva-karmANi bhasmasAt kurute tathA nirbIjIkarotIty arthaH | na hi sAkShAd eva j~nAnAgniH karmANIndhanavat bhasmIkartum shaknoti | tasmAt samyag darshanam sarva-karmaNAm nirbIjatve kAraNam ity abhiprAyaH | sAmarthyAd yena karmaNA arIram Arabdham tat pravR^itta-phalatvAd upabhogenaiva kShIyate | tasya tAvad eva ciram yAvan na vimokShye 'tha sampatsye [ChAU 6.14.1] ato yAny apravR^itta-phalAni j~nAnotpatteH prAk kR^itAni j~nAna-sahabhAvIni cAtItAneka-janma-kR^itAni ca tAny eva sarvANi bhasmasAt kurute ||BhGS_4.37||

==============================

yataH evam ataH--- 

na hi j~nAnena sadR^isham pavitram iha vidyate |
tat svayam yoga-samsiddhaH kAlenAtmani vindati ||BhG_4.38||

na hi j~nAnena sadR^isham tulyam pavitram pAvanam shuddhi-karam iha vidyate | taj j~nAnam svayam eva yoga-samsiddho yogena karma-yogena samAdhi-yogena ca samsiddhaH samskR^ito yogyatAm ApannaH san mumukShuH kAlena mahatA Atmani vindati labhate ity arthaH ||BhGS_4.38|| 

==============================

yenaikAntena j~nAna-prAptir bhavati sa upAya upadishyate --- 

shraddhAvAml labhate j~nAnam tat-paraH samyatendriyaH |
j~nAnam labdhvA parAm shAntim acireNAdhigacchati ||BhG_4.39||

shraddhAvAn shraddhAlur labhate j~nAnam | shraddhAlutve 'pi bhavati kashcin manda-prasthAnaH, ata Aha --- tat-paraH | gurUpAsadanAdAv abhiyukto j~nAna-labdhy-upAye shraddhAvAn | tat-paro 'py ajitendriyaH syAt ity ata Aha --- samyatendriyaH | samyatAni viShayebhyo nivartitAni yasyendriyANi sa samyatendriyaH | ya evambhUtaH shraddhAvAn tat-paraH samyatendriyash ca so 'vashyam j~nAnam labhate | praNipAtAdis tu bAhyo 'naikAntiko 'pi bhavati, mAyAvitvAdi-sambhavAt | na tu tat shraddhAvattvAdau ity ekAntato j~nAna-labdhy-upAyaH | kim punar j~nAna-lAbhAt syAd ity ucyate -- j~nAnam labdhvA param mokShAkhyAm shAntim uparatim acireNa kShipram evAdhigacchati | samyag-darshanAt kShipram eva mokSho bhavatIti sarva-shAstra-nyAya-prasiddhaH sunishcito 'rthaH ||BhGS_4.39||

==============================

atra samshayo na kartavyaH, pApiShTho hi samshayaH | katham ity ucyate --- 

aj~nash cAshraddadhAnash ca samshayAtmA vinashyati |
nAyam loko 'sti na paro na sukham samshayAtmanaH ||BhG_4.40||

aj~nash cAnAtmaj~nash cAshraddadhAnash ca guru-vAkya-shAstreShv avishvAsavAmsh ca samshayAtmA ca samshaya-cittash ca vinashyati | aj~nAshraddadhAnau yadyapi vinashyataH, na tathA yathA samshayAtmA | samshayAtmA tu pApiShThaH sarveShAm | katham ? nAyam sAdhAraNo 'pi loko 'sti | tathA na paro lokaH | na sukham, tatrApi samshayotpatteH samshayAtmanaH samshaya-cittasya | tasmAt samshayo na kartavyaH ||BhGS_4.40|| 


==============================

kasmAt ? ---- 

yoga-samnyasta-karmANam j~nAna-samchinna-samshayam |
Atmavantam na karmANi nibadhnanti dhana¤jaya ||BhG_4.41||

yoga-samnyasta-karmANam paramArtha-darshana-lakShaNena yogena samnyastAni karmANi yena paramArtha-darshinA dharmAdharmAkhyAni tam yoga-samnyasta-karmANam | katham yoga-samnyasta-karmA ? ity Aha - j~nAna-samchinna-samshayam j~nAnenAtmeshvaraikatva-darshana-lakShaNena samchinnaH samshayo yasya yo j~nAna-samchinna-samshayaH | ya evam yoga-samnyasta-karmA tam Atmavantam apramattam guNa-ceShTA-rUpeNa dR^iShTAni karmANi na nibadhnanty aniShTAdi-rUpam phalam nArabhante | he dhanamjaya ||BhGS_4.41|| 

==============================

yasmAt karma-yogAnuShThAnAd ashuddhi-kShaya-hetuka-j~nAna-samchinna-samshayo na nibadhyate karmabhir j~nAnAgni-dagdha-karmatvAd eva, yasmAc ca j~nAna-karmAnuShThAna-viShaye samshayavAn vinashyati --- 

tasmAd aj~nAna-sambhUtam hR^it-stham j~nAnAsinAtmanaH |
chittvainam samshayam yogam AtiShThottiShTha bhArata ||BhG_4.42||

tasmAt pApiShTham aj~nAna-sambhUtam aj~nAnAd avivekAj jAtam hR^it-stham hR^idi buddhau sthitam j~nAnAsinA shoka-mohAdi-doSha-haram samyag darshanam j~nAnam tad evAsiH khaDgas tena j~nAnAsinA AtmanaH svasya, Atma-viShayatvAt samshayasya | na hi parasya samshayaH pareNa cchettavyatAm prAptaH, yena svasyeti visheShyeta | ata Atma-viShayo 'pi svasyaiva bhavati | chittvA enam samshayam sva-vinAsha-hetu-bhUtam, yogam samyag-darshanopAyam karmAnuShThAnam AtiShTha kurv ity arthaH | uttiShTha cedAnIm yuddhAya bhArata iti ||BhGS_4.42|| 

iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrI-govinda-bhagavat-pUjya-pAda- 
shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^itau shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye 
caturtho 'dhyAyaH 
||4||

BhG 5

atha paJNcamo 'dhyAyaH
(shaN^kara-bhAShya)

arjuna uvAca - 

samnyAsam karmaNAm kR^iShNa punar yogam ca shamsasi |
yac chreya etayor ekam tan me brUhi sunishcitam ||BhG_5.1||

samnyAsam parityAgam karmaNAm AstrIyANAm anuShTheya-visheShANAm shamsasi prashamsasi kathayasIty etat | punar yogam ca teShAm eva anuShThAnam avashya-kartavyam shamsasi | ato me katarat shreyaH iti samshayaH - kim karmAnuShThAnam shreyaH, kim vA tad-dhAnam iti | prashasyataram cAnuShTheyam | atash ca yat shreyaH prashasyataram etayoH karma-samnyAsa-karma-yogayor yad-anuShThAnAt shreyo 'vAptir mama syAd iti manyase, tad ekam anyatarat saha eka-puruShAnuShTheyatvAsambhavAt me brUhi sunishcitam abhipretam taveti ||BhGS_5.1|| 

 - o)O(o - 

svAbhiprAyam AcakShANo nirNayAya shrI-bhagavAn uvAca - 

samnyAsaH karma-yogash ca niHshreyasa-karAv ubhau |
tayos tu karma-samnyAsAt karma-yogo vishiShyate ||BhG_5.2||

samnyAsaH karmaNAm parityAgaH karma-yogash ca teShAm anuShThAnam tAv ubhAv api niHshreyasa-karau mokSham kurvAte j~nAnotpatti-hetutvena | ubhau yadyapi niHshreyasa-karau, tathApi tayos tu niHshreyasa-hetvoH karma-samnyAsAt kevalAt karma-yogo vishiShyata iti karma-yogam stauti ||BhGS_5.2|| 

 - o)O(o - 

kasmAt iti Aha - 

j~neyaH sa nitya-samnyAsI yo na dveShTi na kAN^kShati |
nirdvandvo hi mahA-bAho sukham bandhAt pramucyate ||BhG_5.3||

j~neyo j~nAtavyaH sa karma-yogI nitya-samnyAsI iti yo na dveShTi kimcit na kAN^kShati duHkha-sukhe tat-sAdhane ca | evamvidho yaH, karmaNi vartamAno 'pi sa nitya-samnyAsI iti j~nAtavya ity arthaH | nirdvandvo dvandva-varjito hi yasmAt mahAbAho sukham bandhAd anAyAsena pramucyate ||BhGS_5.3|| 

 - o)O(o - 

samnyAsa-karma-yogayor bhinna-puruShAnuShTheyayor viruddhayoH phale 'pi virodho yuktaH | na tUbhayor niHshreyasa-karatvam eveti prApta idam ucyate -

sAmkhya-yogau pR^ithag bAlAH pravadanti na paNDitAH |
ekam apy AsthitaH samyag ubhayor vindate phalam ||BhG_5.4||

sAmkhya-yogau pR^ithag viruddha-bhinna-phalau bAlAH pravadanti na paNDitAH | paNDitAs tu j~nAnina ekam phalam aviruddham icchanti | katham ? ekam api sAmkhya-yogayoH samyag AsthitaH samyag anuShThitavAn ity arthaH, ubhayor vindate phalam | ubhayos tad eva hi niHshreyasam phalam | ato na phale virodho 'sti |

nanu samnyAsa-karma-yoga-shabdena prastutya sAmkhya-yogayoH phalaikatvam katham ihAprakR^itam bravIti ? naiSha doShaH - yadyapy arjunena samnyAsam karma-yogam ca kevalam abhipretya prashnaH kR^itaH | bhagavAms tu tad-aparityAgenaiva svAbhipretam ca visheSham samyojya shabdAntara-vAcyatayA prativacanam dadau sAmkhya-yogAv iti | tAv eva samnyAsa-karma-yogau j~nAna-tad-upAya-sama-buddhitvAdi-samyuktau sAmkhya-yoga-shabda-vAcyAv iti bhagavato matam | ato na aprakR^ita-prakriyeti ||BhGS_5.4||

 - o)O(o - 

ekasyApi samyag anuShThAnAt katham ubhayoH phalam vindate ? ity ucyate - 

yat sAmkhyaiH prApyate sthAnam tad yogair api gamyate |
ekam sAmkhyam ca yogam ca yaH pashyati sa pashyati ||BhG_5.5||

yat sAmkhyair j~nAna-niShThaiH samnyAsibhiH prApyate sthAnam mokShAkhyam tad yogair api j~nAna-prApty-upAyatveneshvare samarpya karmANy AtmanaH phalam anabhisamdhAyAnutiShThanti ye te yogA yoginaH | tair api paramArtha-j~nAna-samnyAsa-prApti-dvAreNa gamyata ity abhiprAyaH | ata ekam sAN^khyam ca yogam ca yaH pashyati phalaikatvAt sa pashyati samyak pashyatIty arthaH ||BhGS_5.5|| 

 - o)O(o - 

evam tarhi yogAt samnyAsa eva vishiShyate | katham tarhIdam uktam tayos tu karma-samnyAsAt karma-yogo vishiShyate [GItA 5.2] iti ? sR^iNu tatra kAraNam - tvayA pR^iShTAm kevalam karma-samnyAsam karma-yogam cAbhipretya tayor anyataraH kaH shreyAn ? iti | tad-anurUpam prativacanam mayoktam karma-samnyAsAt karma-yogo vishiShyate iti j~nAnam anapekShya | j~nAnApekShas tu samnyAsaH sAmkhyam iti mayAbhipretaH | paramArtha-yogash ca sa eva | yas tu karma-yogo vaidikaH sa ca tAdarthyAt yogaH samnyAsa iti copacaryate | katham tAdarthyam ? ity ucyate -

samnyAsas tu mahAbAho duHkham Aptum ayogataH |
yoga-yukto munir brahma nacireNAdhigacchati ||BhG_5.6||

samnyAsas tu pAramArthiko duHkham Aptum prAptum ayogato yogena vinA | yoga-yukto vaidikena karma-yogena vaidikena karma-yogeneshvara-samarpita-rUpeNa phala-nirapekSheNa yukto muniH | mananAd Ishvara-svarUpasya muniH | brahma paramAtma-j~nAna-niShThA-lakShaNatvAt prakR^itaH samnyAso brahmocyate | nyAsa iti brahmA brahmA hi paraH [MahAnArU 78] iti shruteH | brahma paramArtha-samnyAsam paramArtha-j~nAna-niShThA-lakShaNam na cireNa kShipram evAdhigacchati prApnoti | ato mayoktam karma-yogo vishiShyata iti ||BhGS_5.6||

 - o)O(o - 

yadA punar ayam samyag-darshana-prApty-upAyatvena -

yoga-yukto vishuddhAtmA vijitAtmA jitendriyaH |
sarva-bhUtAtma-bhUtAtmA kurvann api na lipyate ||BhG_5.7||

yogena yukto yoga-yukto vishuddhAtmA vishuddha-sattvo vijitAtmA vijita-deho jitendriyash ca sarva-bhUtAtma-bhUtAtmA sarveShAm brahmAdInAm stamba-paryantAnAm bhUtAnAm Atma-bhUta AtmA pratyak-cetano yasya sa sarva-bhUtAtma-bhUtAtmA samyag-darshIty arthaH | sa tatraivam vartamAno loka-samgrahAya karma kurvann api na lipyate na karmabhir badhyate ity arthaH ||BhGS_5.7||

 - o)O(o - 

na cAsau paramArthataH karotIty ataH - 

naiva kim cit karomIti yukto manyeta tattva-vit |
pashya¤ shR^iNvan spR^isha¤ jighrann ashnan gacchan svapa¤ shvasan ||BhG_5.8||
pralapan visR^ijan gR^ihNann unmiShan nimiShann api |
indriyANIndriyArtheShu vartanta iti dhArayan ||BhG_5.9||

yuktaH samAhitaH san manyeta cintayet | tattvavid Atmano yAthAtmyam tattvam vettIti tattva-vit paramArtha-darshIty arthaH | kadA katham vA tattvam avadhArayan manyeta ? ity ucyate | manyeteti pUrveNa sambandhaH | yasyaivam tattva-vidaH sarva-kArya-karaNa-ceShTAsu karmasv akarmaiva pashyataH samyag-darshinas tasya sarva-karma-samnyAsa evAdhikAraH karmaNo 'bhAva-darshanAt | na hi mR^iga-tR^iShNikAyAm udaka-buddhyA pAnAya pravR^itta udakAbhAva-j~nAne 'pi tatraiva pAna-prayojanAya pravartate ||BhGS_5.8-9||

 - o)O(o - 

yas tu punar atattva-vit pravR^ittash ca karma-yoge - 

brahmaNy AdhAya karmANi saN^gam tyaktvA karoti yaH |
lipyate na sa pApena padma-patram ivAmbhasA ||BhG_5.10||

brahmaNIshvara AdhAya nikShipya tad-artham karma karomIti bhR^itya iva svAmy-artham sarvANi karmANi | mokShe 'pi phale saN^gam tyaktvA karoti yaH sarva-karmANi, lipyate na sa pApena na sambadhyate padma-patram ivAmbhasodakena ||BhGS_5.10||

 - o)O(o - 

kevalam sattva-shuddhi-mAtram eva phalam tasya karmaNaH syAt, yasmAt - 

kAyena manasA buddhyA kevalair indriyair api |
yoginaH karma kurvanti saN^gam tyaktvAtma-shuddhaye ||BhG_5.11||

kAyena dehena manasA buddhyA ca kevalair mamatva-varjitaiH IshvarAyaiva karma karomi, na mama phalAya iti mamatva-buddhi-shUnyair indriyair api - kevala-shabdaH kAyAdibhir api pratyekam sambadhyate, sarva-vyApAreShu mamatA-varjanAya | yoginaH karmiNaH karma kurvanti saN^gam tyaktvA phala-viShayam Atma-shuddhaye sattva-shuddhaya ity arthaH | tasmAt tatraiva tavAdhikAra iti kuru karmaiva ||BhGS_5.11|| 

 - o)O(o - 

yasmAc ca - 

yuktaH karma-phalam tyaktvA shAntim Apnoti naiShThikIm |
ayuktaH kAma-kAreNa phale sakto nibadhyate ||BhG_5.12||

yukta IshvarAya karmaNi karomi na mama phalAya ity evam samAhitaH san karma-phalam tyaktvA parityajya shAntim mokShAkhyAm Apnoti naiShThikIm niShThAyAm bhavAm sattva-shuddhi-j~nAna-prApti-sarva-karma-samnyAsa-j~nAna-niShThA-krameNeti vAkya-sheShaH | yas tu punar ayukto 'samAhitaH kAma-kAreNa | karaNam kAraH kAmasya kAraH kAma-kAraH | tena kAma-kAreNa kAma-preritatayety arthaH | mama phalAya idam karomi karma ity evam phale sakto nibadhyate | atas tvam yukto bhava ity arthaH ||BhGS_5.12|| 

 - o)O(o - 

yas tu paramArtha-darshI saH - 

sarva-karmANi manasA samnyasyAste sukham vashI |
nava-dvAre pure dehI naiva kurvan na kArayan ||BhG_5.13||

sarvANi karmANi sarva-karmANi samnyasya parityajya nityam naimittikam kAmyam pratiShiddham ca | tAni sarvANi karmANi manasA viveka-buddhyA, karmAdAv akarma-sandarshanena samtyajyety arthaH | Aste tiShThati sukham | tyakta-vAN^-manaH-kAya-ceShTo nirAyAsaH prasanna-citta Atmano 'nyatra nivR^itta-sarva-bAhya-prayojana iti sukham Aste ity ucyate | vashI jitendriya ity arthaH | kva katham Aste ? ity Aha - nava-dvAre pure | sapta shIrShANyAny Atmana upalabdhi-dvArANi, arvAk dve mUtra-purISha-visargArthe, tair dvArair nava-dvAram puram ucyate sharIram puram iva puram | Atmaika-svAmikam, tad-artha-prayojanaish ca indriya-mano-buddhi-viShayair aneka-phala-vij~nAnasyotpAdakaiH paurair ivAdhiShThitam | tasmin nava-dvAre pure dehI sarvam karma samnyasyAste | 

kim visheShaNena ? sarvo hi dehI samnyAsy asamnyAsI vA dehe evAste | tatrAnarthakam visheShaNam iti | ucyate - yas tv aj~no dehI dehendriya-samghAta-mAtrAtma-darshI sa sarvo 'pi gehe bhUmAv Asane vA ' 'sa iti manyate | na hi deha-mAtrAtma-darshino geha iva dehe Asa iti pratyayaH sambhavati | dehAdi-samghAta-vyatiriktAtma-darshinas tu dehe Ase iti pratyaya upapadyate | para-karmaNAm ca parasminn Atmany avidyayayAdhyAropitAnAm vidyayA viveka-j~nAnena manasA samnyAsa upapadyate | utpanna-viveka-j~nAnasya sarva-karma-samnyAsino 'pi geha iva deha eva nava-dvAre pura Asanam | prArabdha-phala-karma-samskAra-sheShAnuvR^ittyA deha eva visheSha-vij~nAnotpatteH | dehe evAsta ity asty eva visheShaNa-phalam vidvad-avidvat-pratyaya-bhedApekShatvAt |
