yadyapi kArya-karaNa-karmANy avidyayAtmany adhyAropitAni samnyasyAste ity uktam, tathApi AtmasamavAyi tu kartR^itvam kArayitR^itvam ca syAt ity AshaN^kyAha - naiva kurvan svayam na kArya-karaNAni kArayan kriyAsu pravartayan | kim ? yat tat kartR^itvam kArayitR^itvam ca dehinaH svAtma-samavAyi sat samnyAsAn na sambhavati ? yathA gacchato gatir gamana-vyApAra-parityAge na syAt tadvat ? kim vA svata eva Atmano nAsti iti ? atrocyate - nAsty AtmanaH svataH kartR^itvam kArayitR^itvam ca | uktam hi -- avikAryo 'yam ucyate [GItA 2.55], sharIra-stho 'pi kaunteya na karoti na lipyate [GItA 3.26] iti | dhyAyatIva lelAyatIva [BAU 4.3.7] iti ca shruteH ||BhGS_5.13||
- o)O(o - 

kim ca - 

na kartR^itvam na karmANi lokasya sR^ijati prabhuH |
na karma-phala-samyogam svabhAvas tu pravartate ||BhG_5.14||

na kartR^itvam svataH kurv iti nApi karmANi ratha-ghaTa-prAsAdAdInIpsitatamAni lokasya sR^ijaty utpAdayati prabhur AtmA | nApi rathAdi kR^itavatas tat-phalena samyogam na karma-phala-samyogam | yadi kimcid api svato na karoti na kArayati ca dehI, kas tarhi kurvan kArayan ca pravartata iti, ucyate - svabhAvas tu svo bhAvaH svabhAvo 'vidyA-lakShaNA prakR^itir mAyA pravartate daivI hi [GItA 7.14] ity AdinA vakShyamANA ||BhGS_5.14|| 

- o)O(o - 

paramArthatas tu - 

nAdatte kasya cit pApam na caiva sukR^itam vibhuH |
aj~nAnenAvR^itam j~nAnam tena muhyanti jantavaH ||BhG_5.15||

nAdatte na ca gR^ihNAti bhaktasyApi kasyacit pApam | na caivAdatte sukR^itam bhaktaiH prayuktam vibhuH | kim-artham tarhi bhaktaiH pUjAdi-lakShaNam yAga-dAna-homAdikam ca sukR^itam prayujyate ity Aha - aj~nAnenAvR^itam j~nAnam viveka-vij~nAnam, tena muhyanti karomi kArayAmi bhokShye bhojayAmIty evam moham gacchanty avivekinaH samsAriNo jantavaH ||BhGS_5.15|| 

- o)O(o - 

j~nAnena tu tad aj~nAnam yeShAm nAshitam AtmanaH |
teShAm Adityavaj j~nAnam prakAshayati tatparam ||BhG_5.16||

j~nAnena tu yena aj~nAnena AvR^itAH muhyanti jantavas tat aj~nAnam yeShAm jantUnAm viveka-j~nAnena Atma-viShayeNa nAshitam Atmano bhavati, teShAm jantUnAm Adityavat yathAdityaH samastam rUpa-jAtam avabhAsayati tadvat j~nAnam j~neyam vastu sarvam prakAshayati tat param paramArtha-tattvam ||BhGS_5.16||

- o)O(o - 

 yat param j~nAnam prakAshitam - 

tad-buddhayas tad-AtmAnas tan-niShThAs tat-parAyaNAH |
gacchanty apunar-AvR^ittim j~nAna-nirdhUta-kalmaShAH ||BhG_5.17||

tasmin brahmaNi gatA buddhir yeShAm te tad-buddhayaH, tad-AtmAnas tad eva param brahma AtmA yeShAm te tad-AtmanAH, tan-niShThAH niShThA abhiniveshas tAtparyam sarvANi karmANi samnyasya tasmin brahmaNy eva avasthAnam yeShAm te tan-niShThAH, tat-parAyaNA ca tad eva param ayanam parA gatir yeShAm bhavati te tat-parAyaNAH kevalAtma-rataya ity arthaH | yeShAm j~nAnena nAshitam Atmano 'j~nAnam te gacchanti evam-vidyAH apunar-AvR^ittim apunar-deha-sambandham j~nAna-nirdhUta-kalmaShA yathoktena j~nAnena nirdhUto nAshitaH kalmaShaH pApAdi-samsAra-kAraNa-doSho yeShAm te j~nAna-nirdhUta-kalmaShA yatayaH ity arthaH ||BhGS_5.17||

- o)O(o - 

yeShAm j~nAnena nAshitam Atmano 'j~nAnam te paNDitAH katham tattvam payantIty ucyate - 

vidyA-vinaya-sampanne brAhmaNe gavi hastini |
shuni caiva shvapAke ca paNDitAH sama-darshinaH ||BhG_5.18||

vidyA-vinaya-sampanne vidyA ca vinayash ca vidyA-vinayau, vinaya upAmaH, tAbhyAm vidyA-vinayAbhyAm sampanno vidyA-vinaya-sampanno vidvAn vinItash ca yo brAhmaNas tasmin brAhmaNe gavi hastini shuni caiva shvapAke ca paNDitAH sama-darshinaH | vidyA-vinaya-sampanne uttama-samskAravati brAhmaNe sAttvike, madhyamAyAm ca rAjasyAm gavi, samskAra-hInAyAm atyantam eva kevala-tAmase hasty-Adau ca, sattvAdi-guNais taj-jaish ca samskArais tathA rAjasais tathA tAmasaish ca samskArair atyantam evAspR^iShTAm samam ekam avikriyam tad brahma draShTum shIlam yeShAm te paNDitAH sama-darshinaH ||BhGS_5.18||

- o)O(o - 

nanv abhojyAnnAs te doShavantaH, samAsamAbhyAm viShama-same pUjAtaH [Gautama-dharma-sUtra 2.8.20] iti smR^iteH | na te doShavantaH | katham ? -

ihaiva tair jitaH sargo yeShAm sAmye sthitam manaH |
nirdoSham hi samam brahma tasmAd brahmaNi te sthitAH ||BhG_5.19||

ihaiva jIvadbhireva taiH samadarshibhiH paNDitair jito vaIkR^itaH sargo janma, yeShAm sAmye sarva-bhUteShu brahmaNi samabhAve sthitam ni calIbhUtam mano 'ntaHkaraNam | nirdoSham yadyapi doShavatsu vapAkAdiShu mUDhais taddoShair doShavat iva vibhAvyate, tathApi taddoShair aspR^iShTAm iti nirdoSham doShavarjitam hi yasmAt | nApi svaguNabhedabhinnam, nirguNatvAt caitanyasya | vakShyati ca bhagavAn icchAdInAm kShetradharmatvam, anAditvAnnirguNatvAt iti ca | nApy antyA visheShAH Atmano bhedakAH santi, pratisharIram teShAm sattve pramANAnupapatteH | ataH samam brahma ekam ca | tasmAt brahmaNi eva te sthitAH | tasmAt na doShagandhamAtramapi tAn spR^iati, dehAdisamghAtAtma-darshanAbhimAnAbhAvAt teShAm | dehAdisamghAtAtma-darshanAbhimAnavadviShayam tu tat sUtram samAsamAbhyAm viShamasame pUjAtaH iti, pUjAviShayatvena visheShaNAt | dR^ishyate hi brahmavit ShaDAN^gavit caturvedavit iti pUjAdAnAdau guNavisheShasambandhaH kAraNam | brahma tu sarvaguNadoShasambandhavarjitamityatar brahmaNi te sthitAH iti yuktam | karmaviShayam ca samAsamAbhyAm ity Adi | idam tu sarva-karma-samnyAsaviShayam prastutam, sarva-karmANi manasA ityArabhya AdhyAyaparisamApteH ||BhGS_5.19||

- o)O(o - 

yasmAt nirdoSham samam brahmAtmA, tasmAt - 

na prahR^iShyet priyam prApya nodvijet prApya cApriyam |
sthira-buddhir asammUDho brahmavid brahmaNi sthitaH ||BhG_5.20||

na prahR^iSheyet praharSham na kuryAt priyam iShTAm prApya labdhvA | nodvijet prApya cApriyam aniShTAm labdhvA | deha-mAtrAtma-darshinAm hi priyApriya-prAptI harSha-viShAdau kurvAte, na kevalAtma-darshinaH, tasya priyApriya-prApty-asambhavAt | kim ca - sarva-bhUteShv ekaH samo nirdoSha Atmeti sthirA nirvicikitsA buddhir yasya sa sthira-buddhir asammUDhaH sammoha-varjitash ca syAt yathokta-brahmavid brahmaNi sthito 'karma-kR^it sarva-karma-samnyAsIty arthaH ||BhGS_5.20||

- o)O(o - 

kim ca, brahmaNi sthitaH - 

bAhya-sparsheShv asaktAtmA vindaty Atmani yat sukham |
sa brahma-yoga-yuktAtmA sukham akShayam ashnute ||BhG_5.21||

bAhya-sparsheShu bAhyA ca te sparshAsh ca bAhya-sparshAH | spR^ishyante iti sparshAH shabdAdayo viShayAs teShu bAhya-sparsheShu | asakta AtmA antaH-karaNam yasya so 'yam asaktAtmA viShayeShu prIti-varjitaH san vindati labhate | Atmani yat sukham tad vindatIty etat | sa brahma-yoga-yuktAtmA brahmaNi yogaH samAdhir brahma-yogas tena brahma-yogena yuktaH samAhitas tasmin vyApR^ita AtmA antaH-karaNam yasya sa brahma-yoga-yuktAtmA | sukham akShayam ashnute vyApnoti | tasmAd bAhya-viShaya-prIteH kShaNikAyA indriyANi nivartayed Atmany akShaya-sukhArthIty arthaH ||BhGS_5.21||

- o)O(o - 

itash ca nivartayet -

ye hi samsparshajA bhogA duHkha-yonaya eva te |
Ady-anta-vantaH kaunteya na teShu ramate budhaH ||BhG_5.22||

ye hi yasmAt samssparshajA viShayendriya-samsparshebhyo jAtA bhogA bhuktayo duHkha-yonaya eva te, avidyA-kR^itatvAt | dR^ishyante hy AdhyAtmikAdIni duHkhAni tan-nimittAny eva | yathA iha-loke tathA para-loke 'pIti gamyate eva-shabdAt | na samsAre sukhasya gandha-mAtram apy astIti buddhvA viShaya-mR^iga-tR^iShNikAyA indriyANi nivartayet | na kevalam duHkha-yonaya eva, Ady-anta-vantash ca, Adir viShayendriya-samyogo bhogAnAm antash ca tad-viyoga eva | ataH Ady-anta-vanto 'nityAH, madhya-kShaNa-bhAvitvAt ity arthaH | kaunteya, na teShu bhogeShu ramate budho viveky avagata-paramArtha-tattvaH | atyanta-mUDhAnAm eva hi viShayeShu ratir dR^ishyate, yathA pashu-prabhR^itInAm ||BhGS_5.22||

- o)O(o - 

ayam ca shreyo-mArga-pratipakShI kaShTatamo doShaH sarvAnartha-prApti-hetur durnivArash ceti tat-parihAre yatnAdhikyam kartavyam ity Aha bhagavAn -

shaknotIhaiva yaH soDhum prAk sharIra-vimokShaNAt |
kAma-krodhodbhavam vegam sa yuktaH sa sukhI naraH ||BhG_5.23||

shaknoty utsahata ihaiva jIvann eva yaH soDhum prasahitum prAk pUrvam sharIravimokShaNAt A maraNAt ity arthaH | maraNa-sImA-karaNam jIvato 'vayambhAvi hi kAma-krodhodbhavo vegaH, anantanimittavAn hi saH iti yAvat maraNam tAvat na visrAmbhaNIya ity arthaH | kAmaH indriyagocaraprApte iShTo viShaye shrUyamANe smaryamANe vA anubhUte sukhahetau yA ga§dhas tR^iShNA sa kAmaH | krodhash cAtmanaH pratikUleShu duHkha-hetuShu dR^iyamAneShu shrUyamANeShu smaryamANeShu vA yo dveShaH sa krodhaH | tau kAma-krodhAv udbhavo yasya vegasya sa kAma-krodhodbhavo vegaH | romAJNcana-prahR^iShTa-netra-vadanAdi-liN^go 'ntaH-karaNa-prakShobha-rUpaH kAmodbhavo vegaH | gAtra-prakampa-prasveda-samdaShTauShTha-puTa-rakta-netrAdi-liN^gaH krodhodbhavo vegaH | tam kAma-krodhodbhavam vegam ya utsahate prasahate soDhum prasahitum, so yukto yogI sukhI ceha loke naraH || ||BhGS_5.23|| 

- o)O(o - 

katham-bhUtash ca brahmaNi sthito brahma prApnoti ? ity Aha bhagavAn - 

yo 'ntaH-sukho 'ntarArAmas tathAntar-jyotir eva yaH |
sa yogI brahma-nirvANam brahma-bhUto 'dhigacchati ||BhG_5.24||

yo 'ntaH-sukho 'ntar Atmani sukham yasya so 'ntaH-sukhaH, tathAntar evAtmany ArAma AramaNam AkrIDA yasya so 'ntar-ArAmaH | tathaivAntar eva Atmany eva jyotiH prakAsho yasya so 'ntar-jyotir eva, ya IdR^ishaH so yogI brahma-nirvANam brahmaNi nirvR^itim mokSham iha jIvann eva brahma-bhUtaH sann adhigacchati prApnoti ||BhGS_5.24|| 

- o)O(o - 

kim ca - 

labhante brahma-nirvANam R^iShayaH kShINa-kalmaShAH |
chinna-dvaidhA yatAtmAnaH sarva-bhUta-hite ratAH ||BhG_5.25||

labhante brahma-nirvANam mokSham R^iShayaH samyag-darshinaH samnyAsinaH kShINa-kalmaShAH kShINa-pApA nirdoShAsh chinna-dvaidhAH chinna-samshayA yatAtmAnaH samyatendriyAH sarva-bhUta-hite ratAH sarveShAm bhUtAnAm hite AnukUlye ratA ahimsakA ity arthaH ||BhGS_5.25|| 

- o)O(o - 

kim ca - 

kAma-krodha-viyuktAnAm yatInAm yata-cetasAm |
abhito brahma-nirvANam vartate viditAtmanAm ||BhG_5.26||

kAma-krodha-viyuktAnAm kAmash ca krodhash ca kAma-krodhau tAbhyAm viyuktAnAm yatInAm samnyAsinAm yata-cetasAm samyatAntaH-karaNAnAm abhita ubhayato jIvatAm mR^itAnAm ca brahma-nirvANam mokSho vartate viditAtmanAm vidito j~nAta AtmA yeShAm te viditAtmanAm teShAm viditAtmanAm samyag-darshinAm ity arthaH ||BhGS_5.26|| 

- o)O(o - 
samyag darshana-niShThAnAm samnyAsinAm sadyo-muktir uktA | karma-yogash ca IshvarArpita-sarva-bhAveneshvare brahmaNy AdhAya kriyamANaH sattva-shuddhi-j~nAna-prApti-sarva-karma-samnyAsa-krameNa mokShAya iti bhagavAn pade pade 'bravIt, vakShyati ca | athedAnIm dhyAna-yogam samyag-darshanasya antaraN^gam vistareNa vakShyAmIti tasya sUtra-sthAnIyAn shlokAn upadishati sma - 

sparshAn kR^itvA bahir bAhyAmsh cakShush caivAntare bhruvoH |
prANApAnau samau kR^itvA nAsAbhyantara-cAriNau ||BhG_5.27||
yatendriya-mano-buddhir munir mokSha-parAyaNaH |
vigatecchA-bhaya-krodho yaH sadA mukta eva saH ||BhG_5.28||

sparshAn shabdAdIn kR^itvA bahir bAhyAn shrotrAdi-dvAreNAntar-buddhau praveshitAH shabdAdayo viShayAs tAn acintayato shabdAdayo bAhyA bahir eva kR^itA bhavanti | tAn evam bahiH kR^itvA cakShush caivAntare bhruvoH kR^itvety anuShajyate | tathA prANApAnau nAsAbhyantara-cAriNau samau kR^itvA | yatendriya-mano-buddhir yatAni samyatAnIndriyANi mano buddhish ca yasya sa yatendriya-mano-buddhiH | mananAt muniH samnyAsI | mokSha-parAyaNa evam deha-samsthAnAn mokSha-parAyaNo mokSha eva param ayanam parA gatir yasya so 'yam mokSha-parAyaNo munir bhavet | vigatecchA-bhaya-krodha icchA ca bhayam ca krodhash cecchA-bhaya-krodhAs te vigatAH yasmAt sa vigatecchA-bhaya-krodhaH | ya evam vartate sadA samnyAsI, mukta eva saH | na tasya mokSho 'nyaH kartavyo 'sti ||

- o)O(o - 

bhoktAram yaj~na-tapasAm sarva-loka-maheshvaram |
suhR^idam sarva-bhUtAnAm j~nAtvA mAm shAntim R^icchati ||BhG_5.29||

evam samAhita-cittena kim vij~neyam ity ucyate | bhoktAram yaj~na-tapasAm yaj~nAnAm tapasAm ca kartR^i-rUpeNa devatA-rUpeNa ca, sarva-loka-maheshvaram sarveShAm lokAnAm mahAntam Ishvaram suhR^idam sarva-bhUtAnAm sarva-prANinAm pratyupakAra-nirapekShatayA upakAriNam sarva-bhUtAnAm hR^idayeshayam sarva-karma-phalAdhyakSham sarva-pratyaya-sAkShiNam mAm nArAyaNam j~nAtvA shAntim sarva-samsAroparatim R^icchati prApnoti ||BhGS_5.29||

iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrI-govinda-bhagavat-pUjya-pAda-shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^itau shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye paJNcamo 'dhyAyaH || 
||5||  

__________________________________________________________

BhG 6

atha ShaShTho 'dhyAyaH

(shaN^karAcArya-bhAShyaH)

atItAnantarAdhyAyAnte dhyAna-yogasya samyag darshanam praty antaraN^gasya sUtra-bhUtAH shlokAH sparshAn kR^itvA bahiH [GItA 5.27] ity Adaya upadiShTaH | teShAm vR^itti-sthAnIyo 'yam ShaShTho 'dhyAya Arabhyate | tatra dhyAna-yogasya bahiraN^gam karmeti yAvad dhyAna-yogArohaNa-samarthas tAvad gR^ihasthenAdhikR^itena kartavyam karma ity atas tat stauti |

nanu kim-artham dhyAna-yogArohaNa-sImA-karaNam, yAvatAnuShTheyam eva vihitam karma yAvajjIvam | na, ArurukShor muner yogam karma kAraNam ucyate [GItA 3.3] iti visheShaNAt | ArUDhasya ca shamenaiva sambandha-karaNAt | ArurukShor ArUDhasya ca shamaH karmash cobhayam kartavyatvenAbhipretam cet syAt tadArurukShor ArUDhasya ceti shama-karma-viShaya-bhedena visheShaNam vibhAga-karaNam cAnarthakam syAt |

tatrAshramiNAm kashcid yogam ArurukShur bhavati | ArUDhash ca kashcit | anye nArurukShavaH | na cArUDhAH | tAn apekShyArurukShor ArUDhasya ceti visheShaNam vibhAga-karaNam copapadyata eveti cet, na | tasyaiveti vacanAt | punar yoga-grahaNAc ca yogArUDhasyeti | ya AsIt pUrvam yogam ArurukShus tasyaivArUDhasya shama eva kartavyaH | kAraNam yoga-phalam pratyucyateti | ato na yAvaj-jIvam kartavyatva-prAptiH kasyacid api karmaNaH | yoga-vibhraShTa-vacanAc ca |

gR^ihasthasya cet karmiNo yogo vihitaH ShaShThe 'dhyAye, sa yoga-vibhraShTo 'pi karma-gatim karma-phalam prApnotIti tasya nAshAshaN^kAnupapannA syAt | avashyam hi kR^itam karma kAmyam nityam vA mokShasya nityatvAd anArabhyatve svam phalam Arabhata eva | nityasya ca karmaNo veda-pramANAvabuddhatvAt phalena bhavitavyam ity avocAma | anyathA vedasyAnarthArthatva-prasaN^gAd iti | 

na ca karmaNi saty ubhaya-vibhraShTa-vacanam arthavat | karmaNo vibhramsha-kAraNAnupapatteH | karma kR^itam Ishvare samnyasyety ataH kartari karma phalam nArabhateti cen, na | Ishvare samnyAsasyAdhikatara-phala-hetutvopapatteH | mokShAyaiveti cet, sva-karmaNAm kR^itAnAm Ishvare nyAso mokShAyaiva, na phalAntarAya yoga-sahitaH | 

yogAc ca vibhraShTa ity atas tam prati nAsha-shaN^kA yuktaiveti cet, na | ekAkI yata-cittAtmA nirAshIr aparigrahaH [GItA 6.10] brahmacAri-vrate sthitaH [GItA 6.14] iti karma-samnyAsa-vidhAnAt | na cAtra gR^ihasthasya nirAshIr aparigrahaH ity Adi-vacanam anukUlam | ubhaya-vibhraShTa-prashnAnupapattesh ca |

anAshrita ity anena karmiNa eva samnyAsitvam yogitvam coktam, pratiShiddham ca niragneH akriyasya ca samnyAsitvam yogitvam ceti cet, na | dhyAna-yogam prati bahiraN^gasya sataH karmaNaH phalAkAN^kShA-samnyAsa-stuti-paratvAt | 

na kevalam niragnir akriya eva samnyAsI yogI ca | kim tarhi ? karmy api, karma-phalAsaN^gam samnyasya karma-yogam anutiShThan sattva-shuddhy-artham, sa samnyAsI ca yogI ca bhavatIti stUyate | na caikena vAkyena karma-phalAsaN^ga-samnyAsa-stutish caturthAshrama-pratiShedhash copapadyate | na ca prasiddham niragner akriyasya paramArtha-samnyAsinaH shruti-smR^iti-purANetihAsa-yoga-shAstreShu vihitam samnyAsitvam yogitvam ca pratiShedhati bhagavAn | sva-vacana-virodhAc ca - sarva-karmANi manasA samnyasya... naiva kurvan na kArayan Aste [GItA 5.13] maunI samtuShTo yena kenacit... aniketaH sthira-matiH [GItA 12.19] vihAya kAmAn yaH sarvAn pumAmsh carati niHspR^ihaH [GItA 2.71] sarvArambha-parityAgI [GItA 12.16] iti ca tatra tatra bhagavatA sva-vacanAni darshitAni | tair virudhyetash caturthAshrama-pratiShedhaH | tasmAn muner yogam ArurukShoH pratipanna-gArhasthyasyAgnihotrAdi-karma phala-nirapekSham anuShThIyamAnam dhyAna-yogArohaNa-sAdhanatvam sattva-shuddhi-dvAreNa pratipadyata iti sa samnyAsI ca yogI ceti stUyate -

anAshritaH karma-phalam kAryam karma karoti yaH |
sa samnyAsI ca yogI ca na niragnir na cAkriyaH ||BhG_6.1||

anAshrito -- nAshrito 'nAshritaH | kim ? karma-phalam karmaNAm phalam karma-phalam yat tad-anAshritaH, karma-phala-tR^iShNA-rahita ity arthaH | yo hi karma-phale tR^iShNAvAn sa karma-phalam Ashrito bhavati | ayam tu tad-viparItaH, ato 'nAshritaH karma-phalam | evambhUtaH san kAryam kartavyam nityam kAmya-viparItam agnihotrAdikam karma karoti nirvartayati | yaH kashcid IdR^ishaH karmI sa karmy antarebhyo vishiShyate | ity evam artham Aha - sa samnyAsI ca yogI ceti | samnyAsaH parityAgaH sa yasyAsti sa samnyAsI ca yogI ca | yogash citta-samAdhAnam sa yasyAsti sa yogI ceti evamguNa-sampanno 'yam mantavyaH | na kevalam niragnir akriya eva samnyAsI yogI ceti mantavyaH | nirgatAH agnayaH karmAN^ga-bhUtA yasmAt sa niragniH | akriyash cAnagni-sAdhanApy avidyamAnAH kriyAs tapo-dAnAdikA yasyAsAv akriyaH ||BhGS_6.1||

==============================

nanu ca niragneH akriyasyaiva shruti-smR^iti-yoga-shAstreShu samnyAsitvam yogitvam ca prasiddham | katham iha sAgneH sa-kriyasya ca samnyAsitvam yogitvam cAprasiddham ucyata iti | naiSha doShaH, kayAcid guNa-vR^ittyA ubhayasya sampipAdayiShitatvAt | tat katham ? karma-phala-samkalpa-samnyAsAt samnyAsitvam, yogAN^gatvena ca karmAnuShThAnAt karma-phala-samkalpasya ca citta-vikShepa-hetoH parityAgAd yogitvam ceti gauNam ubhayam | na punar mukhyam samnyAsitvam yogitvam cAbhipretam ity etam artham darshayitum Aha - 

yam samnyAsam iti prAhur yogam tam viddhi pANDava |
na hy asamnyasta-samkalpo yogI bhavati kashcana ||BhG_6.2||

yam sarva-karma-tat-phala-parityAga-lakShaNam paramArtha-samnyAsam samnyAsam iti prAhuH shruti-smR^iti-vidaH, yogam karmAnuShThAna-lakShaNam tam paramArtha-samnyAsam viddhi jAnIhi he pANDAva | karma-yogasya pravR^itti-lakShaNasya tad-viparItena nivR^itti-lakShaNena paramArtha-samnyAsena kIdR^isham sAmAnyam aN^gIkR^itya tad-bhAva ucyate ity apekShAyAm idam ucyate - asti hi paramArtha-samnyAsena sAdR^ishyam kartR^i-dvArakam karma-yogasya | yo hi paramArtha-samnyAsI sa tyakta-sarva-karma-sAdhanatayA sarva-karma-tat-phala-viShayam samkalpam pravR^itti-hetu-kAma-kAraNam samnyasyati | ayam api karma-yogI karma kurvANa eva phala-viShayam samkalpam samnyasyatIti | etam artham darshayiShyann Aha - na hi yasmAd asamnyasta-samkalpo 'samnyasto 'parityaktaH saN^kalpo 'bhisandhir yena so 'samnyasta-saN^kalpaH kashcana kashcid api karmI yogI samAdhAnavAn bhavati | na sambhavatIty arthaH | phala-samkalpasya citta-vikShepa-hetutvAt | tasmAd yaH kashcana karmI samnyasta-phala-samkalpo bhavet sa yogI samAdhAnavAn avikShipta-citto bhavet | citta-vikShepa-hetoH phala-samkalpasya samnyastatvAd ity abhiprAyaH | yogAN^gatvena karmAnuShThAnAt karma-phala-saN^kalpasya vA citta-vikShepa-hetoH parityAgAt yogitvam ceti samnyAsitvam cety abhipretam ucyate |[*NOTE: This last sentence not found in all editions.] ||BhGS_6.2||

==============================

evam paramArtha-samnyAsa-karma-yogayoH kartR^i-dvArakam samnyAsa-sAmAnyam apekShya yam samnyAsam iti prAhur yogam tam viddhi pANDAva [GItA 6.2] iti karma-yogasya stuty-artham samnyAsatvam uktam | dhyAna-yogasya phala-nirapekShaH karma-yogo bahiraN^gam sAdhanam iti tam samnyAsatvena stutvAdhunA karma-yogasya dhyAna-yoga-sAdhanatvam darshayati - 

ArurukShor muner yogam karma kAraNam ucyate |
yogArUDhasya tasyaiva shamaH kAraNam ucyate ||BhG_6.3||

ArurukShor AroDhum icchataH, anArUDhasya, dhyAna-yoge 'vasthAtum ashaktasyaivety arthaH | kasya tasyArurukShoH ? muneH, karma-phala-samnyAsina ity arthaH | kim ArurukShoH ? yogam | karma kAraNam sAdhanam ucyate | yogArUDhasya punas tasyaiva shamar upashamaH sarva-karmabhyo nivR^ittiH kAraNam yogArUDhasya sAdhanam ucyate ity arthaH | yAvad yAvat karmabhya uparamate, tAvat tAvat nirAyAsasya jitendriyasya cittam samAdhIyate | tathA sati sa jhaTiti yogArUDho bhavati | tathA coktam vyAsena - 

naitAdR^isham brAhmaNasyAsti vittam
yathaikatA samatA satyatA ca | 
shIlam sthitir daNDa-nidhAnam Arjavam 
tatas tatash coparamaH kriyAbhyaH || [Mbh 12.175.37] iti ||BhGS_6.3||

==============================

athedAnIm kadA yogArUDho bhavatIty ucyate - 

yadA hi nendriyArtheShu na karmasv anuShajjate |
sarva-samkalpa-samnyAsI yogArUDhas tadocyate ||BhG_6.4||

yadA samAdhIyamAna-citto yogI hIndriyArtheShv indriyANAm arthAH shabdAdayas teShv indriyArtheShu karmasu ca nitya-naimittika-kAmya-pratiShiddheShu prayojanAbhAva-buddhyA nAnuShajjate 'nuShaN^gam kartavyatA-buddhim na karotIty arthaH | sarva-samkalpa-samnyAsI sarvAn samkalpAn ihAmutrArtha-kAma-hetUna samnyasitum shIlam asyeti sarva-samkalpa-samnyAsI | yogArUDhaH prApta-yoga ity etat, tadA tasmin kAla ucyate | sarva-samkalpa-samnyAsIti vacanAt sarvAmsh ca kAmAn sarvANi ca karmANi samnyasyed ity arthaH | samkalpa-mUlA hi sarve kAmAH - samkalpa-mUlaH kAmo vai yaj~nAH samkalpa-sambhavAH [Manu 2.3] 

kAma jAnAmi te mUlam samkalpAt tvam hi jAyase | 
na tvAm samkalpayiShyAmi tena me na bhaviShyasi || [Mabh 12.177.25] ity Adi-smR^iteH | 

sarva-kAma-parityAge ca sarva-karma-samnyAsaH siddho bhavati | sa yathA-kAmo bhavati tat-kratur bhavati yat kratur bhavati tat karma kurute [BAU 4.4.5] ity Adi shrutibhyaH | yad yad dhi kurute jantus tat tat kAmasya ceShTitam [Manu 2.4] ity Adi-smR^itibhyash ca | nyAyAc ca - na hi sarva-samkalpa-samnyAse kashcit spanditum api shaktaH | tasmAt sarva-samkalpa-samnyAsIti vacanAt sarvAn kAmAn sarvANi karmANi ca tyAjayati bhagavAn ||BhGS_6.4|| 

==============================

yadaivam yogArUDhaH, tadA tena AtmA udbhR^ito bhavati samsArAd anartha-jAtAt | ataH - 

uddhared AtmanAtmAnam nAtmAnam avasAdayet |
Atmaiva hy Atmano bandhur Atmaiva ripur AtmanaH ||BhG_6.5||

uddharet samsAra-sAgare nimagnam AtmanAtmAnam tata ut Urdhvam hared uddharet, yogArUDhatAm ApAdayed ity arthaH | nAtmAnam avasAdayet nAdho nayeta, nAdho gamayet | Atmaiva hi yasmAd Atmano bandhuH | na hy anyaH kashcit bandhuH, yaH samsAra-muktaye bhavati | bandhur api tAvat mokSham prati pratikUla eva, snehAdi-bandhanAyatanatvAt | tasmAt yuktam avadhAraNam Atmaiva hy Atmano bandhur iti | Atmaiva ripuH shatruH | yo 'nyo 'pakArI bAhyaH shatruH so 'pi Atma-prayukta eveti yuktam evAvadhAraNam Atmaiva ripur Atmana iti ||BhGS_6.5||

==============================

Atmaiva bandhur Atmaiva ripur Atmana ity uktam | tatra kim-lakShaNa AtmA Atmano bandhuH, kim-lakShaNo vA AtmAtmano ripur ity ucyate - 

bandhur AtmAtmanas tasya yenAtmaivAtmanA jitaH |
anAtmanas tu shatrutve vartetAtmaiva shatruvat ||BhG_6.6||

bandhur AtmAtmanas tasya, tasyAtmanaH sa AtmA bandhur yenAtmanAtmaiva jitaH | AtmA kArya-karaNa-samghAto yena vashIkR^itaH, jitendriya ity arthaH | anAtmanas tv ajitAtmanas tu shatrutve shatru-bhAve varteta Atmaiva shatruvat, yathAnAtmA shatrur Atmano 'pakArI, tathAtmA Atmano 'pakAre varteta ity arthaH ||BhGS_6.6||

==============================

jitAtmanaH prashAntasya paramAtmA samAhitaH |
shItoShNa-sukha-duHkheShu tathA mAnApamAnayoH ||BhG_6.7||

jitAtmanaH kArya-karaNa-samghAta AtmA jito yena sa jitAtmA tasya jitAtmanaH, prashAntasya prasannAntaH-karaNasya sataH samnyAsinaH paramAtmA samAhitaH sAkShAd-Atma-bhAvena vartate ity arthaH | kim ca shItoShNa-sukha-duHkheShu tathA mAne 'pamAne ca mAnApamAnayoH pUjA-paribhavayoH samaH syAt ||BhGS_6.7|| 

==============================

j~nAna-vij~nAna-tR^iptAtmA kUTastho vijitendriyaH |
yukta ity ucyate yogI sama-loShTAshma-kAJNcanaH ||BhG_6.8||

j~nAna-vij~nAna-tR^iptAtmA j~nAnam shAstrokta-padArthAnAm parij~nAnam, vij~nAnam tu shAstrato j~nAtAnAm tathaiva svAnubhava-karaNam, tAbhyAm j~nAna-vij~nAnAbhyAm tR^iptaH samjAtAlam-pratyayaH AtmAntaH-karaNam yasya sa j~nAna-vij~nAna-tR^iptAtmA, kUTAstho 'prakampyaH, bhavatIty arthaH | vijitendriyash ca | ya IdR^ishaH, yuktaH samAhita iti sa ucyate kathyate | sa yogI sama-loShTAshma-kAJNcanaH loShTAshma-kAJNcanAni samAni yasya saH sama-loShTAshma-kAJNcanaH ||BhGS_6.8|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

suhR^in-mitrAry-udAsIna-madhya-stha-dveShya-bandhuShu |
sAdhuShv api ca pApeShu sama-buddhir vishiShyate ||BhG_6.9||

suhR^id ity Adi lokArdham ekam padam | suhR^it iti pratyupakAram anapekShya upakartA, mitram snehavAn, ariH shatruH, udAsIno na kasyacit pakSham bhajate, madhya-stho yo viruddhayor ubhayoH hitaiShI, dveShya Atmano 'priyaH, bandhuH sambandhI ity eteShu sAdhuShu shAstrAnuvartiShu api ca pApeShu pratiShiddha-kAriShu sarveShv eteShu sama-buddhiH | kaH kim-karmA ity avyApR^ita-buddhir ity arthaH | vishiShyate, vimucyate iti vA pAThAntaram | yogArUDhAnAm sarveShAm ayam uttama ity arthaH ||BhGS_6.9|| 

==============================

ata evam uttama-phala-prAptaye - 

yogI yu¤jIta satatam AtmAnam rahasi sthitaH |
ekAkI yata-cittAtmA nirAshIr aparigrahaH ||BhG_6.10||

yogI dhyAyI yu¤jIta samAdadhyAt satatam sarvadAtmAnam antaH-karaNam rahasi ekAnte giri-guhAdau sthitaH san ekAkI asahAyaH | rahasi sthitaH ekAkI ceti visheShaNAt samnyAsam kR^itvA ity arthaH | yata-cittAtmA cittam antaH-karaNam AtmA dehash ca samyatau yasya sa yata-cittAtmA, nirAshIr vIta-tR^iShNo 'parigrahaH parigraha-rahitash cety arthaH | samnyAsitve 'pi tyakta-sarva-parigrahaH san yu¤jIta ity arthaH ||BhGS_6.10||

==============================

athedAnIm yogam yu¤jataH AsanAhAra-vihArAdInAm yoga-sAdhanatvena niyamo vaktavyaH, prApta-yogasya lakShaNam tat-phalAdi ca, ity ata Arabhyate | tatrAsanam eva tAvat prathamam ucyate - 

shucau deshe pratiShThApya sthiram Asanam AtmanaH |
nAtyucchritam nAtinIcam cailAjina-kushottaram ||BhG_6.11||

shucau shuddhe vivikte svabhAvataH samskArato vA, deshe sthAne pratiShThApya sthiram acalam Atmana Asanam nAtyucchritam nAtIva ucchritam nApy atinIcam, tac ca cailAjina-kushottaram cailam ajinam kushAsh cottare yasminn Asane tad Asanam cailAjina-kushottaram | pATha-kramAd viparIto 'tra kramash cailAdInAm ||BhGS_6.11||

==============================

pratiShThApya, kim ? 

tatraikAgram manaH kR^itvA yata-cittendriya-kriyaH |
upavishyAsane yu¤jyAd yogam Atma-vishuddhaye ||BhG_6.12||

tatra tasminn Asana upavishya yogam yu¤jyAt | katham ? sarva-viShayebhya upasamhR^itya ekAgram manaH kR^itvA yata-cittendriya-kriyash cittam cendriyANi ca cittendriyANi teShAm kriyAH samyatA yasya sa yata-cittendriya-kriyaH | sa kim-artham yogam yu¤jyAd ity Aha - Atma-vishuddhaye 'ntaH-karaNasya vishuddhy-artham ity etat ||BhGS_6.12||

==============================

bAhyam Asanam uktam | adhunA sharIra-dhAraNam katham ity ucyate - 

samam kAya-shiro-grIvam dhArayann acalam sthiraH |
samprekShya nAsikAgram svam dishash cAnavalokayan ||BhG_6.13||

samam kAya-shiro-grIvam kAyash ca shirash ca grIvA ca kAya-shiro-grIvam tat samam dhArayan acalam ca | samam dhArayatash calanam sambhavati | ato vishinaShTi - acalam iti | sthiraH sthiro bhUtvA ity arthaH | svam nAsikAgram samprekShya samyak prekShaNam darshanam kR^itvaiveti | iva-shabdo lupto draShTavyaH | na hi sva-nAsikAgra-samprekShaNam iha vidhitsitam | kim tarhi ? cakShuSho dR^iShTi-samnipAtaH | sa cAntaH-karaNa-samAdhAnApekSho vivakShitaH | sva-nAsikAgra-samprekShaNam eva ced vivakShitam, manas tatraiva samAdhIyeta, nAtmani | Atmani hi manasaH samAdhAnam vakShyati Atma-samstham manaH kR^itveti | tasmAd iva-shabda-lopenAkShNor dR^iShTi-samnipAta eva samprekShya ity ucyate | dishash cAnavalokayan dishAm cAvalokanam antarA kurvan ity etat ||BhGS_6.13||

==============================
 
kim ca - 

prashAntAtmA vigata-bhIr brahmacAri-vrate sthitaH |
manaH samyamya mac-citto yukta AsIta mat-paraH ||BhG_6.14||

prashAntAtmA prakarSheNa shAntaH AtmAntaH-karaNam yasya so 'yam prashAntAtmA, vigata-bhIH vigata-bhayaH, brahmacAri-vrate sthitaH | brahmacAriNo vratam brahmacaryam guru-shushrUShA-bhikShAnna-bhukty-Adi tasmin sthitaH | tad-anuShThAtA bhaved ity arthaH | kim ca, manaH samyamya manaso vR^ittIr upasamhR^itya ity etat, mac-citto mayi parameshvare cittam yasya so 'yam mac-cittaH, yuktaH samAhitaH sann AsIta upavishet | mat-paro 'ham paro yasya so 'yam mat-paro bhavati | kashcit rAgI strI-cittaH, na tu striyam eva paratvena gR^ihNAti | kim tarhi ? rAjAnam mahA-devam vA | ayam tu mac-citto mat-parash ca ||BhGS_6.14|| 

==============================
 
 athedAnIm yoga-phalam ucyate - 

yu¤jann evam sadAtmAnam yogI niyata-mAnasaH |
shAntim nirvANa-paramAm mat-samsthAm adhigacchati ||BhG_6.15||

yujan samAdhAnAm kurvann evam yathoktena vidhAnena sadAtmanAm sarvadA yogI niyata-mAnaso niyatam samyatam mAnasam mano yasya so 'yam niyata-mAnasaH, shAntim uparatim nirvANa-paramAm nirvANam mokShas tat paramA niShThA yasyAH shAnteH sA nirvANa-paramA tAm nirvANa-paramAm. mat-samsthAm mad-adhInAm adhigacchati prApnoti ||BhGS_6.15|| 

==============================

idAnIm yoginaH AhArAdi-niyama ucyate -

nAtyashnatas tu yogo 'sti na caikAntam anashnataH |
nash cAtisvapna-shIlasya jAgrato naiva cArjuna ||BhG_6.16||

nAtyashnata Atma-sammitam anna-parimANam atItyAshnato 'tyashnato na yogo 'sti | na caikAntam anashnato yogo 'sti | yad u ha vA Atma-sammitam annam tad avati tan na hinasti yad bhUyo hinasti tad yat kanIyo 'nnam na tad avati [ÁatapathaB 9.2.1.2] iti shruteH | tasmAt yogI na Atma-sammitAd annAd adhikam nyUnam vAshnIyAt | athavA, yogino yoga-shAstre paripaThitAd anna-parimANAd atimAtram ashnato yogo nAsti | uktam hi - 

ardham sa-vya¤janAnnasya tR^itIyam udakasya ca | 
vAyoH samcaraNArtham tu caturtham avasheShayet || ity Adi parimANam | 

tathA - na cAtisvapna-shIlasya yogo bhavati naiva cAtimAtram jAgrato bhavati cArjuna || 

==============================
 
katham punar yogo bhavatIty ucyate - 

yuktAhAra-vihArasya yukta-ceShTasya karmasu |
yukta-svapnAvabodhasya yogo bhavati duHkhahA ||BhG_6.17||

yuktAhAra-vihArasya Ahriyata ity AhAro 'nnam, viharaNam vihAraH pAda-kramaH, tau yuktau niyata-parimANau yasya sa yuktAhAra-vihAras tasya, tathA yukta-ceShTasya yuktA niyatA ceShTA yasya karmasu tasya | tathA yukta-svapnAvabodhasya yuktau svapnash cAvabodhash ca tau niyata-kAlau yasya tasya, yuktAhAra-vihArasya yukta-ceShTasya karmasu yukta-svapnAvabodhasya yogino yogo bhavati duHkhahA duHkhAni sarvANi hantIti duHkhahA, sarva-samsAra-duHkha-kShaya-kR^id yogo bhavatIty arthaH ||BhGS_6.17||

==============================


athAdhunA kadA yukto bhavati ? ity ucyate - 

yadA viniyatam cittam Atmany evAvatiShThate |
niHspR^ihaH sarva-kAmebhyo yukta ity ucyate tadA ||BhG_6.18||

yadA viniyatam visheSheNa niyatam samyatam ekAgratAm Apannam cittam hitvA bAhyArtha-cintAm Atmany eva kevale 'vatiShThate, svAtmani sthitim labhate ity arthaH | niHspR^ihaH sarva-kAmebhyo nirgatA dR^iShTAdR^iShTa-viShayebhyaH spR^ihA tR^iShNA yasya yoginaH sa yuktaH samAhita ity ucyate tadA tasmin kAle ||BhGS_6.18|| 

==============================

tasya yoginaH samAhitam yat cittam tasyopamocyate - 

yathA dIpo nivAta-stho neN^gate sopamA smR^itA |
yogino yata-cittasya yu¤jato yogam AtmanaH ||BhG_6.19||

yathA dIpaH pradIpo nivAta-stho nivAte vAta-varjite deshe sthito neN^gate na calati, sopamA upamIyate 'nayety upamA yogaj~naish citta-pracAra-darshibhiH smR^itA cintitA yogino yata-cittasya samyatAntaH-karaNasya yu¤jato yogam anutiShThata AtmanaH samAdhim anutiShThata ity arthaH ||BhGS_6.19|| 
==============================

evam yogAbhyAsa-balAd ekAgrIbhUtam nivAta-pradIpa-kalpam sat - 

yatroparamate cittam niruddham yoga-sevayA |
yatra caivAtmanAtmAnam pashyann Atmani tuShyati ||BhG_6.20||

yatra yasmin kAle uparamate cittam uparatim gacchati niruddham sarvato nivArita-pracAram yoga-sevayA yogAnuShThAnena, yatra caiva yasmimsh ca kAla AtmanA samAdhi-parishuddhenAntaH-karaNenAtmAnam param caitanyam jyotiH-svarUpam pashyann upalabhamAnaH sva evAtmani tuShyati tuShTim bhajate ||BhGS_6.20|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

sukham Atyantikam yat tad buddhi-grAhyam atIndriyam |
vetti yatra na caivAyam sthitash calati tattvataH ||BhG_6.21||

sukham Atyantikam atyantam eva bhavatIty Atyantikam anantam ity arthaH, yat tat buddhi-grAhyam buddhyaiva indriya-nirapekShayA gR^ihyate iti buddhi-grAhyam atIndriyam indriya-gocarAtItam aviShaya-janitam ity arthaH, vetti tad IdR^isham sukham anubhavati yatra yasmin kAle, na caivAyam vidvAn Atma-svarUpe sthitas tasmAn naiva calati tattvatas tattva-svarUpAn na pracyavata ity arthaH ||BhGS_6.21|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

yam labdhvA cAparam lAbham manyate nAdhikam tataH |
yasmin sthito na duHkhena guruNApi vicAlyate ||BhG_6.22||

yam labdhvA yam Atma-lAbham labdhvA prApyash cAparam anyal lAbham lAbhAntaram tato 'dhikam astIti na manyate na cintayati | kim ca, yasmin Atma-tattve sthito duHkhena shastra-nipAtAdi-lakShaNena guruNA mahatApi na vicAlyate ||BhGS_6.22|| 

==============================

yatroparamate ity AdyArabhya yAvadbhir visheShaNair vishiShTa AtmAvasthA-visheSho yoga uktaH - 

tam vidyAd duHkha-samyoga-viyogam yoga-samj~nitam |
sa nishcayena yoktavyo yogo 'nirviNNa-cetasA ||BhG_6.23||

tam vidyAd vijAnIyAd duHkha-samyoga-viyogam duHkhaiH samyogo duHkha-samyogaH, tena viyogo duHkha-samyoga-viyogaH, tam duHkha-samyoga-viyogam yoga ity eva samj~nitam viparIta-lakShaNena vidyAd vijAnIyAd ity arthaH | yoga-phalam upasamhR^itya punar anvArambheNa yogasya kartavyatocyate nishcayAnirvedayor yoga-sAdhanatva-vidhAnArtham | sa yathokta-phalo yogo nishcayenAdhyavasAyena yoktavyo 'nirviNNa-cetasA na nirviNNam anirviNNam | kim tat ? cetas tena nirveda-rahitena cetasA cittenety arthaH ||BhGS_6.23|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

samkalpa-prabhavAn kAmAms tyaktvA sarvAn asheShataH |
manasaivendriya-grAmam viniyamya samantataH ||BhG_6.24||

samkalpa-prabhavAn samkalpaH prabhavo yeShAm kAmAnAm te samkalpa-prabhavAH kAmAs tAn tyaktvA parityajya sarvAn asheShato nirlepena | kim ca, manasaiva viveka-yuktena indriya-grAmam indriya-samudAyam viniyamya niyamanam kR^itvA samantataH samantAt ||BhGS_6.24|| 

==============================

shanaiH shanair uparamed buddhyA dhR^iti-gR^ihItayA |
Atmasamstham manaH kR^itvA na kimcid api cintayet ||BhG_6.25||

shanaiH shanair na sahasoparamed uparatim kuryAt | kayA ? buddhyA | kim-vishiShTayA ? dhR^iti-gR^ihItayA dhR^ityA dhairyeNa gR^ihItayA dhR^iti-gR^ihItayA dhairyeNa yuktayA ity arthaH | Atma-samstham Atmani samsthitam Atmaiva sarvam na tato 'nyat kimcid astIty evam Atma-samstham manaH kR^itvA na kimcid api cintayet | eSha yogasya paramo vidhiH ||BhGS_6.25|| 

==============================

tatra evam Atma-samstham manaH kartum pravR^itto yogI - 

yato yato nishcarati mana caJNcalam asthiram |
tatas tato niyamyaitad Atmany eva vasham nayet ||BhG_6.26||

yato yato yasmAd yasmAn nimittAt shabdAder nishcarati nirgacchati svabhAva-doShAn manash caJNcalam atyartham calam, ata evAsthiram, tatas tatas tasmAt tasmAt shabdAder nimittAn niyamya tat-tan-nimittam yAthAtmya-nirUpaNena shabdAdeH nimittAn niyamya tat-tan-namittam yAthAtmya-nirUpaNena AbhAsIkR^itya vairAgya-bhAvanayA ca etat mana Atmany eva vasham nayet Atma-vashyatAm ApAdayet | evam yogAbhyAsa-balAt yogina Atmany eva prashAmyati manaH ||BhGS_6.26|| 
==============================

prashAnta-manasam hy enam yoginam sukham uttamam |
upaiti shAnta-rajasam brahma-bhUtam akalmaSham ||BhG_6.27||

prashAntamanasam prakarSheNa shAntam mano yasya saH prashAntamanAs tam prashAntamanasam hi enam yoginam sukham uttamam nitishayam upaiti upagacchati shAnta-rajasam prakShINa-mohAdi-klesha-rajasam ity arthaH, brahma-bhUtam jIvanmuktam brahmaiva sarvam ity evam nishcayavantam brahma-bhUtam akalmaSham dharmAdharmAdi-varjitam ||BhGS_6.27|| 

==============================


yu¤jann evam sadAtmAnam yogI vigata-kalmaShaH |
sukhena brahma-samsparsham atyantam sukham ashnute ||BhG_6.28||

yu¤jann evam yathoktena krameNa yogI yogAntarAya-varjitaH sadA sarvadAtmAnam vigata-kalmaSho vigata-pApaH, sukhenAnAyAsena brahma-samsparsham brahmaNA pareNa samsparsho yasya tat brahma-samsparrsham sukham atyantam antam atItya vartata ity atyantam utkR^iShTam niratishayam ashnute vyApnoti ||BhGS_6.28|| 

==============================

idAnIm yogasya yat phalam brahmaikatva-darshanam sarva-samsAra-viccheda-kAraNam tat pradarshayate -

sarva-bhUta-stham AtmAnam sarva-bhUtAni cAtmani |
IkShate yoga-yuktAtmA sarvatra sama-darshanaH ||BhG_6.29||

sarva-bhUta-stham sarveShu bhUteShu sthitam svam AtmAnam sarva-bhUtAni ca Atmani brahmAdIni stamba-paryantAni ca sarva-bhUtAni Atmany ekatAm gatAni IkShate pashyati yoga-yuktAtmA samAhitAntaH-karaNaH sarvatra sama-darshanaH sarveShu brahmAdi-sthAvarAnteShu viShameShu sarva-bhUteShu samam nirvisheSham brahmAtmaikatva-viShayam darshanam j~nAnam yasya sa sarvatra sama-darshanaH ||BhGS_6.29|| 

==============================

etasyAtmaikatva-darshanasya phalam ucyate - 

yo mAm pashyati sarvatra sarvam ca mayi pashyati |
tasyAham na praNashyAmi sa ca me na praNashyati ||BhG_6.30||

yo mAm pashyati vAsudevam sarvasyAtmAnam sarvatra sarveShu bhUteShu sarvam ca brahmAdi-bhUta-jAtam mayi sarvAtmani pashyati, tasya evam Atmaikatva-darshino 'ham Ishvaro na praNashyAmi na parokShatAm gamiShyAmi | sa ca me na praNashyati sa ca vidvAn me mama vAsudevasya na praNashyati na parokSho bhavati, tasya ca mama caikAtmakatvAt | svAtmA hi nAmAtmanaH priya eva bhavati | yasmAc cAham eva sarvAtmaikatva-darshI ||BhGS_6.30|| 

==============================

ity etat pUrva-lokArtham samyag darshanam anUdya tat-phalam mokSho 'bhidhIyate -

sarva-bhUta-sthitam yo mAm bhajaty ekatvam AsthitaH |
sarvathA vartamAno 'pi sa yogI mayi vartate ||BhG_6.31||

sarvathA sarva-prakAraiH vartamAno 'pi samyag-darshI yogI mayi vaiShNave parame pade vartate, nityam ukta eva saH, na mokSham prati kenacit pratibadhyate ity arthaH ||BhGS_6.31||

==============================

kim cAnyat - 

Atmaupamyena sarvatra samam pashyati yo 'rjuna |
sukham vA yadi vA duHkham sa yogI paramo mataH ||BhG_6.32||

Atmaupamyena AtmA svayam evopamIyate 'nayety upamA | tasyA upamAyA bhAva aupamyam tenAtmaupamyena, sarvatra sarva-bhUteShu samam tulyam pashyati yo 'rjuna, sa ca kim samam pashyatIty ucyate - yathA mama sukham iShTam tathA sarva-prANinAm sukham anukUlam | vA-shabdash cArthe | yadi vA yac ca duHkham mama pratikUlam aniShTam yathA tathA sarva-prANinAm duHkham aniShTam pratikUlam ity evam Atmaupamyena sukha-duHkhe 'nukUla-pratikUle tulyatayA sarva-bhUteShu samam pashyati, na kasyacit pratikUlam Acarati, ahimsaka ity arthaH | yaH evam ahimsakaH samyag darshana-niShThaH, sa yogI parama utkR^iShTo mato 'bhipretaH sarva-yoginAm madhye ||BhGS_6.32|| 

==============================

etasya yathoktasya samyag-darshana-lakShaNasya yogasya duHkha-sampAdyatAm AlakShya shushruShur dhruvam tat-prApty-upAyam arjuna uvAca - 

yo 'yam yogas tvayA proktaH sAmyena madhusUdana |
etasyAham na pashyAmi caJNcalatvAt sthitim sthirAm ||BhG_6.33||

yo 'yam yogas tvayA proktaH sAmyena samatvena he madhusUdana etasya yogasyAham na pashyAmi nopalabhe, caJNcalatvAn manasaH | kim ? sthirAm acalAm sthitim ||BhGS_6.33|| 

==============================

asiddham tat - 

caJNcalam hi manaH kR^iShNa pramAthi balavad dR^iDham |
tasyAham nigraham manye vAyor iva suduShkaram ||BhG_6.34||

caJNcalam hi manaH | kR^iShNeti kR^iShater vilekhanArthasya rUpam | bhakta-jana-pApAdi-doShAkarShANAt kR^iShNaH, tasya sambuddhiH he kR^iShNa | hi yasmAt manash caJNcalam na kevalam atyartham caJNcalam, pramAthi ca pramathana-shIlam, pramathnAti sharIram indriyANi ca vikShipat sat para-vashIkaroti | kim ca - balavat prabalam, na kenacit niyantum shakyam, durnivAratvAt | kim ca - dR^iDham tantu-nAga-vad acchedyam | tasya evambhUtasya manaso 'ham nigraham nirodham manye vAyor iva yathA vAyor duShkaro nigrahas tato 'pi duShkaram manye ity abhiprAyaH ||BhGS_6.34|| 

==============================

shrI-bhagavAn uvAca, evam etad yathA bravIShi - 

asamshayam mahAbAho mano durNigraham calam |
abhyAsena tu kaunteya vairAgyeNash ca gR^ihyate ||BhG_6.35||

asamshayam nAsti samshayo mano durnigraham calam ity atra he mahAbAho | kimtv abhyAsena tv abhyAso nAmash citta-bhUmau kasyAmcit samAna-pratyayAvR^ittish cittasya | vairAgyeNa vairAgyam nAma dR^iShTAdR^iShTeShTa-bhogeShu doSha-darshanAbhyAsAd vaitR^iShNyam | tena ca vairAgyeNa gR^ihyate vikShepa-rUpaH pracArash cittasya | evam tan mano gR^ihyate nigR^ihyate nirudhyata ity arthaH ||BhGS_6.35|| 

==============================

yaH punar asamyatAtmA, tena - 

asamyatAtmanA yogo duShprApeti me matiH |
vashyAtmanA tu yatatA shakyo 'vAptum upAyataH ||BhG_6.36||

asamyatAtmanAbhyAsa-vairAgyAbhyAm asamyataH AtmAntaH-karaNam yasya so 'yam asamyatAtmA tenAsamyatAtmanA yogo duShprApo duHkhena prApyateti me matiH | yas tu punar vashyAtmAbhyAsa-vairAgyAbhyAm vashyatvam ApAditaH AtmA mano yasya so 'yam vashyAtmA tena vashyAtmanA tu yatatA bhUyo 'pi prayatnam kurvatA shakyo 'vAptum yogar upAyato yathoktAd upAyAt ||BhGS_6.36|| 

==============================

tatra yogAbhyAsAN^gIkaraNena ihaloka-paraloka-prApti-nimittAni karmANi samnyastAni, yoga-siddhi-phalam ca mokSha-sAdhanam samyag darshanam na prAptam iti, yogI yoga-mArgAt maraNa-kAle calita-citta iti tasya nAsham AshaN^kayArjuna uvAca - 

ayatiH shraddhayopeto yogAc calita-mAnasaH |
aprApya yoga-samsiddhim kAm gatim kR^iShNa gacchati ||BhG_6.37||

ayatir aprayatnavAn yoga-mArge shraddhayAstikya-buddhyA copeto yogAd anta-kAle ca calitam mAnasam mano yasya sa calita-mAnaso bhraShTa-smR^itiH so 'prApya yoga-samsiddhim yoga-phalam samyag-darshanam kAm gatim he kR^iShNa gacchati ||BhGS_6.37|| 

==============================

kaccin nobhaya-vibhraShTash chinnAbhram iva nashyati |
apratiShTho mahAbAho vimUDho brahmaNaH pathi ||BhG_6.38||

kashcit kim na ubhaya-vibhraShTaH karma-mArgAt yoga-mArgAc ca vibhraShTaH san chinnAbhram iva nashyati, kim vA na nashyaty apratiShTho nirAshrayo he mahAbAho vimUDhaH san brahmaNaH pathi brahma-prApti-mArge ||BhGS_6.38|| 

==============================

etan me samshayam kR^iShNash chettum arhasy asheShataH |
tvad-anyaH samshayasyAsya chettA na hy upapadyate ||BhG_6.39||

etan me mama samshayam kR^iShNash chettum apanetum arhasy asheShataH | tvad-anyas tvatto 'nyaH R^iShir devo vA cchettA nAshayitA samshayasyAsya na hi yasmAd upapadyate na sambhavati | atas tvam eva cchettum arhasIty arthaH ||BhGS_6.39|| 

==============================

shrI-bhagavAn uvAca - 

pArtha naiveha nAmutra vinAshas tasya vidyate |
na hi kalyANa-kR^it kashcid durgatim tAta gacchati ||BhG_6.40||

he pArtha naiva iha loke nAmutra parasmin vA loke vinAshas tasya vidyate nAsti | nAsho nAma pUrvasmAt hInajanmaprAptiH sa yogabhraShTasya nAsti | na hi yasmAt kalyANakR^it shubhakR^it kashcit durgatim kutsitAm gatim he tAta, tanoti AtmAnam putrarUpeNeti pitA tAta ucyate | pitaiva putreti putro 'pi tAta ucyate | shiShyo 'pi putra ucyate | yato na gacchati ||BhGS_6.40|| 

==============================

kim tv asya bhavati ? - 

prApya puNya-kR^itAm lokAn uShitvA shAshvatIH samAH |
shucInAm shrImatAm gehe yoga-bhraShTo 'bhijAyate ||BhG_6.41||

yoga-mArge pravR^ittaH samnyAsI sAmarthyAt prApya gatvA puNya-kR^itAm ashvamedhAdi-yAjinAm lokAn, tatra coShitvA vAsam anubhUya shAshvatIr nityAH samAH samvatsarAn, tad-bhoga-kShaye shucInAm yathokta-kAriNAm shrImatAm vibhUti-matAm gehe gR^ihe yoga-bhraShTaH abhijAyate ||BhGS_6.41|| 

==============================

atha vA yoginAm eva kule bhavati dhImatAm |
etad dhi durlabhataram loke janma yad IdR^isham ||BhG_6.42||

athavA shrImatAm kulAt anyasmin yoginAm eva daridrANAm kule bhavati jAyate dhImatAm buddhimatAm | etat hi janma, yat daridrANAm yoginAm kule, durlabhataram duHkha-labhyataram pUrvam apekShya loke janma yad IdR^isham yathokta-visheShaNe kule ||BhGS_6.42|| 

==============================

yasmAt - 

tatra tam buddhi-samyogam labhate paurvadehikam |
yatate ca tato bhUyaH samsiddhau kurunandana ||BhG_6.43||

tatra yoginAm kule tam buddhi-samyogam buddhyA samyogam buddhi-samyogam labhate paurvadehikam pUrvasmin dehe bhavam paurvadehikam | yatate ca prayatnam ca karoti tatas tasmAt pUrva-kR^itAt samskArAt bhUyo bahutaram samsiddhau samsiddhi-nimittam he kuru-nandana ||BhGS_6.43|| 

==============================

katham pUrva-deha-buddhi-samyogeti tad ucyate - 

pUrvAbhyAsena tenaiva hriyate hy avasho 'pi saH |
jij~nAsur api yogasya shabda-brahmAtivartate ||BhG_6.44||

yaH pUrva-janmani kR^ito 'bhyAsaH sa pUrvAbhyAsaH, tenaiva balavatA hriyate samsiddhau hi yasmAd avasho 'pi sa yoga-bhraShTaH | na kR^itam ced yogAbhyAsajAt samskArAt balavattaram adharmAdi-lakShaNam karma, tadA yogAbhyAsa-janitena samskAreNa hriyate | adharmash cet balavattaraH kR^itaH, tena yogajo 'pi samskAro 'bhibhUyata eva, tat-kShaye tu yogajaH samskAraH svayam eva kAryam Arabhate, na dIrgha-kAlasthasyApi vinAshas tasyAstIty arthaH | ato jij~nAsur api yogasya svarUpam j~nAtum icchann api yoga-mArge pravR^ittaH samnyAsI yoga-bhraShTaH, sAmarthyAt so 'pi shabda-brahma vedokta-karmAnuShThAna-phalam ativartate 'tikrAmaty apAkariShyati | kim uta buddhvA yo yogam tan-niShTho 'bhyAsam kuryAt ||BhGS_6.44|| 

==============================

kutash ca yogitvam shreya iti - 

prayatnAd yatamAnas tu yogI samshuddha-kilbiShaH |
aneka-janma-samsiddhas tato yAti parAm gatim ||BhG_6.45||

prayatnAd yatamAnaH, adhikam yatamAna ity arthaH | tatra yogI vidvAn samshuddha-kilbiSho vishuddha-kilbiShaH samshuddha-pApo 'neka-janma-samsiddhir anekeShu janmasu kimcit kimcit samskAra-jAtam upacitya tena upacitenAneka-janma-kR^itena samsiddho 'neka-janma-samsiddhas tataH labdha-samyag-darshanaH san yAti parAm prakR^iShTam gatim ||BhGS_6.45|| 

==============================

yasmAd evam tasmAt - 

tapasvibhyo 'dhiko yogI j~nAnibhyo 'pi mato 'dhikaH |
karmibhyash cAdhiko yogI tasmAd yogI bhavArjuna ||BhG_6.46||

tapasvibhyo 'dhiko yogI, j~nAnibhyo 'pi j~nAnam atra shAstrArtha-pANDityam, tadvadbhyo 'pi mato j~nAto 'dhikaH shreShTha iti | karmibhyaH, agnihotrAdi karma, tadvadbhyo 'dhiko yogI vishiShTo yasmAt tasmAd yogI bhavArjuna ||BhGS_6.46|| 

==============================

yoginAm api sarveShAm mad-gatenAntarAtmanA |
shraddhAvAn bhajate yo mAm sa me yuktatamo mataH ||BhG_6.47||

yoginAm api sarveShAm rUdrAdityAdi-dhyAna-parANAm madhye mad-gatena mayi vAsudeve samAhitenAntarAtmanAntaH-karaNena shraddhAvAn shraddadhAnaH san bhajate sevate yo mAm, sa me mama yuktatamo 'tishayena yukto mato 'bhipreta iti || 

iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrI-govinda-bhagavat-pUjya-pAda- 
shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^ita shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye 
ShaShTo 'dhyAyaH ||6||


__________________________________________________________

BhG 7

atha j~nAna-vij~nAna-yogAkhyaH saptamo 'dhyAyaH

(shaN^kara-bhAShyaH)
 
yoginAm api sarveShAm mad-gatenAntarAtmanA | 
shraddhAvAnbhajate yo mAm sa me yuktatamo mataH [GItA 6.47] 

iti prashna-bIjam upanyasya, svayam eva IdR^isham madIyam tattvam, evam mad-gatAntar-AtmA syAd ity etat vivakShuH shrI-bhagavAn uvAca - 

mayy AsaktamanAH pArtha yogam yu¤jan madAshrayaH |
asamshayam samagram mAm yathA j~nAsyasi tac chR^iNu ||BhG_7.1||

mayi vakShyamANa-visheShaNe parameshvare Asaktam mano yasya saH mayy Asakta-manAH, he pArtha ! yogam yu¤jan manaH-samAdhAnam kurvan, mad-Ashrayo 'ham eva parameshvaraH Ashrayo yasya saH mad-AshrayaH | yo hi kashcit puruShArthena kenacit arthI bhavati sa tat-sAdhanam karmAgnihotrAdi tapo dAnam vA kimcid Ashrayam pratipadyate, ayam tu yogI mAm evAshrayam pratipadyate, hitvAnyat sAdhanAntaram mayy eva Asakta-manA bhavati | yas tvam evam-bhUtaH san asamshayam samagram samastam vibhUti-bala-shakty-aishvaryAdi-guNa-sampannam mAm yathA yena prakAreNa j~nAsyasi samshayam antareNaivam eva bhagavAn iti, tat sR^iNu ucyamAnam mayA ||BhGS_7.1|| 

==============================
 
tac ca mad-viShayam - 

j~nAnam te 'ham sa-vij~nAnam idam vakShyAmy asheShataH |
yaj j~nAtvA neha bhUyo 'nyaj j~nAtavyam avashiShyate ||BhG_7.2||

j~nAnam te tubhyam aham sa-vij~nAnam vij~nAna-sahitam svAnubhava-yuktam idam vakShyAmi kathayiShyAmy asheShataH kArtsnyena | taj j~nAnam vivakShitam stauti shrotuH abhimukhIkaraNAya - yaj j~nAtvA yaj j~nAnam j~nAtvA neha bhUyaH punar anyat j~nAtavyam puruShArtha-sAdhanam avashiShyate nAvashiShTam bhavati | iti mat-tattva-j~no yaH, sa sarvaj~no bhavatIty arthaH | ato vishiShTa-phalatvAt durlabham j~nAnam ||BhGS_7.2|| 

==============================
 
katham ity ucyate - 

manuShyANAm sahasreShu kash cid yatati siddhaye |
yatatAm api siddhAnAm kash cin mAm vetti tattvataH ||BhG_7.3||

manuShyANAm madhye sahasreShu anekeShu kashcit yatati prayatnam karoti siddhaye siddhy-artham | teShAm yatatAm api siddhAnAm, siddhA eva hi te ye mokShAya yatante, teShAm kashcid eva hi mAm vetti tattvato yathAvat ||BhGS_7.3|| 

==============================
 
shrotAram prarocanenAbhimukhIkR^ityAha -

bhUmir Apo 'nalo vAyuH kham mano buddhir eva ca |
ahamkAra itIyam me bhinnA prakR^itir aShTadhA ||BhG_7.4||

bhUmiH pR^ithivI-tanmAtram ucyate, na sthUlA | bhinnA prakR^itir aShTadhA iti vacanAt | tathAb-Adayo 'pi tanmAtrANy eva ucyante - Apo 'nalo vAyuH kham | mana iti manasaH kAraNam ahamkAro gR^ihyate | buddhir ity ahamkAra-kAraNam mahat-tattvam | ahamkAra ity avidyA-samyuktam avyaktam | yathA viSha-samyuktam annam viSham ity ucyate, evam ahamkAra-vAsanAvad avyaktam mUla-kAraNam ahamkAra ity ucyate, pravartakatvAt ahamkArasya | ahamkAra eva hi sarvasya pravR^itti-bIjam dR^iShTam loke | itIyam yathoktA prakR^itir me mamaishvarI mAyA-shaktir aShTadhA bhinnA bhedam AgatA ||BhGS_7.4|| 

==============================
 
apareyam itas tv anyAm prakR^itim viddhi me parAm |
jIva-bhUtAm mahAbAho yayedam dhAryate jagat ||BhG_7.5||

aparA na parA nikR^iShTAshuddhAnartha-karI samsAra-bandhanAtmikeyam | ito 'syAH yathoktAyAs tv anyAm vishuddhAm prakR^itim mamAtma-bhUtAm viddhi me parAm prakR^iShTam jIva-bhUtAm kShetraj~na-lakShaNAm prANa-dhAraNa-nimitta-bhUtAm he mahAbAho, yayA prakR^ityedam dhAryate jagad antaH-praviShTayA ||BhGS_7.5|| 

==============================
 
etad-yonIni bhUtAni sarvANIty upadhAraya |
aham kR^itsnasya jagataH prabhavaH pralayas tathA ||BhG_7.6||

etad-yonIni ete parApare kShetra-kShetraj~na-lakShaNe prakR^itI yonir yeShAm bhUtAnAm tAni etad-yonIni, bhUtAni sarvANIti evam upadhAraya jAnIhi | yasmAt mama prakR^iti yoniH kAraNam sarva-bhUtAnAm, ato 'ham kR^itsnasya samastasya jagataH prabhava utpattiH pralayo vinAshas tathA | prakR^iti-dvaya-dvAreNAham sarvaj~na Ishvaro jagataH kAraNam ity arthaH ||BhGS_7.6||

==============================
 
yatas tasmAt -

mattaH parataram nAnyat kimcid asti dhanamjaya |
mayi sarvam idam protam sUtre maNigaNA iva ||BhG_7.7||

mattaH parameshvarAt parataram anyat kAraNAntaram kimcit nAsti na vidyate, aham eva jagat-kAraNam ity arthaH, he dhanamjaya | yasmAd evam tasmAt mayi parameshvare sarvANi bhUtAni sarvam idam jagat protam anusyUtam anugatam anuviddham grathitam ity arthaH | dIrgha-tantuShu paTavat, sUtre ca maNi-gaNA iva ||BhGS_7.7|| 

==============================
 
kena kena dharmeNa vishiShTo tvayi sarvam idam protam ity ucyate - 

raso 'ham apsu kaunteya prabhAsmi shashi-sUryayoH |
praNavaH sarva-vedeShu shabdaH khe pauruSham nR^iShu ||BhG_7.8||

raso 'ham, apAm yaH sAram sa rasaH, tasmin rasa-bhUte mayi ApaH protA ity arthaH | evam sarvatra | yathAham apsu rasaH, evam prabhAsmi shashi-sUryayoH | praNava omkAraH sarva-vedeShu, tasmin praNava-bhUte mayi sarve vedAH protAH | tathA khe AkAshe shabdaH sAra-bhUtaH, tasmin mayi kham protam | tathA pauruSham puruShasya bhAvaH pauruSham yataH pum-buddhir nR^iShu, tasmin mayi puruShAH protAH ||BhGS_7.8|| 

==============================

gandhaH pR^ithivyAm ca tejash cAsmi vibhAvasau |
jIvanam sarva-bhUteShu tapash cAsmi tapasviShu ||BhG_7.9||

puNyaH surabhir gandhaH pR^ithivyAm cAham | tasmin mayi gandha-bhUte pR^ithivI protA | puNyatvam gandhasya svabhAvata eva pR^ithivyAm darshitam ab-AdiShu rasAdeH puNyatvopalakShaNArtham | apuNyatvam tu gandhAdInAm avidyA-dharmAdy-apekSham samsAriNAm bhUta-visheSha-samsarga-nimittam bhavati | tejash ca dIptish cAsmi vibhAvasau agnau | tathA jIvanam sarva-bhUteShu, yena jIvanti sarvANi bhUtAni tat jIvanam | tapash cAsmi tapasviShu, tasmin tapasi mayi tapasvinaH protAH ||BhGS_7.9|| 

==============================

bIjam mAm sarva-bhUtAnAm viddhi pArtha sanAtanam |
buddhir buddhimatAm asmi tejas tejasvinAm aham ||BhG_7.10||

bIjam praroha-kAraNam mAm viddhi sarva-bhUtAnAm he pArtha sanAtanam cirantanam | kim ca, buddhir viveka-shaktir antaH-karaNasya buddhimatAm viveka-shaktimatAm asmi | tejaH prAgalbhyam tadvatAm tejasvinAm aham ||BhGS_7.10|| 

==============================

balam balavatAm cAham kAma-rAga-vivarjitam |
dharmAviruddho bhUteShu kAmo 'smi bharatarShabha ||BhG_7.11||

balam sAmarthyam ojo balavatAm aham | tac ca balam kAma-rAga-vivarjitam | kAmash ca rAgash ca kAma-rAgau | kAmas tR^iShNA-samnikR^iShTeShu viShayeShu, rAgo ra¤janA prApteShu viShayeShu - tAbhyAm kAma-rAgAbhyAm vivarjitam dehAdi-dhAraNa-mAtrArtham balam sattvam aham asmi | na tu yat samsAriNAm tR^iShNA-rAga-kAraNam | kim ca - dharmAviruddhaH | dharmeNa shAstrArthenAviruddho yaH prANiShu bhUteShu kAmaH, yathA deha-dhAraNa-mAtrAdy-artho 'shana-pAnAdi-viShayaH, sa kAmo 'smi | he bharatarShabha ||BhGS_7.11|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

ye caiva sAttvikA bhAvA rAjasAs tAmasAsh ca ye |
matta eveti tAn viddhi na tv aham teShu te mayi ||BhG_7.12||

ye caiva sAttvikAH sattva-nirvR^ittA bhAvAH padArthAH, rAjasAH rajo-nirvR^ittAs tAmasAs tamo-nirvR^ittAsh ca, ye kecit prANinAm sva-karma-vashAt jAyante bhAvAH, tAn matta eva jAyamAnAn iti evam viddhi sarvAn samastAn eva | evam yady api te matto jAyante, tathApi na tv aham teShu tad-adhInas tad-vashaH, yathA samsAriNaH | te punar mayi mad-vashAH mad-adhInAH ||BhGS_7.12|| 

==============================

evam-bhUtam api parameshvaram nitya-shuddha-buddha-mukta-svabhAvam sarva-bhUtAtmAnam nirguNam samsAra-doSha-bIja-pradAha-kAraNam mAm nAbhijAnAti jagad ity anukrosham darshayati bhagavAn | tac ca kim-nimittam jagato 'j~nAnam ? ity ucyate - 

tribhir guNa-mayair bhAvair ebhiH sarvam idam jagat |
mohitam nAbhijAnAti mAm ebhyaH param avyayam ||BhG_7.13||

tribhir guNa-mayaiH guNa-vikAraiH rAga-dveSha-mohAdi-prakArair bhAvaiH padArthair ebhir yathoktaiH sarvam idam prANi-jAtam jagan mohitam avivekitAm ApAditam san nAbhijAnAni mAm | ebhyo yathoktebhyo guNebhyaH param vyatiriktam vilakShaNam cAvyayam vyaya-rahitam janmAdi-sarva-bhAva-vikAra-varjitam ity arthaH ||BhGS_7.13|| 

==============================

katham punar daivIm etAm triguNAtmikAm vaiShNavIm mAyAm atikrAmatIty ucyate - 

daivI hy eShA guNa-mayI mama mAyA duratyayA |
mAm eva ye prapadyante mAyAm etAm taranti te ||BhG_7.14||

daivI devasya mameshvarasya viShNoH svabhAva-bhUtA hi yasmAd eShA yathoktA guNa-mayI mama mAyA duratyayA duHkhenAtyayo 'tikramaNam yasyAH sA duratyayA | tatraivam sati sarva-dharmAn parityajya mAm eva mAyAvinam svAtma-bhUtam sarvAtmanA ye prapadyante te 
mAyAm etAm sarva-bhUta-mohinIm taranty atikrAmanti | te samsAra-bandhanAn mucyanta ity arthaH ||BhGS_7.14|| 

==============================

yadi tvAm prapannAH mAyAm etAm taranti, kasmAt tvAm eva sarve na prapadyante ? ity ucyate - 

na mAm duShkR^itino mUDhAH prapadyante narAdhamAH |
mAyayApahR^ita-j~nAnA Asuram bhAvam AshritAH ||BhG_7.15||

na mAm parameshvaram nArAyaNam duShkR^itinaH pApa-kAriNaH mUDhAH prapadyante narAdhamA narANAm madhye 'dhamAH nikR^iShTaH | te ca mAyayApahR^ita-j~nAnAH sammuShita-j~nAnA Asuram bhAvam himsAnR^itAdi-lakShaNam AshritAH ||BhGS_7.15||

==============================

ye punar narottamAH puNya-karmANaH - 

catur-vidhA bhajante mAm janAH sukR^itino 'rjuna |
Arto jij~nAsur arthArthI j~nAnI ca bharatarShabha ||BhG_7.16||

catur-vidhAsh catuH-prakArA bhajante sevante mAm janAH sukR^itinaH puNya-karmANo he 'rjuna | Arta Arti-parigR^ihItas taskara-vyAghra-rogAdinAbhibhUta ApannaH | jij~nAsur bhagavat-tattvam j~nAtum icchati yaH | arthArthI dhana-kAmaH | j~nAnI viShNos tattva-vic ca he bharatarShabha ||BhGS_7.16|| 

==============================

teShAm j~nAnI nitya-yukta eka-bhaktir vishiShyate |
priyo hi j~nAnino 'tyartham aham sa ca mama priyaH ||BhG_7.17||

teShAm caturNAm madhye j~nAnI tattva-vit tattva-vittvAn nitya-yukto bhavati | eka-bhaktish ca, anyasya bhajanIyasyAdarshanAt | ataH sa eka-bhaktir vishiShyate visheSham Adhikyam Apadyate, atiricyata ity arthaH | priyo hi yasmAd aham AtmA j~nAnino 'tas tasyAham atyartham priyaH | prasiddham hi loke AtmA priyo bhavatIti | tasmAj j~nAnina AtmatvAd vAsudevaH priyo bhavatIty arthaH | sa ca j~nAnI mama vAsudevasya Atmaiveti mamAtyartham priyaH ||BhGS_7.17|| 

==============================

na tarhy ArtAdayas trayo vAsudevasya priyAH ? na | kim tarhi ? - 

udArAH sarva evaite j~nAnI tv Atmaiva me matam |
AsthitaH sa hi yuktAtmA mAm evAnuttamAm gatim ||BhG_7.18||

udArA utkR^iShTAH sarva evaite | trayo 'pi mama priyA evety arthaH | na hi kashcin mad-bhakto vAsudevasyApriyo bhavati | j~nAnI tv atyartham priyo bhavatIti visheShaH | tat kasmAt ? ity ata Aha - j~nAnI tv Atmaiva, nAnyo matta iti me mama matam nishcayaH | Asthita AroDhum pravR^ittaH sa j~nAnI hi yasmAd aham eva bhagavAn vAsudevo nAnyo 'smIty evam yuktAtmA samAhita-cittaH san mAm eva param brahma gantavyam anuttamAm gatim gantum pravR^itta ity arthaH ||BhGS_7.18|| 

==============================

j~nAnI punar api stUyate - 

bahUnAm janmanAm ante j~nAnavAn mAm prapadyate |
vAsudevaH sarvam iti sa mahAtmA sudurlabhaH ||BhG_7.19||

bahUnAm janmanAm j~nAnArtha-samskArAshrayANAm ante samAptau j~nAnavAn prApta-paripAka-j~nAno mAm vAsudevam pratyag-AtmAnam pratyakShataH prapadyate | katham ? vAsudevaH sarvam iti | ya evam sarvAtmAnam mAm nArAyaNam pratipadyate, sa mahAtmA | na tat-samo 'nyo 'sti, adhiko vA | ataH sudurlabhaH, manuShyANAm sahasreShv iti hy uktam ||BhGS_7.19||

==============================


Atmaiva sarvm vAsudeva ity evam apratipattau kAraNam ucyate - 

kAmais tais tair hR^ita-j~nAnAH prapadyante 'nya-devatAH |
tam tam niyamam AsthAya prakR^ityA niyatAH svayA ||BhG_7.20||

kAmais tais taiH putra-pashu-svargAdi-viShayair hR^ita-j~nAnAH apahR^ita-viveka-vij~nAnAH prapadyante 'nya-devatAH prApnuvanti vAsudevAd Atmano 'nyA devatAH | tam tam niyamam devatArAdhane prasiddho yo yo niyamas tam tam AsthAya Ashritya prakR^ityA svabhAvena janmAntarArjita-samskAra-visheSheNa niyatAH niyamitAH svayAtmIyayA ||BhGS_7.20|| 

==============================

teShAm ca kAminAm - 

yo yo yAm yAm tanum bhaktaH shraddhayArcitum icchati |
tasya tasyAcalAm shraddhAm tAm eva vidadhAmy aham ||BhG_7.21||

yo yaH kAmI yAm yAm devatA-tanum shraddhayA samyukto bhaktash ca sann arcitum pUjayitum icchati, tasya tasya kAmino 'calAm sthirAm shraddhAm tAm eva vidadhAmi sthirIkaromi ||BhGS_7.21|| 

==============================

yayaiva pUrvam pravR^ittaH svabhAvato yo yAm devatA-tanum shraddhayArcitum icchati - 

sa tayA shraddhayA yuktas tasyA rAdhanam Ihate |
labhate ca tataH kAmAn mayaiva vihitAn hi tAn ||BhG_7.22||

sa tayA mad-vihitayA shraddhayA yuktaH san tasyA devatA-tanvA rAdhanam ArAdhanam Ihate ceShTate | labhate ca tatas tasyA ArAdhitAyA devatA-tanvAH kAmAn IpsitAn mayaiva parameshvareNa sarvaj~nena karma-phala-vibhAga-j~natayA vihitAn nirmitAn tAn, hi yasmAt te bhagavatA vihitAH kAmAs tasmAt tAn avashyam labhate ity arthaH | hitAn iti pada-cchede hitatvam kAmAnAm upacaritam kalpyam | na hi kAmA hitAH kasyacit ||BhGS_7.22||

==============================

yasmAd antavat sAdhana-vyApArAvivekinaH kAminash ca te | ataH - 

antavat tu phalam teShAm tad bhavaty alpa-medhasAm |
devAn deva-yajo yAnti mad-bhaktA yAnti mAm api ||BhG_7.23||

antavad vinAshi tu phalam teShAm tad bhavaty alpa-medhasAm alpa-praj~nAnAm | devAn deva-yajo yAnti devAn yajantIti deva-yajaH, te devAn yAnti | mad-bhaktA yAnti mAm api | evam samAne 'py AyAse mAm eva na prapadyante 'nanta-phalAya | aho khalu kaShTam vartata ity anukrosham darshayati bhagavAn ||BhGS_7.23||

==============================

kim-nimittam mAm eva na prapadyanta ity ucyate - 

avyaktam vyaktim Apannam manyante mAm abuddhayaH |
param bhAvam ajAnanto mamAvyayam anuttamam ||BhG_7.24||

avyaktam aprakAsham vyaktim Apannam prakAsham gatam idAnIm manyante mAm nitya-prasiddham Ishvaram api santam abuddhayo 'vivekinaH param bhAvam param Atma-svarUpam ajAnanto 'vivekinaH mamAvyayam vyaya-rahitam anuttamam niratishayam madIyam bhAvam ajAnanto manyanta ity arthaH ||BhGS_7.24|| 

==============================

tad-aj~nAnam kim-nimittam ity ucyate - 

nAham prakAshaH sarvasya yoga-mAyA-samAvR^itaH |
mUDho 'yam nAbhijAnAti loko mAm ajam avyayam ||BhG_7.25||

nAham prakAshaH sarvasya lokasya, keShAmcid eva mad-bhaktAnAm prakAsho 'ham ity abhiprAyaH | yoga-mAyA-samAvR^ito yogo guNAnAm yuktir ghaTanam saiva mAyA yoga-mAyA | tayA yogamAyayA samAvR^itaH, samchanna ity arthaH | ata eva mUDho loko 'yam nAbhijAnAti mAm ajam avyayam ||BhGS_7.25||

==============================

vedAham samatItAni vartamAnAni cArjuna |
bhaviShyANi ca bhUtAni mAm tu veda na kashcana ||BhG_7.26||

yayA yogamAyayA samAvR^itam mAm loko nAbhijAnAti, nAsau yogamAyA madIyA satI mameshvarasya mAyAvino j~nAnam pratibadhnAti | yathAnyasyApi mAyAvino mAyA j~nAnam tadvat | yataH evam, ataH -- aham tu veda jAne samatItAni samatikrAntAni bhUtAni, vartamAnAni cArjuna, bhaviShyANi ca bhUtAni vedAham | mAm tu veda na kashcana mad-bhaktam mac-charaNam ekam muktvA | mat-tattva-vedanAbhAvAd eva na mAm bhajate ||BhGS_7.26|| 

==============================

kena punar mat-tattva-vedana-pratibandhena pratibaddhAni santi jAyamAnAni sarva-bhUtAni mAm na vidanti ? ity apekShAyAm idam Aha - 

icchA-dveSha-samutthena dvandva-mohena bhArata |
sarva-bhUtAni sammoham sarge yAnti parantapa ||BhG_7.27||

icchA-dveSha-samutthena icchA ca dveShash cecchA-dveShau | tAbhyAm samuttiShThatItIcchA-dveSha-samutthas tenecchA-dveSha-samutthena | keneti visheShApekShAyAm idam Aha - dvandva-mohena dvandva-nimitto moho dvandva-mohas tena | tAv eva icchA-dveShau shItoShNavat paraspara-viruddhau sukha-duHkha-tad-dhetu-viShayau yathA-kAlam sarva-bhUtaiH sambadhyamAnau dvandva-shabdenAbhidhIyete | tatra yadecchA-dveShau sukha-duHkha-tad-dhetu-samprAptyA labdhAtmakau bhavataH, tadA tau sarva-bhUtAnAm praj~nAyAH sva-vashApAdana-dvAreNa paramArthAtma-tattva-viShaya-j~nAnotpatti-pratibandha-kAraNam moham janayataH | na hIcchA-dveSha-doSha-vashIkR^ita-cittasya yathA-bhUtArtha-viShaya-j~nAnam utpadyate bahir api | kim u vaktavyam tAbhyAm AviShTa-buddheH sammUDhasya pratyag-Atmani bahu-pratibandhe j~nAnam notpadyateti | atas tena icchA-dveSha-samutthena dvandva-mohena, bhArata bharatAnvayaja, sarva-bhUtAni sammohitAni santi sammoham sammUDhatAm sarge janmani, utpatti-kAle ity etat, yAnti gacchanti he paramtapa | moha-vashAny eva sarva-bhUtAni jAyamAnAni jAyanta ity abhiprAyaH | yata evam atas tena dvandva-mohena pratibaddha-praj~nAnAni sarva-bhUtAni sammohitAni mAm Atma-bhUtam na jAnanti | ata eva Atma-bhAvena mAm na bhajante ||BhGS_7.27||

==============================

ke punar anena dvandva-mohena nirmuktAH santas tvAm viditvA yathA-shAstram Atma-bhAve bhajanta ity apekShitam artham darshayitum ucyate - 

yeShAm tv anta-gatam pApam janAnAm puNya-karmaNAm |
te dvandva-moha-nirmuktA bhajante mAm dR^iDha-vratAH ||BhG_7.28||

yeShAm tu punar anta-gatam samApta-prAyam kShINam pApam janAnAm puNya-karmaNAm puNyam karma yeShAm sattva-shuddhi-kAraNam vidyate te puNya-karmANas teShAm puNya-karmaNAm, te dvandva-moha-nirmuktA yathoktena dvandva-mohena nirmuktA bhajante mAm paramAtmanAm dR^iDha-vratAH | evam eva paramArtha-tattvam nAnyathety evam sarva-parityAga-vratena nishcita-vij~nAnA dR^iDha-vratA ucyante ||BhGS_7.28|| 

==============================

te kim-artham bhajante ? ity ucyate - 

jarA-maraNa-mokShAya mAm Ashritya yatanti ye |
te brahma tad viduH kR^itsnam adhyAtmam karma cAkhilam ||BhG_7.29||

jarA-maraNa-mokShAya jarA-maraNayor mokShArtham mAm parameshvaram Ashritya mat-samAhita-cittAH santo yatanti prayatante ye, te yad brahma param tad viduH kR^itsnam samastam adhyAtmam pratyag-Atma-viShayam vastu tad viduH | karma cAkhilam samastam viduH ||BhGS_7.29|| 

==============================

sAdhibhUtAdhidaivam mAm sAdhiyaj~nam ca ye viduH |
prayANa-kAle 'pi ca mAm te vidur yukta-cetasaH ||BhG_7.30||

sAdhibhUtAdhidaivam adhibhUtam cAdhidaivam cAdhibhUtAdhidaivam, sahAdhibhUtAdhidaivena vartata iti sAdhibhUtAdhidaivam ca mAm ye viduH | sAdhiyaj~nam ca sahAdhiyaj~nena sAdhiyaj~nam ye viduH, prayANa-kAle maraNa-kAle 'pi ca mAm te viduH | yukta-cetasaH samAhita-cittA iti ||BhGS_7.30|| 

iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrI-govinda-bhagavat-pUjya-pAda-
shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^itau shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye
saptamo 'dhyAyaH ||

__________________________________________________________

BhG 8

atha brahmAkShara-nirdesho nAma 
aShTamo 'dhyAyaH

(shrImac-chaN^karAcArya-bhagavat-pAda-viracita-bhAShyaH)

==============================

te brahma tad viduH kR^itsnam ity AdinA bhagavatArjunasya prashna-bIjAni upadiShTani | atas tat-prashnArtham arjuna uvAca -

kim tad brahma kim adhyAtmam kim karma puruShottama |
adhibhUtam ca kim proktam adhidaivam kim ucyate ||BhG_8.1||
adhiyaj~naH katham ko 'tra dehe 'smin madhusUdana |
prayANa-kAle ca katham j~neyo 'si niyatAtmabhiH ||BhG_8.2||

==============================

eShAm prashnAnAm yathA-kramam nirNayAya shrI-bhagavAn uvAca - 

akSharam brahma paramam svabhAvo 'dhyAtmam ucyate |
bhUtabhAvodbhava-karo visargaH karma-samj~nitaH ||BhG_8.3||

akSharam na kSharatIty akSharam para AtmA, etasya vAkSharasya prashAsane gArgi [BAU 3.8.9] iti shruteH | omkArasya ca om ity ekAkSharam brahma [GItA 8.13] iti pareNa visheShaNAd agrahaNam | paramam iti ca niratishaye brahmaNy akShare upapannataram visheShaNam | tasyaiva parasya brahmaNaH pratideham pratyag-Atma-bhAvaH svabhAvaH | svo bhAvaH svabhAvo 'dhyAtmam ucyate | AtmAnam deham adhikR^itya pratyag-AtmatayA pravR^ittam paramArtha-brahmAvasAnam vastu svabhAvo 'dhyAtmam ucyate 'dhyAtma-shabdenAbhidhIyate | bhUta-bhAvodbhava-karo bhUtAnAm bhAvo bhUta-bhAvas tasya udbhavo bhUta-bhAvodbhavas tam karotIti bhUta-bhAvodbhava-karaH, bhUta-vastUtpatti-kara ity arthaH | visargo visarjanam devatoddeshena caru-puroDAshAder dravyasya parityAgaH | sa eSha visarga-lakShaNo yaj~naH karma-samj~nitaH karma-shabdita ity etat | etasmAt hi bIja-bhUtAd vR^iShTyaDAdi-krameNa sthAvara-jaN^gamAni bhUtAny udbhavanti ||BhGS_8.3|| 

==============================

adhibhUtam kSharo bhAvaH puruShash cAdhidaivatam |
adhiyaj~no 'ham evAtra dehe deha-bhR^itAm vara ||BhG_8.4||
 
adhibhUtam prANi-jAtam adhikR^itya bhavatIti | ko 'sau ? kSharaH kSharatIti kSharo vinAshI, bhAvo yat kimcit janimat vastv ity arthaH | puruShaH pUrNam anena sarvam iti, puri shayanAt vA, puruShaH AdityAntargato hiraNyagarbhaH, sarva-prANi-karaNAnAm anugrAhakaH, so 'dhidaivatam | adhiyaj~naH sarva-yaj~nAbhimAninI viShNv-AkhyA devatA, yaj~no vai viShNuH [TaittS 1.7.4] iti shruteH | sa hi viShNur aham eva | atrAsmin dehe yo yaj~nas tasyAham adhiyaj~naH | yaj~no hi deha-nirvartyatvena deha-samavAyIti dehAdhikaraNo bhavati, deha-bhR^itAm vara ! ||BhGS_8.4|| 

==============================

anta-kAle ca mAm eva smaran muktvA kalevaram |
yaH prayAti sa mad-bhAvam yAti nAsty atra samshayaH ||BhG_8.5||

anta-kAle maraNa-kAle ca mAm eva parameshvaram viShNum smaran muktvA parityajya kalevaram sharIram yaH prayAti gacchati | sa mad-bhAvam vaiShNavam tattvam yAti | nAsti na vidyate 'trAsminn arthe samshayaH - yAti vA na veti || 

==============================

na mad-viShaya evAyam niyamaH | kim tarhi ? - 

yam yam vApi smaran bhAvam tyajaty ante kalevaram |
tam tam evaiti kaunteya sadA tad-bhAva-bhAvitaH ||BhG_8.6||

yam yam vApi yam yam bhAvam devatA-visheSham smaran cintayan tyajati parityajaty ante 'nta-kAle prANa-viyoga-kAle kalevaram sharIram tam tam eva smR^itam bhAvam eva eti nAnyam kaunteya, sadA sarvadA tad-bhAva-bhAvitas tasmin bhAvas tad-bhAvaH sa bhAvitaH smaryamANatayAbhyasto yena sa tad-bhAva-bhAvitaH san ||BhGS_8.6|| 

==============================

yasmAd evam antyA bhAvanA dehAntara-prAptau kAraNam - 

tasmAt sarveShu kAleShu mAm anusmara yudhya ca |
mayy arpita-mano-buddhir mAm evaiShyasy asamshayaH ||BhG_8.7||

tasmAt sarveShu kAleShu mAm anusmara yathA-shAstram | yudhyash ca yuddham sva-dharmam kuru | mayi vAsudeve 'rpite mano-buddhI yasya tava sa tvam mayy arpita-mano-buddhiH san mAm eva yathA-smR^itam eShyasy AgamiShyasi | asamshayo na samshayo 'tra vidyate ||BhGS_8.7|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

abhyAsa-yoga-yuktena cetasA nAnya-gAminA |
paramam puruSham divyam yAti pArthAnucintayan ||BhG_8.8||

abhyAsa-yoga-yuktena mayi citta-samarpaNa-viShaya-bhUta ekasmims tulya-pratyayAvR^itti-lakShaNo vilakShaNa-pratyayAnantarito 'bhyAsaH sa cAbhyAso yogas tena yuktam tatraiva vyApR^itam yoginash cetas tena | cetasA nAnya-gAminA nAnyatra viShayAntare gantum shIlam asyeti nAnya-gAmi tena nAnya-gAminA, paramam niratishayam puruSham divyam divi sUrya-maNDAle bhavam yAti gacchati he pArthAnucintayan shAstrAcAryopadesham anudhyAyan ity etat ||BhGS_8.8|| 

==============================

kim-vishiShTam ca puraSham yAti ? ity ucyate - 

kavim purANam anushAsitAram
aNor aNIyAmsam anusmared yaH |
sarvasya dhAtAram acintya-rUpam
Aditya-varNam tamasaH parastAt ||BhG_8.9||

kavim krAnta-darshinam sarva-j~nam purANam cirantanam anushAsitAram sarvasya jagataH prashAsitAram aNoH sUkShmAd apy aNIyAmsam sUkShmataram anusmared anucintayed yaH kashcit, sarvasya karma-phala-jAtasya dhAtAram vidhAtAram vicitratayA prANibhyo vibhaktAram, acintya-rUpam nAsya rUpam niyatam vidyamAnam api kenacit cintayitum shakyata ity acintya-rUpas tam, Aditya-varNam Adityasyeva nitya-caitanya-prakAsho varNo yasya tam Aditya-varNam, tamasaH parastAt, aj~nAna-lakShaNAn mohAndhakArAt param tam anucintayad yAtIti pUrveNa sambandhaH ||BhGS_8.9|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

prayANa-kAle manasAcalena
bhaktyA yukto yoga-balena caiva |
bhruvor madhye prANam Aveshya samyak
sa tam param puruSham upaiti divyam ||BhG_8.10||

prayANa-kAle maraNa-kAle manasAcalena calana-varjitena bhaktyA yukto bhajanam bhaktis tayA yukto yoga-balena caiva yogasya balam yoga-balam samAdhija-samskAra-pracaya-janita-citta-sthairya-lakShaNam yoga-balam tena ca yukta ity arthaH | pUrvam hR^idaya-puNDArIke vashIkR^itya cittam tata Urdhva-gAminyA nADyA bhUmi-jaya-krameNa bhruvor madhye prANam Aveshya sthApayitvA samyag-ApramattaH san, sa evam buddhimAn yogI kavim purANam ity Adi-lakShaNam tam param parataram puruSham upaiti pratipadyate divyam dyotanAtmakam ||BhGS_8.10|| 

==============================

[yoga-mArgAnugamanenaiva brahma-vidyAm antareNApi brahma prApyata ity evam prAptam idam ucyate ] punar api vakShyamANenopAyena pratipitsitasya brahmaNo veda-vidvad-anAdi-visheShaNa-visheShyasyAbhidhAnam karoti bhagavAn - 
 
yad akSharam veda-vido vadanti
vishanti yad yatayo vIta-rAgAH |
yad icchanto brahmacaryam caranti
tat te padam samgraheNa pravakShye ||BhG_8.11||

yad akSharam na kSharatIty akSharam avinAshi vedavido vedArthaj~nAH vadanti | tad vA etad akSharam gArgi brAhmaNA abhivadanti [BAU 3.8.8] iti shruteH | sarva-visheSha-nivartakatvenAbhivadanty asthUlam aNv ity Adi | kim ca - vishanti pravishanti samyag-darshana-prAptau satyAm yad yatayo yatana-shIlAH samnyAsino vIta-rAgAH vIto vigataH rAgo yebhyas te vIta-rAgAH | yac cAkSharam icchanto j~nAtum iti vAkya-sheShaH brahmacaryam gurau caranti Acaranti, tat te padam tad akSharAkhyam padam padanIyam te tava samgraheNa, samgrahaH samkShepas tena, samkShepeNa pravakShye kathayiShyAmi ||BhGS_8.11|| 

==============================

sa yo ha vai tad bhagavan manuShyeShu prAyaNAntam omkAram abhidhyAyIta | katamam vAva sa tena lokam jayatIti | tasmai sa hovAca - etad vai satya-kAma param cAparam ca brahma yad omkAraH [PrashnaU 5.1-2] ity upakramya, yaH punar etam trimAtreNa om ity etenaivAkShareNa param puruSham abhidhyAyIta sa sAmabhir unnIyate brahma-lokam [PrashnaU 5.5] ity AdinA vacanena, anyatra dharmAd anyatrAdharmAd [KaThU 1.2.14] iti copakramya 

sarve vedA yat padam Amananti 
tapAmsi sarvANi ca yad vadanti | 
yad icchanto brahmacaryam caranti 
tat te padam samgraheNa bravImy om ity etad [KaThU 1.2.15] 

ity Adibhish ca vacanaiH parasya brahmaNo vAcaka-rUpeNa, pratimAvat pratIka-rUpeNa vA, para-brahma-pratipatti-sAdhanatvena manda-madhyama-buddhInAm vivakShitasya omkArasyopAsanam kAlAntare mukti-phalam uktam yat, tad evehApi kavim purANam anushAsitAram [GItA 8.9] yad akSharam veda-vido vadanti [GItA 8.11] iti copanyastasya parasya brahmaNaH pUrvokta-rUpeNa pratipatty-upAya-bhUtasya omkArasya kAlAntara-mukti-phalam upAsanam yogadhAraNA-sahitam vaktavyam | prasaktAnuprasaktam ca yat kimcid ity evam artha uttare grantha Arabhyate - 

sarva-dvArANi samyamya mano hR^idi nirudhya ca |
mUrdhny AdhAyAtmanaH prANam Asthito yoga-dhAraNAm ||BhG_8.12||
 
sarva-dvArANi sarvANi ca tAni dvArANi ca sarva-dvArANy upalabdhau, tAni sarvANi samyasya samyamanam kR^itvA mano hR^idi hR^idaya-puNDArIke nirUdhya nirodham kR^itvA niShpracAram ApAdya, tatra vashIkR^itena manasA hR^idayAd Urdhva-gAminyA nADyordhvam ArUhya mUrdhny AdhAya AtmanaH prANam AsthitaH pR^ivR^itto yoga-dhAraNAm dhArayitum ||BhGS_8.12|| 

==============================

tatraiva ca dhArayan -

om ity ekAkSharam brahma vyAharan mAm anusmaran |
yaH prayAti tyajan deham sa yAti paramAm gatim ||BhG_8.13||

om iti ekAkSharam brahma brahmaNo 'bhidhAna-bhUtam omkAram vyAharan ucArayan, tad-artha-bhUtam mAm Ishvaram anusmaran anucintayan yaH prayAti mriyate, sa tyajan parityajan deham sharIram - tyajan deham iti prayANa-visheShaNArtham deha-tyAgena prayANam AtmanaH, na svarUpa-nAshenety arthaH - sa evam yAti gacchati paramAm prakR^iShTAm gatim ||BhGS_8.13|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

ananya-cetAH satatam yo mAm smarati nityashaH |
tasyAham sulabhaH pArtha nitya-yuktasya yoginaH ||BhG_8.14||

ananya-cetA nAnya-viShaye ceto yasya so 'yam ananya-cetAH | yogI satatam sarvadA yo mAm parameshvaram smarati | nityashaH satatam iti nairantaryam ucyate, nityashaH iti dIrgha-kAlatvam ucyate | na ShaN-mAsam samvatsaram vA | kim tarhi ? yAvaj-jIvam nairantaryeNa yo mAm smaratIty arthaH | tasya yogino 'ham sulabhaH sukhena labhyo he pArtha, nitya-yuktasya sadA samAhita-cittasya yoginaH | yata evam, ato 'nanya-cetAH san mayi sadA samAhito bhavet ||BhGS_8.14|| 

==============================

tava saulabhyena kim syAt ? ity ucyate | sR^iNu tan mama saulabhyena yad bhavati - 

mAm upetya punar-janma duHkhAlayam ashAshvatam |
nApnuvanti mahAtmAnaH samsiddhim paramAm gatAH ||BhG_8.15||

mAm upetya mAm Ishvaram upetya mad-bhAvam Apadya punar janma punar utpattim nApnuvanti na prApnuvanti | kim-vishiShTam punar-janma na prApnuvanti ? iti, tad-visheShaNam Aha - duHkhAlayam duHkhAnAm AdhyAtmikAdInAm Alayam Ashrayam | AlIyante yasmin duHkhAnIti duHkhAlayam janma | na kevalam duHkhAlayam, ashAshvatam anavasthita-svarUpam ca | nApnuvanti IdR^isham punar-janma mahAtmAno yatayaH samsiddhim mokShAkhyAm paramAm prakR^iShTAm gatAH prAptAH | ye punar mAm na prApnuvanti te punar Avartante ||BhGS_8.15|| 

==============================
 
kim punas tvatto 'nyat prAptAH punar Avartante ? ity ucyate - 

A brahma-bhuvanAl lokAH punar-Avartino 'rjuna |
mAm upetya tu kaunteya punar-janma na vidyate ||BhG_8.16||

A brahma-bhuvanAt bhavanty asmin bhUtAnIti bhuvanam | brahmaNo bhuvanam brahma-bhuvanam, brahma-loka ity arthaH | A brahma-bhuvanAt saha brahma-bhuvanena lokAH sarve punar-AvartinaH punar-Avartana-svabhAvAH | he 'rjuna | mAm ekam upetya tu kaunteya punar-janma punar-utpattiH na vidyate ||BhGS_8.16|| 

==============================

brahma-loka-sahitA lokAH kasmAt punar-AvartinaH ? kAla-paricchinnatvAt | katham ? - 

sahasra-yuga-paryantam ahar yad brahmaNo viduH |
rAtrim yuga-sahasrAntAm te 'ho-rAtra-vido janAH ||BhG_8.17||

sahasra-yuga-paryantam sahasrANi yugAni paryantaH paryavasAnam yasyAhnas tat ahaH sahasra-yuga-paryantam | brahmaNaH prajApater virAjo viduH | rAtrim api yuga-sahasrAntAm ahaH-parimANAm eva | ke vidur ity Aha - te 'ho-rAtra-vidaH kAla-samkhyA-vido janA ity arthaH | yata evam kAla-paricchinnAs te, ataH punar-Avartino lokAH ||BhGS_8.17|| 

==============================

prajApater ahani yad bhavati rAtrau ca, tad ucyate - 

avyaktAd vyaktayaH sarvAH prabhavanty ahar-Agame |
rAtry-Agame pralIyante tatraivAvyakta-samj~nake ||BhG_8.18||

avyaktAd avyaktam prajApateH svApAvasthA | tasmAd avyaktAd vyaktayo vyajyanta iti vyaktayaH sthAvara-jaN^gama-lakShaNAH sarvAH prajAH prabhavanty abhivyajyante, ahna Agamo 'har-Agamas tasmin ahar-Agame kAle brahmaNaH prabodha-kAle | tathA rAtry-Agame brahmaNaH svApa-kAle pralIyante sarvA vyaktayas tatraiva pUrvokte 'vyakta-samj~nake ||BhGS_8.18|| 

==============================

akR^itAbhyAgama-kR^ita-vipraNAsha-doSha-parihArArtham bandha-mokSha-shAstra-pravR^itti-sAphalya-pradarshanArtham avidyAdi-klesha-mUla-karmAshaya-vashAc cAvasho bhUta-grAmo bhUtvA bhUtvA pralIyata ity ataH samsAre vairAgya-pradarshanArtham cedam Aha - 

bhUta-grAmaH sa evAyam bhUtvA bhUtvA pralIyate |
rAtry-Agame 'vashaH pArtha prabhavaty ahar-Agame ||BhG_8.19||

bhUta-grAmo bhUta-samudAyaH sthAvara-jaN^gama-lakShaNo yaH pUrvasmin kalpa AsIt sa evAyam nAnyaH | bhUtvA bhUtvAhar-Agame | pralIyate punaH punaH rAtry-Agame 'hnaH kShaye 'vasho 'svatantra eva | he pArtha | prabhavati jAyate 'vasha evAhar-Agame ||BhGS_8.19||

 ==============================

yad upanyastam akSharam, tasya prApty-upAyo nirdiShTa om ity ekAkSharam brahma [GItA 8.13] ity AdinA | athedAnIm akSharasyaiva svarUpa-nirdidikShayedam ucyate, anena yoga-mArgeNedam gantavyam iti - 

paras tasmAt tu bhAvo 'nyo 'vyakto 'vyaktAt sanAtanaH |
yaH sa sarveShu bhUteShu nashyatsu na vinashyati ||BhG_8.20||

paro vyatirikto bhinnaH | kutaH ? tasmAt pUrvoktAt | tu-shabdo 'kSharasya vivakShitasyAvyaktAd vailakShaNya-visheShaNArthaH | bhAvo 'kSharAkhyam param brahma | vyatiriktatve saty api sAlakShaNya-prasaN^go 'stIti tad-vinivR^itty-artham Aha - anya iti | anyo vilakShaNaH | sa cAvyakto 'nindriya-gocaraH | paras tasmAd ity uktam | kasmAt punaH paraH ? pUrvoktAd bhUta-grAma-bIja-bhUtAd avidyA-lakShaNAd avyaktAt | anyo vilakShaNo bhAva ity abhiprAyaH | sanAtanash cirantano yaH sa bhAvaH sarveShu bhUteShu brahmAdiShu nashyatsu na vinashyati ||BhGS_8.20||

==============================

avyakto 'kShara ity uktas tam AhuH paramAm gatim |
yam prApya na nivartante tad dhAma paramam mama ||BhG_8.21||

yo 'sAv avyakto 'kShara ity uktas tam evAkShara-samj~nakam avyaktam bhAvam AhuH paramAm prakR^iShTAm gatim | yam param bhAvam prApya gatvA na nivartante samsArAya, tad dhAma sthAnam paramam prakR^iShTam mama, viShNoH paramam padam ity arthaH ||BhGS_8.21|| 

==============================

tal-labdher upAya ucyate - 

puruShaH sa paraH pArtha bhaktyA labhyas tv ananyayA |
yasyAntaH-sthAni bhUtAni yena sarvam idam tatam ||BhG_8.22||

puruShaH puri shayanAt pUrNatvAd vA | sa paraH pArtha, paro niratishayaH, yasmAt puruShAn na param kimcit | sa bhaktyA labhyas tu j~nAna-lakShaNayAnanyayA Atma-viShayayA | yasya puruShasyAntaH-sthAni madhya-sthAni bhUtAni kArya-bhUtAni | kAryam hi kAraNasyAntarvarti bhavati | yena puruSheNa sarvam idam jagat tatam vyAptam AkAsheneva ghaTAdi ||BhGS_8.22||

==============================

prakR^itAnAm yoginAm praNavAveshita-brahma-buddhInAm kAlAntara-mukti-bhAjAm brahma-pratipattaya uttaro mArgo vaktavya iti yatra kAle ity Adi vivakShitArtha-samarpaNArtham ucyate, AvR^itti-mArgopanyAsaH itara-mArga-stuty-artham ucyate - 

yatra kAle tv anAvR^ittim AvR^ittim caiva yoginaH |
prayAtA yAnti tam kAlam vakShyAmi bharatarShabha ||BhG_8.23||
