yatra kAle prayAtA iti vyavahitena sambandhaH | yatra yasmin kAle tv anAvR^ittim apunar-janma AvR^ittim tad-viparItAm caiva | yogina iti yoginaH karmiNash cocyante | karmiNas tu guNataH karma-yogena yoginAm iti visheShaNAd yoginaH | yatra kAle prayAtA mR^itA yogino 'nAvR^ittim yAnti, yatra kAle ca prayAtAH AvR^ittim yAnti, tam kAlam vakShyAmi bharatarShabha || 

==============================

tam kAlam Aha - 

agnir jyotir ahaH shuklaH ShaN-mAsA uttarAyaNam |
tatra prayAtA gacchanti brahma brahma-vido janAH ||BhG_8.24||

agniH kAlAbhimAninI devatA | tathA jyotir api devataiva kAlAbhimAninI | athavA, agni-jyotiShI yathA shrute eva devate | bhUyasA tu nirdesho yatra kAle tam kAlam iti Amra-vanavat | tathAhar devatAhar-abhimAninI | shuklaH shukla-pakSha-devatA | ShaN-mAsA uttarAyaNam, tatrApi devataiva mArga-bhUtA [BAU 4.3.4] iti sthito 'nyatrAyam nyAyaH | tatra tasmin mArge prayAtA mR^itA gacchanti brahma brahma-vido brahmopAsakA brahmopAsana-parA janAH | krameNeti vAkya-sheShaH | na hi sadyo-mukti-bhAjAm samyag darshana-niShThAnAm gatir Agatir vA kvacid asti | na tasya prANA utkrAmanti [BAU 4.4.6] iti shruteH | brahmasamlInaprANaiva te brahmamayA brahma-bhUtaiva te | 

 ==============================

dhUmo rAtris tathA kR^iShNaH ShaN-mAsA dakShiNAyanam |
tatra cAndramasam jyotir yogI prApya nivartate ||BhG_8.25||

dhUmo rAtrir dhUmAbhimAninI rAtry-abhimAninI ca devatA | tathA kR^iShNaH kR^iShNa-pakSha-devatA | ShaN-mAsA dakShiNAyanam iti ca pUrvavat devataiva | tatra candramasi bhavam cAndramasam jyotiH phalam iShTAdi-kArI yogI karmI prApya bhuktvA tat-kShayAd iha punar nivartate ||BhGS_8.25||

==============================

shukla-kR^iShNe gatI hy ete jagataH shAshvate mate |
ekayA yAty anAvR^ittim anyayAvartate punaH ||BhG_8.26||

shukla-kR^iShNe shuklA ca kR^iShNA ca shukla-kR^iShNe, j~nAna-prakAshakatvAt shuklA, tadabhAvAt kR^iShNA | ete shukla-kR^iShNe hi gatI jagataH ity adhikR^itAnAm j~nAna-karmaNoH, na jagataH sarvasyaiva ete gatI sambhavataH | shAshvate nitye, samsArasya nityatvAt, mate 'bhiprete | tatraikayA shuklayA yAty anAvR^ittim, anyayA itarayA Avartate punar bhUyaH ||BhGS_8.26|| 
==============================

naite sR^itI pArtha jAnan yogI muhyati kashcana |
tasmAt sarveShu kAleShu yoga-yukto bhavArjuna ||BhG_8.27||

na ete yathokte sR^itI mArgau pArtha jAnan samsArAya ekA, anyA mokShAyeti | yogI na muhyati kashcana kashcid api | tasmAt sarveShu kAleShu yoga-yuktaH samAhito bhavArjuna ||BhGS_8.27||

==============================

shR^iNu tasya yogasya mAhAtmyam - 

vedeShu yaj~neShu tapaHsu caiva
dAneShu yat puNya-phalam pradiShTam |
atyeti tat sarvam idam viditvA
yogI param sthAnam upaiti cAdyam ||BhG_8.28||

vedeShu samyag-adhIteShu yaj~neShu ca sAdguNyenAnutiShThiteShu tapaHsu ca sutapteShu dAneShu ca samyag-datteShu yad eteShu puNya-phalam puNyasya phalam puNya-phalam pradiShTam shAstreNa, atyety atItya gacchati sat sarvam phala-jAtam | idam viditvA sapta-prashna-nirNaya-dvAreNoktam artham samyag avadhAryAnuShThAya yogI param prakR^iShTam aishvaram sthAnam upaiti ca pratipadyate | Adyam Adau bhavam kAraNam brahmety arthaH ||BhGS_8.28|| 


iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrI-govinda-bhagavat-pUjya-pAda-
shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^itau shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye
brahmAkShara-nirdesho nAma aShTamo 'dhyAyaH 
||8||


__________________________________________________________

BhG 9

atha rAja-vidyA-rAja-guhya-yogo nAma 
navamo 'dhyAyaH

(shAN^kara-bhAShyaH)

aShTame nADy-Adi-dvAreNa dhAraNA-yogaH saguNa uktaH | tasya ca phalam agny-arcir-Adi-krameNa kAlAntare brahma-prApti-lakShaNam evAnAvR^itti-rUpam nirdiShTam | tatrAnenaiva prakAreNa mokSha-prApti-phalam adhigamyate, nAnyathA iti tad AshaN^kA-vyAvivartayiShayA shrI-bhagavAn uvAca - 

idam tu te guhyatamam pravakShyAmy anasUyave |
j~nAnam vij~nAna-sahitam yaj j~nAtvA mokShyase 'shubhAt ||BhG_9.1||

idam brahma-j~nAnam vakShyamANam uktam ca pUrveShu adhyAyeShu, tat buddhau samnidhIkR^itya idam ity Aha | tu-shabdo visheSha-nirdhAraNArthaH | idam eva tu samyag-j~nAnam sAkShAt mokSha-prApti-sAdhanam vAsudevaH sarvam iti [GItA 7.12], Atmaivedam sarvam [ChAU 7.25.2] ekam evAdvitIyam [ChAU 6.2.1] ity Adi-shruti-smR^itibhyaH | nAnyat, atha te ye 'nyathAto vidur anya-rAjAnas te kShayya-lokA bhavanti [ChAU 7.25.2] ity Adi-shrutibhyash ca | te tubhyam guhyatamam gopyatamam pravakShyAmi kathayiShyAmy anasUyave 'sUyA-rahitAya | kim tat ? j~nAnam | kim-vishiShTam ? vij~nAna-sahitam anubhava-yuktam, yaj j~nAtvA prApya mokShyase 'shubhAt samsAra-bandhanAt ||BhGS_9.1|| 

==============================

tac ca - 

rAja-vidyA rAja-guhyam pavitram idam uttamam |
pratyakShAvagamam dharmyam susukham kartum avyayam ||BhG_9.2||

rAja-vidyA vidyAnAm rAjA, dIpty-atishayavattvAt | dIpyate hIyam atishayena brahma-vidyA sarva-vidyAnAm | tathA rAja-guhyam guhyAnAm rAjA | pavitram pAvanam idam uttamam sarveShAm pAvanAnAm shuddhi-kAraNam brahma-j~nAnam utkR^iShTatamam | aneka-janma-sahasra-samcitam api dharmAdharmAdi sa-mUlam karma kShaNa-mAtrAd eva bhasmIkarotIty ataH kim tasya pAvanatvam vaktavyam ? kim ca - pratyakShAvagamam pratyakSheNa sukhAder ivAvagamo yasya tat pratyakShAvagamam | aneka-guNavato 'pi dharma-viruddhatvam dR^iShTam, na tathAtma-j~nAnam dharma-virodhi, kimtu dharmyam dharmAd anapetam | evam api, syAd duHkha-sampAdyam ity ata Aha - susukham kartum, yathA ratna-viveka-vij~nAnam | tatrAlpAyAsAnAm anyeShAm karmaNAm sukha-sampAdyAnAm alpa-phalatvam duShkarANAm ca mahA-phalatvam dR^iShTam iti, idam tu sukha-sampAdyatvAt phala-kShayAt vyetIti prApte, Aha - avyayam iti | nAsya phalataH karmavat vyayo 'stIty avyayam | ataH shraddheyam Atma-j~nAnam ||BhGS_9.2|| 

==============================

ye punaH - 

ashraddadhAnAH puruShA dharmasyAsya paramtapa |
aprApya mAm nivartante mR^ityu-samsAra-vartmani ||BhG_9.3||

ashraddadhAnAH shraddhA-virahitA Atma-j~nAnasya dharmasyAsya svarUpe tat-phale ca nAstikAH pApa-kAriNaH, asurANAm upaniShadam deha-mAtrAtma-darshanam eva pratipannAH | asutR^ipaH pApAH puruShA ashraddadhAnAH | paramtapa ! aprApya mAm parameshvaram, mat-prAptau naivAshaN^keti mat-prApti-mArga-bheda-bhakti-mAtram apy aprApya ity arthaH | nivartante nishcayena vartante | kva ? - mR^ityu-samsAra-vartmani mR^ityu-yuktaH samsAro mR^ityu-samsAras, tasya vartma naraka-tiryag-Adi-prApti-mArgaH, tasminn eva vartanta ity arthaH ||BhGS_9.3|| 

==============================

stutyArjunam abhimukhIkR^ityAha - 

mayA tatam idam sarvam jagad avyakta-mUrtinA |
mat-sthAni sarva-bhUtAni na cAham teShv avasthitaH ||BhG_9.4||

mayA mama yaH paro bhAvas tena tatam vyAptam sarvam idam jagad avyakta-mUrtinA | na vyaktA mUrtiH svarUpam yasya mama so 'ham avyakta-mUrtis tena mayAvyakta-mUrtinA, karaNAgocara-svarUpeNety arthaH | tasmin mayy avyakta-mUrtau sthitAni mat-sthAni, sarva-bhUtAni brahmAdIni stamba-paryantAni | na hi nirAtmakam kimcit bhUtam vyavahArAyAvakalpate | ato mat-sthAni mayAtmanA Atmavattvena sthitAni | ato mayi sthitAnIty ucyante | teShAm bhUtAnAm aham evAtmA ity atas teShu sthita iti mUDha-buddhInAm avabhAsate | ato bravImi - na cAham teShu bhUteShv avasthitaH | mUrtavat samshleShAbhAvena AkAshasyApy antaratamo hy aham | na hy asamsargi vastu kvacit Adheya-bhAvenAvasthitam bhavati ||BhGS_9.4|| 

==============================

ata evAsamsargitvAn mama - 

na ca mat-sthAni bhUtAni pashya me yogam aishvaram |
bhUta-bhR^in na ca bhUta-stho mamAtmA bhUta-bhAvanaH ||BhG_9.5||

na ca mat-sthAni bhUtAni brahmAdIni | pashya me yogam yuktim ghaTAnam me mama aishvaram Ishvarasyemam aishvaram, yogam Atmano yAthAtmyam ity arthaH | tathA ca shrutir asamsargitvAd asaN^gatAm darshayati - asaN^go na hi sajjate [BAU 3.9.26] iti | idam cAshcaryam anyat pashya - bhUta-bhR^id asaN^go 'pi san bhUtAni bibharti | na ca bhUta-sthaH | yathoktena nyAyena darshitatvAt bhUta-sthatvAnupapatteH | katham punar ucyate 'sau mamAtmeti ? vibhajya dehAdi-saN^ghAtam tasminn ahamkAram adhyAropya loka-buddhim anusaran vyapadishati mamAtmeti, na punar Atmana AtmAnya iti lokavad ajAnan | tathA bhUta-bhAvano bhUtAni bhAvayaty utpAdayati vardhayatIti vA bhUta-bhAvanaH ||BhGS_9.5|| 

==============================

yathoktena shloka-dvayenoktam artham dR^iShTantenopapAdayann Aha -

yathAkAsha-sthito nityam vAyuH sarvatra-go mahAn |
tathA sarvANi bhUtAni mat-sthAnIty upadhAraya ||BhG_9.6||

yathA loke AkAsha-sthita AkAshe sthito nityam sadA vAyuH sarvatra gacchatIti sarvatra-go mahAn parimANataH, tathA AkAshavat sarva-gate mayy asamshleSheNaiva sthitAnIty evam upadhAraya vijAnIhi ||BhGS_9.6|| 

==============================

evam vAyur AkAshe iva mayi sthitAni sarva-bhUtAni sthiti-kAle | tAni - 

sarva-bhUtAni kaunteya prakR^itim yAnti mAmikAm |
kalpa-kShaye punas tAni kalpAdau visR^ijAmy aham ||BhG_9.7||

sarva-bhUtAni kaunteya prakR^itim triguNAtmikAm aparAm nikR^iShTam yAnti mAmikAm madIyAm kalpa-kShaye pralaya-kAle | punar bhUyas tAni bhUtAni utpatti-kAle kalpAdau visR^ijAmi utpAdayAmy aham pUrvavat ||BhGS_9.7|| 

==============================

evam avidyA-lakShaNAm - 

prakR^itim svAm avaShTabhya visR^ijAmi punaH punaH |
bhUta-grAmam imam kR^itsnam avasham prakR^iter vashAt ||BhG_9.8||

prakR^itim svAm svIyAm avaShTabhya vashIkR^itya visR^ijAmi punaH punaH prakR^itito jAtam bhUta-grAmam bhUta-samudAyam imam vartamAnam kR^itsnam avasham asvatantram | avidyAdi-doShaiH paravashIkR^itam | prakR^iter vashAt svabhAva-vashAt ||BhGS_9.8|| 

==============================

tarhi tasya te parameshvarasya bhUta-grAmam imam viShamam vidadhataH, tan-nimittAbhyAm dharmAdharmAbhyAm sambandhaH syAd itIdam Aha bhagavAn - 

na ca mAm tAni karmANi nibadhnanti dhanamjaya |
udAsInavad AsInam asaktam teShu karmasu ||BhG_9.9||

na ca mAm Ishvaram tAni bhUta-grAmasya viShama-sarga-nimittAni karmANi nibadhnanti dhanamjaya | tatra karmaNAm asambandhitve kAraNam Aha - udAsInavat AsInam yathA udIsIna upekShakaH kashcit tadvad AsInam Atmano 'vikriyatvAt | asaktam phalAsaN^ga-rahitam, abhimAna-varjitam, aham karomIti teShu karmasu | ato 'nyasyApi kartR^itvAbhimAnAbhAvaH phalAsaN^gAbhAvash cAsambandha-kAraNam, anyathA karmabhir badhyate mUDhaH kosha-kAravad ity abhiprAyaH ||BhGS_9.9||
 
==============================

tatra bhUta-grAmam imam visR^ijAmy udAsInavad AsInam iti ca viruddham ucyate, iti tat-parihArArtham Aha - 

mayAdhyakSheNa prakR^itiH sUyate sa-carAcaram |
hetunAnena kaunteya jagad viparivartate ||BhG_9.10||

mayAdhyakSheNa sarvato dR^ishi-mAtra-svarupeNAvikriyAtmanAdhyakSheNa mayA, mama mAyA triguNAtmikAvidyA-lakShaNA prakR^itiH sUyate utpAdayati sa-carAcaram jagat | tathA ca mantra-varNaH - 

eko devaH sarva-bhUteShu gUDhaH 
sarva-vyApI sarva-bhUtAntarAtmA | 
karmAdhyakShaH sarva-bhUtAdhivAsaH 
sAkShI cetA kevalo nirguNash ca || [ÁvetU 6.11] iti |

hetunA nimittenAnenAdhyakShatvena kaunteya jagat sa-carAcaram vyaktAvyaktAtmakam viparivartate sarvAvasthAsu | dR^ishi-karmatvApatti-nimittA hi jagataH sarvA pravR^ittiH - aham idam bhokShye, pashyAmIdam, shR^iNomIdam, sukham anubhavAmi, duHkham anubhavAmi, tad-artham idam kariShye, idam j~nAsyAmi, ity AdyAvagati-niShThAvagaty-avasAnaiva | yo asyAdhyakShaH parame vyoman [ãk 8.7.17.7, TaittB 2.8.9] ity Adayash ca mantrA etam artham darshayanti | tatash caikasya devasya sarvAdhyakSha-bhUta-caitanya-mAtrasya paramArthataH sarva-bhogAnabhisambandhino 'nyasya cetanAntarasyAbhAve bhoktur anyasyAbhAvAt | kim-nimitteyam sR^iShTir ity atra prashna-prativacane 'nupapanne, ko addhA veda ka iha pravocat | kuta AjAtA kuta iyam visR^iShTiH [ãk 8.7.17.8] ity Adi-mantra-varNebhyaH | darshitam ca bhagavatA - aj~nAnenAvR^itam j~nAnam tena muhyanti jantavaH [GItA 5.15] iti ||BhGS_9.10|| 

==============================
 
evam mAm nitya-shuddha-buddham ukta-svabhAvam sarvaj~nam sarva-jantUnAm AtmAnam api santam - 

avajAnanti mAm mUDhA mAnuShIm tanum Ashritam |
param bhAvam ajAnanto mama bhUta-maheshvaram ||BhG_9.11||

avajAnanty avaj~nAm paribhavam kurvanti mAm mUDhA avivekinaH | mAnuShIm manuShyasambandhinIm tanum deham Ashritam, manuShyadehena vyavaharantamity etat, param prakR^iShTam bhAvam param Atma-tattvam AkAsha-kalpam AkAshAd apy antaratamam ajAnanto mama bhUta-maheshvaram sarva-bhUtAnAm mahAntam Ishvaram svAtmAnam | tatash ca tasya mamAvaj~nAna-bhAvanena AhatAs te varAkAH ||BhGS_9.11|| 

==============================

katham ? - 

moghAshA mogha-karmANo mogha-j~nAnA vicetasaH |
rAkShasIm AsurIm caiva prakR^itim mohinIm shritAH ||BhG_9.12||

moghAshA vR^ithA AshA AshiSho yeShAm te moghAshAH | tathA mogha-karmANo yAni cAgnihotrAdIni tair anuShThIyamAnAni karmANi tAni ca, teShAm bhagavat-paribhavAt, svAtma-bhUtasyAvaj~nAnAt moghAny eva niShphalAni karmANi bhavantIti mogha-karmANaH | tathA mogha-j~nAnA mogham niShphalam j~nAnam yeShAm te mogha-j~nAnAH, j~nAnam api teShAm niShphalam eva syAt | vicetaso vigata-vivekAsh ca te bhavantIty abhiprAyaH | kim ca - te bhavanti rAkShasIm rakShasAm prakR^itim svabhAvam AsurIm asurANAm ca prakR^itim mohinIm moha-karIm dehAtma-vAdinIm shritAH AshritAH, | chindhi, bhindhi, piba, khAda, parasvam apahara, ity evam vadana-shIlAH krUra-karmANo bhavantIty arthaH | asuryA nAma te lokAH [ýshaU 3] iti shruteH ||BhGS_9.12|| 

==============================

ye punaH shraddadhAnA bhagavad-bhakti-lakShaNe mokSha-mArge pravR^ittAH - 

mahAtmAnas tu mAm pArtha daivIm prakR^itim AshritAH |
bhajanty ananya-manaso j~nAtvA bhUtAdim avyayam ||BhG_9.13||

mahAtamAnas tv akShudra-cittAH mAm Ishvaram pArtha daivIm devAnAm prakR^itim shama-dama-dayA-shraddhAdi-lakShaNAm AshritAH santo bhajanti sevante 'nanya-manaso 'nanya-cittA j~nAtvA bhUtAdim bhUtAnAm viyad-AdInAm prANinAm cAdim kAraNam avyayam ||BhGS_9.13|| 

==============================

katham ? -

satatam kIrtayanto mAm yatantash ca dR^iDha-vratAH |
namasyantash ca mAm bhaktyA nitya-yuktA upAsate ||BhG_9.14||

satatam sarvadA bhagavantam brahma-svarUpam mAm kIrtayantaH, yatantash ca indriyopasamhAra-shama-dama-dayAhimsAdi-lakShaNair dharmaiH prayatantash ca, dR^iDha-vratA dR^iDham sthiram acAlyam vratam yeShAm te dR^iDha-vratA namasyantash ca mAm hR^idayeshayam AtmAnam bhaktyA nitya-yuktAH santa upAsate sevante ||BhGS_9.14|| 

==============================


te kena kena prakAreNa upAsate ity ucyate - 

j~nAna-yaj~nena cApy anye yajanto mAm upAsate |
ekatvena pR^ithaktvena bahudhA vishvato-mukham ||BhG_9.15||

j~nAna-yaj~nena j~nAnam eva bhagavad-viShayam yaj~nas tena j~nAna-yaj~nena, yajantaH pUjayantaH mAm Ishvaram cApy anye 'nyAm upAsanAm parityajyopAsate | tac ca j~nAnam - ekatvenaikam eva param brahmeti paramArtha-darshanena yajanta upAsate | kecic ca pR^ithaktvena Aditya-candrAdi-bhedena sa eva bhagavAn viShNur avasthita ity upAsate | kecit bahudhAvasthitaH sa eva bhagavAn sarvato-mukho vishva-rUpa iti tam vishva-rUpam sarvato-mukham bahudhA bahu-prakAreNopAsate ||BhGS_9.15|| 

==============================

yadi bahubhiH prakArair upAsate, katham tvAm eva upAsata iti | ata Aha - 

aham kratur aham yaj~naH svadhAham aham auShadham |
mantro 'ham aham evAjyam aham agnir aham hutam ||BhG_9.16||

aham kratuH shrauta-karma-bhedo 'ham eva | aham yaj~naH smArtaH | kim ca svadhAnnam aham, pitR^ibhyo yad dIyate | aham auShadham sarva-prANibhir yat adyate tat auShadha-shabda-shabditam vrIhi-yavAdi-sAdhAraNam | athavA svadheti sarva-prANi-sAdhAraNam annam, auShadham iti vyAdhy-upashamanArtham bheShajam | mantro 'ham, yena pitR^ibhyo devatAbhyash ca havir dIyate | aham eva Ajyam havish ca | aham agniH, yasmin hUte haviH so 'gnir aham | aham hutam havana-karmash ca ||BhGS_9.16|| 

==============================
kim ca -

pitAham asya jagato mAtA dhAtA pitAmahaH |
vedyam pavitram omkAra R^ik sAma yajur eva ca ||BhG_9.17||

pitA janayitAham asya jagataH, mAtA janayitrI, dhAtA karma-phalasya prANibhyo vidhAtA, pitAmahaH pituH pitA, vedyam veditavyam, pavitram pAvanam omkAraH, R^ik sAma yajue eva ca ||BhGS_9.17|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

gatir bhartA prabhuH sAkShI nivAsaH sharaNam suhR^it |
prabhavaH pralayaH sthAnam nidhAnam bIjam avyayam ||BhG_9.18||

gatiH karma-phalam, bhartA poShTA, prabhuH svAmI, sAkShI prANinAm kR^itAkR^itasya, nivAso yasmin prANino nivasanti, sharaNam ArtAnAm, prapannAnAm Arti-haraH | suhR^it pratyupakArAnapekShaH sann upakArI, prabhava utpattir jagataH, pralayaH pralIyate 'smin iti, tathA sthAnam tiShThaty asminn iti, nidhAnam nikShepaH kAlAntaropabhogyam prANinAm, bIjam praroha-kAraNam praroha-dharmiNAm, avyayam yAvat-samsAra-bhAvitvAt avyayam, na hy abIjam kimcit prarohati | nityam ca praroha-darshanAd bIja-samtatir na vyetIti gamyate ||BhGS_9.18|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

tapAmy aham aham varSham nigR^ihNAmy utsR^ijAmi ca |
amR^itam caiva mR^ityush ca sad asac cAham arjuna ||BhG_9.19||

tapAmy aham Adityo bhUtvA kaishcit rashmibhir ulbaNaiH | aham varSham kaishcid rashmibhir utsR^ijAmi | utsR^ijya punar nigR^ihNAmi kaishcid rashmibhir aShTabhir mAsaiH punar utsR^ijAmi prAvR^iShi | amR^itam caiva devAnAm, mR^ityush ca martyAnAm | sad yasya yat sambandhitayA vidyamAnam tat, tad-viparItam asac caivAham arjuna | na punar atyantam evAsad bhagavAn, svayam kArya-kAraNe vA sad-asatI ||BhGS_9.19|| 

==============================

ye pUrvoktair nivR^itti-prakArair ekatva-pR^ithaktvAdi-vij~nAnair yaj~nair mAm pUjayanta upAsate j~nAna-vidaH, te yathA-vij~nAnam mAm eva prApnuvanti | ye punar aj~nAH kAma-kAmAH - 

traividyA mAm somapAH pUta-pApA
yaj~nair iShTvA svar-gatim prArthayante |
te puNyam AsAdya surendra-lokam
ashnanti divyAn divi deva-bhogAn ||BhG_9.20||
 
traividyA R^ig-yajuH-sAma-vido mAm vasv-Adi-deva-rUpiNam somapAH somam pibantIti somapAH, tenaiva soma-pAnena pUta-pApAH shuddha-kilbiShAH, yaj~nair agniShTomAdibhir iShTvA pUjayitvA svar-gatim svarga-gamanam svar eva gatiH svar-gatis tAm, prArthayante | te ca puNyam puNya-phalam AsAdya samprApya surendra-lokam shatakratoH sthAnam ashnanti bhu¤jate divyAn divi bhavAn aprAkR^itAn deva-bhogAn devAnAm bhogAn ||BhGS_9.20|| 

==============================

te tam bhuktvA svarga-lokam vishAlam
kShINe puNye martya-lokam vishanti |
evam trayI-dharmam anuprapannA
gatAgatam kAma-kAmA labhante ||BhG_9.21||

te tam bhuktvA svarga-lokam vishAlam vistIrNam kShINe puNye martya-lokam vishanti Avishanti | evam yathoktena prakAreNa trayI-dharmam kevalam vaidikam karmAnuprapannA gatAgatam gatam cAgatam ca gatAgatam gamanAgamanam kAma-kAmAH kAmAn kAmayanta iti kAma-kAmA labhante gatAgatam eva, na tu svAtantryam kvacil labhanta ity arthaH ||BhGS_9.21||

==============================

ye punar niShkAmAH samyag-darshinaH -

ananyAsh cintayanto mAm ye janAH paryupAsate |
teShAm nityAbhiyuktAnAm yoga-kShemam vahAmy aham ||BhG_9.22||

ananyA apR^ithag-bhUtAH param devam nArAyaNam Atmatvena gatAH santash cintayanto mAm ye janAH samnyAsinaH paryupAsate, teShAm paramArtha-darshinAm nityAbhiyuktAnAm satatAbhiyoginAm yoga-kShemam yogo 'prAptasya prApaNam kShemas tad-rakShaNam tad-ubhayam vahAmi prApayAmy aham | j~nAnI tv Atmaiva me matam [GItA 7.18] sa ca mama priyaH [GItA 7.17] yasmAd tasmAt te mamAtma-bhUtAH priyAsh ceti |

nanv anyeShAm api bhaktAnAm yoga-kShemam vahaty eva bhagavAn | satyam vahaty eva | kimtv ayam visheShaH - anye ye bhaktAs te AtmArtham svayam api yoga-kShemam Ihante | ananya-darshinas tu nAtmArtham yoga-kShemam Ihante | na hi te jIvite maraNe vAtmano gR^iddhim kurvanti | kevalam eva bhagavac-charaNAs te | ato bhagavAn eva teShAm yoga-kShemam vahatIti ||BhGS_9.22||

==============================

nanv anyApi devatAs tvam eva cet tad-bhaktAsh ca tvAm eva yajante | satyam evam - 

ye 'py anya-devatA-bhaktA yajante shraddhayAnvitAH |
te 'pi mAm eva kaunteya yajanty avidhi-pUrvakam ||BhG_9.23||

ye 'py anya-devatA-bhaktA anyAsu devatAsu bhaktA anya-devatA-bhaktAH santo yajante pUjayanti shraddhayA Astikya-buddhyAnvitA anugatAH, te 'pi mAm eva kaunteya yajanty avidhi-pUrvakam avidhir aj~nAnam tat-pUrvakam yajanta ity arthaH ||BhGS_9.23|| 

==============================

kasmAt te 'vidhi-pUrvakam yajanta ity ucyate | yasmAt - 

aham hi sarva-yaj~nAnAm bhoktA ca prabhur eva ca |
na tu mAm abhijAnanti tattvenAtash cyavanti te ||BhG_9.24||

aham hi sarva-yaj~nAnAm shrautAnAm smArtAnAm ca sarveShAm yaj~nAnAm devatAtmatvena bhoktA ca prabhur eva ca | mat-svAmiko hi yaj~naH, adhiyaj~no 'ham evAtra [GItA 8.4] iti hy uktam | tathA na tu mAm abhijAnanti tattvena yathAvat | atash cAvidhi-pUrvakam iShTvA yAga-phalAc cyavanti pracyavante te ||BhGS_9.24|| 

==============================

ye 'py anya-devatA-bhakti-mattvenAvidhi-pUrvakam yajante, teShAm api yAga-phalam avashyambhAvi | katham ? - 

yAnti deva-vratA devAn pitÌn yAnti pitR^i-vratAH |
bhUtAni yAnti bhUtejyA yAnti mad-yAjino 'pi mAm ||BhG_9.25||

yAnti gacchanti deva-vratA deveShu vratam niyamo bhaktish ca yeShAm te deva-vratA devAn yAnti | pitÌn agniShv AttAdIn yAnti pitR^i-vratAH shrAddhAdi-kriyA-parAH pitR^i-bhaktAH | bhUtAni vinAyaka-mAtR^i-gaNa-catur-bhaginyAdIni yAnti bhUtejyA bhUtAnAm pUjakAH | yAnti mad-yAjino mad-yajana-shIlA vaiShNavA mAm eva yAnti | samAne 'py AyAse mAm eva na bhajante 'j~nAnAt, tena te 'lpa-phala-bhAjo bhavantIty arthaH ||BhGS_9.25|| 

==============================

na kevalam mad-bhaktAnAm anAvR^itti-lakShaNam ananta-phalam, sukhArAdhanash cAham | katham ? - 

patram puShpam phalam toyam yo me bhaktyA prayacchati |
tad aham bhakty-upahR^itam ashnAmi prayatAtmanaH ||BhG_9.26||

patram puShpam phalam toyam udakam yaH me mahyam bhaktyA prayacchati, tat aham patrAdi bhaktyA upahR^itam bhakti-pUrvakam prApitam bhakty-upahR^itam ashnAmi gR^ihNAmi prayatAtmanaH shuddha-buddheH ||BhGS_9.26|| 

==============================

yataH evam, ataH - 

yat karoShi yad ashnAsi yaj juhoShi dadAsi yat |
yat tapasyasi kaunteya tat kuruShva mad-arpaNam ||BhG_9.27||

yat karoShi svataH prAptam, yad ashnAsi, yac ca juhoShi havanam nirvartayasi shrautam smArtam vA, yad dadAsi prayacchasi brAhmaNAdibhyo hiraNyAnnAjyAdi, yat tapasyasi tapash carasi kaunteya, tat kuruShva mad-arpaNam mat-samarpaNam ||BhGS_9.27||

==============================

evam kurvatas tava yat bhavati, tat sR^iNu - 

shubhAshubha-phalair evam mokShyase karma-bandhanaiH |
samnyAsa-yoga-yuktAtmA vimukto mAm upaiShyasi ||BhG_9.28||

shubhAshubha-phalaiH shubhAshubhe iShTAniShTe phale yeShAm tAni shubhAshubha-phalAni karmANi taiH shubhAshubha-phalaiH karma-bandhanaiH karmANy eva bandhanAni karma-bandhanAni taiH karma-bandhanair evam mad-arpaNam kurvan mokShyase | so 'yam samnyAsa-yogo nAma, samnyAsash cAsau mat-samarpaNatayA karmatvAd yogash cAsAv iti, tena samnyAsa-yogena yukta AtmAntaH-karaNam yasya tava sa tvam samnyAsa-yoga-yuktAtmA san vimuktaH karma-bandhanair jIvann eva patite cAsmin sharIre mAm upaiShyasi AgamiShyasi ||BhGS_9.28|| 

==============================

rAga-dveShavAms tarhi bhagavAn, yato bhaktAn anugR^ihNAti, netarAn iti tan na - 

samo 'ham sarva-bhUteShu na me dveShyo 'sti na priyaH |
ye bhajanti tu mAm bhaktyA mayi te teShu cApy aham ||BhG_9.29||

samas tulyo 'ham sarva-bhUteShu | na me dveShyo 'sti na priyaH | agnivad aham - dUra-sthAnAm yathAgniH shItam nApanayati, samIpam upasarpatAm apanayati | tathAham bhaktAn anugR^ihNAmi, netarAn | ye bhajanti tu mAm Ishvaram bhaktyA mayi te - svabhAvata eva, na mama rAga-nimittam - vartante | teShu cApy aham svabhAvata eva varte, netareShu | naitAvatA teShu dveSho mam ||BhGS_9.29|| 

==============================

sR^iNu mad-bhakter mAhAtmyam - 

api cet sudurAcAro bhajate mAm ananya-bhAk |
sAdhur eva sa mantavyaH samyag vyavasito hi saH ||BhG_9.30||
 
api cet yady api sudurAcAraH suShThu durAcAro 'tIva kutsitAcAro 'pi bhajate mAm ananya-bhAk ananya-bhaktiH san, sAdhur eva samyag-vR^itta eva sa mantavyo j~nAtavyaH | samyag yathAvad vyavasito hi saH, yasmAt sAdhu-nishcayaH saH ||BhGS_9.30|| 

==============================

utsR^ijyash ca bAhyAm durAcAratAm antaH samyag-vyavasAya-sAmarthyAt - 

kShipram bhavati dharmAtmA shashvac-chAntim nigacchati |
kaunteya pratijAnIhi na me bhaktaH praNashyati ||BhG_9.31||

kShipram shIghram bhavati dharmAtmA dharma-citta eva | shashvan nityam shAntim copashamam nigacchati prApnoti | sR^iNu paramArtham, kaunteya pratijAnIhi nishcitAm pratij~nAm kuru, na me mama bhakto mayi samarpitAntarAtmA mad-bhakto na praNashyatIti ||BhGS_9.31|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

mAm hi pArtha vyapAshritya ye 'pi syuH pApa-yonayaH |
striyo vaishyAs tathA shUdrAs te 'pi yAnti parAm gatim ||BhG_9.32||

mAm hi yasmAt pArtha vyapAshritya mAm Ashrayatvena gR^ihItvA ye 'pi syuH pApa-yonayaH pApA yonir yeShAm te pApa-yonayaH syur bhaveyuH | pApa-yonayaH pApA yonir yeShAm te pApa-yonayaH pApa-janmAnaH | ke te ? ity Aha -striyo vaishyAs tathA shUdrAs te 'pi yAnti gacchanti parAm prakR^iShTAm gatim ||BhGS_9.32|| 

==============================

kim punar brAhmaNAH puNyA bhaktA rAjarShayas tathA |
anityam asukham lokam imam prApya bhajasva mAm ||BhG_9.33||

kim punar brAhmaNAH puNyAH puNya-yonayo bhaktA rAjarShayas tathA rAjAnash ca te R^iShayash ceti rAjarShayaH | yata evam, ato 'nityam kShaNa-bhaN^guram asukham ca sukha-varjitam imam lokam manuShya-lokam prApya puruShArtha-sAdhanam durlabham manuShyatvam labdhvA bhajasva sevasva mAm ||BhGS_9.33|| 

==============================

katham ? - 

man-manA bhava mad-bhakto mad-yAjI mAm namaskuru |
mAm evaiShyasi yuktvaivam AtmAnam mat-parAyaNaH ||BhG_9.34||

mayi vAsudeve mano yasya tava sa tvam man-manA bhava | tathA mad-bhakto bhava | mad-yAjI mad-yajana-shIlo bhava | mAm eva ca namaskuru | mAm eveshvarasyAgamiShyasi yuktvA samAdhAya cittam | evam AtmAnam mAm aham hi sarveShAm bhUtAnAm AtmA parA ca gatiH param ayanam tam mAm evambhUtam eShyastIty atItena padena sambandhaH | mat-parAyaNaH sann ity arthaH ||BhGS_9.34|| 

iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrI-govinda-bhagavat-pUjya-pAda-
shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^itau shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye
rAja-vidyA-rAja-guhya-yogo nAma navamo 'dhyAyaH 
||9||

BhG 10

atha vibhUti-yogo nAma dashamo 'dhyAyaH

(bhagavat-pAda-shrImac-chaN^karAcArya-kR^ita-bhAShyam)

saptame 'dhyAye bhagavatas tattvam vibhUtayash ca prakAshitAH, navame ca | athedAnIm yeShu yeShu bhAveShu cintyo bhagavAms te te bhAvA vaktavyAH | tattvam ca bhagavato vaktavyam uktam api, durvij~neyatvAt, ity ataH shrI-bhagavAn uvAca - 

bhUya eva mahA-bAho shR^iNu me paramam vacaH |
yat te 'ham prIyamANAya vakShyAmi hita-kAmyayA ||BhG_10.1||

bhUya eva bhUyaH punar he mahAbAho sR^iNu me madIyam paramam prakR^iShTam niratishaya-vastunaH prakAshakam vaco vAkyam yat paramam te tubhyam prIyamANAya - mad-vacanAt prIyase tvam atIvAmR^itam iva piban, tataH - vakShyAmi hita-kAmyayA hitecchayA ||BhGS_10.1|| 

==============================

kim-artham aham vakShyAmIty ata Aha - 

na me viduH suragaNAH prabhavam na maharShayaH |
aham Adir hi devAnAm maharShINAm ca sarvashaH ||BhG_10.2||

na me vidur na jAnanti sura-gaNA brahmAdayaH | kim te na viduH ? mama prabhavam prabhAvam prabhu-shakty-atishayam, athavA prabhavam prabhavanam utpattim | nApi maharShayo bhR^igv-Adayo viduH | kasmAt te na vidur ity ucyate - aham AdiH kAraNam hi yasmAd devAnAm maharShINAm ca sarvashaH sarva-prakAraiH ||BhGS_10.2|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

yo mAm ajam anAdim ca vetti loka-maheshvaram |
asammUDhaH sa martyeShu sarva-pApaiH pramucyate ||BhG_10.3||

yaH mAm ajam anAdim ca, yasmAt aham Adir devAnAm maharShINAm ca, na mamAnyaH AdiH vidyate | ato 'ham ajo 'nAdi ca | anAditvam ajatve hetuH, tam mAm ajam anAdim ca yo vetti vijAnAti lokamaheshvaram lokAnAm mahAntam Ishvaram turIyam aj~nAnatatkAryavarjitam asammUDhaH sammohavarjitaH saH matryeShu manuShyeShu, sarvapApaiH sarveH pApair mati-pUrvAmatipUrva-kR^itaiH pramucyate pramokShyate ||BhGS_10.3||

==============================
 
itash cAham maheshvaro lokAnAm - 

buddhir j~nAnam asammohaH kShamA satyam damaH shamaH |
sukham duHkham bhavo 'bhAvo bhayam cAbhayam eva ca ||BhG_10.4||

buddhir antaH-karaNasya sUkShmAdy-arthAvabodhana-sAmarthyam, tadvantam buddhimAn iti hi vadanti | j~nAnam AtmAdi-padArthAnAm avabodhaH | asammohaH pratyutpanneShu boddhavyeShu viveka-pUrvikA pravR^ittiH | kShamA AkruShTasya tADitasya vAvikR^ita-cittatA | satyam yathA-dR^iShTasya yathA-shrutasya cAtmAnubhavasya para-buddhi-samkrAntaye tathaivoucAryamANA vAk satyam ucyate | damo bAhyendriyopashamaH | shamo 'ntaH-karaNasyopashamaH | sukham AhlAdaH | duHkham santApaH | bhava udbhavaH | abhAvas tad-viparyayaH | bhayam ca trAsaH, abhayam eva ca tad-viparItam ||BhGS_10.4||

==============================

ahimsA samatA tuShTis tapo dAnam yasho 'yashaH |
bhavanti bhAvA bhUtAnAm matta eva pR^ithag-vidhAH ||BhG_10.5||

ahimsApIDA prANinAm | samatA sama-cittatA | tuShTiH samtoShaH paryApta-buddhir lAbheShu | tapa indriya-samyama-pUrvakam sharIra-pIDAnam | dAnam yathA-shakti samvibhAgaH | yasho dharma-nimittA kIrtiH | ayashas tv adharma-nimittA kIrtiH | bhavanti bhAvA yathoktA buddhy-Adayo bhUtAnAm prANinAm matta eveshvarAt pR^ithag-vidhAH nAnA-vidhAH sva-karmAnurUpeNa ||BhGS_10.5||

==============================

kim ca - 

maharShayaH sapta pUrve catvAro manavas tathA |
mad-bhAvA mAnasA jAtA yeShAm loka imAH prajAH ||BhG_10.6||

maharShayaH sapta bhR^igv-AdayaH pUrve 'tIta-kAla-sambandhinaH, catvAro manavas tathA sAvarNA iti prasiddhAH | te ca mad-bhAvA mad-gata-bhAvanA vaiShNavena sAmarthyena upetAH | mAnasA manasaivotpAditA mayA jAtA utpannAH | yeShAm manUnAm maharShINAm ca sR^iShTir loka imAH sthAvara-jaN^gama-lakShaNAH prajAH ||BhGS_10.6|| 

==============================

etAm vibhUtim yogam ca mama yo vetti tattvataH |
so 'vikampena yogena yujyate nAtra samshayaH ||BhG_10.7||

etAm yathoktAm vibhUtim vistAram yogam ca yuktim cAtmano ghaTanam, athavA yogaishvarya-sAmarthyam sarva-j~natvam yoga-jam yoga ucyate, mama madIyam yogam yo vetti tattvatas tattvena yathAvad ity etat, so 'vikampenApracalitena yogena samyag darshana-sthairya-lakShaNena yujyate sambadhyate | nAtra samshayo nAsminn arthe samshayo 'sti ||BhGS_10.7||

==============================

kIdR^ishenAvikampena yogena yujyate ? ity ucyate - 

aham sarvasya prabhavo mattaH sarvam pravartate |
iti matvA bhajante mAm budhA bhAva-samanvitAH ||BhG_10.8||

aham param brahma vAsudevAkhyam sarvasya jagataH prabhava utpattiH | matta eva sthiti-nAsha-kriyA-phalopabhoga-lakShaNam vikriyA-rUpam sarvam jagat pravartate | ity evam matvA bhajante sevante mAm budhA avagata-paramArtha-tattvAH | bhAva-samanvitA bhAvo bhAvanA paramArtha-tattvAbhiniveshas tena samanvitAH samyuktAH ity arthaH ||BhGS_10.8|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

mac-cittA mad-gata-prANA bodhayantaH parasparam |
kathayantash ca mAm nityam tuShyanti ca ramanti ca ||BhG_10.9||

mac-cittAH, mayi cittam yeShAm te mac-cittAH | mad-gata-prANAH mAm gatAH prAptAsh cakShur-AdayaH prANA yeShAm te mad-gata-prANAH | mayy upasamhR^ita-karaNAH ity arthaH | athavA, mad-gata-prANAH mad-gata-jIvanA ity etat | bodhayanto 'vagamayantaH parasparam anyonyam, kathayantash ca j~nAna-bala-vIryAdi-dharmair vishiShTam mAm | tuShyanti ca paritoSham upayAnti ca ramanti ca ratim ca prApnuvanti priya-samgatyeva ||BhGS_10.9|| 

==============================

ye yathoktaiH prakArair bhajante mAm bhaktAH santaH - 

teShAm satata-yuktAnAm bhajatAm prIti-pUrvakam |
dadAmi buddhi-yogam tam yena mAm upayAnti te ||BhG_10.10||

teShAm satata-yuktAnAm nityAbhiyuktAnAm nivR^itta-sarva-bAhyaiShaNAnAm bhajatAm sevamAnAnAm | kim arthitvAdinA kAraNena ? nety Aha - -prIti-pUrvakam prItiH snehas tat-pUrvakam mAm bhajatAm ity arthaH | dadAmi prayacchAmi buddhi-yogam buddhiH samyag darshanam mat-tattva-viShayam tena yogo buddhi-yogas tam buddhi-yogam, yena buddhi-yogena samyag darshana-lakShaNena mAm parameshvaram Atma-bhUtam Atmatvena upayAnti pratipadyante | ke ? te ye mac-cittatvAdi-prakArair mAm bhajante ||BhGS_10.10|| 

==============================

kim-artham kasya vA tvat-prApti-pratibandha-hetor nAshakam buddhi-yogam teShAm tvad-bhaktAnAm dadAsi ? ity apekShAyAm Aha - 

teShAm evAnukampArtham aham aj~nAna-jam tamaH |
nAshayAmy Atma-bhAva-stho j~nAna-dIpena bhAsvatA ||BhG_10.11||

teShAm eva katham nu nAma shreyaH syAt ity anukampArtham dayA-hetor aham aj~nAna-jam avivekato jAtam mithyA-pratyaya-lakShaNam mohAndhakAram tamo nAshayAmi, Atma-bhAva-stha Atmano bhAvo 'ntaH-karaNAshayas tasminn eva sthitaH san j~nAna-dIpena viveka-pratyaya-rUpeNa bhakti-prasAda-snehAbhiShiktena mad-bhAvanAbhinivesha-vAteritena brahmacaryAdi-sAdhana-samskAra-vat-praj~nAvartinA viraktAntaH-karaNAdhAreNa viShaya-vyAvR^itta-citta-rAga-dveShAkaluShita-nivAtApavaraka-sthena nitya-pravR^ittaikAgrya-dhyAna-janita-samyag-darshana-bhAsvatA j~nAna-dIpenety arthaH ||BhGS_10.11|| 

==============================

yathoktAm bhagavato vibhUtim yogam ca shrutvArjuna uvAca - 

param brahma param dhAma pavitram paramam bhavAn |
puruSham shAshvatam divyam Adi-devam ajam vibhum ||BhG_10.12||

param brahma paramAtmA param dhAma param tejaH pavitram pAvanam paramam prakR^iShTam bhavAn | puruSham shAshvatam nityam divyam divi bhavam Adi-devam sarva-devAnAm Adau bhavam Adi-devam ajam vibhum vibhavana-shIlam ||BhGS_10.12||

==============================

IdR^isham - 

Ahus tvAm R^iShayaH sarve devarShir nAradas tathA |
asito devalo vyAsaH svayam caiva bravIShi me ||BhG_10.13||

AhuH kathayanti tvAm R^iShayo vasiShThAdayaH sarve devarShir nAradas tathA | asito devalo 'pi evam evAha, vyAsash ca, svayam caiva tvam ca bravIShi me ||BhGS_10.13|| 

==============================

sarvam etad R^itam manye yan mAm vadasi keshava |
na hi te bhagavan vyaktim vidur devA na dAnavAH ||BhG_10.14||

sarvam etad yathoktam R^iShibhis tvayA caitad R^itam satyam eva manye, yan mAm prati vadasi bhAShase he keshava | na hi te tava bhagavan vyaktim prabhavam vidur na devA na dAnavAH ||BhGS_10.14||

==============================

yatas tvam devAdInAm AdiH, ataH - 

svayam evAtmanAtmAnam vettha tvam puruShottama |
bhUta-bhAvana bhUtesha deva-deva jagatpate ||BhG_10.15||

svayam eva AtmanAtmAnam vettha jAnAsi tvam niratishaya-j~nAnaishvarya-balAdi-shaktimantam Ishvaram | puruShottama ! bhUtAni bhAvayatIti bhUta-bhAvanaH | he bhUtabhAvana ! bhUtesha ! bhUtAnAm IshitaH ! he deva-deva ! jagat-pate ! ||BhGS_10.15|| 

==============================

vaktum arhasy asheSheNa divyA hy Atma-vibhUtayaH |
yAbhir vibhUtibhir lokAn imAms tvam vyApya tiShThasi ||BhG_10.16||

vaktum kathayitum arhasy asheSheNa | divyA hy Atma-vibhUtayaH | Atmano vibhUtayo yAs tAH vaktum arhasi | yAbhir vibhUtibhir Atmano mAhAtmya-vistarair imAn lokAn tvam vyApya tiShThasi ||BhGS_10.16|| 

==============================

katham vidyAm aham yogims tvAm sadA paricintayan |
keShu keShu ca bhAveShu cintyo 'si bhagavan mayA ||BhG_10.17||

katham vidyAm vijAnIyAm aham he yogin tvAm sadA paricintayan | keShu keShu ca bhAveShu vastuShu cintyo 'si dhyeyo 'si bhagavan mayA ||BhGS_10.17|| 

==============================

vistareNAtmano yogam vibhUtim ca janArdana |
bhUyaH kathaya tR^iptir hi shR^iNvato nAsti me 'mR^itam ||BhG_10.18||

vistareNAtmano yogam yogaishvarya-shakti-visheSham vibhUtim ca vistaram dhyeya-padArthAnAm he janArdana, ardater gati-karmaNo rUpam, asurANAm deva-pratipakSha-bhUtAnAm janAnAm narakAdi-gamayitR^itvAt janArdano 'bhyudaya-niHshreyasa-puruShArtha-prayojanam sarvair janair yAcyate iti vA | bhUyaH pUrvam uktam api kathaya | tR^iptiH paritoSho hi yasmAn nAsti me mama shR^iNvatas tvan-mukha-niHsR^ita-vAkyAmR^itam ||BhGS_10.18|| 

==============================

shrI-bhagavAn uvAca - 

hanta te kathayiShyAmi divyA hy Atma-vibhUtayaH |
prAdhAnyataH kuru-shreShTha nAsty anto vistarasya me ||BhG_10.19||

hanta idAnIm te tava divyA divi bhavA Atma-vibhUtayo 'tmano mama vibhUtayo yAs tAH kathayiShyAmIty etat | prAdhAnyato yatra yatra pradhAnA yA yA vibhUtis tAm tAm pradhAnAm prAdhAnyataH kathayiShyAmy aham kuru-shreShTha ! asheShatas tu varSha-shatenApi na shakyA vaktum, yato nAsty anto vistarasya me mama vibhUtInAm ity arthaH ||BhGS_10.19||

==============================

tatra prathamam eva tAvat sR^iNu - 

aham AtmA guDAkesha sarva-bhUtAshaya-sthitaH |
aham Adish ca madhyam ca bhUtAnAm anta eva ca ||BhG_10.20||

aham AtmA pratyag-AtmA guDAkesha, guDAkA nidrA tasyAH Isho guDAkeshaH, jita-nidra ity arthaH | ghana-kesheti vA | sarva-bhUtAshaya-sthitaH sarveShAm bhUtAnAm Ashaye 'ntar-hR^idi sthito 'ham AtmA pratyag-AtmA nityam dhyeyaH | tad-ashaktena cottareShu bhAveShu cintyo 'ham | yasmAd aham eva Adir bhUtAnAm kAraNam tathA madhyam ca sthitir antaH pralayash ca ||BhGS_10.20||

==============================

evam ca dhyeyo 'ham - 

AdityAnAm aham viShNur jyotiShAm ravir amshumAn |
marIcir marutAm asmi nakShatrANAm aham shashI ||BhG_10.21||

AdityAnAm dvAdashAnAm viShNur nAma Adityo 'ham | jyotiShAm raviH prakAshayitÌNAm amshumAn rashmimAn | marIcir nAma marutAm marud-devatA-bhedAnAm asmi | nakShatrANAm aham shashI candramAH ||BhGS_10.21|| 

==============================

vedAnAm sAma-vedo 'smi devAnAm asmi vAsavaH |
indriyANAm manash cAsmi bhUtAnAm asmi cetanA ||BhG_10.22||

vedAnAm madhye sAma-vedo 'smi | devAnAm rUdrAdityAdInAm vAsava indro 'smi | indriyANAm ekAdashAnAm cakShur-AdInAm manash cAsmi samkalpa-vikalpAtmakam manash cAsmi | bhUtAnAm asmi cetanA kArya-karaNa-samghAte nityAbhivyaktA buddhi-vR^ittish cetanA ||BhGS_10.22||

==============================

rudrANAm shamkarash cAsmi vittesho yakSha-rakShasAm |
vasUnAm pAvakashcAsmi meruH shikhariNAm aham ||BhG_10.23||

rudrANAm ekAdashAnAm shamkarash cAsmi | vitteshaH kuvero yakSha-rakShasAm yakShANAm rakShasAm ca | vasUnAm aShTanAm pAvakash cAsmy agniH | meruH shikhariNAm shikharavatAm aham ||BhGS_10.23|| 

==============================
 

purodhasAm ca mukhyam mAm viddhi pArtha bR^ihaspatim |
senAnInAm aham skandaH sarasAm asmi sAgaraH ||BhG_10.24||

purodhasAm ca rAja-purohitAnAm ca mukhyam pradhAnam mAm viddhi he pArtha bR^ihaspatim | sa hIndrasyeti mukhyaH syAt purodhAH | senAnInAm senApatInAm aham skando deva-senApatiH | sarasAm yAni deva-khAtAni sarAmsi teShAm sarasAm sAgaro 'smi bhavAmi ||BhGS_10.24||

==============================

maharShINAm bhR^igur aham girAm asmy ekam akSharam |
yaj~nAnAm japa-yaj~no 'smi sthAvarANAm himAlayaH ||BhG_10.25||

maharShINAm bhR^igur aham | girAm vAcAm pada-lakShaNAnAm ekam akSharam omkAro 'smi | yaj~nAnAm japa-yaj~no 'smi, sthAvarANAm sthiti-matAm himAlayaH ||BhGS_10.25|| 

==============================

ashvatthaH sarva-vR^ikShANAm devarShINAm ca nAradaH |
gandharvANAm citrarathaH siddhAnAm kapilo muniH ||BhG_10.26||

ashvatthaH sarva-vR^ikShANAm, devarShINAm ca nArado devAH eva santaH R^iShitvam prAptAH mantra-darshitvAt te devarShayaH | teShAm nArado 'smi | gandharvANAm citraratho nAma gandharvo 'smi | siddhAnAm janmanaiva dharma-j~nAna-vairAgyaishvaryAtishayam prAptAnAm kapilo muniH ||BhGS_10.26|| 

==============================

uccaiHshravasam ashvAnAm viddhi mAm amR^itodbhavam |
airAvatam gajendrANAm narANAm ca narAdhipam ||BhG_10.27||

ucaiHshravasam a vAnAm ucaiHshravAH nAmA varAjas tam mAm viddhi vijAnIhy amR^itodbhavam amR^ita-nimitta-mathanodbhavam | airAvatam irAvatyAH apatyam gajendrANAm hastIshvarANAm, tam mAm viddhIty anuvartate | narANAm ca manuShyANAm narAdhipam rAjAnam mAm viddhi jAnIhi ||BhGS_10.27|| 

==============================

AyudhAnAm aham vajram dhenUnAm asmi kAma-dhuk |
prajanash cAsmi kandarpaH sarpANAm asmi vAsukiH ||BhG_10.28||

AyudhAnAm aham vajram dadhIcy-asthi-sambhavam | dhenUnAm dogdhrINAm asmi kAma-dhuk vasiShThasya sarva-kAmAnAm dogdhrI, sAmAnyA vA kAma-dhuk | prajanaH prajanayitAsmi kandarpaH kAmaH | sarpANAm sarpa-bhedAnAm asmi vAsukiH sarpa-rAjaH ||BhGS_10.28|| 

==============================

anantash cAsmi nAgAnAm varuNo yAdasAm aham |
pitÌNAm aryamA cAsmi yamaH samyamatAm aham ||BhG_10.29||

anantash cAsmi nAgAnAm nAga-visheShANAm nAgarAjash cAsmi | varuNo yAdasAm aham ab-devatAnAm rAjAham | pitÌNAm aryamA nAma pitR^i-rAjash cAsmi | yamaH samyamatAm samyamanam kurvatAm aham ||BhGS_10.29|| 

==============================

prahlAdash cAsmi daityAnAm kAlaH kalayatAm aham |
mR^igANAm ca mR^igendro 'ham vainateyash ca pakShiNAm ||BhG_10.30||

prahlAdo nAmash cAsmi daityAnAm diti-vamshyAnAm | kAlaH kalayatAm kalanam gaNanam kurvatAm aham | mR^igANAm ca mR^igendraH simho vyAghro vAham | vainateyash ca garutmAn vinatA-sutaH pakShiNAm patatriNAm ||BhGS_10.30|| 

==============================

pavanaH pavatAm asmi rAmaH shastra-bhR^itAm aham |
jhaShANAm makarash cAsmi srotasAm asmi jAhnavI ||BhG_10.31||

pavano vAyuH pavatAm pAvayitaÌNAm asmi | rAmaH shastra-bhR^itAm aham shastrANAm dhArayitÌNAm dAsharathiH rAmo 'ham | jhaShANAm matsyAdInAm makaro nAma jAti-visheSho 'ham | srotasAm sravantInAm asmi jAhnavI gaN^gA ||BhGS_10.31|| 

==============================

sargANAm Adir antash ca madhyam caivAham arjuna |
adhyAtma-vidyA vidyAnAm vAdaH pravadatAm aham ||BhG_10.32||

sargANAm sR^iShTInAm Adir antash ca madhyam caivAham utpatti-sthiti-layA aham arjuna | bhUtAnAm jIvAdhiShThitAnAm eva Adir antash cety Ady uktam upakrame, iha tu sarvasyaiva sarga-mAtrasyeti visheShaH | adhyAtma-vidyA vidyAnAm mokShArthatvAt pradhAnam asmi | vAdo 'rtha-nirNaya-hetutvAt pravadatAm pradhAnam, ataH so 'ham asmi | pravaktR^i-dvAreNa vadana-bhedAnAm eva vAda-jalpa-vitaNDAnAm iha grahaNam pravadatAm iti ||BhGS_10.32|| 

==============================

akSharANAm akAro 'smi dvandvaH sAmAsikasya ca |
aham evAkShayaH kAlo dhAtAham vishvato-mukhaH ||BhG_10.33||

akSharANAm varNAnAm akAro varNo 'smi | dvandvaH samAso 'smi sAmAsikasya ca samAsa-samUhasya | kim cAham evAkShayaH kAlaH prasiddhaH kShaNAdy-AkhyaH, athavA parameshvaraH kAlasyApi kAlo 'smi | dhAtAham karma-phalasya vidhAtA sarva-jagato vishvato-mukhaH sarvato-mukhaH ||BhGS_10.33|| 

==============================

mR^ityuH sarva-harash cAham udbhavash ca bhaviShyatAm |
kIrtiH shrIr vAk ca nArINAm smR^itir medhA dhR^itiH kShamA ||BhG_10.34||

mR^ityur dvividho dhanAdi-haraH prANa-harash ca | tatra yaH prANa-haraH, sa sarva-hara ucyate | so 'ham ity arthaH | athavA, para IshvaraH pralaye sarva-haraNAt sarva-haraH, so 'ham | udbhava utkarShaH abhyudayas tat-prApti-hetush cAham | keShAm ? bhaviShyatAm bhAvi-kalyANAnAm, utkarSha-prApti-yogyAnAm ity arthaH | kIrtiH shrIH vAk ca nArINAm smR^itir medhA dhR^itiH kShamA ity etA uttamAH strINAm aham asmi, yAsAm AbhAsa-mAtra-sambandhenApi lokaH kR^itArtham AtmAnam manyate ||BhGS_10.34|| 

==============================

bR^ihat-sAma tathA sAmnAm gAyatrI chandasAm aham |
mAsAnAm mArgashIrSho 'ham R^itUnAm kusumAkaraH ||BhG_10.35||

bR^ihat-sAma tathA sAmnAm pradhAnam asmi | gAyatrI cchandasAm aham gAyatry-Adi-cchando-vishiShTAnAm R^icAm gAyatrI R^ig aham asmIty arthaH | mAsAnAm mArgashIrSho 'ham, R^itUnAm kusumAkaro vasantaH ||BhGS_10.35|| 

==============================

dyUtam chalayatAm asmi tejas tejasvinAm aham |
jayo 'smi vyavasAyo 'smi sattvam sattvavatAm aham ||BhG_10.36||

dyUtam akSha-devanAdi-lakShaNam chalayatAm chalasya kartÌNAm asmi | tejasvinAm tejo 'ham | jayo 'smi jetÌNAm | vyavasAyo 'smi vyavasAyinAm | sattvam sattvavatAm sAttvikAnAm aham ||BhGS_10.36|| 

==============================

vR^iShNInAm vAsudevo 'smi pANDavAnAm dhanamjayaH |
munInAm apy aham vyAsaH kavInAm ushanA kaviH ||BhG_10.37||

vR^iShNInAm yAdavAnAm vAsudevo 'smy ayam evAham tvatsakhaH | pANDAvAnAm dhanamjayas tvam eva | munInIm mananashIlAnAm sarvapadArthaj~nAninAm apy aham vyAsaH, kavInAm ktrAntadarshinAm ushanA kavir asmi ||BhGS_10.37|| 

==============================

daNDo damayatAm asmi nItir asmi jigIShatAm |
maunam caivAsmi guhyAnAm j~nAnam j~nAnavatAm aham ||BhG_10.38||

daNDo damayatAm damayitÌNAm asmy adAntAnAm damana-kAraH | nItir asmi jigIShatAm jetum icchatAm | maunam caivAsmi guhyAnAm gopyAnAm | j~nAnam j~nAnavatAm aham ||BhGS_10.38|| 

==============================

yac cApi sarva-bhUtAnAm bIjam tad aham arjuna |
na tad asti vinA yat syAn mayA bhUtam carAcaram ||BhG_10.39||

yac cApi sarva-bhUtAnAm bIjam praroha-kAraNam, tad aham arjuna | prakaraNopa-samhArArtham vibhUti-samkShepam Aha - na tad asti bhUtam carAcaram caram acaram vA, mayA vinA yat syAt bhavet | mayApakR^iShTam parityaktam nirAtmakam shUnyam hi tat syAt | ato mad-Atmakam sarvam ity arthaH ||BhGS_10.39|| 

==============================

nAnto 'sti mama divyAnAm vibhUtInAm parantapa |
eSha tUddeshataH prokto vibhUter vistaro mayA ||BhG_10.40||

nAnto 'sti mama divyAnAm vibhUtInAm vistarANAm parantapa | na hIshvarasya sarvAtmano divyAnAm vibhUtInAm iyattA shakyA vaktum j~nAtum vA kenacit | eSha tUddeshata eka-deshena prokto vibhUter vistaraH mayA ||BhGS_10.40|| 

==============================

yad yad vibhUtimat sattvam shrImad Urjitam eva vA |
tat tad evAvagaccha tvam mama tejo 'msha-sambhavam ||BhG_10.41||

yad yal loke vibhUtimad vibhUti-yuktam sattvam vastu shrImad Urjitam eva vA shrIr lakShmIs tayA sahitam utsAhopetam vA | tat tad evAvagaccha tvam jAnIhi mameshvarasya tejo 'msha-sambhavam tejaso 'msha eka-deshaH sambhavo yasya tat tejo 'msha-sambhavam ity avagaccha tvam ||BhGS_10.41|| 

==============================

atha vA bahunaitena kim j~nAtena tavArjuna |
viShTabhyAham idam kR^itsnam ekAmshena sthito jagat ||BhG_10.42||

athavA bahunaitena evam AdinA kim j~nAtena tavArjuna syAt sAvasheSheNa | asheShatas tvam ucyamAnam artham sR^iNu - viShTabhya visheShataH stambhanam dR^iDham kR^itvedam kR^itsnam jagad ekAmshenaikAvayavenaika-pAdena, sarva-bhUta-svarUpeNety etat | tathA ca mantra-varNaH - pAdo 'sya vishvA bhUtAni [ãk 8.4.17.3] iti | sthito 'ham iti ||BhGS_10.42|| 

iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovandibhagavatpUjyapAda-
shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^itau shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye
dashamo 'dhyAyaH ||


__________________________________________________________

BhG 11

athaikAdasho 'dhyAyaH
vishva-rUpa-darshana-yogaH

(shrI-shaN^karAcArya-bhagavat-pAda-kR^ita-bhAShyam)

bhagavato vibhUtaya uktAH | tatra ca viShTabhyAham idam kR^itsnam ekAmshena sthito jagat [GItA 10.42] iti bhagavatAbhihitam shrutvA yat jagad-Atma-rUpam, Adyam aishvaram tat sAkShAt-kartum icchann arjuna uvAca - 

mad-anugrahAya paramam guhyam adhyAtma-samj~nitam |
yat tvayoktam vacas tena moho 'yam vigato mama ||BhG_11.1||

mad-anugrahAya mamAnugrahArtham paramam niratishayam guhyam gopyam adhyAtma-samj~nitam AtmAnAtma-viveka-viShayam yat tvayoktam vaco vAkyam tena te vacasA moho 'yam vigato mama | aviveka-buddhir apagatety arthaH ||BhGS_11.1|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

bhavApyayau hi bhUtAnAm shrutau vistarasho mayA |
tvattaH kamala-patrAkSha mAhAtmyam api cAvyayam ||BhG_11.2||

bhava utpattir apyayaH pralayas tau bhavApyayau hi bhUtAnAm shrutau vistarashaH mayA, na samkShepataH | tvattas tvat-sakAshAt | kamala-patrAkSha kamalasya patram kamala-patram tadvad akShiNI yasya tava sa tvam kamala-patrAkSho, he kamalapatrAkSha ! mahAtmano bhAvo mAhAtmyam api cAvyayam akShayam | shrutam ity anuvartate ||BhGS_11.2|| 

==============================

evam etad yathAttha tvam AtmAnam parameshvara |
draShTum icchAmi te rUpam aishvaram puruShottama ||BhG_11.3||

evam etan nAnyathA yathA yena prakAreNa Attha kathayasi tvam AtmAnam parameshvara | tathApi draShTum icchAmi te tava j~nAnaishvarya-shakti-bala-vIrya-tejobhiH sampannam aishvaram vaiShNavam rUpam puruShottama ||BhGS_11.3||

==============================

manyase yadi tac chakyam mayA draShTum iti prabho |
yogeshvara tato me tvam darshayAtmAnam avyayam ||BhG_11.4||

manyase cintayasi yadi mayArjunena tac chakyam draShTum iti prabho ! svAmin ! yogeshvara yogino yogAs teShAm Ishvaro yogeshvaraH, he yogeshvara ! yasmAd aham atIvArthI draShTum, tatas tasmAn me mad-artham tvam AtmAnam avyayam ||BhGS_11.4|| 

==============================

evam codito 'rjunena bhagavAn uvAca - 

pashya me pArtha rUpANi shatasho 'tha sahasrashaH |
nAnA-vidhAni divyAni nAnA-varNAkR^itIni ca ||BhG_11.5||

pashya me pArtha ! rUpANi shatasho 'tha sahasrashaH | anekasha ity arthaH | tAni ca nAnA-vidhAny aneka-prakArANi divi bhavAni divyAny aprAkR^itAni nAnA-varNAkR^itIni ca nAnA vilakShaNA nIla-pItAdi-prakArA varNAs tathAkR^itayash cAvayava-samsthAna-visheSho yeShAm rUpANAm tAni nAnA-varNAkR^itInI ca ||BhGS_11.5|| 

==============================

pashyAdityAn vasUn rudrAn ashvinau marutas tathA |
bahUny adR^iShTa-pUrvANi pashyAshcaryANi bhArata ||BhG_11.6||

pashyAdityAn dvAdasha | vasUn aShTau | rudrAn ekAdasha | ashvinau dvau | marutaH sapta-sapta-gaNA ye tAn | tathA ca bahUny anyAny apy adR^iShTa-pUrvANi manuShya-loke tvayA tvatto 'nyena vA kenacit | pashyAshcaryANy adbhutAni bhArata ||BhGS_11.6|| 

==============================

na kevalam etAvad eva - 

ihaikastham jagat kR^itsnam pashyAdya sa-carAcaram |
mama dehe guDAkesha yac cAnyad draShTum icchasi ||BhG_11.7||

ihaika-stham ekasminn eva sthitam jagat kR^itsnam samastam pashyAdya idAnIm sa-carAcaram saha careNAcareNa ca vartate mama dehe guDAkesha | yac cAnyat jaya-parAjayAdi | yat shaN^kase, yad vA jayema yadi vA no jayeyur [GItA 2.6] iti yat avocaH, tad api draShTum yadIcchasi ||BhGS_11.7|| 

==============================

kim tu - 
na tu mAm shakyase draShTum anenaiva sva-cakShuShA |
divyam dadAmi te cakShuH pashya me yogam aishvaram ||BhG_11.8||

na tu mAm vishva-rUpa-dharam shakyase draShTum anenaiva prAkR^itena sva-cakShuShA svakIyena cakShuShA | yena tu shakyase draShTum divyena, tad divyam dadAmi te tubhyam cakShuH | tena pashya me yogam aishvaram Ishvarasya mama aishvaram yogam yoga-shakty-atishayam ity arthaH ||BhGS_11.8|| 

==============================

samjaya uvAca - 

evam uktvA tato rAjan mahA-yogeshvaro hariH |
darshayAm Asa pArthAya paramam rUpam aishvaram ||BhG_11.9||

evam yathokta-prakAreNoktvA tato 'nantaram rAjan dhR^itarAShTra ! mahA-yogeshvaro mahAmsh cAsau yogeshvarash mahA-yogeshvaro harir nArAyaNo darshayAmAsa darshitavAn pArthAya pR^ithA-sutAya paramam rUpam vishva-rUpam aishvaram ||BhGS_11.9||

==============================

aneka-vaktra-nayanam anekAdbhuta-darshanam |
aneka-divyAbharaNam divyAnekodyatAyudham ||BhG_11.10||

aneka-vaktra-nayanam anekAni vaktrANi nayanAni ca yasmin rUpe tad aneka-vaktra-nayanam, anekAdbhuta-darshanam anekAny adbhutAni vismApakAni darshanAni yasmin rUpe tad anekAdbhuta-darshanam rUpam | tathAneka-divyAbharaNam anekAni divyAny AbharaNAni yasmin tad aneka-divyAbharaNam | tathA divyAnekodyatAyudham divyAny anekAny asyAdIni udyatAny AyudhAni yasmin tad divyAnekodyatAyudham | darshayAmAseti pUrveNa sambandhaH ||BhGS_11.10|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

divya-mAlyAmbara-dharam divya-gandhAnulepanam |
sarvAshcarya-mayam devam anantam vishvato-mukham ||BhG_11.11||

divya-mAlyAmbara-dharam divyAni mAlyAni puShpANy ambarANi vasrANi ca dhriyante yeneshvareNa tam divya-mAlyAmbara-dharam, divya-gandhAnulepanam divyam gandhAnulepanam yasya tam divya-gandhAnulepanam, sarvAshcarya-mayam sarvAshcarya-prAyam devam anantam nAsyAnto 'stIty anantas tam, vishvato-mukham sarvato-mukham sarva-bhUtAtma-bhUtatvAt, tam darshayAmAsa | arjuno dadarsheti vAdhyAhriyate ||BhGS_11.11||

==============================

yA punar bhagavato vishva-rUpasya bhAH, tasyA upamocyate - 

divi sUrya-sahasrasya bhaved yugapad utthitA |
yadi bhAH sadR^ishI sA syAd bhAsas tasya mahAtmanaH ||BhG_11.12||

antarikShe vA divi sUryANAm sahasram sUrya-sahasram tasya yugapad utthitasya sUrya-sahasrasya yA yugapad utthitA bhAH, sA yadi, sadR^ishI syAt tasya mahAtmano vishva-rUpasyaiva bhAsaH | yadi vA na syAt, tato vishva-rUpasyaiva bhA atiricyate ity abhiprAyaH ||BhGS_11.12||

==============================

kim ca - 
tatraikastham jagat kR^itsnam pravibhaktam anekadhA |
apashyad deva-devasya sharIre pANDavas tadA ||BhG_11.13||

tatra tasmin vishva-rUpa ekasmin sthitam eka-stham jagat kR^itsnam pravibhaktam anekadhA deva-pitR^i-manuShyAdi-bhedair apashyad dR^iShTavAn deva-devasya hareH sharIre pANDAvo 'rjunas tadA ||BhGS_11.13|| 

==============================

tataH sa vismayAviShTo hR^iShTa-romA dhanamjayaH |
praNamya shirasA devam kR^itA¤jalir abhAShata ||BhG_11.14||

tatas tam dR^iShTvA sa vismayenAviShTo vismayAviShTo hR^iShTAni romANi yasya so 'yam hR^iShTa-romA cAbhavad dhana¤jayaH | praNamya prakarSheNa namanam kR^itvA prahvI-bhUtaH san shirasA devam vishva-rUpa-dharam kR^itA¤jaliH namaskArArtham sampuTIkR^ita-hastaH sann abhAShata uktavAn ||BhGS_11.14|| 

==============================

katham ? yat tvayA darshitam vishva-rUpam, tad aham pashyAmIti svAnubhavam AviShkurvann arjuna uvAca - 

pashyAmi devAms tava deva dehe
sarvAms tathA bhUta-visheSha-samghAn |
brahmANam Isham kamalAsana-stham
R^iShImsh ca sarvAn uragAmsh ca divyAn ||BhG_11.15||

pashyAmy upalabhe he deva, tava dehe devAn sarvAn, tathA bhUta-visheSha-samghAn bhUta-visheShANAm sthAvara-jaN^gamAnAm nAnA-samsthAna-visheShANAm samghA bhUta-visheSha-samghAs tAn, kim ca - brahmANam catur-mukham Isham IshitAram prajAnAm kamalAsana-stham pR^ithivI-padma-madhye meru-karNikAsana-stham ity arthaH | R^iShImsh ca vasiShThAdIn sarvAn, uragAmsh ca vAsuki-prabhR^itIn divyAn divi bhavAn ||BhGS_11.15||

==============================


aneka-bAhUdara-vaktra-netram
pashyAmi tvA sarvato 'nanta-rUpam |
nAntam na madhyam na punas tavAdim
pashyAmi vishveshvara vishva-rUpa ||BhG_11.16||

aneka-bAhUdara-vaktra-netram aneke bAhavar udarANi vaktrANi netrANi ca yasya tava sa tvam aneka-bAhUdara-vaktra-netras tam aneka-bAhUdara-vaktra-netram | pashyAmi tvA tvAm sarvataH sarvatrAnanta-rUpam anantAni rUpANy asya ity ananta-rUpas tam ananta-rUpam | nAntam, anto 'vasAnam, na madhyam, madhyam nAma dvayoH koTyor antaram | na punas tavAdim - na devasyAntam pashyAmi, na madhyam pashyAmi, na punar Adim pashyAmi | he vishveshvara vishva-rUpa ||BhGS_11.16|| 

==============================

kim ca - 
kirITinam gadinam cakriNam ca
tejo-rAshim sarvato dIptimantam |
pashyAmi tvAm durnirIkShyam samantAd
dIptAnalArka-dyutim aprameyam ||BhG_11.17||

kirITiAnam kirITAm nAma shirobhUShaNavisheShas tat yasyAsti saH kirITI tam kirITiAnam, tathA gadinam gadAsya vidyate iti gadI tam gadinam, tathA cakriNam caktram asyAstIti cakrI tam cakriNam ca, tejo-rAshim tejaHpujam sarvatodIptimantam sarvatodIptir asyAstIti sarvatodIptimAn, tam sarvatodIptimantam pashyAmi tvAm durnirIkShyam samantAt samantataH sarvatra dIptAnalArkadyutim analash cArkash cAnalArkau dIptau analArkau dIptAnalArkau tayoH dIptAnalArkayoH dyutiriva dyutis tejo yasya tava sa tvam dIptAnalArkadyutis tam tvAm dIptAnalArkadyatim aprameyam na prameyam ashakyaparicchedam ity etat ||BhGS_11.17||

==============================

ita eva te yoga-shakti-darshanAt anuminomi - 

tvam akSharam paramam veditavyam
tvam asya vishvasya param nidhAnam |
tvam avyayaH shAshvata-dharma-goptA
sanAtanas tvam puruSho mato me ||BhG_11.18||

tvam akSharam na kSharatIti, paramam brahma veditavyam j~nAtavyam mumukShubhiH | tvam asya vishvasya samastasya jagataH param prakR^iShTam nidhAnam nidhIyate 'sminn iti nidhAnam para Ashraya ity arthaH | kim ca, tvam avyayo na tava vyayo vidyata ity avyayaH | shAshvata-dharma-goptA shashvad-bhavaH shAshvato nityo dharmas tasya goptA shAshvata-dharma-goptA | sanAtanash cirantanas tvam puruShaH paramaH mato 'bhipretaH me mama ||BhGS_11.18|| 

==============================

kim ca - 
anAdi-madhyAntam ananta-vIryam
ananta-bAhum shashi-sUrya-netram |
pashyAmi tvAm dIpta-hutAsha-vaktram
sva-tejasA vishvam idam tapantam ||BhG_11.19||

anAdi-madhyAntam Adi ca madhyam cAntash ca na vidyate yasya so 'yam anAdi-madhyAntas, tam tvAm anAdi-madhyAntam | ananta-vIryam na tava vIryasyAnto 'stIty ananta-vIryas, tam tvAm ananta-vIryam | tathAnanta-bAhum anantA bAhavo yasya tava sa tvam, ananta-bAhus tam tvAm ananta-bAhum | shashi-sUrya-netram shashi-sUryau netre yasya tava sa tvam shashi-sUrya-netras, tam tvAm shashi-sUrya-netram candrAditya-nayanam | pashyAmi tvAm dIpta-hutAsha-vaktram dIptash cAsau hutAshash ca vaktram yasya tava sa tvam dIpta-hutAsha-vaktras, tam tvAm dIpta-hutAsha-vaktram | sva-tejasA vishvam idam samastam tapantam || 

==============================

dyAv-ApR^ithivyor idam antaram hi
vyAptam tvayaikena dishash ca sarvAH |
dR^iShTvAdbhutam rUpam idam tavogram
loka-trayam pravyathitam mahAtman ||BhG_11.20||

dyAv-ApR^ithivyor idam antaram hy antarikSham vyAptam tvayaikena vishva-rUpa-dhareNa dishash ca sarvA vyAptAH | dR^iShTvA upalabhyAdbhutam vismApakam rUpam idam tavogram krUram lokAnAm trayam loka-trayam pravyathitam bhItam pracalitam vA | he mahAtman ! akShudra-svabhAva ||BhGS_11.20|| 

==============================

athAdhunA purA yad vA jayema yadi vA no jayeyuH [GItA 2.6] ity arjunasya yaH samshaya AsIt, tan-nirNayAya pANDava-jayam aikAntikam darshayAmIti pravR^itto bhagavAn | tam pashyann Aha | kim ca -
amI hi tvA sura-samghA vishanti
kecid bhItAH prA¤jalayo gR^iNanti |
svastIty uktvA maharShi-siddha-samghAH
stuvanti tvAm stutibhiH puShkalAbhiH ||BhG_11.21||

amI hi yudhyamAnA yoddhAras tvA tvAm sura-samghAH ye 'tra bhU-bhArAvatArAyAvatIrNA vasv-Adi-deva-samghA manuShya-samsthAnAs tvAm vishanti pravishanto dR^ishyante | tatra kecit bhItAH prA¤jalayaH santo gR^iNanti stuvanti tvAm anye palAyane 'py ashaktAH santaH | yuddhe pratyupasthita utpAtAdi-nimittAni upalakShya svasty astu jagata iti uktvA maharShi-siddha-samghAH maharShINAm siddhAnAm ca samghAH stuvanti tvAm stutibhiH puShkalAbhiH sampUrNAbhiH ||BhGS_11.21|| 

==============================

kim cAnyat - 
rudrAdityA vasavo ye ca sAdhyA
vishve 'shvinau marutash coShmapAsh ca |
gandharva-yakShAsura-siddha-samghA
vIkShante tvAm vismitAsh caiva sarve ||BhG_11.22||

rudrAdityAH vasavo ye ca sAdhyAH rudrAdayo gaNAH vishve-devA ashvinau ca devau marutash ca UShmapA ca pitaraH, gandharvayakShAsurasiddhasamghAH gandharShaH hAhAhUhUprabhR^itayo yakShAH kuberaprabhR^itayo 'surAH virocanaprabhR^itayaH siddhAH kapilAdayas teShAm samghAH gandharvayakShAsurasiddhasamghAH, te vIkShante pashyanti tvAm vismitAH vismayamApannAH santas te eva sarve ||BhGS_11.22|| 

==============================

yasmAt - 
rUpam mahat te bahu-vaktra-netram
mahA-bAho bahu-bAhUru-pAdam |
bahUdaram bahu-damShTrA-karAlam
dR^iShTvA lokAH pravyathitAs tathAham ||BhG_11.23||

rUpam mahad atipramANam te tava bahu-vaktra-netram bahUni vaktrANi mukhAni cakShUmShi ca yasmin tad rUpam bahu-vaktra-netram | he mahA-bAho ! bahu-bAhUru-pAdam bahavo bAhava UravaH pAdAsh ca yasmin rUpe tad bahu-bAhUru-pAdam | kim ca, bahUdaram bahUni udarANi yasminn iti bahUdaram | bahu-damShTrA-karAlam bahvIbhir damShTrAbhiH karAlam vikR^itam tad bahu-damShTrA-karAlam | dR^iShTvA rUpam IdR^isham lokA laukikAH prANinaH pravyathitAH pracalitA bhayena | tathAham api ||BhGS_11.23|| 

==============================

tatredam kAraNam - 
nabhaH-spR^isham dIptam aneka-varNam
vyAttAnanam dIpta-vishAla-netram |
dR^iShTvA hi tvAm pravyathitAntarAtmA
dhR^itim na vindAmi shamam ca viShNo ||BhG_11.24||

nabhaH-spR^isham dyu-sparsham ity arthaH | dIptam prajvalitam | aneka-varNam aneke varNA bhayaN^karAH nAnA-samsthAnA yasmin tvayi tam tvAm aneka-varNam | vyAttAnanam vyAttAni vivR^itAni AnanAni mukhAni yasmin tvayi tam tvAm vyAttAnanam | dIpta-vishAla-netram dIptAni prajvalitAni vishAlAni vistIrNAni netrANi yasmin tvayi tam tvAm dIpta-vishAla-netram dR^iShTvA hi tvAm pravyathitAntarAtmA pravyathitaH prabhIto 'ntarAtmA mano yasya mama so 'ham pravyathitAntarAtmA san dhR^itim dhairyam na vindAmi na labhe shamam copashamanam manas-tuShTim | he viShNo ||BhGS_11.24|| 

==============================
 
kasmAt ? 
damShTrA-karAlAni ca te mukhAni
dR^iShTvaiva kAlAnala-samnibhAni |
disho na jAne na labhe ca sharma
prasIda devesha jagan-nivAsa ||BhG_11.25||

damShTrA-karAlAni damShTrAbhiH karAlAni vikR^itAni te tava mukhAni dR^iShTvaivopalabhya kAlAnala-samnibhAni pralaya-kAle lokAnAm dAhako 'gniH kAlAnalas tat-sadR^ishAni kAlAnala-samnibhAni mukhAni dR^iShTvety etat | dishaH pUrvApara-vivekena na jAne diN^-mUDho jAto 'smi | ato na labhe ca nopalabhe ca sharma sukham | ataH prasIda prasanno bhava he devesha, jagan-nivAsa ||BhGS_11.25|| 

==============================

yebhyo mama parAjayAshaN^kA yAsIt sA cApagatA | yataH - 

amI ca tvAm dhR^itarAShTrasya putrAH
sarve sahaivAvanipAla-samghaiH |
bhIShmo droNaH sUta-putras tathAsau
sahAsmadIyair api yodha-mukhyaiH ||BhG_11.26||

amI ca tvAm dhR^itarAShTrasya putrAH duryodhana-prabhR^itayaH - tvaramANAH vishantIti vyavahitena sambandhaH - sarve sahaiva sahitAH avani-pAla-samghair avanim pR^ithvIm pAlayantIty avani-pAlAs teShAm samghaiH, kim ca bhIShmo droNaH sUta-putraH karNas tathAsau sahAsmadIyair api dhR^iShTadyumna-prabhR^itibhir yodha-mukhyair yodhAnAm mukhyaiH pradhAnaiH saha ||BhGS_11.26|| 

==============================

kim ca - 
vaktrANi te tvaramANA vishanti
damShTrA-karAlAni bhayAnakAni |
kecid vilagnA dashanAntareShu
sandR^ishyante cUrNitair uttamAN^gaiH ||BhG_11.27||

vaktrANi mukhAni te tava tvaramANAs tvarA-yuktAH santo vishanti | kim-vishiShTani mukhAni ? damShTrA-karAlAni bhayAnakAni bhayaN^karANi | kim ca, kecit mukhAni praviShTAnAm madhye vilagnA dashanAntareShu mAmsam iva bhakShitam samdR^ishyanta upalabhyante cUrNitaish cUrNIkR^itair uttamAN^gaiH shirobhiH ||BhGS_11.27||

==============================

katham pravishanti mukhAni ? ity Aha - 

yathA nadInAm bahavo 'mbu-vegAH
samudram evAbhimukhA dravanti |
tathA tavAmI nara-loka-vIrA
vishanti vaktrANy abhivijvalanti ||BhG_11.28||

yathA nadInAm sravantInAm bahavo 'neke 'mbUnAm vegA ambu-vegAs tvarA-visheShAH samudram evAbhimukhAH pratimukhA dravanti pravishanti | tathA tadvat tavAmI bhIShmAdayo nara-loka-vIrA manuShya-loke shUrAH vishanti vaktrANy abhivijvalanti prakAshamAnAni ||BhGS_11.28|| 

==============================

te kim-artham pravishanti katham ca ? ity Aha - 

yathA pradIptam jvalanam pataN^gA
vishanti nAshAya samR^iddha-vegAH |
tathaiva nAshAya vishanti lokAs
tavApi vaktrANi samR^iddha-vegAH ||BhG_11.29||

yathA pradIptam jvalanam agnim pataN^gAH pakShiNo vishanti nAshAya vinAshAya samR^iddha-vegAH samR^iddha udbhUto vego gatir yeShAm te samR^iddha-vegAH | tathaiva nAshAya vishanti lokAH prANinas tavApi vaktrANi samR^iddha-vegAH ||BhGS_11.29|| 

==============================

tvam punaH - 

lelihyase grasamAnaH samantAl
lokAn samagrAn vadanair jvaladbhiH |
tejobhir ApUrya jagat samagram
bhAsas tavogrAH pratapanti viShNo ||BhG_11.30||

lelihyase AsvAdayasi grasamAno 'ntaH praveshayan samantAt samantataH lokAn samagrAn samastAn vadanair vaktrair jvaladbhir dIpyamAnais tejobhir ApUrya samvyApya jagat samagram sahAgreNa samastam ity etat | kim ca, bhAso dIptayas tavogrAH krUrAH pratapanti pratApam kurvanti he viShNo vyApana-shIla ||BhGS_11.30||

==============================

yataH evam ugra-svabhAvaH, ataH - 

AkhyAhi me ko bhavAn ugra-rUpo
namo 'stu te deva-vara prasIda |
vij~nAtum icchAmi bhavantam Adyam
na hi prajAnAmi tava pravR^ittim ||BhG_11.31||

AkhyAhi kathaya me mahyam ko bhavAn ugra-rUpaH krUrAkAraH | namo 'stu te tubhyam he deva-vara devAnAm pradhAna, prasIda prasAdam kuru | vij~nAtum visheSheNa j~nAtum icchAmi bhavantam Adyam Adau bhavam Adyam, na hi yasmAt prajAnAmi tava tvadIyAm pravR^ittim ceShTam ||BhGS_11.31||

==============================

shrI-bhagavAn uvAca - 
kAlo 'smi loka-kShaya-kR^it pravR^iddho
lokAn samAhartum iha pravR^ittaH |
R^ite 'pi tvA na bhaviShyanti sarve
ye 'vasthitAH pratyanIkeShu yodhAH ||BhG_11.32||

kAlo 'smi loka-kShaya-kR^it lokAnAm kShayam karotIti loka-kShaya-kR^it pravR^iddho vR^iddhim gataH | yad-artham pravR^iddhas tac chR^iNu - lokAn samAhartum samhartum ihAsmin kAle pravR^ittaH | R^ite 'pi vinApi tvA tvAm na bhaviShyanti bhIShma-droNa-karNa-prabhR^itayaH sarve, yebhyas tava AshaN^kA, ye 'vasthitAH pratyanIkeShu anIkam anIkam prati pratyanIkeShu pratipakSha-bhUteShu anIkeShu yodhA yoddhAraH ||BhGS_11.32|| 

==============================

yasmAd evam - 
tasmAt tvam uttiShTha yasho labhasva
jitvA shatrUn bhuN^kShva rAjyam samR^iddham |
mayaivaite nihatAH pUrvam eva
nimitta-mAtram bhava savyasAcin ||BhG_11.33||

tasmAt tvam uttiShTha bhIShma-prabhR^itayo 'tirathA ajeyA devair apy arjunena jitA iti yashaH labhasva | kevalam puNyair hi tat prApyate | jitvA shatrUn duryodhana-prabhR^itIn bhuN^kShva rAjyam samR^iddham asapatnam akaNTakam | mayaivaite nihatA nishcayena hatAH prANair viyojitAH pUrvam eva | nimitta-mAtram bhava tvam | he savyasAcin ! savyena vAmenApi hastena sharANAm kShepAt savyasAcIty ucyate 'rjunaH ||BhGS_11.33||

==============================

droNam ca bhIShmam ca jayadratham ca
karNam tathAnyAn api yodha-vIrAn |
mayA hatAms tvam jahi mA vyathiShThA
yudhyasva jetAsi raNe sapatnAn ||BhG_11.34||

droNam ca, yeShu yeShu yodheShv arjunasyAshaN^kA tAms tAn vyapadishati bhagavAn mayA hatAn iti | tatra droNa-bhIShmayos tAvat prasiddham AshaN^kA-kAraNam | droNas tu dhanur-vedAcAryo divyAstra-sampannaH | Atmanash ca visheShato gurur gariShThaH | bhIShmash ca svacchanda-mR^ityur divyAstra-sampannash ca parashurAmeNa dvandva-yuddham agamat, na ca parAjitaH | tathA jayadrathaH | yasya pitA tapash carati mama putrasya shiro bhUmau nipAtayiShyati yaH, tasyApi shiraH patiShyatIti | karNo 'pi vAsava-dattayA shaktyA tv amoghayA sampannaH sUrya-putraH kAnIno yataH, atas tan-nAmnaiva nirdeshaH | mayA hatAn tvam jahi nimitta-mAtreNa | mA vyathiShThAs tebhyo bhayam mA kArShIH | yudhyasva jetAsi duryodhana-prabhR^itIn raNe yuddhe sapatnAn shatrUn ||BhGS_11.34|| 

==============================

samjaya uvAca - 

etac chrutvA vacanam keshavasya
kR^itA¤jalir vepamAnaH kirITI |
namaskR^itvA bhUya evAha kR^iShNam
sa-gadgadam bhIta-bhItaH praNamya ||BhG_11.35||

etat shrutvA vacanam keshavasya pUrvoktam kR^itA¤jaliH san vepamAnaH kampamAnaH kirITI namaskR^itvA | bhUyaH punar evAhoktavAn kR^iShNam sa-gadgadam bhayAviShTasya duHkhAbhighAtAt snehAviShTasya ca harShodbhavAt, ashru-pUrNa-netratve sati shleShmaNA kaNThAvarodhaH | tatash ca vAco 'pATavam manda-shabdatvam yat sa-gadgadas tena saha vartateti sa-gadgadam vacanam Aheti vacana-kriyA-visheShaNam etat | bhIta-bhItaH punaH punar bhayAviShTa-cetAH san praNamya prahvo bhUtvA | Aheti vyavahitena sambandhaH ||BhGS_11.35|| 

==============================

arjuna uvAca - 
sthAne hR^iShIkesha tava prakIrtyA
jagat prahR^iShyaty anurajyate ca |
rakShAmsi bhItAni disho dravanti
sarve namasyanti ca siddha-samghAH ||BhG_11.36||

sthAne yuktam | kim tat ? tava prakItryA tvan-mAhAtmya-kIrtanena shrutena | he hR^iShIkesha ! yat jagat prahR^iShyati praharSham upaiti, tat sthAne yuktam ity arthaH | athavA viShaya-visheShaNam sthAna iti | yukto harShAdi-viShayo bhagavAn, yata IshvaraH sarvAtmA sarva-bhUta-suhR^ic ceti | tathAnurajyate 'nurAgam copaiti | tac ca viShaya iti vyAkhyeyam | kim ca, rakShAmsi bhItAni bhayAviShTani disho dravanti gacchanti | tac ca sthAne viShaye | sarve namasyanti namaskurvanti ca siddha-samghAH siddhAnAm samudAyAH kapilAdInAm, tac ca sthAne ||BhGS_11.36||

==============================

bhagavato harShAdi-viShayatve hetum darshayati - 

kasmAc ca te na nameran mahAtman
garIyase brahmaNo 'py Adi-kartre |
ananta devesha jagan-nivAsa
tvam akSharam sad asat tat-param yat ||BhG_11.37||

kasmAc ca hetos te tubhyam na nameran namaskuryur he mahAtman ! garIyase gurutarAya | yato brahmaNo hiraNyagarbhasyApi Adi-kartA kAraNam atas tasmAd Adi-kartre | katham ete na namaskuryuH ? ato harShAdInAm namaskArasya ca sthAnam tvam arho viShaya ity arthaH | he 'nanta devesha he jagan-nivAsa tvam akSharam tat param, yad vedAnteShu shrUyate | kim tat ? sad asad iti | sad vidyamAnam, asac ca yatra nAstIti buddhiH | ta upadhAna-bhUte sad-asatI yasyAkSharasya, yad-dvAreNa sad asad ity upacaryate | paramArthatas tu sad-asatoH param tat akSharam yad akSharam veda-vido vadanti [GItA 8.11] | tat tvam eva, nAnyad ity abhiprAyaH ||BhGS_11.37||

==============================

punar api stauti - 
tvam Adi-devaH puruShaH purANas
tvam asya vishvasya param nidhAnam |
vettAsi vedyam ca param ca dhAma
tvayA tatam vishvam ananta-rUpa ||BhG_11.38||

tvam Adi-devo jagataH sraShTR^itvAt | puruShaH, puri shayanAt purANash cirantanas tvam evAsya vishvasya param prakR^iShTam nidhAnam nidhIyate 'smin jagat sarvam mahA-pralayAdAv iti | kim ca, vettAsi, veditAsi sarvasyaiva vedya-jAtasya | yac ca vedyam vedanArham tac cAsi param ca dhAma paramam padam vaiShNavam | tvayA tatam vyAptam vishvam samastam | he 'nanta-rUpa ! anto na vidyate tava rUpANAm ||BhGS_11.38|| 

==============================

kim ca - 
vAyur yamo 'gnir varuNaH shashAN^kaH
prajApatis tvam prapitAmahash ca |
namo namas te 'stu sahasra-kR^itvaH
punash ca bhUyo 'pi namo namas te ||BhG_11.39||

vAyus tvam yamash cAgniH varuNo 'pAm patiH shashAN^kash candramAH prajApatis tvam kashyapAdiH prapitAmahash ca pitAmahasyApi pitA prapitAmahaH, brahmaNo 'pi pitA ity arthaH | namo namas te tubhyam astu sahasra-kR^itvaH | punash ca bhUyo 'pi namo namas te | bahusho namaskAra-kriyAbhyAsAvR^itti-gaNanam kR^itva-sucocyate | punash ca bhUyo 'pIti shraddhA-bhakta-yati-shayAd aparitoSham Atmano darshayati ||BhGS_11.39|| 

==============================

tathA - 
namaH purastAd atha pR^iShThatas te
namo 'stu te sarvata eva sarva |
ananta-vIryAmita-vikramas tvam
sarvam samApnoShi tato 'si sarvaH ||BhG_11.40||

namaH purastAt pUrvasyAm dishi tubhyam, atha pR^iShThatas te pR^iShThato 'pi ca te namo 'stu te sarvata eva sarvAsu dikShu sarvatra sthitAya | he sarva ! ananta-vIryAmita-vikramo 'nantam vIryam asya, amito vikramo 'sya | vIryam sAmarthyam vikramaH parAkramaH | vIryavAn api kashcit shatru-vadhAdi-viShaye na parAkramate, manda-parAkramo vA | tvam tv ananta-vIryo 'mita-vikramash cety ananta-vIryAmita-vikramaH | sarvam samastam jagat samApnoShi samyag ekenAtmanA vyApnoShi yataH, tatas tasmAd asi bhavasi sarvas tvam | tvayA vinAbhUtam na kimcid astIty abhiprAyaH ||BhGS_11.40||

==============================

yato 'ham tvan-mAhAtmyAparij~nAnAd aparAddhaH | ataH - 

sakheti matvA prasabham yad uktam
he kR^iShNa he yAdava he sakheti |
ajAnatA mahimAnam tavedam
mayA pramAdAt praNayena vApi ||BhG_11.41||

sakhA samAna-vayA iti matvA j~nAtvA viparIta-buddhyA prasabham abhibhUya prasahya yad uktam he kR^iShNa he yAdava he sakheti cAjAnatAj~nAninA mUDhena | kim ajAnatA ? ity Aha - mahimAnam mAhAtmyam tavedam Ishvarasya vishva-rUpam | tavedam mahimAnam ajAnateti vaiyadhikaraNyena sambandhaH | tavemam iti pATho yady asti, tadA sAmAnAdhikaraNyam eva | mayA pramAdAt vikShipta-cittatayA, praNayena vApi | praNayo nAma sneha-nimitto visrambhaH | tenApi kAraNena yad uktavAn asmi ||BhGS_11.41|| 

==============================

yac cAvahAsArtham asatkR^ito 'si
vihAra-shayyAsana-bhojaneShu |
eko 'tha vApy acyuta tat-samakSham
tat kShAmaye tvAm aham aprameyam ||BhG_11.42||

yac cAvahAsArtham parihAsa-prayojanAyAsatkR^itaH paribhUto 'si bhavasi | kva ? vihAra-shayyAsana-bhojaneShu | viharaNam vihAraH pAda-vyAyAmaH, shayanam shayyA, Asanam AsthAyikA, bhojanam adanam, ity eteShu vihAra-shayyAsana-bhojaneShu, ekaH parokShaH sann asatkR^ito 'si paribhUto 'si | athavApi he 'cyuta ! tat samakSham, tac-chabdaH kriyA-visheShaNArthaH, pratyakSham vAsatkR^ito 'si tat sarvam aparAdha-jAtam kShAmaye kShamAm kAraye tvAm aham aprameyam pramANAtItam ||BhGS_11.42|| 

==============================

yatas tvam - 

pitAsi lokasya carAcarasya
tvam asya pUjyash ca gurur garIyAn |
na tvat-samo 'sty abhyadhikaH kuto 'nyo
loka-traye 'py apratima-prabhAva ||BhG_11.43||

pitAsi janayitAsi lokasya prANi-jAtasya carAcarasya sthAvara-jaN^gamasya | na kevalam tvam asya jagataH pitA | pUjyash ca pUjArhaH, yato gurur garIyAn gurutaraH | kasmAd gurutaras tvam ity Aha - na tvat-samas tvat-tulyo 'sti | na hIshvara-dvayam sambhavati, aneke varatve vyavahArAnupapatteH | tvat-sama eva tAvad anyo na sambhavati | kuta evAnyo 'bhyadhikaH syAt loka-traye 'pi sarvasmin ? apratima-prabhAva ! pratimIyate yayA sA pratimA, na vidyate pratimA yasya tava prabhAvasya sa tvam apratima-prabhAvo he 'pratima-prabhAva niratishaya-prabhAva ity arthaH ||BhGS_11.43|| 

==============================

yata evam - 

tasmAt praNamya praNidhAya kAyam
prasAdaye tvAm aham Isham IDyam |
piteva putrasya sakheva sakhyuH
priyaH priyAyArhasi deva soDhum ||BhG_11.44||

tasmAt praNamya namaskR^itya, praNidhAya prakarSheNa nIcair dhR^itvA kAyam sharIram, prasAdaye prasAdam kAraye tvAm aham Isham IshitAram, IDyam stutyam | tvam punaH putrasyAparAdham pitA yathA kShamate, sarvam sakheva sakhyur aparAdham, yathA vA priyaH priyAyA aparAdham kShamate | evam arhasi he deva ! soDhum prasahitum kShantum ity arthaH ||BhGS_11.44|| 

==============================

adR^iShTa-pUrvam hR^iShito 'smi dR^iShTvA
bhayena ca pravyathitam mano me |
tad eva me darshaya deva rUpam
prasIda devesha jagan-nivAsa ||BhG_11.45||

adR^iShTa-pUrvam na kadAcid api dR^iShTa-pUrvam idam vishva-rUpam tava mayAnyairvA, tat aham dR^iShTvA hR^iShito 'smi | bhayena ca pravyathitam manaH me | atas tad eva me mama darshaya he deva rUpam yat matsakham | prasIda devesha, jagan-nivAsa jagato nivAso jagan-nivAsaH, he jagan-nivAsa ||BhGS_11.45|| 

==============================

kirITinam gadinam cakra-hastam
icchAmi tvAm draShTum aham tathaiva |
tenaiva rUpeNa catur-bhujena
sahasra-bAho bhava vishva-mUrte ||BhG_11.46||

kirITinam kirITavantam tathA gadinam gadAvantam cakra-hastam icchAmi tvAm prArthaye tvAm draShTum aham, tathaiva pUrvavad ity arthaH | yata evam, tasmAt tenaiva rUpeNa vasudeva-putra-rUpeNa catur-bhujena, sahasra-bAho ! vArtamAnikena vishva-rUpeNa, bhava vishva-mUrte | upasamhR^itya vishva-rUpam, tenaiva rUpeNa bhavety arthaH ||BhGS_11.46|| 

==============================

arjunam bhItam upalabhya, upasamhR^itya vishva-rUpam, priya-vacanena AshvAsayan shrI-bhagavAn uvAca - 

mayA prasannena tavArjunedam
rUpam param darshitam Atma-yogAt |
tejo-mayam vishvam anantam
Adyam yan me tvad-anyena na dR^iShTa-pUrvam ||BhG_11.47||

mayA prasannena, prasAdo nAma tvayy anugraha-buddhiH, tadvatA prasannena mayA tava | he 'rjuna ! idam param rUpam vishva-rUpam darshitam Atma-yogAd Atmana aishvaryasya sAmarthyAt | tejo-mayam tejaH-prAyam vishvam samastam anantam anta-rahitam Adau bhavam Adyam, yad rUpam me mama tvad-anyena tvatto 'nyena kenacin na dR^iShTa-pUrvam ||BhGS_11.47|| 

==============================

Atmano mama rUpa-darshanena kR^itArtha eva tvam samvR^itta iti tat stauti - 

na veda yaj~nAdhyayanair na dAnair
na ca kriyAbhir na tapobhir ugraiH |
evam-rUpaH shakya aham nR^i-loke
draShTum tvad-anyena kuru-pravIra ||BhG_11.48||

na veda-yaj~nAdhyayanaish caturNAm api vedAnAm adhyayanair yathAvat yaj~nAdhyayanaish ca - vedAdhyayanair eva yaj~nAdhyayanasya siddhatvAt pR^ithak yaj~nAdhyayana-grahaNam yaj~na-vij~nAnopalakShaNArtham - tathA na dAnais tulA-puruShAdibhiH, na ca kriyAbhir agnihotrAdibhiH shrautAdibhiH, nApi tapobhir ugraish cAndrAyaNAdibhir ugrair ghoraiH, evam-rUpo yathA-darshitam vishva-rUpam yasya so 'ham evam-rUpo na shakyo 'ham nR^i-loke manuShya-loke draShTum tvad-anyena tvatto 'nyena kura-pravIra ||BhGS_11.48|| 

==============================

mA te vyathA mA ca vimUDha-bhAvo
dR^iShTvA rUpam ghoram IdR^iN^ mamedam |
vyapeta-bhIH prIta-manAH punas tvam
tad eva me rUpam idam prapashya ||BhG_11.49||

mA te vyathA mA bhUt te bhayam, mA ca vimUDha-bhAvo vimUDha-cittatA, dR^iShTvopalabhya rUpam ghoram IdR^ik yathA-darshitam mamedam | vyapeta-bhIr vigata-bhayaH, prIta-manAsh ca san punar bhUyas tvam tad eva catur-bhujam rUpam shaN^kha-cakra-gadAdharam taveShTam rUpam idam prapashya ||BhGS_11.49|| 

==============================

samjaya uvAca - 
ity arjunam vAsudevas tathoktvA
svakam rUpam darshayAm Asa bhUyaH |
AshvAsayAm Asa ca bhItam enam
bhUtvA punaH saumya-vapur mahAtmA ||BhG_11.50||

ity evam arjunam vAsudevas tathA-bhUtam vacanam uktvA, svakam vasudevasya gR^ihe jAtam rUpam darshayAmAsa darshitavAn bhUyaH punaH | AshvAsayAmAsa ca AshvAsitavAn bhItam enam, bhUtvA punaH saumya-vapuH prasanna-deho mahAtmA ||BhGS_11.50|| 

==============================

arjuna uvAca - 
dR^iShTvedam mAnuSham rUpam tava saumyam janArdana |
idAnIm asmi samvR^ittaH sa-cetAH prakR^itim gataH ||BhG_11.51||

dR^iShTvedam mAnuSham rUpam mat-sakham prasannam tava saumyam janArdana, idAnIm, adhunAsmi samvR^ittaH samjAtaH | kim ? sa-cetAH prasanna-cittaH prakR^itim svabhAvam gatash cAsmi ||BhGS_11.51|| 

==============================

shrI-bhagavAn uvAca - 

sudurdarsham idam rUpam dR^iShTavAn asi yan mama |
devA apy asya rUpasya nityam darshana-kAN^kShiNaH ||BhG_11.52||

sudurdarsham suShThu duHkhena darshanam asyeti sudurdarsham | idam rUpam dR^iShTavAn asi yan mama, devA apy asya mama rUpasya nityam sarvadA darshana-kAN^kShiNaH | darshanepsavo 'pi na tvam iva dR^iShTavantaH, na drakShyanti cety abhiprAyaH ||BhGS_11.52||

==============================

kasmAt ? - 

nAham vedair na tapasA na dAnena na cejyayA |
shakya evam-vidho draShTum dR^iShTavAn asi mAm yathA ||BhG_11.53||

nAham vedaiH R^ig-yajuH-sAmAtharva-vedaish caturbhir api, na tapasA ugreNa cAndrAyaNAdinA, na dAnena go-bhU-hiraNyAdinA, na cejyayA yaj~nena pUjayA vA shakyaH evam-vidho yathA-darshita-prakAro draShTum dR^iShTavAn asi mAm yathA tvam ||BhGS_11.53|| 

==============================

katham punaH shakya ity ucyate - 

bhaktyA tv ananyayA shakya aham evam-vidho 'rjuna |
j~nAtum draShTum ca tattvena praveShTum ca parantapa ||BhG_11.54||

bhaktyA tu kim-vishiShTayA ity Aha - ananyayApR^ithag-bhUtayA, bhagavato 'nyatra pR^ithaN^ na kadAcid api yA bhavati sA tv ananyA bhaktiH | sarvair api karaNaiH vAsudevAd anyan na upalabhyate yayA, sAnanyA bhaktiH, tayA bhaktyA shakyo 'ham evam-vidho vishva-rUpa-prakAro he 'rjuna, j~nAtum shAstrataH | na kevalam j~nAtum shAstrataH, draShTum ca sAkShAt-kartum tattvena tattvataH, praveShTum ca mokSham ca gantum parantapa ||BhGS_11.54||

==============================

adhunA sarvasya gItA-shAstrasya sAra-bhUto 'rtho niHshreyasArtho 'nuShTheyatvena samuccityocyate - 

mat-karma-kR^in mat-paramo mad-bhaktaH saN^ga-varjitaH |
nirvairaH sarva-bhUteShu yaH sa mAm eti pANDava ||BhG_11.55||

mat-karma-kR^in mad-artham karma mat-karma, tat karotIti mat-karma-kR^it | mat-paramaH - karoti bhR^ityaH svAmi-karma, na tv AtmanaH paramA pretya gantavyA gatir iti svAminam pratipadyate | ayam tu mat-karma-kR^in mAm eva paramAm gatim pratipadyate iti mat-paramaH, aham paramaH parA gatir yasya so 'yam mat-paramaH | tathA mad-bhakto mAm eva sarva-prakAraiH sarva-prakAraiH sarvAtmanA sarvotsAhena bhajate iti mad-bhaktaH | saN^ga-varjito dhana-putra-mitra-kalatra-bandhu-vargeShu saN^ga-varjitaH saN^gaH prItiH snehas tad-varjitaH | nirvairo nirgata-vairaH sarva-bhUteShu shatru-bhAva-rahita Atmano ' tyantApakAra-pravR^itteShv api | ya IdR^isho mad-bhaktaH sa mAm eti | aham eva tasya parA gatiH, nAnyA gatiH kAcit bhavati | ayam tavopadesha iShTo mayA upadiShTaH | he pANDAva ! iti ||BhGS_11.55|| 

iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrI-govinda-bhagavat-pUjya-pAda-
shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^itau shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye
ekAdasho 'dhyAyaH ||11||

BhG 12

atha bhakti-yogo nAma dvAdasho 'dhyAyaH

(shrI-shaN^karAcArya-bhagavat-pAda-kR^ita-bhAShyam)
