dvitIyAdhyAya-prabhR^itiShu vibhUty-anteShu adhyAyeShu paramAtmano brahmaNo 'kSharasya vidhvasta-sarvopAdhi-visheShasyopAsanam uktam | sarva-yogaishvarya-sarva-j~nAna-shaktimat-sattvopAdher Ishvarasya tatra copAsanam tatra tatroktam | vishva-rUpAdhyAye tv aishvaram Adyam samasta-jagad-Atma-rUpam vishva-rUpam tvadIyam darshitam upAsanArtham eva tvayA | tac ca darshayitvA uktavAn asi mat-karma-kR^id [GItA 11.55] ity Adi | ato 'ham anayor ubhayoH pakShayor vishiShTatara-bubhutsayA tvAm pR^icchAmIty arjuna uvAca - 

evam satata-yuktA ye bhaktAs tvAm paryupAsate |
ye cApy akSharam avyaktam teShAm ke yoga-vittamAH ||BhG_12.1||

evam ity atItAnantara-lokena uktam artham parAmR^ishati mat-karma-kR^id ity AdinA | evam satata-yuktAH, nairantaryeNa bhagavat-karmAdau yathokte 'rthe samAhitAH santaH pravR^ittA ity arthaH | ye bhaktA ananya-sharaNAH santas tvAm yathA-darshitam vishva-rUpam paryupAsate dhyAyanti | ye cAnye 'pi tyakta-sarveShaNAH samnyasta-sarva-karmANo yathA-visheShitam brahmAkSharam nirasta-sarvopAdhitvAd avyaktam akaraNa-gocaram | yad dhi karaNa-gocaram tad vyaktam ucyate, a¤jer dhAtos tat-karmakatvAt | idam tv akSharam tad-viparItam, shiShTau ca ucyamAnair visheShaNair vishiShTam, tad ye cApi paryupAsate, teShAm ubhayeShAm madhye ke yogi-vittamAH ? ke 'tishayena yoga-vida ity arthaH ||BhGS_12.1|| 

==============================

shrI-bhagavAn uvAca - ye tv akSharopAsakAH samyag-darshino nivR^ittaiShaNAs te tAvat tiShThantu | tAn prati yad vaktavyam, tad upariShTAd vakShyAmaH | ye tv itare - 

mayy Aveshya mano ye mAm nitya-yuktA upAsate |
shraddhayA parayopetAs te me yuktatamA matAH ||BhG_12.2||

mayi vishva-rUpe parameshvara Aveshya samAdhAya mano ye bhaktAH santaH, mAm sarva-yoge varANAm adhIshvaram sarvaj~nam vimukta-rAgAdi-klesha-timira-dR^iShTim, nitya-yuktA atItAnantarAdhyAyAntokta-shlokArtha-nyAyena satata-yuktAH santa upAsate shraddhayA parayA prakR^iShTayopetAH, te me mama matA abhipretA yuktatamA iti | nairantaryeNa hi te mac-cittatayAho-rAtram ativAhayanti | ato yuktam tAn prati yuktatamA iti vaktum ||BhGS_12.2|| 

==============================
 
kim itare yuktatamA na bhavanti ? na | kimtu tAn prati yad vaktavyam, tac chR^iNu - 

ye tv akSharam anirdeshyam avyaktam paryupAsate |
sarvatra-gam acintyam ca kUTastham acalam dhruvam ||BhG_12.3||

ye tv akSharam anirdeshyam, avyaktatvAd ashabda-gocareti na nirdeShTum shakyate, ato 'nirdeshyam | avyaktam na kenApi pramANena vyajyata ity avyaktam paryupAsate pari samantAd upAsate | upAsanam nAma yathA-shAstram upAsyasyArthasya viShayI-karaNena sAmIpyam upagamya taila-dhArAvat samAna-pratyaya-pravAheNa dIrgha-kAlam yad Asanam, tad upAsanam AcakShate | akSharasya visheShaNam Aha - sarvatra-gam vyomavad vyApy acintyam cAvyaktatvAd acintyam | yad dhi karaNa-gocaram, tan manasApi cintyam, tad-viparItatvAd acintyam akSharam, kUTa-stham dR^ishyamAna-guNam antar-doSham vastu kUTam | kUTa-rUpam kUTa-sAkShyam ity Adau kUTa-shabdaH prasiddho loke | tathA cAvidyAdy-aneka-samsAra-bIjam antar-doShavan mAyA-vyAkR^itAdi-shabda-vAcyatayA mAyAm tu prakR^itim vidyAn mAyinam tu maheshvaram [ÁvetU 4.10], mama mAyA duratyayA [GItA 7.14] ity Adau prasiddham yat tat kUTam, tasmin kUTe sthitam kUTa-stham tad-adhyakShatayA | athavA, rAshir iva sthitam kUTa-stham ata evAcalam | yasmAd acalam, tasmAd dhruvam, nityam ity arthaH ||BhGS_12.3||

==============================

samniyamyendriya-grAmam sarvatra sama-buddhayaH |
te prApnuvanti mAm eva sarva-bhUta-hite ratAH ||BhG_12.4||

samniyamya samyak niyamya upasamhR^itya indriya-grAmam indriya-samudAyam sarvatra sarvasmin kAle sama-buddhayaH samA tulyA buddhir yeShAm iShTAniShTa-prAptau te sama-buddhayaH | te ye evam-vidhAs te prApnuvanti mAm eva sarva-bhUta-hite ratAH | na tu teShAm vaktavyam kimcit mAm te prApnuvantIti | j~nAnI tv Atmaiva me matam iti hy uktam | na hi bhagavat-svarUpANAm satAm yuktatamatvam ayuktatamatvam vA vAcyam ||BhGS_12.4|| 

==============================

kim tu - 
klesho 'dhikataras teShAm avyaktAsakta-cetasAm |
avyaktA hi gatir duHkham dehavadbhir avApyate ||BhG_12.5||

klesho 'dhikataraH | yadyapi mat-karmAdi-parANAm klesho 'dhika eva | klesho 'dhikataras tv akSharAtmanAm paramArtha-darshinAm dehAbhimAna-parityAga-nimittaH | avyaktAsakta-cetasAm avyakta Asaktam ceto yeShAm te 'vyaktAsakta-cetasas teShAm avyaktAsakta-cetasAm | avyaktA hi yasmAd yA gatir akSharAtmikA duHkham sA dehavadbhir dehAbhimAnavadbhir avApyate | ataH klesho 'dhikataraH | akSharopAsakAnAm yad vartanam, tad upariShTAd vakShyAmaH ||BhGS_12.5|| 

==============================

ye tu sarvANi karmANi mayi samnyasya mat-parAH |
ananyenaiva yogena mAm dhyAyanta upAsate ||BhG_12.6||

ye tu sarvANi karmANi mayIshvare samnyasya mat-parA aham paro yeShAm te mat-parAH santo 'nanyenaivAvidyamAnam anyat Alambanam vishva-rUpam devam AtmAnam muktvA yasya so 'nanyas tenAnanyenaiva | kena ? yogena samAdhinA mAm dhyAyantash cintayanta upAsate ||BhGS_12.6|| 

==============================

teShAm kim ? - 

teShAm aham samuddhartA mR^ityu-samsAra-sAgarAt |
bhavAmi nacirAt pArtha mayy Aveshita-cetasAm ||BhG_12.7||

teShAm mad-upAsanaika-parANAm aham IshvaraH samuddhartA | kutaH ? ity Aha - mR^ityu-samsAra-sAgarAn mR^ityu-yuktaH samsAro mR^ityu-samsAraH, sa eva sAgara iva sAgaraH, dustaratvAt, tasmAt mR^ityu-samsAra-sAgarAt aham teShAm samuddhartA bhavAmi na cirAt | kim tarhi ? kShipram eva he pArtha, mayi Aveshita-cetasAm mayi vishva-rUpa Aveshitam samAhitam ceto yeShAm te mayy Aveshita-cetasas teShAm ||BhGS_12.7|| 

==============================

yata evam, tasmAt - 

mayy eva mana Adhatsva mayi buddhim niveshaya |
nivasiShyasi mayy eva ata Urdhvam na samshayaH ||BhG_12.8||

mayy eva vishva-rUpa Ishvare manaH samkalpa-vikalpAtmakam Adhatsva sthApaya | mayy evAdhyavasAyam kurvatIm buddhim Adhatsva niveshaya | tatas te kim syAd iti sR^iNu - nivasiShyasi nivatsyasi nishcayena mad-AtmanA mayi nivAsam kariShyasi | evAtaH sharIra-pAtAd Urdhvam | na samshayaH, samshayo 'tra na kartavyaH ||BhGS_12.8|| 

==============================

atha cittam samAdhAtum na shaknoShi mayi sthiram |
abhyAsa-yogena tato mAm icchAptum dhana¤jaya ||BhG_12.9||

atha evam yathAvocam tathA mayi cittam samAdhAtum sthApayitum sthiram acalam na shaknoShi cet, tataH pashcAd abhyAsa-yogena | cittasyaikasmin Alambane sarvataH samAhR^itya punaH punaH sthApanam abhyAsaH | tat-pUrvako yogaH samAdhAna-lakShaNas tenAbhyAsa-yogena mAm vishva-rUpam iccha prArthayasva Aptum prAptum | he dhana¤jaya ||BhGS_12.9|| 

==============================

abhyAse 'py asamartho 'si mat-karma-paramo bhava |
mad-artham api karmANi kurvan siddhim avApsyasi ||BhG_12.10||

abhyAse 'py asamartho 'sy ashakto 'si, tarhi mat-karma-paramo bhava mad-artham karma mat-karma tat-paramaH mat-karma-paramaH, mat-karma-pradhAna ity arthaH | abhyAsena vinA mad-artham api karmANi kevalam kurvan siddhim sattva-shuddhi-yoga-j~nAna-prApti-dvAreNAvApsyasi ||BhGS_12.10|| 

==============================

athaitad apy ashakto 'si kartum mad-yogam AshritaH |
sarva-karma-phala-tyAgam tataH kuru yatAtmavAn ||BhG_12.11||

atha punar etad api yad uktam mat-karma-paramatvam, tat kartum ashakto 'si, mad-yogam, Ashrito mayi kriyamANAni karmANi samnyasya yat karaNam teShAm anuShThAnam sa mad-yogaH, tam AshritaH san, sarva-karma-phala-tyAgam sarveShAm karmaNAm phala-samnyAsam sarva-karma-phala-tyAgam tato 'nantaram kuru yatAtmavAn samyata-cittaH san ity arthaH ||BhGS_12.11|| 

==============================

idAnIm sarva-karma-phala-tyAgam stauti - 

shreyo hi j~nAnam abhyAsAj j~nAnAd dhyAnam vishiShyate |
dhyAnAt karma-phala-tyAgas tyAgAc chAntir anantaram ||BhG_12.12||

shreyo hi prashasyataram j~nAnam | kasmAt ? viveka-pUrvakAd abhyAsAt | tasmAd api j~nAnAj j~nAna-pUrvakam dhyAnam vishiShyate | j~nAnavato dhyAnAd api karma-phala-tyAgo vishiShyata ity anuShajyate | evam karma-phala-tyAgAt pUrva-visheShaNavataH shAntir upashamaH sa-hetukasya samsArasyAnantaram eva syAt, na tu kAlAntaram apekShate |

aj~nasya karmaNi pravR^ittasya pUrvopadiShTopAyAnuShThAnAshaktau sarva-karmaNAm phala-tyAgaH shreyaH-sAdhanam upadiShTam, na prathamam eva | atash ca shreyo hi j~nAnam abhyAsAd ity uttarottara-vishiShTatvopadeshena sarva-karma-phala-tyAgaH stUyate, sampanna-sAdhanAnuShThAnAshaktau anuShTheyatvena shrutatvAt | kena sAdharmyeNa stutitvam ? yadA sarve pramucyanta iti sarva-kAma-prahANAd amR^itatvam uktam | tat prasiddham | kAmAsh ca sarve shrauta-smArta-karmaNAm phalAni | tat-tyAge ca viduSho dhyAna-niShThasyAnantaraiva shAntir iti sarva-kAma-tyAga-sAmAnyam aj~na-karma-phala-tyAgasyAstIti tat-sAmAnyAt sarva-karma-phala-tyAga-stutir iyam prarocanArthA | yathAgastyena brAhmaNena samudraH pIta itIdAnImtanA api brAhmaNA brAhmaNatva-sAmAnyAt stUyante, evam karma-phala-tyAgAt karma-yogasya shreyaH sAdhanatvam abhihitam ||BhGS_12.12||

==============================

atra cAtmeshvara-bhedam Ashritya vishva-rUpa Ishvare cetaH-samAdhAna-lakShaNo yoga uktaH, IshvarArtham karmAnuShThAnAdi ca | athaitad apy ashakto 'si [GItA 12.11] ity aj~nAna-kArya-sUcanAn nAbheda-darshino 'kSharopAsakasya karma-yoga upapadyata iti darshayati | tathA karma-yogino 'kSharopAsanAnupapattim | te prApnuvanti mAm eva [GItA 12.4] ity akSharopAsakAnAm kaivalya-prAptau svAtantryam uktvA, itareShAm pAratantryAd IshvarAdhInatAm darshitavAn teShAm aham samuddhartA [GItA 12.7] iti | yadi hIshvarasyAtma-bhUtAs te matA abheda-darshitvAt, akShara-svarUpA eva ta iti samuddharaNa-karma-vacanam tAn praty apeshalam syAt | yasmAc cArjunasyAtyantam eva hitaiShI bhagavAn tasya samyag-darshanAnanvitam karma-yogam bheda-dR^iShTimantam eva upadishati | na cAtmAnam Ishvaram pramANato buddhvA kasyacid guNa-bhAvam jigamiShati kashcid, virodhAt | tasmAd akSharopAsakAnAm samyag darshana-niShThAnAm samnyAsinAm tyakta-sarveShaNAnAm adveShTA sarva-bhUtAnAm ity Adi-dharma-pUgam sAkShAd amR^itatva-kAraNam vakShyAmIti pravartate - 

adveShTA sarva-bhUtAnAm maitraH karuNa eva ca |
nirmamo nirahamkAraH sama-duHkha-sukhaH kShamI ||BhG_12.13||

adveShTA sarva-bhUtAnAm na dveShTA, Atmano duHkha-hetum api na kimcid dveShTi, sarvANi bhUtAny Atmatvena hi pashyati | maitro mitra-bhAvo maitrI mitratayA vartata iti maitraH | karuNa eva ca, karuNA kR^ipA duHkhiteShu dayA, tadvAn karuNaH, sarva-bhUtAbhaya-pradaH, samnyAsIty arthaH | nirmamo mama-pratyaya-varjitaH | nirahamkAro nirgatAham-pratyayaH | sama-duHkha-sukhaH same duHkha-sukhe dveSha-rAgayor apravartake yasya sa sama-duHkha-sukhaH | kShamI kShamAvAn, AkruShTo 'bhihato vAvikriya evAste ||BhGS_12.13|| 

==============================

samtuShTaH satatam yogI yatAtmA dR^iDha-nishcayaH |
mayy arpita-mano-buddhir yo mad-bhaktaH sa me priyaH ||BhG_12.14||

samtuShTaH satatam nityam deha-sthiti-kAraNasya lAbhe 'lAbhe ca utpannAlam-pratyayaH | tathA guNaval-lAbhe viparyaye ca samtuShTaH | satatam yogI samAhita-cittaH | yatAtmA samyata-svabhAvaH | dR^iDha-nishcayo dR^iDhaH sthiro nishcayo 'dhyavasAyo yasyAtma-tattva-viShaye sa dR^iDha-nishcayaH | mayy arpita-mano-buddhiH samkalpa-vikalpAtmakam manaH, adhyavasAya-lakShaNA buddhiH, te mayy evArpite sthApite yasya samnyAsinaH sa mayy arpita-mano-buddhiH | ya IdR^isho mad-bhaktaH sa me priyaH | priyo hi j~nAnino 'ty artham aham sa ca mama priya iti saptame 'dhyAye sUcitam, tad iha prapaJNcyate ||BhGS_12.14|| 

==============================

yasmAn nodvijate loko lokAn nodvijate ca yaH |
harShAmarSha-bhayodvegair mukto yaH sa ca me priyaH ||BhG_12.15||

yasmAt samnyAsino nodvijate nodvegam gacchati na santapyate na samkShubhyati lokaH, tathA lokAn nodvijate ca yaH, harShAmarSha-bhayodvegair harShash cAmarShash ca bhayam codvegash ca tair harShAmarSha-bhayodvegair muktaH | harShaH priya-lAbhe 'ntaH-karaNasyotkarSho romAJNcanAshrupAtAdi-liN^gaH | amarSho 'sahiShNutA | bhayam trAsaH | udvega udvignatA | tair mukto yaH sa ca me priyaH ||BhGS_12.15|| 

==============================

anapekShaH shucir dakSha udAsIno gata-vyathaH |
sarvArambha-parityAgI yo mad-bhaktaH sa me priyaH ||BhG_12.16||

dehendriya-viShaya-sambandhAdiShu apekShA-viShayeShu anapekSho niHspR^ihaH | shucir bAhyena AbhyantareNa ca shaucena sampannaH | dakShaH pratyutpanneShu kAryeShu sadyo yathAvat pratipattum samarthaH | udAsIno na kasyacit mitrAdeH pakSham bhajate yaH, sa udAsIno yatiH | gata-vyatho gata-bhayaH | sarvArambha-parityAgI Arabhyanteti | ArambhA ihAmutra-phala-bhogArthAni kAma-hetUni karmANi sarvArambhAH, tAn parityaktum shIlam asyeti sarvArambha-parityAgI yaH mad-bhaktaH saH me priyaH ||BhGS_12.16|| 

==============================

kim ca - 
yo na hR^iShyati na dveShTi na shocati na kAN^kShati |
shubhAshubha-parityAgI bhaktimAn yaH sa me priyaH ||BhG_12.17||

yo na hR^iShyatIShTa-prAptau, na dveShTy aniShTa-prAptau, na shocati priya-viyoge, na cAprAptam kAN^kShati, shubhAshubhe karmaNI parityaktum shIlam asyeti shubhAshubha-parityAgI bhaktimAn yaH sa me priyaH ||BhGS_12.17|| 

==============================

samaH shatrau ca mitre ca tathA mAnApamAnayoH |
shItoShNa-sukha-duHkheShu samaH saN^ga-vivarjitaH ||BhG_12.18||

samaH shatrau ca mitre ca, tathA mAnApamAnayoH pUjA-paribhavayoH, shItoShNa-sukha-duHkheShu samaH | sarvatra ca saN^ga-vivarjitaH ||BhGS_12.18|| 

==============================

kim ca - 
tulya-nindA-stutir maunI samtuShTo yena kenacit |
aniketaH sthira-matir bhaktimAn me priyo naraH ||BhG_12.19||

tulya-nindA-stutiH | nindA ca stutish ca nindA-stutI | te tulye yasya sa tulya-nindA-stutiH | maunI maunavAn samyata-vAk | samtuShTaH yena kenacit sharIra-sthiti-hetu-mAtreNa | tathA coktam - 

yena kenacid Acchanno yena kenacid AshitaH | 
yatra kvacana shAyI syAt tam devA brAhmaNam viduH || [Mbh 12.245.12] iti | 

kim ca, aniketo niketa Ashrayo nivAso niyato na vidyate yasya so 'niketaH, nAgAre ity Adi-smR^ity-antarAt | sthira-matiH sthirA paramArtha-viShayA yasya matiH saH sthira-matiH | bhaktimAn me priyo naraH ||BhGS_12.19|| 

==============================

adveShTA sarva-bhUtAnAm [GItA 12.13] ity AdinAkSharopAsakAnAm nivR^itta-sarveShaNAnAm samnyAsinAm paramArtha-j~nAna-niShThAnAm dharma-jAtam prakrAntam upasamhriyate - 

ye tu dharmyAmR^itam idam yathoktam paryupAsate |
shraddadhAnA mat-paramA bhaktAs te 'tIva me priyAH ||BhG_12.20||

ye tu samnyAsino dharmyAmR^itam dharmAd anapetam dharmyam ca tad amR^itam ca tat, amR^itatva-hetutvAt, idam yathoktam, adveShTA sarva-bhUtAnAm ity AdinA paryupAsate 'nutiShThanti shraddadhAnAH santaH mat-paramAH yathokto 'ham akSharAtmA paramo niratishayA gatir yeShAm te mat-paramAH, mad-bhaktAsh cottamAm paramArtha-j~nAna-lakShaNAm bhaktim AshritAH, te 'tIva me priyAH | priyo hi j~nAnino 'ty artham [GItA 7.18] iti yat sUcitam tat vyAkhyAyehopasamhR^itam bhaktAs te 'tIva me priyA iti | yasmAd dharmyAmR^itam idam yathoktam anutiShThan bhagavato viShNoH parameshvarasyAtIva priyo bhavati, tasmAd idam dharmyAmR^itam mumukShuNA yatnato 'nuShTheyam viShNoH priyam param dhAma jigamiShuNeti vAkyArthaH ||BhGS_12.20|| 

iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrI-govinda-bhagavat-pUjya-pAda-
shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^itau shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye
dvAdasho 'dhyAyaH ||


__________________________________________________________

BhG 13

[*NOTE: Numbering of this adhyaya out of tune with standard editions 
and probably defective; "13.33" missing!]


atha kShetra-kShetraj~na-yogo nAma 
trayodasho 'dhyAyaH

(shrI-shaN^karAcArya-bhagavat-pAda-kR^ita-bhAShyam)

saptame 'dhyAye sUcite dve prakR^itI Ishvarasya triguNAtmikAShTadhA bhinnAparA samsAra-hetutvAt, parA cAnyA jIva-bhUtA kShetraj~na-lakShaNeshvarAtmikA | yAbhyAm prakR^itibhyAm Ishvaro jagad-utpatti-sthiti-laya-hetutvam pratipadyate | tatra kShetra-kShetraj~na-lakShaNa-prakR^iti-dvaya-nirUpaNa-dvAreNa tadvata Ishvarasya tattva-nirdhAraNArtham kShetrAdhyAya Arabhyate | atItAnantarAdhyAye ca adveShTA sarva-bhUtAnAm [GItA 12.13] ity AdinA yAvad-adhyAya-parisamAptis tAvat tattva-j~nAninAm sannyAsinAm niShThA yathA te vartanta ity etad uktam | kena punas te tattva-j~nAnena yuktA yathokta-dharmAcaraNAd bhagavataH priyA bhavanty evam arthash cAyam adhyAya Arabhyate | prakR^itish ca triguNAtmikA sarva-kArya-karaNa-viShayAkAreNa pariNatA puruShasya bhogApavargArtha-kartavyatayA dehendriyAdyAkAreNa samhanyate | so 'yam saN^ghAta idam sharIram | tad etad bhagavAn uvAca --

idam sharIram kaunteya kShetram ity abhidhIyate |
etad yo vetti tam prAhuH kShetraj~na iti tad-vidaH ||BhG_13.1||

idam iti sarva-nAmnoktam vishinaShTi shariram iti | he kaunteya ! kShata-trANAt kShayAt kSharaNAt, kShetravad vAsmin karma-phala-niShpatteH kShetram iti | iti-shabda evam-shabdedArthakaH | kShetram ity evam abhidhIyate kathyate | etac charIram kShetram yo vetti vijAnAti, ApAda-tala-mastakam j~nAnena viShayIkaroti, svAbhAvikenaupadeshikena vA vedanena viShayIkaroti vibhAgashaH, tam veditAram prAhuH kathayanti kShetraj~na iti | iti-shabdaH evam-shabda-padArthaka eva pUrvavat | kShetraj~naH ity evam AhuH | ke ? tad-vidas tau kShetra-kShetraj~nau ye vidanti te tad-vidaH ||BhGS_13.1||

==============================

evam kShetra-kShetraj~nau uktau | kim etAvan-mAtreNa j~nAnena j~nAtavyau? iti nety ucyate - 

kShetraj~nam cApi mAm viddhi sarva-kShetreShu bhArata |
kShetra-kShetraj~nayor j~nAnam yat taj j~nAnam matam mama ||BhG_13.2||

kShetraj~nam yathokta-lakShaNam cApi mAm parameshvaram asamsAriNam viddhi jAnIhi | sarva-kShetreShu yaH kShetraj~no brahmAdi-stamba-paryantAneka-kShetropAdhi-pravibhaktaH | tam nirasta-sarvopAdhi-bhedam sad-asad-Adi-shabda-pratyayAgocaram viddhIty abhiprAyaH | he bhArata ! yasmAt kShetra-kShetraj~neshvara-yAthAtmya-vyatirekeNa na j~nAna-gocaram anyad avashiShTam asti, tasmAt kShetra-kShetraj~nayor j~neya-bhUtayor yaj j~nAnam kShetra-kShetraj~nau yena j~nAnena viShayIkriyete, taj j~nAnam samyag-j~nAnam iti matam abhiprAyaH mameshvarasya viShNoH || 

nanu sarva-kShetreShv eka eveshvaraH | nAnyas tad-vyatirikto bhoktA vidyate cet, tata Ishvarasya samsAritvam prAptam | Ishvara-vyatirekeNa vA samsAriNo 'nyasyAbhAvAt samsArAbhAva-prasaN^gaH | tac cobhayam aniShTam, bandha-mokSha-tad-dhetu-shAstrAnarthakya-prasaN^gAt, pratyakShAdi-pramANa-virodhAc ca | pratyakSheNa tAvat sukha-duHkha-tad-dhetu-lakShaNaH samsAra upalabhyate | jagad-vaicitryopalabdhe ca dharmAdharma-nimittaH samsAro 'numIyate | sarvam etad anupapannam Atmeshvaraikatve | na | j~nAnAj~nAnayor anyatvenopapatteH | dUram ete viparIte viShUcI avidyA yA ca vidyeti j~nAtA [KaThU 1.2.4] tathA tayor vidyAvidyA-viShayayoH phala-bhedo 'pi viruddho nirdiShTaH - shreyash ca preyash ca [KaThU 1.2.2] iti | vidyA-viShayaH shreyaH, preyas tv avidyA-kAryam iti | tathA ca vyAsaH - dvAv imAv atha panthAnau [Mbh 12.241.6] ity Adi, imau dvAv eva panthAnAv ity Adi ca | iha ca dve niShThe ukte | avidyA ca saha kAryeNa vidyayA hAtavyeti shruti-smR^iti-nyAyebhyo 'vagamyate | 

shrutayas tAvat - iha ced avedId atha satyam asti na ced ihAvedIn mahatI vinaShTiH [KenaU 2.5], 
tam evam vidvAn amR^ita iha bhavati [Taittù 3.12], nAnyaH panthA vidyate 'yanAya [ÁvetU 3.8] vidvAn na bibheti kutashcana [TaittU 2.9] | 

aviduShas tu - atha tasya bhayam bhavati [TaittU 2.7], avidyAyAm antare vartamAnAH [KaThU 1.2.5], brahma veda brahmaiva bhavati [MuNDU 3.2.9], anyo 'sAv anyo 'ham asmIti na sa veda yathA pashur evam sa devAnAm [BAU 1.4.10] | Atmavid yaH sa idam sarvam bhavati [BAU 1.4.10], yadA carmavat [ÁvetU 6.20] ity AdyAH sahasrashaH | 

smR^itayash ca - aj~nAnenAvR^itam j~nAnam tena muhyanti jantavaH [GItA 5.25], ihaiva tair jitaH sargo yeShAm sAmye sthitam manaH [GItA 5.19], samam pashyan hi sarvatra [GItA 13.29] ity AdyAH | 

nyAyatash ca - 
sarpAn kushAgrANi tathodapAnam 
j~nAtvA manuShyAH parivarjayanti | 
aj~nAnatas tatra patanti kecij j~nAne 
phalam pashya yathA-vishiShTam || [Mbh 12.201.17] iti |

tathA ca - dehAdiShu Atma-buddhir avidvAn rAga-dveShAdi-prayukto dharmAdharmAnuShThAna-kR^ij jAyate mriyate cety avagamyate | dehAdi-vyatiriktAtma-darshino rAga-dveShAdi-prahANApekSha-dharmAdharma-pravR^itty-upashamAn mucyanta iti na kenacit pratyAkhyAtum shakyam nyAyataH | tatraivam sati, kShetraj~nasyeshvarasyaiva sato 'vidyA-kR^itopAdhi-bhedataH samsAritvam iva bhavati, yathA dehAdy-Atmatvam AtmanaH | sarva-jantUnAm hi prasiddho dehAdiShv anAtmasu Atma-bhAvo nishcito 'vidyA-kR^itaH, yathA sthANau puruSha-nishcayaH | na caitAvatA puruSha-dharmaH sthANor bhavati, sthANu-dharmo vA puruShasya | tathA na caitanya-dharmo dehasya, deha-dharmo vA cetanasya sukha-duHkha-mohAtmakatvAdir Atmano na yuktaH | avidyA-kR^itatvAvisheShAt, jarA-mR^ityuvat |

na, atulyatvAt | iti cet - sthANu-puruShau j~neyAv eva santau j~nAtrAnyonyasminn adhyastAv avidyayA | dehAtmanos tu j~neya-j~nAtror eva itaretarAdhyAsaH, iti na samo dR^iShTAntaH | 

ato deha-dharmo j~neyo 'pi j~nAtur Atmano bhavatIti cet, na | acaitanyAdi-prasaN^gAt | yadi hi j~neyasya dehAdeH kShetrasya dharmAH sukha-duHkha-mohecchAdayo j~nAtur bhavanti, tarhi, j~neyasya kShetrasya dharmAH kecit Atmano bhavanty avidyAdhyAropitAH, jarA-maraNAdayas tu na bhavantIti visheSha-hetur vaktavyaH | na bhavantIty asty anumAnam - avidyAdhyAropitatvAj jarA-maraNAdivad iti, heyatvAt, upAdeyatvAc cety Adi | 

tatraivam sati, kartR^itva-bhoktR^itva-lakShaNaH samsAro j~neya-stho j~nAtary avidyayAdhyAropita iti, na tena j~nAtuH kimcid duShyati | yathA bAlair adhyAropitenAkAshasya tala-malinatvAdinA |

evam ca sati, sarva-kShetreShv api sato bhagavataH kShetraj~nasyeshvarasya samsAritva-gandha-mAtram api nAshaN^kayam | na hi kvacid api loke 'vidyAdhyastena dharmeNa kasyacid upakAro 'pakAro vA dR^iShTaH | 

yat tUktam - na samo dR^iShTAnta iti, tad asat | katham ? avidyAdhyAsa-mAtram hi dR^iShTAnta-dArShTAntikayoH sAdharmyam vivakShitam | tan na vyabhicarati | yat tu j~nAtari vyabhicaratIti manyase, tasyApy anaikAntikatvam darshitam jarAdibhiH || 

avidyAvattvAt kShetraj~nasya samsAritvam iti cet, na | avidyAyAs tAmasatvAt | tAmaso hi pratyayaH, AvaraNAtmakatvAd avidyA viparIta-grAhakaH, samshayopasthApako vA, agrahaNAtmako vA | viveka-prakAsha-bhAve tad-abhAvAt tAmase cAvaraNAtmake timirAdi-doShe saty agrahaNAder avidyA-trayasya upalabdheH || 

atrAha - evam tarhi j~nAtR^i-dharmo 'vidyA | na | karaNe cakShuShi taimirikatvAdi-doShopalabdheH | yat tu manyase - j~nAtR^i-dharmo 'vidyA, tad eva cAvidyA-dharmavattvam kShetraj~nasya samsAritvam | tatra yad uktam Ishvara eva kShetraj~naH, na samsArIty etad ayuktam iti, tan na | yathA karaNe cakShuShi viparIta-grAhakAdi-doShasya darshanAt | na viparItAdi-grahaNam tan-nimittam vA taimirikatvAdi-doSho grahItuH, cakShuShaH samskAreNa timire 'panIte grahItur adarshanAn na grahItur dharmo yathA | tathA sarvatraivAgrahaNa-viparIta-samshaya-pratyayAs tan-nimittAH karaNasyaiva kasyacit bhavitum arhanti, na j~nAtuH kShetraj~nasya | samvedyatvAc ca teShAm pradIpa-prakAshavan na j~nAtR^i-dharmatvam | samvedyatvAd eva svAtma-vyatirikta-samvedyatvam | sarva-karaNa-viyoge ca kaivalye sarva-vAdibhir avidyAdi-doShavat-tvAnabhyupagamAt | Atmano yadi kShetraj~nasyAgny-uShNavat svo dharmaH, tato na kadAcid api tena viyogaH syAt | avikriyasya ca vyomavat sarva-gatasyAmUrtasya AtmanaH kenacit samyoga-viyogAnupapatteH, siddham kShetraj~nasya nityam eveshvaratvam | anAditvAn nirguNatvAd [GItA 13.32] ity AdIshvara-vacanAc ca || 

nanv evam sati samsAra-samsAritvAbhAve shAstrAnarthakyAdi-doShaH syAd iti cet, na | sarvair abhyupagatatvAt | sarvair hy Atma-vAdibhir abhyupagato doSho naikena parihartavyo bhavati | katham abhyupagata iti ? muktAtmanAm hi samsAra-samsAritva-vyavahArAbhAvaH sarvair eva Atma-vAdibhir iShyate | na ca teShAm shAstrAnarthakyAdi-doSha-prAptir abhyupagatA | tathA naH kShetraj~nAnAm Ishvaraikatve sati, shAstrAnarthakyam bhavatu | avidyA-viShaye cArthavattvam - yathA dvaitinAm sarveShAm bandhAvasthAyAm eva shAstrAdy-arthavattvam, na muktAvasthAyAm, evam || 

nanv Atmano bandha-muktAvasthe paramArthata eva vastu-bhUte dvaitinAm sarveShAm | ato heyopAdeya-tat-sAdhana-sad-bhAve shAstrAdy-arthavattvam syAt | advaitinAm punaH, dvaitasyAparamArthatvAt, avidyA-kR^itatvAd bandhAvasthAyAsh cAtmano 'paramArthatve nirviShayatvAt, shAstrAdyAnarthakyam iti cet, na | Atmano 'vasthA-bhedAnupapatteH | yadi tAvat Atmano bandha-muktAvasthe, yugapat syAtAm, krameNa vA | yugapat tAvat virodhAn na sambhavataH sthiti-gatI ivaikasmin | krama-bhAvitve ca, nirnimittatvam sa-nimittatvam vA ? nirnimittatve 'nirmokSha-prasaN^gaH | sa-nimittatve ca svato 'bhAvAt aparamArthatva-prasaN^gaH | tathA ca saty abhyupagama-hAniH | 

kim ca, bandha-muktAvasthayoH paurvAparya-nirUpaNAyAm bandhAvasthA pUrvam prakalpyA, anAdimaty antavatI ca | tac ca pramANa-viruddham | tathA mokShAvasthAdimaty anantA ca pramANa-viruddhaivAbhyupagamyate | na cAvasthAvato 'vasthAntaram gacchato nityatvam upapAdayitum shakyam | athAnityatva-doSha-parihArAya bandha-muktAvasthA-bhedo na kalpyate | ato dvaitinAm api shAstrAnarthakyAdi-doSho 'parihArya eva | iti samAnatvAn nAdvaita-vAdinA parihartavyo doShaH || 

na ca shAstrAnarthakyam, yathA-prasiddhAvidvat-puruSha-viShayatvAc chAstrasya | aviduShAm hi phala-hetvor anAtmanor Atma-darshanam, na viduShAm | viduShAm hi phala-hetubhyAm Atmano 'nyatva-darshane sati, tayor aham ity Atma-darshanAnupapatteH | na hy atyanta-mUDha unmattAdir api jalAgnyosh chAyA-prakAshayor vaikAtmyam pashyati | kim uta vivekI | tasmAn na vidhi-pratiShedha-shAstram tAvat phala-hetubhyAm Atmano 'nyatva-darshino bhavati | 

na hi "devadatta, tvam idam kuru" iti kasmimshcit karmaNi niyukte, "viShNumitro 'ham niyuktaH" iti tatra-stho niyogam sR^iNvann api pratipadyate | viyoga-viShaya-vivekAgrahaNAt tUpapadyate pratipattiH | tathA phala-hetvor api || 

nanu prAkR^ita-sambandhApekShayA yuktaiva pratipattiH shAstrArtha-viShayA - phala-hetubhyAm anyAtma-viShaya-darshane 'pi sati - iShTa-phala-hetau pravartito 'smi, aniShTa-phala-hetosh ca nivartito 'smIti | yathA pitR^i-putrAdInAm itaretarAtmAnyatva-darshane saty apy anyonya-niyoga-pratiShedhArtha-pratipattiH | na | vyatiriktAtma-darshana-pratipatteH prAg eva phala-hetvor AtmAbhimAnasya siddhatvAt | pratipanna-niyoga-pratiShedhArtho hi phala-hetubhyAm Atmano 'nyatvam pratipadyate, na pUrvam | tasmAd vidhi-pratiShedha-shAstram avidvad-viShayam iti siddham || 

nanu svarga-kAmo yajeta [Ap.Ár.S. 10.2.1] na kala¤jam bhakShayed ity AdAv Atma-vyatireka-darshinAm apravR^ittau, kevala-dehAdy-Atma-dR^iShTInAm ca | ataH kartur abhAvAc chAstrAnarthakyam iti cet, na | yathA-prasiddhita eva pravR^itti-nivR^itty-upapatteH | Ishvara-kShetraj~naikatva-darshI brahma-vit tAvan na pravartate | tathA nairAtmyavAdy api nAsti para-loka iti na pravartate | yathA-prasiddhitas tu vidhi-pratiShedha-shAstra-shravaNAnyathAnupapattyAnumitAtmAstitva Atma-visheShAnabhij~naH karma-phala-samjAta-tR^iShNaH shraddadhAnatayA ca pravartate | iti sarveShAm na pratyakSham | ato na shAstrAnarthakyam || 

vivekinAm apravR^itti-darshanAt tad-anugAminAm apravR^ittau shAstrAnarthakyam iti cet, na | kasyacid eva vivekopapatteH | anekeShu hi prANiShu kashcid eva vivekI syAt, yathedAnIm | na ca vivekinam anuvartante mUDhAH, rAgAdi-doSha-tantratvAt pravR^itteH, abhicaraNAdau ca pravR^itti-darshanAt, svAbhAvyAc ca pravR^itteH | svabhAvas tu pravartate [GItA 5.14] iti hi uktam || 

tasmAt avidyA-mAtram samsAro yathA-dR^iShTa-viShaya eva | na kShetraj~nasya kevalasyAvidyA tat-kAryam ca | na ca mithyA-j~nAnam paramArtha-vastu dUShayitum samartham | na hy UShara-desham snehena paN^kI-kartum shaknoti marIcy-udakam | tathAvidyA kShetraj~nasya na kimcit kartum shaknoti | atash cedam uktam - kShetraj~nam cApi mAm viddhi | aj~nAnenAvR^itam j~nAnam [GItA 5.15] iti ca || 

atha kim idam samsAriNAm ivAham evam mamaivedam iti paNDitAnAm api ? sR^iNu | idam tat pANDityam, yat kShetra evAtma-darshanam | yadi punaH kShetraj~nam avikriyam pashyeyus tato na bhogam karma vAkAN^kSheyur mama syAd iti | vikriyaiva bhoga-karmaNI | athaivam sati, phalArthitvAd avidvAn pravartate | viduShaH punar avikriyAtma-darshinaH phalArthitvAbhAvAt pravR^itty-anupapattau kArya-karaNa-samghAta-vyApAroparame nivR^ittir upacaryate || 

idam cAnyat pANDityam kasyacid astu - kShetraj~na Ishvara eva | kShetram cAnyat kShetraj~nasyaiva viShayaH | aham tu samsArI sukhI duHkhI ca | samsAroparamash ca mama kartavyaH kShetra-kShetraj~na-vij~nAnena, dhyAnena ceshvaram kShetraj~nam sAkShAt kR^itvA tat-svarUpAvasthAneneti | yash caivam budhyate, yash ca bodhayati, nAsau kShetraj~na iti | evam manvAno yaH sa paNDitApashabdaH | samsAra-mokShayoH shAstrasya cArthavattvam karomIti | AtmahA svayam mUDho 'nyAm ca vyAmohayati shAstrArtha-sampradAya-rahitatvAt, shruta-hAnim ashruta-kalpanAm ca kurvan | tasmAt asampradAya-vit sarva-shAstra-vid api mUrkhavad eva upekShaNIyaH || 

yat tUktam Ishvarasya kShetraj~naikatve samsAritvam prApnoti | kShetraj~nAnAm ceshvaraikatve samsAriNo 'bhAvAt samsArAbhAva-prasaN^ga iti | etau doShau pratyuktau vidyAvidyayor vailakShaNyAbhyupagamAd iti | katham ? avidyA-parikalpita-doSheNa tad-viShayam vastu pAramArthikam na duShyatIti | tathA ca dR^iShTanto darshitaH - marIcy-ambhasA UShara-desho na paN^kIkriyata iti | samsAriNo 'bhAvAt samsArAbhAva-prasaN^ga-doSho 'pi samsAra-samsAriNor avidyA-kalpitatvopapattyA pratyuktaH || 

nanu avidyAvattvam eva kShetraj~nasya samsAritva-doShaH | tat-kR^itam ca sukhitva-duHkhitvAdi pratyakSham upalabhyate iti cet, na | j~neyasya kShetra-dharmatvAt, j~nAtuH kShetraj~nasya tat-kR^ita-doShAnupapatteH | yAvat kimcit kShetraj~nasya doSha-jAtam avidyamAnam Asa¤jayasi, tasya j~neyatvopapatteH kShetra-dharmatvam eva, na kShetraj~na-dharmatvam | na ca tena kShetraj~no duShyati, j~neyena j~nAtuH samsargAnupapatteH | yadi hi samsargaH syAt, j~neyatvam eva nopapadyeta | yady Atmano dharmo 'vidyAvattvam duHkhitvAdi ca katham bhoH pratyakSham upalabhyate | katham vA kShetraj~na-dharmaH | j~neyam ca sarvam kShetram j~nAtaiva kShetraj~na ity avadhArite, avidyA-duHkhitvAdeH kShetraj~na-visheShaNatvam kShetraj~na-dharmatvam tasya ca pratyakShopalabhyatvam iti viruddham ucyate 'vidyA-mAtrAvaShTambhAt kevalam || 

atrAha - sAvidyA kasya ? iti | yasya dR^ishyate tasyaiva | kasya dR^ishyate ? iti | atrocyate - avidyA kasya dR^ishyate iti prashno nirarthakaH | katham ? dR^ishyate ced avidyA, tadvantam api pashyasi | na ca tadvaty upalabhyamAne sA kasya ? iti prashno yuktaH | na hi gomati upalabhyamAne gAvaH kasya ? iti prashno 'rthavAn bhavati | 

nanu viShamo dR^iShTAntaH | gavAm tadvatash ca pratyakShatvAt tat-sambandho 'pi pratyakSha iti prashno nirarthakaH | na tathAvidyA tadvAmsh ca pratyakShau, yataH prashno nirarthakaH syAt | apratyakSheNAvidyAvatAvidyA-sambandhe j~nAte, kim tava syAt ? avidyAyA anartha-hetutvAt parihartavyA syAt | yasyAvidyA, sa tAm parihariShyati | 

nanu mamaivAvidyA | jAnAsi tarhy avidyAm tadvantam ca AtmAnam | jAnAmi, na tu pratyakSheNa | anumAnenash cej jAnAsi, katham sambandhagrahaNam ? na hi tava j~nAtuH j~neya-bhUtayAvidyayA tat-kAle sambandho grahItum shakyate, avidyAyA viShayatvenaiva j~nAtur upayuktatvAt | na ca j~nAtur avidyAyA ca sambandhasya yo grahItA, j~nAnam cAnyat tad-viShayam sambhavati | anavasthA-prApteH | yadi j~nAtrApi j~neya-sambandho j~nAyate, anyo j~nAtA kalpyaH syAt, tasyApy anyaH, tasyApy anyaH ity anavasthAparihAryA | yadi punar avidyA j~neyA, anyad vA j~neyam j~neyam eva | tathA j~nAtApi j~nAtaiva, na j~neyam bhavati | yadA caivam, avidyA-duHkhitvAdyair na j~nAtuH kShetraj~nasya kimcit duShyati || 

nanu ayam eva doShaH, yat doShavat-kShetra-vij~nAtR^itvam | na ca vij~nAna-svarUpasyaivAvikriyasya vij~nAtR^itvopacArAt | yathoShNatA-mAtreNAgnes tapti-kriyopacAraH, tadvat | yathAtra bhagavatA kriyAkAraka-phalAtmatvAbhAva Atmani svata eva darshitaH - avidyAdhyAropita eva kriyA-kArakAdir Atmany upacaryate | tathA tatra tatra ya enam vetti hantAram [GItA 2.19], prakR^iteH kriyamANAni guNaiH karmANi sarvashaH [GItA 3.27], nAdatte kasyacit pApam [GItA 5.15] ity Adi-prakaraNeShu darshitaH | tathaiva ca vyAkhyAtam asmAbhiH | uttareShu ca prakaraNeShu darshayiShyAmaH || 

hanta ! tarhy Atmani kriyA-kAraka-phalAtmatAyAH svato 'bhAve, avidyayA cAdhyAropitatve, karmANy avidvat-kartavyAny eva, na viduShAm iti prAptam | satyam evam prAptam, etad eva ca na hi deha-bhR^itA shakyam ity atra darshayiShyAmaH | sarva-shAstrArthopasamhAra-prakaraNe ca samAsenaiva kaunteya niShThA j~nAnasya yA parA ity atra visheShato darshayiShyAmaH | alam iha bahu-prapaJNcanena, iti upasamhriyate ||BhGS_13.2||

==============================

idam sharIram [GItA 13.2] ity-Adi-shlokopadiShTasya kShetrAdhyAyArthasya samgraha-shloko 'yam upanyasyate tat kShetram yac cety Adi, vyAcikhyAsitasya hy arthasya samgrahopanyAso nyAyya iti - 

tat kShetram yac ca yAdR^ik ca yad-vikAri yatash ca yat |
sa ca yo yat-prabhAvash ca tat samAsena me shR^iNu ||BhG_13.3||

yan nirdiShTam idam sharIram iti tat tac-chabdena parAmR^ishati | yac ca idam nirdiShTam kShetram tat yAdR^ik yAdR^isham svakIyair dharmaiH | ca-shabdaH samuccayArthaH | yad-vikAri yo vikAro yasya tat yad-vikAri, yato yasmAc ca yat, kAryam utpadyate iti vAkya-sheShaH | sa ca yaH kShetraj~no nirdiShTaH sa yat-prabhAvo ye prabhAvA upAdhi-kR^itAH shaktayo yasya sa yat-prabhAvash ca | tat kShetra-kShetraj~nayor yAthAtmyam yathA-visheShitam samAsena samkShepeNa me mama vAkyataH shR^iNu | shrutvAvadhAraya ity arthaH ||BhGS_13.3|| 

==============================

tat kShetra-kShetraj~na-yAthAtmyam vivakShitam stauti shrotR^i-buddhi-prarocanArtham - 

R^iShibhir bahudhA gItam chandobhir vividhaiH pR^ithak |
brahma-sUtra-padaish caiva hetumadbhir vinishcitaiH ||BhG_13.4||

R^iShibhir vasiShThAdibhir bahudhA bahu-prakAram gItam kathitam | chandobhish chandAmsi R^ig-AdIni taish chandobhir vividhair nAnA-bhAvair nAnA-prakAraiH pR^ithag vivekato gItam | kim ca, brahma-sUtra-padaish caiva brahmaNaH sUcakAni vAkyAni brahma-sUtrANi taiH padyate gamyate j~nAyata iti tAni padAny ucyante tair eva ca kShetra-kShetraj~na-yAthAtmyam gItam ity anuvartate | Atmety evopAsIta ity evam Adibhir brahma-sUtra-padair AtmA j~nAyate | hetumadbhir yukti-yuktair vinishcitair niHsamshaya-rUpair nishcita-pratyayotpAdakair ity arthaH ||BhGS_13.4||

==============================

stutyAbhimukhIbhUtAyArjunAyAha bhagavAn - 

mahA-bhUtAny ahamkAro buddhir avyaktam eva ca |
indriyANi dashaikam ca paJNca cendriya-gocarAH ||BhG_13.5||

mahA-bhUtAni mahAnti ca tAni sarva-vikAra-vyApakatvAd bhUtAni ca sUkShmANi | sthUlAni tv indriya-gocara-shabdenAbhidhAyiShyante | ahamkAro mahA-bhUta-kAraNam aham-pratyaya-lakShaNaH | ahamkAra-kAraNam buddhir adhyavasAya-lakShaNA | tat-kAraNam avyaktam eva ca, na vyaktam avyaktam avyAkR^itam Ishvara-shaktir mama mAyA duratyayA ity uktam | eva-shabdaH prakR^ity-avadhAraNArtha etAvaty evAShTadhA bhinnA prakR^itiH | ca-shabdo bheda-samuccayArthaH | indriyANi dasha, shrotrAdIni paJNca buddhy-utpAdakatvAd buddhIndriyANi | vAk-pANy-AdIni paJNca karma-nirvartakatvAt karmendriyANi | tAni dasha | ekam ca | kim tat ? mana ekAdasham samkalpAdyAtmakam | paJNca cendriya-gocarAH shabdAdayo viShayAH | tAny etAni sAmkhyAsh catur-vimshati-tattvAny AcakShate ||BhGS_13.5|| 

==============================

athedAnIm Atma-guNAH iti yAn AcakShate vaisheShikAs te 'pi kShetra-dharmA eva, na tu kShetraj~nasyety Aha bhagavAn -

icchA dveShaH sukham duHkham samghAtash cetanA dhR^itiH |
etat kShetram samAsena sa-vikAram udAhR^itam ||BhG_13.6||

icchA yaj-jAtIyam sukha-hetum artham upalabdhavAn pUrvam, punas taj-jAtIyam upalabhamAnas tam AdAtum icchati sukha-hetur iti | seyam icchAntaH-karaNa-dharmo j~neyatvAt kShetram | tathA dveShaH, yaj-jAtIyam artham duHkha-hetutvenAnubhUtavAn, punas taj-jAtIyam artham upalabhamAnas tam dveShTi | so 'yam dveSho j~neyatvAt kShetram eva | tathA sukham anukUlam prasanna-sattvAtmakam j~neyatvAt kShetram eva | duHkham pratikUlAtmakam | j~neyatvAt tad api kShetram | samghAto dehendriyANAm samhatiH | tasyAm abhivyaktAntaHkaraNa-vR^ittiH, tapta iva loha-piNDe 'gniH | Atma-caitanyAbhAsa-rasa-viddhA cetanA | sA ca kShetram j~neyatvAt | dhR^itir yayAvasAda-prAptAni dehendriyANi dhriyante | sA ca j~neyatvAt kShetram | sarvAntaH-karaNa-dharmopalakShaNArtham icchAdi-grahaNam | yata uktam upasamharati - etad iti | etat kShetram samAsena sa-vikAram saha vikAreNa mahad-AdinA udAhR^itam uktam ||BhGS_13.6|| 

==============================

yasya kShetra-bheda-jAtasya samhatiH idam sharIram kShetram [GItA 13.2] ity uktam | tat kShetram vyAkhyAtam mahA-bhUtAdi-bheda-bhinnam dhR^ity-antam | kShetraj~no vakShyamANa-visheShaNaH - yasya sa-prabhAvasya kShetraj~nasya parij~nAnAd amR^itatvam bhavati, tam j~neyam yat tat pravakShyAmIty AdinA sa-visheShaNam svayam eva vakShyati bhagavAn | adhunA tu taj-j~nAna-sAdhana-gaNam amAnitvAdi-lakShaNam, yasmin sati taj-j~neya-vij~nAne yogyo 'dhikR^ito bhavati, yat-paraH samnyAsI j~nAna-niShTha ucyate, tam amAnitvAdi-gaNam j~nAna-sAdhanatvAj j~nAna-shabda-vAcyam vidadhAti bhagavAn - 

amAnitvam adambhitvam ahimsA kShAntir Arjavam |
AcAryopAsanam shaucam sthairyam Atma-vinigrahaH ||BhG_13.7||

amAnitvam mAnino bhAvaH mAnitvam Atmano shlAghanam, tad-abhAvo 'mAnitvam | adambhitvam sva-dharma-prakaTIkaraNam dambhitvam, tad-abhAvo 'dambhitvam | ahimsA himsanam prANinAm apIDAnam | kShAntiH parAparAdha-prAptAv avikriyA | Arjavam R^iju-bhAvo 'vakratvam | AcAryopAsanam mokSha-sAdhanopadeShTur AcAryasya shushrUShAdi-prayogeNa sevanam | shaucam kAya-malAnAm mR^ij-jalAbhyAm prakShAlanam | antash ca manasaH pratipakSha-bhAvanayA rAgAdi-malAnAm apanayanam shaucam | sthairyam sthira-bhAvaH, mokSha-mArga eva kR^itAdhyavasAyatvam | Atma-vinigraha Atmano 'pakArakasya Atma-shabda-vAcyasya kArya-karaNa-samghAtasya vinigrahaH svabhAvena sarvataH pravR^ittasya san-mArga eva nirodha Atma-vinigrahaH ||BhGS_13.7|| 

==============================

kim ca - 
indriyArtheShu vairAgyam anahamkAra eva ca |
janma-mR^ityu-jarA-vyAdhi-duHkha-doShAnudarshanam ||BhG_13.8||
 
indriyArtheShu shabdAdiShu dR^iShTAdR^iShTeShu bhogeShu virAga-bhAvo vairAgyam | anahamkAro 'hamkArAbhAva eva ca | janma-mR^ityu-jarA-vyAdhi-duHkha-doShAnudarshanam janma ca mR^ityush ca jarA ca vyAdhayash ca duHkhAni ca teShu janmAdi-duHkhAnteShu pratyekam doShAnudarshanam | janmani garbha-vAsa-yoni-dvAra-niHsaraNam doShaH, tasyAnudarshanam Alocanam | tathA mR^ityau doShAnudarshanam | tathA jarAyAm praj~nA-shakti-tejo-nirodha-doShAnudarshanam paribhUtatA ceti | tathA vyAdhiShu shiro-rogAdiShu doShAnudarshanam | tathA duHkheShu adhyAtmAdhibhUtAdhidaiva-nimitteShu | athavA duHkhAny eva doSho duHkha-doShas tasya janmAdiShu pUrvavad anudarshanam | duHkham janma, duHkham mR^ityuH, duHkham jarA, duHkham vyAdhayaH | duHkha-nimittatvAj janmAdayo duHkham, na punaH svarUpeNaiva duHkham iti | evam janmAdiShu duHkha-doShAnudarshanAd dehendriyAdi-viShaya-bhogeShu vairAgyam upajAyate | tataH pratyag-Atmani pravR^ittiH karaNAnAm Atma-darshanAya | evam j~nAna-hetutvAj j~nAnam ucyate janmAdi-duHkha-doShAnudarshanam ||BhGS_13.8|| 

==============================

kim ca -
asaktir anabhiShvaN^gaH putra-dAra-gR^ihAdiShu |
nityam ca sama-cittatvam iShTAniShTopapattiShu ||BhG_13.9||

asaktiH saktiH saN^ga-nimitteShu viShayeShu prIti-mAtram, tad-abhAvo 'saktiH | anabhiShvaN^go 'bhiShvaN^gAbhAvaH | abhiShvaN^go nAma Asakti-visheSha evAnanyAtma-bhAvanA-lakShaNaH | yathAnyasmin sukhini duHkhini vAham eva sukhI, duHkhI ca, jIvati mR^ite vAham eva jIvAmi mariShyAmi ceti | kva ? ity Aha - putra-dAra-gR^ihAdiShu | putreShu dAreShu gR^iheShv Adi-grahaNAd anyeShv apy atyanteShTeShu dAsa-vargAdiShu | tac cobhayam j~nAnArthatvAj j~nAnam ucyate | nityam ca sama-cittatvam tulya-cittatA | kva ? iShTAniShTopapattiShv iShTAnAm aniShTAnAm copapattayaH samprAptayas tAsv iShTAniShTopapattiShu nityam eva tulya-cittatA | iShTopapattiShu na hR^iShyati, na kupyati cAniShTopapattiShu | tac caitan nityam sama-cittatvam j~nAnam ||BhGS_13.9|| 

==============================

kim ca - 
mayi cAnanya-yogena bhaktir avyabhicAriNI |
vivikta-desha-sevitvam aratir jana-samsadi ||BhG_13.10||

mayi ceshvare 'nanya-yogena apR^ithak-samAdhinA nAnyo bhagavato vAsudevAt paro 'sti, ataH sa eva no gatir ity evam nishcitAvyabhicAriNI buddhir ananya-yogaH, tena bhajanam bhaktir na vyabhicaraNa-shIlA avyabhicAriNI | sA ca j~nAnam | vivikta-desha-sevitvam | viviktaH svabhAvataH samskAreNa vAshucy-AdibhiH sarpa-vyAghrAdibhish ca rahito 'raNya-nadI-pulina-deva-gR^ihAdibhir vivikto deshaH, tam sevitum shIlam asyeti vivikta-desha-sevI, tad-bhAvo vivikta-desha-sevitvam | vivikteShu hi desheShu cittam prasIdati yatas tataH AtmAdi-bhAvanA vivikta upajAyate | ato vivakta-desha-sevitvam j~nAnam ucyate | aratir aramaNam jana-samsadi | janAnAm prAkR^itAnAm samskAra-shUnyAnAm avinItAnAm samsat samavAyo jana-samsat | na samskAravatAm vinItAnAm samsat | tasyA j~nAnopakArakatvAt | ataH prAkR^ita-jana-samsady aratir j~nAnArthatvAj j~nAnam ||BhGS_13.10|| 

 ==============================

 kim ca - 
adhyAtma-j~nAna-nityatvam tattva-j~nAnArtha-darshanam |
etaj j~nAnam iti proktam aj~nAnam yad ato 'nyathA ||BhG_13.11||

adhyAtma-j~nAna-nityatvam AtmAdi-viShayam j~nAnam adhyAtma-j~nAnam, tasmin nitya-bhAvo nityatvam | amAnitvAdInAm j~nAna-sAdhanAnAm bhAvanA-paripAka-nimittam tattva-j~nAnam, tasyArtho mokShaH samsAroparamaH | tasyAlocanam tattva-j~nAnArtha-darshanam | tattva-j~nAna-phalAlocane hi tat-sAdhanAnuShThAne pravR^ittiH syAd iti | etad amAnitvAdi-tattva-j~nAnArtha-darshanAntam uktam j~nAnam iti proktam j~nAnArthatvAt | aj~nAnam yad ato 'smAd yathoktAd anyathA viparyayeNa | mAnitvam dambhitvam himsA kShAntir anArjavam ity Ady aj~nAnam vij~neyam pariharaNAya, samsAra-pravR^itti-kAraNatvAd iti ||BhGS_13.11|| 

==============================

yathoktena j~nAnena j~nAtavyam kim ? ity AkAN^kShAyAm Aha - 

j~neyam yat tat pravakShyAmi yaj j~nAtvAmR^itam ashnute |
anAdimat param brahma na sat tan nAsad ucyate ||BhG_13.12||

nanu yamAH niyamAsh cAmAnitvAdayaH | na tair j~neyam j~nAyate | na hy amAnitvAdi kasyacit vastunaH paricchedakam dR^iShTam | sarvatraiva ca yad-viShayam j~nAnam tad eva tasya j~neyasya paricchedakam dR^ishyate | na hy anya-viShayeNa j~nAnenAnyad upalabhyate, yathA ghaTa-viShayeNa j~nAnenAgniH | naiSha doShaH | j~nAna-nimittatvAj j~nAnam ucyata iti hy avocAma | j~nAna-sahakAri-kAraNatvAc ca | j~neyam j~nAtavyam yat tat pravakShyAmi prakarSheNa yathAvat vakShyAmi | kim-phalam tat ? iti prarocanena shrotur abhimukhIkaraNAyAha - yaj j~neyam j~nAtvAmR^itam amR^itatvam ashnute, na punar mriyata ity arthaH | anAdimat Adir asyAstIti Adimat, nAdimad anAdimat | kim tat ? param niratishayam brahma, j~neyam iti prakR^itam |

atra kecit anAdi mat-param iti padam chindanti, bahu-vrIhiNokte 'rthe matupa Anarthakyam aniShTam syAd iti | artha-visheSham ca darshayanti - aham vAsudevAkhyA parA shaktir yasya tan mat-param iti | satyam evam apunar-uktam syAt | arthash cet sambhavati | na tv arthaH sambhavati, brahmaNaH sarva-visheSha-pratiShedhenaiva vijij~nApayiShitvAn na sat tan nAsad ucyate iti | vishiShTa-shaktimattva-pradarshanam visheSha-pratiShedhash ceti vipratiShiddham | tasmAt matupo bahu-vrIhiNA samAnArthatve 'pi prayogo shloka-pUraNArthaH | amR^itatva-phalam j~neyam mayocyata iti prarocanenAbhimukhIkR^ityAha - na sat taj j~neyam ucyate iti nApy asat tad ucyate || 

nanu mahatA parikara-bandhena kaNTha-raveNodghuShya j~neyam pravakShyAmIti, ananurUpam uktam na sat tan nAsad ucyata iti | na, anurUpam evoktam | katham ? sarvAsu hy upaniShatsu j~neyam brahma neti neti [BAU 2.3.6] asthUlam anaNu [BAU 3.8.8] ity Adi-visheSha-pratiShedhenaiva nirdishyate, nedam tad iti vAco 'gocatvAt || 

nanu na tad asti, yad vastv asti-shabdena nocyate | athAsti-shabdena nocyate, nAsti taj j~neyam | vipratiShiddham ca - j~neyam tad asti-shabdena nocyate iti ca | na tAvan nAsti, nAsti-buddhy-aviShayatvAt || 

nanu sarvA buddhayo 'sti-nAsti-buddhy-anugatA eva | tatraivam sati j~neyam apy asti-buddhy-anugata-pratyaya-viShayam vA syAt, nAsti-buddhy-anugata-pratyaya-viShayam vA syAt | na, atIndriyatvenobhaya-buddhy-anugata-pratyayAviShayatvAt | yad dhIndriya-gamyam vastu ghaTAdikam, tad asti-buddhy-anugata-pratyaya-viShayam vA syAt, nAsti-buddhy-anugata-pratyaya-viShayam vA syAt | idam tu j~neyam atIndriyatvena shabdaika-pramANa-gamyatvAn na ghaTAdivad ubhaya-buddhy-anugata-pratyaya-viShayam ity ato na sat tan nAsad ity ucyate || 

yat tUktam - viruddham ucyate, j~neyam tan na sat tan nAsad ucyata iti | na viruddham, anyad eva tad-viditAd atho aviditAd adhi [KenaU 1.3] iti shruteH | shrutir api viruddhArthA iti cet - yathA yaj~nAya shAlAm Arabhya yaj~nam ko hi tad veda yady amuShmin loke 'sti vA na veti [TaittS 6.1.1] ity evam iti cet, na | viditAviditAbhyAm anyatva-shruter avashya-vij~neyArtha-pratipAdana-paratvAt yady amuShmin ity Adi tu vidhi-sheSho 'rtha-vAdaH | upapattesh ca sad-asad-Adi-shabdair brahma nocyata iti | 

sarvo hi shabdo 'rtha-prakAshanAya prayuktaH shrUyamANash ca shrotR^ibhir jAti-kriyA-guNa-sambandha-dvAreNa samketa-grahaNa-sa-vyapekShArtham pratyAyayati | nAnyathA, adR^iShTatvAt | tad yathA - gaur ashva iti vA jAtitaH, pacati paThatIti vA kriyAtaH, shuklaH kR^iShNa iti vA guNataH, dhanI gomAn iti vA sambandhataH | na tu brahma jAtimat, ato na sad-Adi-shabda-vAcyam | nApi guNavat, yena guNa-shabdenocyeta, nirguNatvAt | nApi kriyA-shabda-vAcyam niShkriyatvAn niShkalam niShkriyam shAntam [ÁvetU 6.19] iti shruteH | na ca sambandhI, ekatvAt | advayatvAd aviShayatvAd AtmatvAc ca na kenacit, shabdenocyata iti yuktam | yato vAco nivartante [TaittU 2.9] ity Adi-shrutibhish ca ||BhGS_13.12|| 

==============================

sac-chabda-pratyayAviShayatvAd asattvAshaN^kAyAm j~neyasya sarva-prANi-karaNopAdhi-dvAreNa tad-astitvam pratipAdayan tad-AshaN^kA-nivR^itty-artham Aha - 

sarvataH pANi-pAdam tat sarvato 'kShi-shiro-mukham |
sarvataH shrutimal loke sarvam AvR^itya tiShThati ||BhG_13.13||

sarvataH pANi-pAdam sarvataH pANayaH pAdAsh cAsyeti sarvataH pANi-pAdam taj j~neyam | sarva-prANi-karaNopAdhibhiH kShetraj~nasyAstitvam vibhAvyate | kShetraj~nash ca kShetropAdhita ucyate | kShetram ca pANi-pAdAdibhir anekadhA bhinnam | kShetropAdhi-bheda-kR^itam visheSha-jAtam mithyaiva kShetraj~nasya, iti tad-apanayanena j~neyatvam uktam na sat tan nAsad ucyate iti | upAdhi-kR^itam mithyA-rUpam apy astitvAdhigamAya j~neya-dharmavat parikalpya ucyate sarvataH pANi-pAdam ity Adi | tathA hi sampradAya-vidAm vacanam - adhyAropApavAdAbhyAm niShprapaJNcam prapaJNcyate iti | sarvatra sarva-dehAvayavatvena gamyamAnAH pANi-pAdAdayo j~neya-shakti-sad-bhAva-nimitta-svakAryA iti j~neya-sad-bhAve liN^gAni j~neyasyeti upacArata ucyante | tathA vyAkhyeyam anyat | sarvataH pANi-pAdam taj j~neyam | sarvato 'kShi-shiro-mukham sarvato 'kShINi shirAmsi mukhAni ca yasya tat sarvato 'kShi-shiro-mukham | sarvataH shrutimat | shrutiH shravaNendriyam, tat yasya tat shrutimat | loke prANi-nikAye | sarvam AvR^itya samvyApya tiShThati sthitim labhate ||BhGS_13.13|| 

==============================

upAdhibhUta-pANi-pAdAdIndriyAdhyAropaNAj j~neyasya tadvattAshaN^kA mA bhUd ity evam arthaH shlokArambhaH - 

sarvendriya-guNAbhAsam sarvendriya-vivarjitam |
asaktam sarva-bhR^ic caiva nirguNam guNa-bhoktR^i ca ||BhG_13.14||

sarvendriya-guNAbhAsam sarvANi ca tAnIndriyANi shrotrAdIni buddhIndriya-karmendriyAkhyAni, antaH-karaNe ca buddhi-manasI, j~neyopAdhitvasya tulyatvAt, sarvendriya-grahaNena gR^ihyante | api ca, antaH-karaNopAdhi-dvAreNaiva shrotrAdInAm api upAdhitvam ity ato 'ntaH-karaNa-bahiShkaraNopAdhi-bhUtaiH sarvendriya-guNair adhyavasAya-samkalpa-shravaNa-vacanAdibhir avabhAsate iti sarvendriya-guNAbhAsam sarvendriya-vyApArair vyApR^itam iva taj j~neyam ity arthaH | dhyAyatIva lelAyatIva [BAU 4.3.7] iti shruteH | 

kasmAt punaH kAraNAn na vyApR^itam eveti gR^ihyata ity ataH Aha - sarvendriya-vivarjitam, sarva-karaNa-rahitam ity arthaH | ato na karaNa-vyApAraiH vyApR^itam taj j~neyam | yas tv ayam mantraH - apANi-pAdo javano grahItA pashyaty acakShuH sa sR^iNoty akarNaH [ÁvetU 3.19] ity AdiH | sa sarvendriyopAdhi-guNAnuguNya-bhajana-shaktimat taj j~neyam ity evam pradarshanArthaH, na tu sAkShAd eva javanAdi-kriyAvattva-pradarshanArthaH | andho maNim avindad [Taittù 1.11] ity Adi-mantrArthavat tasya mantrasyArthaH | yasmAt sarva-karaNa-varjitam j~neyam, tasmAd asaktam sarva-samshleShavarjitam | yadyapy evam, tathApi sarva-bhR^ic caiva | sad-Aspadam hi sarvam sarvatra sad-buddhy-anugamAt | na hi mR^igatR^iShNikAdayo 'pi nirAspadA bhavanti | ataH sarva-bhR^it sarvam bibhartIti | syAd idam cAnyaj j~neyasya sattvAdhigama-dvAram - nirguNam sattva-rajas-tamAmsi guNAs tair varjitam taj j~neyam, tathApi guNa-bhoktR^i ca guNAnAm sattva-rajas-tamasAm shabdAdi-dvAreNa sukha-duHkha-mohAkAra-pariNatAnAm bhoktR^i copalabdhR^i ca taj j~neyam ity arthaH ||BhGS_13.14|| 

==============================

kim ca - 
bahir antash ca bhUtAnAm acaram caram eva ca |
sUkShmatvAt tad avij~neyam dUra-stham cAntike ca tat ||BhG_13.15||

bahis tvak-paryantam deham AtmatvenAvidyA-kalpitam apekShya tam evAvavadhim kR^itvA bahir ucyate | tathA pratyag-AtmAnam apekShya deham evAvadhim kR^itvA antar ucyate | bahir antash cety ukte madhye 'bhAve prApte, idam ucyate - acaram caram eva ca, yac carAcaram dehAbhAsam api tad eva j~neyam, yathA rajju-sarpAbhAsaH | 

yady acaram caram eva ca syAt vyavahAra-viShayam sarvam j~neyam, kim-artham idam iti sarvair na vij~neyam ? ity ucyate - satyam sarvAbhAsam tat | tathApi vyomavat sUkShmam | ataH sUkShmatvAt svena rUpeNa taj j~neyam apy avij~neyam aviduShAm | viduShAm tu, Atmaivedam sarvam [BAU 7.25.2] brahmaivedam sarvam [BAU 2.5.1] ity Adi-pramANato nityam vij~nAtam | avij~nAtatayA dUra-stham varSha-sahasra-koTyApy aviduShAm aprApyatvAt | antike ca tat, AtmatvAd viduShAm ||BhGS_13.15|| 

==============================

kim ca - 
avibhaktam ca bhUteShu vibhaktam iva ca sthitam |
bhUta-bhartR^i ca taj j~neyam grasiShNu prabhaviShNu ca ||BhG_13.16||

avibhaktam ca pratideham vyomavat tad ekam | bhUteShu sarva-prANiShu vibhaktam iva ca sthitam deheShv eva vibhAvyamAnatvAt | bhUta-bhartR^i ca bhUtAni bibharti taj j~neyam bhUta-bhartR^i ca sthiti-kAle | pralaya-kAle grasiShNu grasana-shIlam | utpatti-kAle prabhaviShNu ca prabhavana-shIlam yathA rajjvAdiH sarpAder mithyA-kalpitasya ||BhGS_13.16|| 

==============================

kim ca, sarvatra vidyamAnam api san nopalabhyate cet, j~neyam tamas tarhi ? na | kim tarhi ? - 

jyotiShAm api taj jyotis tamasaH param ucyate |
j~nAnam j~neyam j~nAna-gamyam hR^idi sarvasya viShThitam ||BhG_13.17||

jyotiShAm Adity-AdInAm api taj j~neyam jyotiH | Atma-caitanya-jyotiSheddhAni hy Adity-AdIni jyotImShi dIpyante, yena sUryas tapati tejaseddhaH [TaittBr 3.12.9], tasya bhAsA sarvam idam vibhAti [ÁvetU 6.14] Ity Adi-shrutibhyaH | smR^ite ca ihaiva - yad Aditya-gatam tejaH [GItA 15.12] ity AdeH | tamaso 'j~nAnAt param aspR^iShTam ucyate | j~nAnAder duHsampAdana-buddhyA prAptAvasAdasyottambhanArtham Aha - j~nAnam amAnitvAdi | j~neyam j~neyam yat tat pravakShyAmIty [GItA 13.13] Adinoktam | j~nAna-gamyam j~neyam eva j~nAtam saj j~nAna-phalam iti j~nAna-gamyam ucyate | j~nAyamAnam tu j~neyam | tad etat trayam api hR^idi buddhau sarvasya prANi-jAtasya viShThitam visheSheNa sthitam | tatraiva hi trayam vibhAvyate ||BhGS_13.17|| 
==============================

 yathoktArthopasamhArArtho 'yam shloka Arabhyate - 

iti kShetram tathA j~nAnam j~neyam coktam samAsataH |
mad-bhakta etad vij~nAya mad-bhAvAyopapadyate ||BhG_13.18||

ity evam kShetram mahA-bhUtAdi-dhR^ity-antam, tathA j~nAnam amAnitvAdi tattva-j~nAnArtha-darshana-paryantam, j~neyam ca j~neyam yat tat ity Adi tamasaH param ucyate ity evam antam uktam samAsataH samkShepataH | etAvAn sarvo hi vedArtho gItArthash copasamhR^ityoktaH | asmin samyag-darshane ko 'dhikriyate ? ity ucyate - mad-bhakto mayIshvare sarvaj~ne parama-gurau vAsudeve samarpita-sarvAtma-bhAvo yat pashyati shR^iNoti spR^ishati vA sarvam eva bhagavAn vAsudevaH ity evam-grahAviShTa-buddhir mad-bhaktaH sa etad yathoktam samyag darshanam vij~nAya, mad-bhAvAya mama bhAvo mad-bhAvaH paramAtma-bhAvas tasmai mad-bhAvAya upapadyate, mokSham gacchati ||BhGS_13.18||

 ==============================

tatra saptame Ishvarasya dve prakR^itI upanyaste parApare kShetra-kShetraj~na-lakShaNe | etad-yonIni bhUtAni [GItA 7.7] iti coktam | kShetra-kShetraj~na-prakR^iti-dvaya-yonitvam katham bhUtAnAm ity ayam artho 'dhunocyate - 

prakR^itim puruSham caiva viddhy anAdI ubhAv api |
vikArAmsh ca guNAmsh caiva viddhi prakR^iti-sambhavAn ||BhG_13.19||

prakR^itim puruSham caiva Ishvarasya prakR^itI | tau prakR^iti-puruShau ubhAv apy anAdi viddhi, na vidyate Adir yayos tau anAdI | nityeshvaratvAd Ishvarasya tat-prakR^ityor api yuktam nityatvena bhavitum | prakR^iti-dvayavattvam eva hIshvarasyeshvaratvam | yAbhyAm prakR^itibhyAm Ishvaro jagad-utpatti-sthiti-pralaya-hetus te dve 'nAdI satyau samsArasya kAraNam || 

nAdI anAdI iti tat-puruSha-samAsam kecit varNayanti | tena hi kileshvarasya kAraNatvam sidhyati | yadi punaH prakR^iti-puruShAv eva nityau syAtAm tat-kR^itam eva jagat, neshvarasya jagataH kartR^itvam | tad asat | prAk prakR^iti-puruShayor utpatter IshitavyAbhAvAd IshvarasyAnIshvaratva-prasaN^gAt, samsArasya nirnimittatve 'nirmokSha-prasaN^gAt shAstrAnarthakya-prasaN^gAd bandha-mokShAbhAva-prasaN^gAc ca | nityatve punar Ishvarasya prakR^ityoH sarvam etad upapannam bhavet | katham ? vikArAmsh ca guNAmsh caiva | vakShyamANAn vikArAn buddhy-Adi-dehendriyAntAn guNAmsh ca sukha-duHkha-moha-pratyayAkAra-pariNatAn viddhi jAnIhi prakR^iti-sambhavAn | prakR^itir Ishvarasya vikAra-kAraNa-shaktis triguNAtmikA mAyA | sA sambhavo yeShAm vikArANAm guNAnAm ca tAn vikArAn guNAmsh ca viddhi prakR^iti-sambhavAn prakR^iti-pariNAmAn ||BhGS_13.19||

==============================
 
ke punas te vikArAH guNAsh ca prakR^iti-sambhavAH ? ity Aha --

kArya-karaNa-kartR^itve hetuH prakR^itir ucyate |
puruShaH sukha-duHkhAnAm bhoktR^itve hetur ucyate ||BhG_13.20||

kArya-karaNa-kartR^itve - kAryam sharIram karaNAni tat-sthAni trayodasha | dehasyArambhakANi bhUtAni paJNca viShayAsh ca prakR^iti-sambhavAH vikArAH pUrvoktA iha kArya-grahaNena gR^ihyante | guNAsh ca prakR^iti-sambhavAH sukha-duHkha-mohAtmakAH karaNAshrayatvAt karaNa-grahaNena gR^ihyante | teShAm kArya-karaNAnAm kartR^itvam utpAdakatvam yat tat kArya-karaNa-kartR^itvam tasmin kArya-karaNa-kartR^itve hetuH kAraNam Arambhakatvena prakR^itir ucyate | evam kArya-karaNa-kartR^itvena samsArasya kAraNam prakR^itiH | 

kArya-kAraNa-kartR^itve ity asminn api pAThe, kAryam yat yasya pariNAmas tat tasya kAryam vikAro vikAri kAraNam tayor vikAra-vikAriNoH kArya-kAraNayoH kartR^itve iti | athavA, ShoDAsha vikArAH kAryam sapta prakR^iti-vikR^itayaH kAraNam tAny eva kArya-kAraNAny ucyante teShAm kartR^itve hetuH prakR^itir ucyate, Arambhakatvenaiva | 

puruShash ca samsArasya kAraNam yathA syAt tad ucyate - puruSho jIvaH kShetraj~no bhoktA iti paryAyaH, sukha-duHkhAnAm bhogyAnAm bhoktR^itve upalabdhR^itve hetur ucyate | katham punar anena kArya-karaNa-kartR^itvena sukha-duHkha-bhoktR^itvena ca prakR^iti-puruShayoH samsAra-kAraNatvam ucyate ? ity atrocyate - kArya-karaNa-sukha-duHkha-rUpeNa hetu-phalAtmanA prakR^iteH pariNAmAbhAve, puruShasya ca cetanasyAsati tad-upalabdhR^itve, kutaH samsAraH syAt ? yadA punaH kArya-karaNa-sukha-duHkha-svarUpeNa hetu-phalAtmanA pariNatayA prakR^ityA bhogyayA puruShasya tad-viparItasya bhoktR^itvenAvidyA-rUpaH samyogaH syAt, tadA samsAraH syAd iti | ato yat prakR^iti-puruShayoH kArya-karaNa-kartR^itvena sukha-duHkha-bhoktR^itvena ca samsAra-kAraNatvam uktam, tad yuktam | kaH punar ayam samsAro nAma ? sukha-duHkha-sambhogaH samsAraH | puruShasya ca sukha-duHkhAnAm sambhoktR^itvam samsAritvam iti ||BhGS_13.20|| 

==============================

yat puruShasya sukha-duHkhAnAm bhoktR^itvam samsAritvam ity uktam tasya tat kim-nimittam ity ucyate - 

puruShaH prakR^iti-stho hi bhuN^kte prakR^itijAn guNAn |
kAraNam guNa-saN^go 'sya sad-asad-yoni-janmasu ||BhG_13.21||

puruSho bhoktA prakR^iti-sthaH | prakR^itAv avidyA-lakShaNAyAm kArya-karaNa-rUpeNa pariNatAyAm sthitaH prakR^iti-sthaH | prakR^itim Atmatvena gataH ity etat | hi yasmAt | tasmAd bhuN^kte upalabhata ity arthaH | prakR^itijAn prakR^itito jAtAn sukha-duHkha-mohAkArAbhivyaktAn guNAn sukhI, duHkhI, mUDhaH, paNDito 'ham ity evam | satyAm apy avidyAyAm sukha-duHkha-moheShu guNeShu bhujyamAneShu yaH saN^ga Atma-bhAvaH samsArasya sa pradhAnam kAraNam yasya puruShasya janmanaH | sa yathA-kAmo bhavati tat kratur bhavati [BAU 4.4.5] ity Adi shruteH | tad etad Aha - kAraNam hetur guNa-saN^go guNeShu saN^go 'sya puruShasya bhoktuH sad-asad-yoni-janmasu | satyash cAsatyash ca yonayaH sad-asad-yonayas tAsu sad-asad-yonuShu janmAni sad-asad-yoni-janmAni, teShu sad-asad-yoni-janmaShu viShaya-bhUteShu kAraNam guNa-saN^gaH | athavA, sad-asad-yoni-janmasu asya samsArasya kAraNam guNa-saN^ga iti samsAra-pada-madhyAhAryam | sad-yonayo devAdi-yonayaH | asad-yonayaH pashvAdi-yonayaH | sAmarthyAt sad-asad-yonayaH manuShya-yonayo 'py aviruddhAH draShTAvyAH || 

etad uktam bhavati - prakR^iti-sthatvAkhyAvidyA guNeShu ca saN^gaH kAmaH samsArasya kAraNam iti | tac ca parivarjanAya ucyate | asya ca nivR^itti-kAraNam j~nAna-vairAgye sa-samnyAse gItA-shAstre prasiddham | tac ca j~nAnam purastAd upanyastam kShetra-kShetraj~na-viShayam yaj j~nAtvAmR^itam ashnute [GItA 12.13] iti | uktam cAnyApohenAtad-dharmAdhyAropeNa ca ||BhGS_13.21|| 

==============================
 
tasyaiva punaH sAkShAn nirdeshaH kriyate - 

upadraShTAnumantA ca bhartA bhoktA maheshvaraH |
paramAtmeti cApy ukto dehe 'smin puruShaH paraH ||BhG_13.22||

upadraShTA samIpa-sthaH san draShTA svayam avyApR^itaH | yathA R^itvig-yajamAneShu yaj~na-karma-vyApR^iteShu taTastho 'nyo 'vyApR^ito yaj~na-vidyA-kushalaH R^itvig-yajamAna-vyApAra-guNa-doShANAm IkShitA, tadvac ca kArya-karaNa-vyApAreShu sa-vyApArANAm sAmIpyena draShTA upadraShTA | athavA, deha-cakShur-mano-buddhy-AtmAno draShTAraH | teShAm bAhyo draShTA dehaH | tata ArabhyAntaratamash ca pratyak samIpe AtmA draShTA, yataH paro 'ntaratamo nAsti draShTA | so 'tishaya-sAmIpyena draShTR^itvAd upadraShTA syAt | yaj~nopadraShTR^iavad vA sarva-viShayI-karaNAd upadraShTA | anumantA ca | anumodanam anumananam kurvatsu tat-kriyAsu paritoShas tat-kartAnumantA ca | athavA, anumantA kArya-karaNa-pravR^ittiShu svayam apravR^itto 'pi pravR^itta iva tad-anukUlo vibhAvyate, tenAnumantA | athavA, pravR^ittAn sva-vyApAreShu tat-sAkShi-bhUtaH kadAcid api na nivArayatIty anumantA | 

bhartA | bharaNam nAma dehendriya-mano-buddhInAm samhatAnAm caitanyAtma-pArArthyena nimitta-bhUtena caitanyAbhAsAnAm yat svarUpa-dhAraNam, tac caitanyAtma-kR^itam eveti bhartA Atmety ucyate | bhoktA | agny-uShNavan nitya-caitanya-svarUpeNa buddheH sukha-duHkha-mohAtmakAH pratyayAH sarva-viShaya-viShayAsh caitanyAtma-grastA iva jAyamAnA vibhaktA vibhAvyante iti bhoktA Atmocyate | maheshvaraH | sarvAtmatvAt svatantratvAc ca mahAn Ishvarash ceti maheshvaraH | paramAtmA | dehAdInAm buddhy-antAnAm pratyag-Atmatvena kalpitAnAm avidyayA parama upadraShTR^itvAdi-lakShaNa Atmeti paramAtmA | so 'ntaH paramAtmA ity anena shabdena cApy uktaH kathitaH shrutau | kvAsau ? asmin dehe puruShaH paro 'vyaktAt | uttamaH puruShas tv anyaH paramAtmety udAhR^itaH [GItA 13.3] iti yo vakShyamANaH kShetraj~nam cApi mAm viddhi [GItA 13.2] iti upanyasto vyAkhyAyopasamhR^itash ca ||BhGS_13.22|| 

==============================
 
tam etam yathokta-lakShaNam AtmAnam - 

ya evam vetti puruSham prakR^itim ca guNaiH saha |
sarvathA vartamAno 'pi na sa bhUyo 'bhijAyate ||BhG_13.23||

ya evam yathokta-prakAreNa vetti puruSham sAkShAd Atma-bhAvena "ayam aham asmi" iti prakR^itim ca yathoktAm avidyA-lakShaNAm guNaiH sva-vikAraiH saha nivartitAm abhAvam ApAditAm vidyayA, sarvathA sarva-prakAreNa vartamAno 'pi sa bhUyaH punaH patite 'smin vidvac-charIre dehAntarAya nAbhijAyate notpadyate, dehAntaram na gR^ihNAtIty arthaH | api-shabdAt kim u vaktavyam ? sva-vR^itta-stho na jAyate ity abhiprAyaH || 

nanu, yady api j~nAnotpatty-anantaram punar-janmAbhAva uktaH, tathApi prAg j~nAnotpatteH kR^itAnAm karmaNAm uttara-kAla-bhAvinAm ca yAni cAtikrAntAneka-janma-kR^itAni teShAm ca phalam adattvA nAsho na yukta iti | syus trINi janmAni kR^ita-vipraNAsho hi na yukta iti, yathA phale pravR^ittAnAm Arabdha-janmanAm karmaNAm | na ca karmaNAm visheSho 'vagamyate | tasmAt tri-prakArANy api karmANi trINi janmAny Arabheran | samhatAni vA sarvANy ekam janmArabheran | anyathA kR^ita-vinAshe sati sarvatrAnAshvAsa-prasaN^gaH, shAstrAnarthakyam ca syAt | ity ataH idam ayuktam uktam na sa bhUyo 'bhijAyate iti | na | kShIyante cAsya karmANi [MuNDU 2.2.8], brahma veda brahmaiva bhavati [MuNDU 3.2.9], tasya tAvad eva ciram [ChAU 6.14.2], iShIkA-tUlavat sarvANi karmANi pradUyante [ChAU 5.24.3] ity Adi-shruti-shatebhya ukto viduShaH sarva-karma-dAhaH | 

ihApi cokto yathaidhAmsi [GItA 4.37] ity AdinA sarva-karma-dAhaH | vakShyati copapattesh ca | avidyA-kAma-klesha-bIja-nimittAni hi karmANi janmAntarAN^kuram Arabhante | ihApi ca sAhamkArAbhisamdhIni karmANi phalArambhakANi, netarANIti tatra tatra bhagavatoktam | 

bIjAny agny-upadagdhAni na rohanti yathA punaH | 
j~nAna-dagdhais tathA kleshair nAtmA sampadyate punaH [Mbh 3.200.10] iti ca | 

astu tAvaj j~nAnotpatty-uttara-kAla-kR^itAnAm karmaNAm j~nAnena dAhaH, j~nAna-saha-bhAvitvAt | na tv iha janmani j~nAnotpatteH prAk kR^itAnAm karmaNAm atIta-janma-kR^itAnAm ca dAho yuktaH | na | sarva-karmANIti visheShaNAt | j~nAnottara-kAla-bhAvinAm eva sarva-karmaNAm iti cet, na | samkoce kAraNAnupapatteH | yat tUktam yathA vartamAna-janmArambhakANi karmANi na kShIyante phala-dAnAya pravR^ittAny eva saty api j~nAne, tathAnArabdha-phalAnAm api karmaNAm kShayo na yukta iti, tad asat | katham ? teShAm mukteShuvat pravR^itta-phalatvAt | yathA pUrvam lakShya-vedhAya mukta iShuH dhanuSho lakShya-vedhottara-kAlam api Arabdha-vega-kShayAt patanenaiva nivartate, evam sharIrArambhakam karma sharIra-sthiti-prayojane nivR^itte 'pi, A samskAra-vega-kShayAt pUrvavat vartata eva | yathA sa eva iShuH pravR^itti-nimittAnArabdha-vegas tv amukto dhanuShi prayukto 'pi upasamhriyate, tathAnArabdha-phalAni karmANi svAshraya-sthAny eva j~nAnena nirbIjI-kriyanta iti | patite 'smin vidvac-charIre na sa bhUyo 'bhijAyate iti yuktam evoktam iti siddham ||BhGS_13.23|| 

==============================

atrAtma-darshane upAya-vikalpA ime dhyAnAdaya ucyante - 

dhyAnenAtmani pashyanti kecid AtmAnam AtmanA |
anye sAmkhyena yogena karma-yogena cApare ||BhG_13.24||

dhyAnena | dhyAnam nAma shabdAdibhyo viShayebhyaH shrotrAdIni karaNAni manasy upasamhR^itya, manash ca pratyak-cetanayitari, ekAgratayA yac cintanam tad dhyAnam | tathA, dhyAyatIva bakaH, dhyAyatIva pR^ithivI, dhyAyantIva parvatAH [ChAU 7.6.1] iti upamopAdAnAt | taila-dhArAvat samtato 'vicchinna-pratyayo dhyAnam | tena dhyAnena Atmani buddhau pashyanty AtmAnam pratyak-cetanam AtmanA svenaiva pratyak-cetanena dhyAna-samskR^itenAntaH-karaNena kecid yoginaH | anye sAmkhyena yogena | sAmkhyam nAma ime sattva-rajas-tamAmsi guNA mayA dR^ishyA aham tebhyo 'nyas tad-vyApAra-sAkShi-bhUto nityo guNa-vilakShaNa Atmeti cintanam eSha sAmkhyo yogaH | tena pashyanti AtmAnam Atmanety anuvartate | karma-yogena | karmaiva yogaH | IshvarArpaNa-buddhyAnuShThIyamAnam ghaTana-rUpam yogArthatvAd yoga ucyate guNataH | tena sattva-shuddhi-j~nAnotpatti-dvAreNa cApare ||BhGS_13.24|| 

==============================

anye tv evam ajAnantaH shrutvAnyebhya upAsate |
te 'pi cAtitaranty eva mR^ityum shruti-parAyaNAH ||BhG_13.25||

anye tv eShu vikalpeShu anyatamenApy evam yathoktam AtmAnam ajAnanto 'nyebhyaH AcAryebhyaH shrutvA "idam eva cintayata" ity uktA upAsate shraddadhAnAH santash cintayanti | te 'pi cAtitaranty eva atikrAmanty eva mR^ityum mR^ityu-yuktam samsAram ity etat | shruti-parAyaNAH shrutiH shravaNam param ayanam gamanam mokSha-mArga-pravR^ittau param sAdhanam yeShAm te shruti-parAyaNAH | kevala-paropadesha-pramANAH svayam viveka-rahitA ity abhiprAyaH | kim u vaktavyam pramANam prati svatantrA vivekino mR^ityum atitarantIty abhiprAyaH ||BhGS_13.25|| 

==============================

kShetraj~nam cApi mAm viddhi [GItA 13.3] iti kShetraj~neshvarakatva-viShayam j~nAnam mokSha-sAdhanam, yaj j~nAtvAmR^itam ashnute [GItA 13.13] ity uktam | tat kasmAt hetoH ? iti tad-dhetu-pradarshanArtham shloka Arabhyate - 

yAvat samjAyate kimcit sattvam sthAvara-jaN^gamam |
kShetra-kShetraj~na-samyogAt tad viddhi bharatarShabha ||BhG_13.26||

yAvat yat kimcit samjAyate samutpadyate sattvam vastu | kim avisheSheNa ? nety Aha - sthAvara-jaN^gamam sthAvaram jaN^gamam ca kShetra-kShetraj~na-samyogAt taj jAyate ity evam viddhi jAnIhi bharatarShabha | 

kaH punar ayam kShetra-kShetraj~nayoH samyogo 'bhipretaH ? na tAvat rajjveva ghaTasyAvayava-samshleSha-dvArakaH sambandha-visheShaH samyogaH kShetreNa kShetraj~nasya sambhavati, AkAshavat niravayavatvAt | nApi samavAya-lakShaNas tantu-paTayor iva kShetra-kShetraj~nayor itaretara-kArya-kAraNa-bhAvAnabhyupagamAt | ity ucyate - kShetra-kShetraj~nayor viShaya-viShayiNor bhinna-svabhAvayor itaretara-tad-dharmAdhyAsa-lakShaNaH samyogaH kShetra-kShetraj~na-svarUpa-vivekA-bhAva-nibandhanaH, rajju-shuktikAdInAm tad-viveka-j~nAnAbhAvAd adhyAropita-sarpa-rajatAdi-samyogavat | so 'yam adhyAsa-svarUpaH kShetra-kShetraj~na-samyogo mithyA-j~nAna-lakShaNaH | yathA-shAstram kShetra-kShetraj~na-lakShaNa-bheda-parij~nAna-pUrvakam prAk darshita-rUpAt kShetrAn mu¤jAd iveShIkAm yathokta-lakShaNam kShetraj~nam pravibhajya na sat tan nAsad ucyate [GItA 13.13] ity anena nirasta-sarvopAdhi-visheSham j~neyam brahma-svarUpeNa yaH pashyati, kShetram ca mAyA-nirmita-hasti-svapna-dR^iShTa-vastuvad gandharva-nagarAdivad asad eva sad ivAvabhAsate | ity evam nishcita-vij~nAno yaH, tasya yathokta-samyag-darshana-virodhAd apagacchati mithyA-j~nAnam | tasya janma-hetor apagamAd ya evam vetti puruSham prakR^itim ca guNaiH saha [GItA 13.25] ity anena vidvAn bhUyo nAbhijAyate iti yad uktam, tad upapannam uktam ||BhGS_13.26|| 

==============================
 
na sa bhUyo 'bhijAyate [GItA 13.24] iti samyag darshana-phalam avidyAdi-samsAra-bIja-nivR^itti-dvAreNa janmAbhAva uktaH | janma-kAraNam cAvidyA-nimittakaH kShetra-kShetraj~na-samyoga uktaH | atas tasyAH avidyAyA nivartakam samyag-darshanam uktam api punaH shabdAntareNocyate - 

samam sarveShu bhUteShu tiShThantam parameshvaram |
vinashyatsv avinashyantam yaH pashyati sa pashyati ||BhG_13.27||

samam nirvisheSham tiShThantam sthitim kurvantam | kva ? sarveShu samasteShu bhUteShu brahmAdi-sthAvarAnteShu prANiShu | kam ? parameshvaram dehendriya-mano-buddhy-avyaktAtmano 'pekShya parameshvaraH, tam sarveShu bhUteShu samam tiShThantam | tAni vishinaShTi vinashyatsv iti | tam ca parameshvaram avinashyantam iti, bhUtAnAm parameshvarasya cAtyanta-vailakShaNya-pradarshanArtham | katham ? sarveShAm hi bhAva-vikArANAm jani-lakShaNo bhAva-vikAro mUlam | janmottara-kAla-bhAvino 'nye sarve bhAva-vikArA vinAshAntAH | vinAshAt paro na kashcid asti bhAva-vikAraH, bhAvAbhAvAt | sati hi dharmiNi dharmA bhavanti | ato 'ntya-bhAva-vikArAbhAvAnuvAdena pUrva-bhAvinaH sarve bhAva-vikArAH pratiShiddhA bhavanti saha kAryaiH | tasmAt sarva-bhUtaiH vailakShaNyam atyantam eva parameshvarasya siddham, nirvisheShatvam ekatvam ca | ya evam yathoktam parameshvaram pashyati, sa pashyati |

nanu sarvo 'pi lokaH pashyati, kim visheShaNeneti | satyam pashyati | kim tu viparItam pashyati | ato vishinaShTi - sa eva pashyatIti | yathA timira-dR^iShTir anekam candram pashyati, tam apekShya eka-candra-darshI vishiShyate - sa eva pashyatIti | tathaivehApy ekam avibhaktam yathoktam AtmAnam yaH pashyati, sa vibhaktAn ekAtma-viparIta-darshibhyo vishiShyate - sa eva pashyatIti | itare pashyanto 'pi na pashyanti | viparIta-darshitvAt aneka-candra-darshivad ity arthaH ||BhGS_13.27|| 

==============================
 
yathoktasya samyag-darshanasya phala-vacanena stutiH kartavyA iti shloka Arabhyate - 

samam pashyan hi sarvatra samavasthitam Ishvaram |
na hinasty AtmanAtmAnam tato yAti parAm gatim ||BhG_13.28||

samam pashyann upalabhamAno hi yasmAt sarvatra sarva-bhUteShu samavasthitam tulyatayAvasthitam Ishvaram atItAnantara-shlokokta-lakShaNam ity arthaH | samam pashyan kim ? na hinasti himsAm na karoti AtmanA svenaiva svam AtmAnam | tat-tad-ahimsanAd yAti parAm prakR^iShTAm gatim mokShAkhyAm || 

nanu naiva kashcit prANI svayam svam AtmAnam hinasti | katham ucyate 'prAptam na hinastIti ? yathA na pR^ithivyAm nAntarikShe na divy agnish cetavyaH [TaittS 5.2.7.1] ity Adi | naiSha doShaH, aj~nAnAm Atma-tiraskaraNopapatteH | sarvo hy aj~no 'tyanta-prasiddham sAkShAd aparokShAd AtmAnam tiraskR^ityAnAtmAnam Atmatvena parigR^ihya, tam api dharmAdharmau kR^itvopAttam AtmAnam hatvAnyam AtmAnam upAdatte navam, tam caivam hatvAnyam | evam tam api hatvAnyam ity evam upAttam upAttam AtmAnam hantIty AtmahA sarvo 'j~naH | yas tu paramArthAtmAsAv api sarvadAvidyayA hata iva vidyamAna-phalAbhAvAd iti sarve Atma-hana evAvidvAmsaH | yas tv itaro yathoktAtma-darshI, sa ubhayathApi AtmanAtmAnam na hinasti na hanti | tato yAti parAm gatim yathoktam phalam tasya bhavatIty arthaH ||BhGS_13.28|| 

==============================
 
sarva-bhUta-stham Ishvaram samam pashyan na hinasty AtmanAtmAnam [GItA 13.28] ity uktam | tad anupapannam sva-guNa-karma-vailakShaNya-bheda-bhinneShv Atmasu, ity etad AshaN^kyAha - 

prakR^ityaiva ca karmANi kriyamANAni sarvashaH |
yaH pashyati tathAtmAnam akartAram sa pashyati ||BhG_13.29||

prakR^ityA prakR^itir bhagavato mAyA triguNAtmikA | mAyAm tu prakR^itim vidyAd [ÁvetU 4.10] iti mantra-varNAt | tayA prakR^ityaiva ca nAnyena mahad-Adi-kArya-kAraNAkAra-pariNatayA karmANi vAN^-manaH-kAyArabhyANi kriyamANAni nirvartyamAnAni sarvashaH sarva-prakArair yaH pashyaty upalabhate, tathAtmAnam kShetraj~nam akartAram sarvopAdhi-vivarjitam sa pashyati, sa paramArtha-darshIty abhiprAyaH | nirguNasyAkartur nirvisheShasyAkAshasyeva bhede pramANAnupapattir ity arthaH ||BhGS_13.29|| 

==============================

punar api tad eva samyag darshanam shabdAntareNa prapaJNcayati - 

yadA bhUta-pR^ithag-bhAvam ekastham anupashyati |
tata eva ca vistAram brahma sampadyate tadA ||BhG_13.30||

yadA yasmin kAle bhUta-pR^ithag-bhAvam bhUtAnAm pR^ithag-bhAvam pR^ithaktvam ekasminn Atmani sthitam eka-stham anupashyati shAstrAcAryopadesham anu AtmAnam pratyakShatvena pashyaty Atmaivedam sarvam [ChAU 7.25.2] iti | tata eva ca tasmAd eva ca vistAram utpattim vikAsam AtmataH prANa Atmata AshA AtmataH smara Atmata AkAsha Atmatas teja Atmata Apa Atmata AvirbhAva-tirobhAvAv Atmato 'nnam [ChAU 7.26.1] ity evam Adi-prakArair vistAram yadA pashyati brahma sampadyate bhavati tadA tasmin kAla ity arthaH ||BhGS_13.30|| 

==============================

ekasyAtmAnaH sarva-dehAtmatve tad-doSha-sambandhe prApte, idam ucyate - 

anAditvAn nirguNatvAt paramAtmAyam avyayaH |
sharIra-stho 'pi kaunteya na karoti na lipyate ||BhG_13.31||

anAditvAt | anAder bhAvo 'nAditvam, AdiH kAraNam, tad yasya nAsti tad anAdi | yad dhy Adimat tat svenAtmanA vyeti | ayam tv anAditvAn niravayava iti kR^itvA na vyeti | tathA nirguNatvAt | saguNo hi guNa-vyayAt vyeti | ayam tu nirguNatvAc ca na vyeti | iti paramAtmAyam avyayaH | nAsya vyayo vidyata ity avyayaH | yata evam ataH sharIra-stho 'pi, sharIreShu Atmana upalabdhir bhavatIti sharIra-stha ucyate | tathApi na karoti | tad-akaraNAd eva tat-phalena na lipyate | yo hi kartA, sa karma-phalena lipyate | ayam tv akartA, ato na phalena lipyate ity arthaH |

kaH punar deheShu karoti lipyate ca ? yadi tAvat anyaH paramAtmano dehI karoti lipyate ca, tataH idam anupapannam uktam kShetraj~neshvaraikatvam kShetraj~nam cApi mAm viddhi [GItA 13.2] ity Adi | atha nAsti IshvarAd anyo dehI | kaH karoti lipyate ca ? iti vAcyam | paro vA nAstIti sarvathA durvij~neyam durvAcyam ceti bhagavat-proktam aupaniShadam darshanam parityaktam vaisheShikaiH sAmkhyArhata-bauddhaish ca | tatrAyam parihAro bhagavatA svenaiva uktaH svabhAvas tu pravartate [GItA 5.14] iti | avidyA-mAtra-svabhAvo hi karoti lipyate iti vyavahAro bhavati, na tu paramArthata ekasmin paramAtmani tad asti | ata evaitasmin paramArtha-sAmkhya-darshane sthitAnAm j~nAna-niShThAnAm paramahamsa-parivrAjakAnAm tiraskR^itAvidyA-vyavahArANAm karmAdhikAro nAstIti tatra tatra darshitam bhagavatA ||BhGS_13.31||

 ==============================

kim iva na karoti na lipyate ity atra dR^iShTAntam Aha - 

yathA sarva-gatam saukShmyAd AkAsham nopalipyate |
sarvatrAvasthito dehe tathAtmA nopalipyate ||BhG_13.32||

yathA sarva-gatam vyApy api sat saukShmyAt sUkShma-bhAvAd AkAsham kham nopalipyate na sambadhyate, sarvatrAvasthito dehe tathAtmA nopalipyate ||BhGS_13.32|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

yathA prakAshayaty ekaH kR^itsnam lokam imam raviH |
kShetram kShetrI tathA kR^itsnam prakAshayati bhArata ||BhG_13.34||

yathA prakAshayaty avabhAsayati ekaH kR^itsnam lokam imam raviH savitA AdityaH, tathA tadvat mahA-bhUtAdi-dhR^ity-antam kShetram ekaH san prakAshayati | kaH ? kShetrI paramAtmA ity arthaH | ravi-dR^iShTanto 'tra Atmana ubhayArtho 'pi bhavati | ravivat sarva-kShetreShv eka evAtmA, alepakash ceti ||BhGS_13.34|| 

==============================

samastAdhyAyArthopasamhArArtho 'yam shlokaH - 

kShetra-kShetraj~nayor evam antaram j~nAna-cakShuShA |
bhUta-prakR^iti-mokSham ca ye vidur yAnti te param ||BhG_13.35||

kShetra-kShetraj~nayor yathA-vyAkhyAtayor evam yathA-pradarshita-prakAreNAntaram itaretara-vailakShaNya-visheSham j~nAna-cakShuShA shAstrAcArya-prasAdopadesha-janitam Atma-pratyayikam j~nAnam cakShuH, tena j~nAna-cakShuShA, bhUta-prakR^iti-mokSham ca, bhUtAnAm prakR^itir avidyA-lakShaNAvyaktAkhyA, tasyA bhUta-prakR^iter mokShaNam abhAva-gamanam ca ye vidur vijAnanti, yAnti gacchanti te param paramAtma-tattvam brahma, na punar deham Adadate ity arthaH ||BhGS_13.35|| 

==============================

iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrI-govinda-bhagavat-pUjya-pAda-
shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^itau shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye
kShetra-kShetraj~na-yogo nAma trayodasho 'dhyAyaH ||


__________________________________________________________

BhG 14

atha guNa-traya-vibhAga-yogo nAma 
caturdasho 'dhyAyaH
(shrImac-chamkara-bhagavat-pAda-viracitam shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShyam)

sarvam utpadyamAnam kShetra-kShetraj~na-samyogAd utpadyata ity uktam | tat kathamiti, tat-pradarshanArtham param bhUya ity Adir adhyAya Arabhyate | athavA, Ishvara-paratantrayoH kShetra-kShetraj~nayoH jagat-kAraNatvam na tu sAmkhyAnAm iva svatantrayor ity evam artham | prakR^iti-sthatvam guNeShu ca saN^gaH samsAra-kAraNam ity uktam | kasmin guNe katham saN^gaH ? ke vA guNAH ? katham vA te badhnantIti ? guNebhyash ca mokShaNam katham syAt ? muktasya ca lakShaNam vaktavyam, ity evam artham ca bhagavAn uvAca - 

param bhUyaH pravakShyAmi j~nAnAnAm j~nAnam uttamam |
yaj j~nAtvA munayaH sarve parAm siddhim ito gatAH ||BhG_14.1||

param j~nAnam iti vyavahitena sambandhaH | bhUyaH punaH pUrveShu sarveShv adhyAyeShu asakR^id uktam api pravakShyAmi | tac ca param para-vastu-viShayatvAt | kim tat ? j~nAnam sarveShAm j~nAnAnAm uttamam, uttama-phalatvAt | j~nAnAnAm iti nAmAnitvAdInAm | kim tarhi ? yaj~nAdi-j~neya-vastu-viShayANAm iti | tAni na mokShAya, idam tu mokShAyeti parottama-shabdAbhyAm stauti shrotR^i-buddhi-rucy-utpAdanArtham | yaj j~nAtvA yaj j~nAnam j~nAtvA prApya munayaH samnyAsino manana-shIlAH sarve parAm siddhim mokShAkhyAm ito 'smAt deha-bandhanAt Urdhvam gatAH prAptAH ||BhGS_14.1|| 

==============================
 
asyAsh ca siddhair aikAntikatvam darshayati - 

idam j~nAnam upAshritya mama sAdharmyam AgatAH |
sarge 'pi nopajAyante pralaye na vyathanti ca ||BhG_14.2||

idam j~nAnam yathoktam upAshritya, j~nAna-sAdhanam anuShThAya ity etat, mama parameshvarasya sAdharmyam mat-svarUpatAm AgatAH prAptA ity arthaH | na tu samAna-dharmatA sAdharmyam, kShetraj~neshvarayor bhedAnabhyupagamAd gItA-shAstre | phala-vAdash cAyam stuty-artham ucyate | sarge 'pi sR^iShTi-kAle 'pi nopajAyante | notpadyante | pralaye brahmaNo 'pi vinAsha-kAle na vyathanti ca vyathAm nApadyante, na cyavantIty arthaH ||BhGS_14.2|| 

==============================

kShetra-kShetraj~na-samyoga IdR^isho bhUta-kAraNam ity Aha - 

mama yonir mahad brahma tasmin garbham dadhAmy aham |
sambhavaH sarva-bhUtAnAm tato bhavati bhArata ||BhG_14.3||

mama sva-bhUtA madIyA mAyA triguNAtmikA prakR^itir yoniH sarva-bhUtAnAm kAraNam | sarva-kAryebhyo mahattvAt kAraNatvAd bR^imhaNAc ca [bharaNAc ca] sva-vikArANAm mahad brahma iti yonir eva vishiShyate | tasmin mahati brahmaNi yonau garbham hiraNyagarbhasya janmano bIjam sarva-bhUta-janma-kAraNam bIjam dadhAmi nikShipAmi kShetra-kShetraj~na-prakR^iti-dvaya-shaktimAn Ishvaro 'ham, avidyA-kAma-karmopAdhi-svarUpAnuvidhAyinam kShetraj~nam kShetreNa samyojayAmIty arthaH | sambhava utpattiH sarva-bhUtAnAm hiraNyagarbhotpatti-dvAreNa tatas tasmAd gabrhAdhAnAd bhavati | he bhArata ||BhGS_14.3|| 

==============================

sarva-yoniShu kaunteya mUrtayaH sambhavanti yAH |
tAsAm brahma mahad yonir aham bIja-pradaH pitA ||BhG_14.4||
 
deva-pitR^i-manuShya-pashu-mR^igAdi-sarva-yoniShu kaunteya, mUrtayo deha-samsthAna-lakShaNA mUrcchitAN^gAvayavA mUrtayaH sambhavanti yAH, tAsAm mUrtInAm brahma mahat sarvAvastham yoniH kAraNam aham Ishvaro bIja-prado garbhAdhAnasya kartA pitA ||BhGS_14.4|| 

==============================

ke guNAH ? katham badhnanti ? ity ucyate - 

sattvam rajas tama iti guNAH prakR^iti-sambhavAH |
nibadhnanti mahA-bAho dehe dehinam avyayam ||BhG_14.5||

sattvam rajas tama ity evam-nAmAno guNA iti pAribhAShikaH shabdaH | na rUpAdivad dravyAshritA guNAH | na ca guNa-guNinor anyatvam atra vivakShitam | tasmAd guNA iva nitya-para-tantrAH kShetraj~nam praty avidyAtmakatvAt kShetraj~nam nibadhnantIva tam AspadIkR^ityAtmAnam pratilabhanta iti nibadhnantIty ucyate | te ca prakR^iti-sambhavA bhagavan-mAyA-sambhavA nibadhnantIva | he mahAbAho | mahAntau samarthatarAv AjAnu-pralambau bAhU yasya saH mahAbAhuH he mahAbAho | dehe sharIre dehinam dehavantam avyayam, avyayatvam coktam anAditvAd [GItA 13.32] ity Adi shlokena | nanu dehI na lipyate [GItA 13.32] ity uktam | tat katham iha nibadhnantIty anyathocyate ? parihR^itam asmAbhir iva-shabdena nibadhnantIveti ||BhGS_14.5|| 

==============================

tatra sattvAdInAm sattvasyaiva tAval lakShaNam ucyate - 

tatra sattvam nirmalatvAt prakAshakam anAmayam |
sukha-saN^gena badhnAti j~nAna-saN^gena cAnagha ||BhG_14.6||

nirmalatvAt sphaTika-maNir iva prakAshakam anAmayam nirupadravam sattvam tan nibadhnAti | katham ? sukha-saN^gena sukhy aham iti viShaya-bhUtasya sukhasya viShayiNy Atmani samshleShApAdanam mR^iShaiva sukhe sa¤janam iti | saiShAvidyA | na hi viShaya-dharmo viShayiNo bhavati | icchAdi ca dhR^ity-antam kShetrasyaiva viShayasya dharmaH ity uktam bhagavatA | ato 'vidyayaiva svakIya-dharma-bhUtayA viShaya-viShayy-aviveka-lakShaNayAsvAtma-bhUte sukhe samjayatIva, Asaktam iva karoti, asaN^gam saktam iva karoti, asukhinam sukhinam iva | tathA j~nAna-saN^gena ca, j~nAnam iti sukha-sAhacaryAt kShetrasyaiva viShayasyAntaH-karaNasya dharmaH, nAtmanaH | Atma-dharmatve saN^gAnupapatteH, bandhAnupapattesh ca | sukha iva j~nAnAdau saN^go mantavyaH | he anagha avyasana ||BhGS_14.6|| 

==============================

rajo rAgAtmakam viddhi tR^iShNAsaN^ga-samudbhavam |
tan nibadhnAti kaunteya karma-saN^gena dehinam ||BhG_14.7||

rajaH rAgAtmakam rajanAd rAgo gairikAd iva drAg Atmakam viddhi jAnIhi | tR^iShNAsaN^ga-samudbhavam tR^iShNA aprAptAbhilAShaH | AsaN^gaH prApte viShaye manasaH prIti-lakShaNaH samshleShaH | tR^iShNAsaN^gayoH samudbhavam tR^iShNAsaN^ga-samudbhavam | tan nibadhnAti tad rajo nibadhnAti kaunteya karma-saN^gena, dR^iShTAdR^iShTArtheShu karmasu sa¤janam tat-paratA karma-saN^gas tena nibadhnAti rajo dehinam ||BhGS_14.7|| 

==============================

tamas tv aj~nAna-jam viddhi mohanam sarva-dehinAm |
pramAdAlasya-nidrAbhis tan nibadhnAti bhArata ||BhG_14.8||
