tamas tR^itIyo guNo 'j~nAna-jam aj~nAnAj jAtam aj~nAna-jam viddhi | mohanam moha-karam aviveka-karam sarva-dehinAm sarveShAm dehavatAm | pramAdAlasya-nidrAbhiH pramAdash cAlasyam ca nidrA ca pramAdAlasya-nidrAs tAbhiH pramAdAlasya-nidrAbhis tat tamo nibadhnAti bhArata ||BhGS_14.8|| 

==============================

punar guNAnAm vyApAraH samkShepata ucyate - 

sattvam sukhe samjayati rajaH karmaNi bhArata |
j~nAnam AvR^itya tu tamaH pramAde samjayaty uta ||BhG_14.9||

sattvam sukhe samjayati samshleShayati, rajaH karmaNi he bhArata samjayatIty anuvartate | j~nAnam sattva-kR^itam vivekam AvR^itya AcchAdya tu tamaH svena AvaraNAtmanA pramAde samjayaty uta | pramAdo nAma prApta-kartavyAkaraNam ||BhGS_14.9|| 

==============================

uktam kAryam kadA kurvanti guNAH ? ity ucyate -

rajas tamash cAbhibhUya sattvam bhavati bhArata |
rajaH sattvam tamash caiva tamaH sattvam rajas tathA ||BhG_14.10||

rajas tamash ca ubhAv apy abhibhUya sattvam bhavati udbhavati vardhate yadA, tadA labdhAtmakam sattvam sva-kAryam j~nAna-sukhAdy Arabhate | he bhArata ! tathA rajo-guNaH sattvam tamash caiva ubhAv apy abhibhUya vardhate yadA, tadA karma tR^iShNAdi sva-kAryam Arabhate | tama-Akhyo guNaH sattvam rajash ca ubhAv apy abhibhUya tathaiva vardhate yadA, tadA j~nAnAvaraNAdi sva-kAryam Arabhate ||BhGS_14.10|| 

==============================

yadA yo guNa udbhUto bhavati, tadA tasya kim liN^gam ? ity ucyate - 

sarva-dvAreShu dehe 'smin prakAsha upajAyate |
j~nAnam yadA tadA vidyAd vivR^iddham sattvam ity uta ||BhG_14.11||

sarva-dvAreShu, Atmana upalabdhi-dvArANi shrotrAdIni sarvANi karaNAni, teShu sarva-dvAreShu antaH-karaNasya buddher vR^ittiH prakAsho dehe 'smin upajAyate | tad eva j~nAnam | yadaivam prakAsho j~nAnAkhya upajAyate, tadA j~nAna-prakAshena liN^gena vidyAd vivR^iddham udbhUtam sattvam ity utApi ||BhGS_14.11|| 

==============================

rajasa udbhUtasyedam cihnam -

lobhaH pravR^ittir ArambhaH karmaNAm ashamaH spR^ihA |
rajasy etAni jAyante vivR^iddhe bharatarShabha ||BhG_14.12||

lobhaH para-dravyAditsA | pravR^ittiH pravartanam | sAmAnya-ceShTA ArambhaH | kasya ? karmaNAm | ashamo 'nupashamaH harSha-rAgAdi-pravR^ittiH | spR^ihA sarva-sAmAnya-vastu-viShayA tR^iShNA | rajasi guNe vivR^iddha etAni liN^gAni jAyante | he bharatarShabha ||BhGS_14.12|| 

==============================

aprakAsho 'pravR^ittish ca pramAdo moha eva ca |
tamasy etAni jAyante vivR^iddhe kuru-nandana ||BhG_14.13||

aprakAsho 'vivekaH | atyantam apravR^ittish ca pravR^itty-abhAvas tat-kAryam pramAdo moha eva ca | aviveko mUDhatA ity arthaH | tamasi guNe vivR^iddha etAni liN^gAni jAyante he kuru-nandana ! ||BhGS_14.13|| 

==============================

maraNa-dvAreNApi yat phalam prApyate, tad api saN^ga-rAga-hetukam sarvam gauNam eveti darshayan Aha - 

yadA sattve pravR^iddhe tu pralayam yAti deha-bhR^it |
tadottama-vidAm lokAn amalAn pratipadyate ||BhG_14.14||

yadA sattve pravR^iddha udbhUte tu pralayam maraNam yAti pratipadyate deha-bhR^id AtmA, tadottama-vidAm mahad-Adi-tattva-vidAm ity etat | lokAn amalAn mala-rahitAn pratipadyate prApnotIty etat ||BhGS_14.14|| 

==============================

rajasi pralayam gatvA karma-saN^giShu jAyate |
tathA pralInas tamasi mUDha-yoniShu jAyate ||BhG_14.15||

rajasi guNe vivR^iddhe pralayam maraNam gatvA prApya karma-saN^giShu karmAsakti-yukteShu manuShyeShu jAyate | tathA tadvad eva pralIno mR^itas tamasi vivR^iddhe mUDha-yoniShu pashv-Adi-yoniShu jAyate ||BhGS_14.15|| 

==============================

atIta-shlokArthasyaiva samkShepa ucyate -

karmaNaH sukR^itasyAhuH sAttvikam nirmalam phalam |
rajasas tu phalam duHkham aj~nAnam tamasaH phalam ||BhG_14.16||

karmaNaH sukR^itasya sAttvikasya ity arthaH, AhuH shiShTaH sAttvikam eva nirmalam phalam iti | rajasas tu phalam duHkham rAjasasya karmaNa ity arthaH, karmAdhikArAt phalam api duHkham eva, kAraNAnurUpyAt, rAjasam eva | tathA aj~nAnam tamasas tAmasasya karmaNo 'dharmasya pUrvavat ||BhGS_14.16||

==============================

kim ca, guNebhyo bhavati - 

sattvAt samjAyate j~nAnam rajaso lobha eva ca |
pramAda-mohau tamaso bhavato 'j~nAnam eva ca ||BhG_14.17||

sattvAl labdhAtmakAt samjAyate samutpadyate j~nAnam, rajaso lobha eva ca, pramAda-mohau ca ubhau tamaso bhavataH, aj~nAnam eva ca bhavati ||BhGS_14.17|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

Urdhvam gacchanti sattva-sthA madhye tiShThanti rAjasAH |
jaghanya-guNa-vR^itta-sthA adho gacchanti tAmasAH ||BhG_14.18||

Urdhvam gacchanti devalokAdiShUtpadyante sattva-sthAH sattva-guNa-vR^itta-sthAH | madhye tiShThanti manuShyeShUtpadyante rAjasAH | jaghanya-guNa-vR^itta-sthA jaghanyash cAsau guNash ca jaghanya-guNas tamaH, tasya vR^ittam nidrAlasyAdi, tasmin sthitAH jaghanya-guNa-vR^itta-sthAH mUDhAH adho gacchanti pashv-AdiShUtpadyante tAmasAH ||BhGS_14.18|| 

==============================

puruShasya prakR^iti-sthatva-rUpeNa mithyA-j~nAnena yuktasya bhogyeShu guNeShu sukha-duHkha-mohAtmakeShu sukhI duHkhI mUDho 'ham asmIty evam-rUpo yaH saN^gas tat-kAraNam puruShasya sad-asad-yoni-janma-prApti-lakShaNasya samsArasyeti samAsena pUrvAdhyAye yad uktam, tad iha sattvam rajas tama iti guNAH prakR^iti-sambhavA ity Arabhya guNa-svarUpam, guNa-vR^ittam, sva-vR^ittena ca guNAnAm bandhakatvam, guNa-vR^itta-nibaddhasya ca purUShasya yA gatiH, ity etat sarvam mithyA-j~nAna-mUlam bandha-kAraNam vistareNoktvA, adhunA samyag-darshanAn mokSho vaktavya ity ata Aha bhagavAn - 

nAnyam guNebhyaH kartAram yadA draShTAnupashyati |
guNebhyash ca param vetti mad-bhAvam so 'dhigacchati ||BhG_14.19||

nAnyam kArya-karaNa-viShayAkAra-pariNatebhyo guNebhyaH kartAram anyam yadA draShTA vidvAn san nAnupashyati, guNA eva sarvAvasthAH sarva-karmaNAm kartAra ity evam pashyati, guNebhyash ca param guNa-vyApAra-sAkShi-bhUtam vetti, mad-bhAvam mama bhAvam sa draShTAdhigacchati ||BhGS_14.19|| 

==============================
 
katham adhigacchati ? ity ucyate - 

guNAn etAn atItya trIn dehI deha-samudbhavAn |
janma-mR^ityu-jarA-duHkhair vimukto 'mR^itam ashnute ||BhG_14.20||

guNAn etAn yathoktAn atItya jIvann evAtikramya mAyopAdhi-bhUtAn trIn dehI deha-samudbhavAn dehotpatti-bIja-bhUtAn janma-mR^ityu-jarA-duHkhair janma ca mR^ityush ca jarA ca duHkhAni ca janma-mR^ityu-jarA-duHkhAni tair jIvann eva vimuktaH san vidvAn amR^itam ashnute | evam mad-bhAvam adhigacchatIty arthaH ||BhGS_14.20|| 

==============================

jIvann eva guNAn atItyAmR^itam ashnute iti prashna-bIjam pratilabhyArjuna uvAca - 

kair liN^gais trIn guNAn etAn atIto bhavati prabho |
kim-AcAraH katham caitAms trIn guNAn ativartate ||BhG_14.21||

kair liN^gaish cihnais trIn etAn vyAkhyAtAn guNAn atIto 'tikrAnto bhavati prabho, kim-AcAraH ? ko 'sya AcAra iti kim-AcAraH | katham kena ca prakAreNa etAn trIn guNAn ativartate 'tItya vartate ||BhGS_14.21|| 

==============================

guNAtItasya lakShaNam guNAtItatvopAyam cArjunena pR^iShTo 'smin shloke prashna-dvayArtham prativacanam bhagavAn uvAca | yat tAvat kair liN^gair yukto guNAtIto bhavatIti tat shR^iNu - 

prakAsham ca pravR^ittim ca moham eva ca pANDava |
na dveShTi sampravR^ittAni na nivR^ittAni kAN^kShati ||BhG_14.22||

prakAsham ca sattvakAryam pravR^ittim ca rajaHkAryam moham eva ca tamaHkAryam ity etAni na dveShTi sampravR^ittAni samyagviShayabhAvena udbhUtAni - mama tAmasaH pratyayo jAtaH, tenAham mUDhaH | tathA rAjasI pravR^ittir mama utpannA duHkhAtmikA, tenAham rajasA pravartitaH pracalitaH svarUpAt | kaShTam mama vartate yo 'yam matsvarUpAvasthAnAt bhramshaH | tathA sAttviko guNaH prakAshAtmA mAm vivekitvam ApAdayan sukhe ca sajayan badhnAtIti tAni dveShTy asamyag-darshitvena | tat evam guNAtIto na dveShTi sampravR^ittAni | yathA ca sAttvikAdipuruShaH sattvAdikAryANi AtmAnam prati prakAshya nivR^ittAni kAN^kShati, na tathA guNAtIto nivR^ittAni kAN^kShatIty arthaH | etat na parapratyakSham liN^gam | kim tarhi ? svAtmapratyakShatvAt AtmArtham eva etat lakShaNam | na hi svAtmaviShayam dveShamAkAN^kShAm vA paraH pashyati ||BhGS_14.22|| 

==============================

atha idAnIm guNAtItaH kim-AcAraH ? iti prashnasya prativacanam Aha - 

udAsInavad AsIno guNair yo na vicAlyate |
guNA vartanta ity eva yo 'vatiShThati neN^gate ||BhG_14.23||

udAsInavad yathA udAsIno na kasyacit pakSham bhajate, tathAyam guNAtItatvopAya-mArge 'vasthita AsIna Atmavid guNair yaH samnyAsI na vicAlyate viveka-darshanAvasthAtaH | tad etat sphuTIkaroti - guNAH kArya-karaNa-viShayAkAra-pariNatA anyonyasmin vartante iti yo 'vatiShThati | chando-bhaN^ga-bhayAt parasmaipada-prayogaH | yo 'nutiShThatIti vA pAThAntaram | neN^gate na calati, svarUpAvastha eva bhavatIty arthaH ||BhGS_14.23||

==============================

kim ca - 

sama-duHkha-sukhaH svasthaH sama-loShTAshma-kAJNcanaH |
tulya-priyApriyo dhIras tulya-nindAtma-samstutiH ||BhG_14.24||

sama-duHkha-sukhaH same duHkha-sukhe yasya saH sama-duHkha-sukhaH, svasthaH sve Atmani sthitaH prasannaH sama-loShTAshma-kAJNcanaH loShTam cAshmA ca kAJNcanam ca loShTAshmakAJNcanAni samAni yasya saH samaloShTAshmakAJNcanaH, tulyapriyApriyaH priyam cApriyam ca priyApriye tulye same yasya so 'yam tulyapriyApriyaH, dhIro dhImAn, tulyanindAtmasamstutiH nindA ca Atmasamstuti ca nindAtmasamstutI, tulye nindAtmasamstutI yasya yateH sa tulyanindAtmasamstutiH ||BhGS_14.24|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

mAnApamAnayos tulyas tulyo mitrAri-pakShayoH |
sarvArambha-parityAgI guNAtItaH sa ucyate ||BhG_14.25||

mAnApamAnayos tulyaH samo nirvikAraH | tulyo mitrAri-pakShayoH | yadyapy udAsInA bhavanti kecit svAbhiprAyeNa, tathApi parAbhiprAyeNa mitrAri-pakShayor iva bhavantIti tulyo mitrAri-pakShayor ity Aha | sarvArambha-parityAgI | dR^iShTAdR^iShTArthAni karmANy Arabhyanta ity ArambhAH | sarvAn ArambhAn parityaktum shIlam asyeti sarvArambha-parityAgI | deha-dhAraNa-mAtra-nimitta-vyatirekeNa sarva-karma-parityAgIty arthaH | guNAtItaH sa ucyate ||BhGS_14.25|| 

==============================

udAsInavad ity Adi guNAtItaH sa ucyate ity etad-antam uktam yAvat yatna-sAdhyam tAvat samnyAsino 'nuShTheyam guNAtItatva-sAdhanam mumukShoH | sthirI-bhUtam tu sva-samvedyam sad guNAtItasya yater lakShaNam bhavatIti | adhunA katham ca trInguNAn ativartate ? ity asya prashnasya prativacanam Aha - 

mAm ca yo 'vyabhicAreNa bhakti-yogena sevate |
sa guNAn samatItyaitAn brahma-bhUyAya kalpate ||BhG_14.26||

mAm ca Ishvaram nArAyaNam sarva-bhUta-hR^idayAshritam yo yatiH karmI vA avyabhicAreNa na kadAcid yo vyabhicarati bhakti-yogena bhajanam bhaktiH saiva yogas tena bhakti-yogena sevate, sa guNAn samatItya etAn yathoktAn | brahma-bhUyAya | bhavanam bhUyaH, brahma-bhUyAya brahma-bhavanAya mokShAya kalpate samartho bhavatIty arthaH ||BhGS_14.26|| 

==============================
 
kuta etad ? ity ucyate - 

brahmaNo hi pratiShThAham amR^itasyAvyayasya ca |
shAshvatasya ca dharmasya sukhasyaikAntikasya ca ||BhG_14.27||
brahmaNaH paramAtmano hi yasmAt pratiShThAham pratitiShThaty asmin iti pratiShThAham pratyag-AtmA | kIdR^ishasya brahmaNaH ? amR^itasya avinAshinaH | avyayasya avikAriNaH | shAshvatasya ca nityasya dharmasya dharma-j~nAnasya j~nAna-yoga-dharma-prApyasya sukhasya Ananda-rUpasya aikAntikasya avyabhicAriNo 'mR^itAdi-svabhAvasya paramAnanda-rUpasya paramAtmanaH pratyag-AtmA pratiShThA | 

samyag-j~nAnena paramAtmatayA nishcIyate | tad etad brahma-bhUyAya kalpata ity uktam | yayA ceshvara-shaktyA bhaktAnugrahAdi-prayojanAya brahma pratiShThate pravartate, sA shaktir brahmaivAham | shakti-shaktimator ananyatvAd ity abhiprAyaH | athavA, brahma-shabda-vAcyatvAt sa-vikalpakam brahma | tasya brahmaNo nirvikalpako 'ham eva nAnyaH pratiShThAshrayaH | kim-vishiShTasya ? amR^itasyAmaraNa-dharmakasyAvyayasya vyaya-rahitasya | kim ca, shAshvatasya ca nityasya dharmasya j~nAna-niShThA-lakShaNasya sukhasya taj-janitasya aikAntikasya ekAnta-niyatasya ca, pratiShThAham iti vartate ||BhGS_14.27|| 

==============================

iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrI-govinda-bhagavat-pUjya-pAda-
shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^itau shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye
caturdasho 'dhyAyaH 
||14||


__________________________________________________________

BhG 15

atha puruShottama-yogo nAma 
paJNcadasho 'dhyAyaH

(shrImac-chamkara-bhagavat-pAda-viracitam shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShyam)

yasmAn mad-adhInam karmiNAm karma-phalam j~nAninAm ca j~nAna-phalam, ato bhakti-yogena mAm ye sevante te mama prasAdAj j~nAna-prApti-krameNa guNAtItA mokSham gacchanti | kim u vaktavyam Atmanas tattvam eva samyak vijAnanta ity ato bhagavAn arjunenApR^iShTo 'py Atmanas tattvam vivakShur uvAca Urdhva-mUlam ity AdinA | tatra tAvad vR^ikSha-rUpaka-kalpanayA vairAgya-hetoH samsAra-svarUpam varNayati - viraktasya hi samsArAt bhagavat-tattva-j~nAne 'dhikAraH, nAnyasyeti | shrI-bhagavAn uvAca - 

shrI-bhagavAn uvAca
Urdhva-mUlam adhaH-shAkham ashvattham prAhur avyayam |
chandAmsi yasya parNAni yas tam veda sa veda-vit ||BhG_15.1||

Urdhva-mUlam kAlataH sUkShmatvAt kAraNatvAn nityatvAt mahattvAc cordhvam | ucyate brahmAvyaktam mAyA shaktimat, tan mUlam asyeti so 'yam samsAra-vR^ikShaH Urdhva-mUlaH | shrutesh ca - Urdhva-mUlo 'vAk-shAkha eSho 'shvatthaH sanAtanaH [KaThU 2.3.1] iti | purANe ca - 

       avyakta-mUla-prabhavas tasyaivAnugrahotthitaH |
       buddhi-skandha-mayash caiva indriyAntara-koTaraH ||
       mahA-bhUta-vishAkhash ca viShayaiH patravAms tathA |
       dharmAdharma-supuShpash ca sukha-duHkha-phalodayaH ||
       AjIvyaH sarva-bhUtAnAm brahma-vR^ikShaH sanAtanaH |
       etad brahma-vanam cAsya brahmAcarati sAkShivat ||
       etac chittvA ca bhittvA ca j~nAnena paramAsinA |
       tatash cAtma-gatim prApya tasmAn nAvartate punaH || [Mbh 14.35.20-22] ity Adi | 

tam Urdhva-mUlam samsAram mAyA-mayam vR^ikSham AhuH | adhaH-shAkham mahad-ahamkAra-tanmAtrAdayaH shAkhA ivAsyAdho bhavantIti so 'yam adhaH-shAkhaH, tam adhaH-shAkham | na shvo 'pi sthAtety ashvatthas tam kShaNa-pradhvamsinam ashvattham prAhuH kathayanty avyayam samsAra-mAyAyA anAdi-kAla-pravR^ittatvAt so 'yam samsAra-vR^ikSho 'vyayaH, anAdy-anta-dehAdi-samtAnAshrayo hi suprasiddhaH, tam avyayam | tasyaiva samsAra-vR^ikShasya idam anyat visheShaNam - chandAmsi yasya parNAni, chandAmsi cchAdanAd R^ig-yajuH-sAma-lakShaNAni yasya samsAra-vR^ikShasya parNAnIva parNAni | yathA vR^ikShasya parirakShaNArthAni parNAni, tathA vedAH samsAra-vR^ikSha-parirakShaNArthA dharmAdharma-tad-dhetu-phala-prakAshanArthatvAt | yathA-vyAkhyAtam samsAra-vR^ikSham sa-mUlam yas tam veda sa veda-vit, vedArtha-vid ity arthaH | na hi sa-mUlAt samsAra-vR^ikShAd asmAj j~neyo 'nyo 'Nu-mAtro 'py avashiShTo 'stIty ataH sarvaj~naH sarva-vedArtha-vid iti sa-mUla-samsAra-vR^ikSha-j~nAnam stauti ||BhGS_15.1|| 

==============================

tasyaitasya samsAra-vR^ikShasyAparAvayava-kalpanocyate - 

adhash cordhvam prasR^itAs tasya shAkhA
guNa-pravR^iddhA viShaya-pravAlAH |
adhash ca mUlAny anusamtatAni
karmAnubandhIni manuShya-loke ||BhG_15.2||

adho manuShyAdibhyo yAvat sthAvaram, ata Urdhvam ca yAvad brahmaNo vishva-sR^ijo dhAma ity etad-antam yathA-karma yathA-shrutam j~nAna-karma-phalAni, tasya vR^ikShasya shAkhA iva shAkhAH prasR^itAH pragatAH | guNa-pravR^iddhAH guNaiH sattva-rajas-tamobhiH pravR^iddhAH sthUlIkR^itA upAdAna-bhUtaiH | viShaya-pravAlA viShayAH shabdAdayaH pravAlA iva dehAdi-karma-phalebhyaH shAkhAbhyo 'N^kurI-bhavantIva, tena viShaya-pravAlAH shAkhAH | samsAra-vR^ikShasya parama-mUlam upAdAna-kAraNam pUrvam uktam | athedAnIm karma-phala-janita-rAga-dveShAdi-vAsanA mUlAnIva dharmAdharma-pravR^itti-kAraNAny avAntara-bhAvIni tAny adhash ca devAdy-apekShayA mUlAny anusantatAny anupraviShTani karmAnubandhIni karma dharmAdharma-lakShaNam anubandhaH pashcAd-bhAvi, yeShAm udbhUtim anu udbhavati, tAni karmAnubandhIni manuShya-loke visheShataH | atra hi manuShyANAm karmAdhikAraH prasiddhaH ||BhGS_15.2|| 

==============================

yas tv ayam varNitaH samsAra-vR^ikShaH - 

na rUpam asyeha tathopalabhyate
nAnto na cAdir na ca sampratiShThA |
ashvattham enam su-virUDha-mUlam
asaN^ga-shastreNa dR^iDhena chittvA ||BhG_15.3||

na rUpam asyeha yathopavarNitam tathA naiva upalabhyate, svapna-marIcy-udaka-mAyA-gandharva-nagara-samatvAt | dR^iShTa-naShTa-svarUpo hi sa ity ata eva nAnto na paryanto niShThA parisamAptir vA vidyate | tathA na cAdiH | "ita ArabhyAyam pravR^ittaH" iti na kenacid gamyate | na ca sampratiShThA sthitir madhyam asya na kenacid upalabhyate | ashvattham enam yathoktam suvirUDha-mUlam suShThu virUDhAni viroham gatAni sudR^iDhAni mUlAni yasya tam enam suvirUDha-mUlam | asaN^ga-shastreNa asaN^gaH putra-vitta-lokaiShaNAbhyo vyutthAnam tenAsaN^ga-shastreNa dR^iDhena paramAtmAbhimukhya-nishcaya-dR^iDhIkR^itena punaH punar vivekAbhyAsAshma-nishitena cchitvA samsAra-vR^ikSham sa-bIjam uddhR^itya ||BhGS_15.3||

==============================

tataH padam tat parimArgitavyam
yasmin gatA na nivartanti bhUyaH |
tam eva cAdyam puruSham prapadye
yataH pravR^ittiH prasR^itA purANI ||BhG_15.4||

tataH pashcAt yat padam vaiShNavam tat parimArgitavyam, parimArgaNam anveShaNam j~nAtavyam ity arthaH | yasmin pade gatAH praviShTA na nivartanti nAvartante bhUyaH punaH samsArAya | katham parimArgitavyam ity Aha - tam eva ca yaH pada-shabdenokta Adyam Adau bhavam Adyam puruSham prapadye ity evam parimArgitavyam tac-charaNatayA ity arthaH | ko 'sau puruShaH ? ity ucyate - yato yasmAt puruShAt samsAra-mAyA-vR^ikSha-pravR^ittiH prasR^itA niHsR^itA aindrajAlikAd iva mAyA | purANI ciramtanI ||BhGS_15.4|| 

==============================

katham-bhUtAs tat padam gacchantIty ucyate - 

nirmAna-mohA jita-saN^ga-doShA
adhyAtma-nityA vinivR^itta-kAmAH |
dvandvair vimuktAH sukha-duHkha-samj~nair
gacchanty amUDhAH padam avyayam tat ||BhG_15.5||

nirmAna-mohA mAnash ca mohash ca mAna-mohau, tau nirgatau yebhyas te nirmAna-mohA mAna-moha-varjitAH | jita-saN^ga-doShAH saN^ga eva doShaH saN^ga-doShaH, jitaH saN^ga-doSho yais te jita-saN^ga-doShAH | adhyAtma-nityAH paramAtma-svarUpAlocana-nityAs tat-parAH | vinivR^itta-kAmA visheShato nirlepena nivR^ittAH kAmA yeShAm te vinivR^itta-kAmAH | yatayaH samnyAsino dvandvaiH priyApriyAdibhir vimuktAH sukha-duHkha-samj~naiH parityaktA gacchanty amUDhA moha-varjitAH padam avyayam tad yathoktam ||BhGS_15.5|| 

==============================

tad eva padam punar visheShyate - 

na tad bhAsayate sUryo na shashAN^ko na pAvakaH |
yad gatvA na nivartante tad dhAma paramam mama ||BhG_15.6||

tat dhAmeti vyavahitena dhAmnA sambadhyate | tad dhAma tejo-rUpam padam na bhAsayate sUrya AdityaH sarvAvabhAsana-shaktimattve 'pi sati | tathA na shashAN^kash candraH, na pAvako nAgnir api | yad dhAma vaiShNavam padam gatvA prApya na nivartante, yac ca sUryAdir na bhAsayate, tad dhAma padam paramam viShNor mama padam ||BhGS_15.6|| 


==============================

nanu sarvA hi gatir Agaty-antAH | samyogAH viprayogAntAH [Mbh 11.2.3] iti hi prasiddham | katham ucyate tat dhAma gatAnAm nAsti nivR^ittiH ? iti | sR^iNu tatra kAraNam - 

mamaivAmsho jIva-loke jIva-bhUtaH sanAtanaH |
manaH-ShaShThAnIndriyANi prakR^iti-sthAni karShati ||BhG_15.7||

mamaiva param Atmano nArAyaNasya, amsho bhAgo 'vayava eka-desha ity anarthAntaram jIva-loke jIvAnAm loke samsAre jIva-bhUtaH kartA bhokteti prasiddhaH sanAtanash cirantanaH | yathA jala-sUryakaH sUryAmsho jala-nimittApAye sUryam eva gatvA na nivartate ca tenaivAtmanA gacchati, evam eva | yathA ghaTAdy-upAdhi-paricchinno ghaTAdy-AkAsha AkAshAmshaH san ghaTAdi-nimittApAye AkAsham prApya na nivartate | ata upapannam uktam yad gatvA na nivartante iti | 

nanu niravayavasya paramAtmanaH kuto 'vayava eka-desho 'mshaH iti ? sAvayavatve ca vinAsha-prasaN^go 'vayava-vibhAgAt | naiSha doShaH, avidyA-kR^itopAdhi-paricchinna eka-desho 'msha iva kalpito yataH | darshitash cAyam arthaH kShetrAdhyAye vistarashaH | sa ca jIvo mad-amshatvena kalpitaH katham samsaraty utkrAmati ca ? ity ucyate - manaH-ShaShThAnIndriyANi shrotrAdIni prakR^iti-sthAni sva-sthAne karNa-shaShkuly-Adau prakR^itau sthitAni karShati AkarShati ||BhGS_15.7|| 

==============================

kasmin kAle ? - 

sharIram yad avApnoti yac cApy utkrAmatIshvaraH |
gR^ihItvaitAni samyAti vAyur gandhAn ivAshayAt ||BhG_15.8||

yac cApi yadA cApi utkrAmatIshvaro dehAdi-samghAta-svAmI jIvaH, tadA karShati [15.8] iti shlokasya dvitIya-pAdo 'rtha-vashAt prAthamyena sambadhyate | yadA ca pUrvasmAt sharIrAt sharIrAntaram avApnoti tadA gR^ihItvaitAni manaH-ShaShThAnIndriyANi samyAti samyak yAti gacchati | kim iva ? ity Aha - vAyuH pavano gandhAn iva AshayAt puShpAdeH ||BhGS_15.8|| 

==============================

kAni punas tAni - 

shrotram cakShuH sparshanam ca rasanam ghrANam eva ca |
adhiShThAya manash cAyam viShayAn upasevate ||BhG_15.9||

shrotram cakShuH sparshanam ca tvag-indriyam rasanam ghrANam eva ca manash ca ShaShTham pratyekam indriyeNa saha, adhiShThAya deha-stho viShayAn shabdAdIn upasevate ||BhGS_15.9|| 

==============================

evam deha-gatam dehAt - 

utkrAmantam sthitam vApi bhu¤jAnam vA guNAnvitam |
vimUDhA nAnupashyanti pashyanti j~nAna-cakShuShaH ||BhG_15.10||

utkrAmantam deham pUrvopAttam parityajantam sthitam vApi dehe tiShThantam bhu¤jAnAm vA shabdAdImsh copalabhamAnam guNAnvitam sukha-duHkha-mohAdyair guNair anvitam anugatam samyuktam ity arthaH | evam-bhUtam apy enam atyanta-darshana-gocara-prAptam vimUDhA dR^iShTAdR^iShTa-viShaya-bhoga-balAkR^iShTa-cetas tayAnekadhA mUDhA nAnupashyanti | aho kaShTam vartate ity anukroshati ca bhagavAn | ye tu punaH pramANa-janita-j~nAna-cakShuShas ta enam pashyanti j~nAna-cakShuSho vivikta-dR^iShTaya ity arthaH ||BhGS_15.10||

==============================

yatanto yoginash cainam pashyanty Atmany avasthitam |
yatanto 'py akR^itAtmAno nainam pashyanty acetasaH ||BhG_15.11||

yatantaH prayatnam kurvanto yoginash ca samAhita-cittA enam prakR^itam AtmAnam pashyanty ayam aham asmIty upalabhanta Atmani svasyAm buddhAv avasthitam | yatanto 'pi shAstrAdi-pramANair akR^itAtmAno 'samskR^itAtmAnas tapasA indriya-jayena ca, dushcaritAd anuparatAH, ashAnta-darpAH prayatnam kurvanto 'pi nainam pashyanty acetaso 'vivekinaH ||BhGS_15.11|| 

==============================

yat padam sarvasyAvabhAsakamapy agnyAdity Adikam jyotiH nAvabhAsayate, yat prAptA ca mumukShavaH punaH samsArAbhimukhAH na nivartante, yasya ca padasya upAdhi-bhedam anuvidhIyamAnAH jIvAH - ghaTAkAshAdayaH iva AkAshasya - amshAH, tasya padasya sarvAtmatvam sarvavyavahArAspadatvam ca vivakShush caturbhiH shlokaiH vibhUtisamkShepamAha bhagavAn - 

yad Aditya-gatam tejo jagad bhAsayate 'khilam |
yac candramasi yac cAgnau tat tejo viddhi mAmakam ||BhG_15.12||

yat Aditya-gatam AdityAshrayam | kim tat ? tejo dIptiH prakAsho jagad bhAsayate prakAshayaty akhilam samastam | yac candramasi shashabhR^iti tejo 'vabhAsakam vartate, yac cAgnau hutavahe, tat tejo viddhi vijAnIhi mAmakam madIyam mama viShNos taj jyotiH | athavA, Aditya-gatam tejash caitanyAtmakam jyotir yac candramasi, yac cAgnau vartate tat tejo viddhi mAmakam madIyam mama viShNos taj jyotiH |

nanu sthAvareShu jaN^gameShu ca tat samAnam caitanyAtmakam jyotiH | tatra katham idam visheShaNam - yad Aditya-gatam ity Adi | naiSha doShaH, sattvAdhikyAd vistaratvopapatteH | Adity-AdiShu hi sattvam atyanta-prakAsham atyanta-bhAsvaram | atas tatraivAvistaram jyotir iti tad vishiShyate, na tu tatraiva tad adhikam iti | yathA hi loke tulye 'pi mukha-samsthAne na kAShTha-kuDyAdau mukham Avirbhavati, AdarshAdau tu svacche svacchatare ca tAratamyenAvirbhavati, tadvat ||BhGS_15.12|| 

==============================

kim ca - 
gAm Avishya ca bhUtAni dhArayAmy aham ojasA |
puShNAmi cauShadhIH sarvAH somo bhUtvA rasAtmakaH ||BhG_15.13||

gAm pR^ithivIm Avishya pravishya dhArayAmi bhUtAni jagad aham ojasA balena | yad balam kAma-rAga-vivarjitam aishvaram rUpam jagad-vidhAraNAya pR^ithivyAm praviShTam yena pR^ithivI gurvI nAdhaH patati na vidIryate ca | tathA ca mantra-varNaH - yena dyaur ugrA pR^ithivI ca dR^iDhA [TaittS 4.1.8] iti, sa dAdhAra pR^ithivIm [ãk 8.7.3.1] ity Adish ca | ato gAm Avishya ca bhUtAni carAcarANi dhArayAmIti yuktam uktam | kim ca, pR^ithivyAm jAtA oShadhIH sarvAH vrIhi-yavAdyAH puShNAmi puShTi-matIH rasa-svAdumatI ca karomi somo bhUtvA rasAtmakaH somaH san rasAtmakaH rasa-svabhAvaH | sarva-rasAnAm AkaraH somaH | sa hi sarva-rasAtmakaH sarvAH oShadhIH svAtma-rasAn anupraveshayan puShNAti ||BhGS_15.13|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

aham vaishvAnaro bhUtvA prANinAm deham AshritaH |
prANApAna-samAyuktaH pacAmy annam catur-vidham ||BhG_15.14||

aham eva vai vaishvAnara udara-stho 'gnir bhUtvA - ayam agnir vaishvAnaro yo 'yam antaH puruShe yenedam annam pacyate yad idam adyate [BAU 5.9.1] ity Adi-shruteH | vaishvAnaraH san prANinAm prANavatAm deham AshritaH praviShTaH prANApAna-samAyuktaH prANApAnAbhyAm samAyuktaH samyuktaH pacAmi paN^kti karomy annam ashanam caturvidham catuShprakAram bhojyam bhakShyam coShyam lehyam ca | bhoktA vai vAnaro 'gniH | agner bhojyam annam somaH | tad etad ubhayam agnIShomau sarvam iti pashyato 'nna-doSha-lepo na bhavati ||BhGS_15.14|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

sarvasya cAham hR^idi samniviShTo
mattaH smR^itir j~nAnam apohanam ca |
vedaish ca sarvair aham eva vedyo
vedAnta-kR^id veda-vid eva cAham ||BhG_15.15||

sarvasya ca prANi-jAtasyAham AtmA san hR^idi buddhau samniviShTaH | ato matta AtmanaH sarva-prANinAm smR^itir j~nAnam tad-apohanam cApagamanam ca | yeShAm yathA puNya-karmaNAm puNya-karmAnurodhena j~nAna-smR^itI bhavataH, tathA pApa-karmaNAm pApa-karmAnurUpeNa smR^iti-j~nAnayor apohanam cApAyanam apagamanam ca | vedaish ca sarvair aham eva paramAtmA vedyo veditavyaH | vedAnta-kR^id vedAntArtha-sampradAya-kR^id ity arthaH, veda-vid vedArtha-vid eva cAham ||BhGS_15.15|| 

==============================

bhagavata Ishvarasya nArAyaNAkhyasya vibhUti-samkShepa ukto vishiShTopAdhi-kR^ito yad Aditya-gatam tejaH [GItA 15.12] ity AdinA | athAdhunA tasyaiva kSharAkSharopAdhi-pravibhaktatayA nirupAdhikasya kevalasya tattva-svarUpa-nirdidhArayiShayottara-shlokA Arabhyante | tatra sarvam evAtItAn AgatAn antarAdhyAyArtha-jAtam tridhA rAshIkR^itya Aha - 

dvAv imau puruShau loke kSharash cAkShara eva ca |
kSharaH sarvANi bhUtAni kUTastho 'kShara ucyate ||BhG_15.16||

dvAv imau pR^ithag-rAshI-kR^itau puruShAv ity ucyete loke samsAre - kSharash ca kSharatIti kSharo vinAshI ity eko rAshiH | aparaH puruSho 'kSharas tad-viparItaH, bhagavato mAyA-shaktiH, kSharAkhyasya puruShasya utpatti-bIjam aneka-samsAri-jantu-kAma-karmAdi-samskArAshraya akSharaH puruSha ucyate | kau tau puruShau ? ity Aha svayam eva bhagavAn - kSharaH sarvANi bhUtAni, samastam vikAra-jAtam ity arthaH | kUTAsthaH kUTAH rAshI rAshir iva sthitaH | athavA, kUTA mAyA vacanA jihmatA kuTilatA iti paryAyAH | aneka-mAyA-vacanAdi-prakAreNa sthitaH kUTAsthaH | samsAra-bIjAnantyAt, na kSharatIty akShara ucyate ||BhGS_15.16|| 

==============================

AbhyAm kSharAkSharAbhyAm anyo vilakShaNaH kSharAkSharopAdhi-dvaya-doSheNAspR^iShTaH nitya-shuddha-buddham ukta-svabhAvaH - 

uttamaH puruShas tv anyaH paramAtmety udAhR^itaH |
yo loka-trayam Avishya bibharty avyaya IshvaraH ||BhG_15.17||

uttama utkR^iShTatamaH puruShas tv anyo 'tyanta-vilakShaNa AbhyAm paramAtmeti paramash cAsau dehAdy-avidyA-kR^itAtmabhyaH, Atmash ca sarva-bhUtAnAm pratyak-cetanaH, ity ataH paramAtmety udAhR^ita ukto vedAnteShu | sa eva vishiShyate yo loka-trayam bhUr-bhuvaH-svar-Akhyam svakIyayA caitanya-bala-shaktyA Avishya pravishya bibharti svarUpa-sad-bhAva-mAtreNa bibharti dhArayati | avyayo nAsya vyayo vidyata ity avyayaH | kaH ? IshvaraH sarvaj~no nArAyaNAkhya Ishana-shIlaH ||BhGS_15.17|| 

==============================

yathA-vyAkhyAtasyeshvarasya puruShottama ity etat nAma prasiddham | tasya nAma-nirvacana-prasiddhayArthavattvam nAmno darshayan niratishayo 'ham Ishvara ity AtmAnam darshayati bhagavAn - 

yasmAt kSharam atIto 'ham akSharAd api cottamaH |
ato 'smi loke vede ca prathitaH puruShottamaH ||BhG_15.18||

yasmAt kSharam atIto 'ham samsAra-mAyA-vR^ikSham ashvatthAkhyam atikrAnto 'ham akSharAd api samsAra-mAyA-rUpa-vR^ikSha-bIja-bhUtAd api cottama utkR^iShTatamaH Urdhvatamo vA | atas tAbhyAm kSharAkSharAbhyAm uttamatvAd asmi loke vede ca prathitaH prakhyAtaH | puruShottama ity evam mAm bhakta-janA viduH | kavayaH kAvyAdiShu cedam nAma nibadhnanti | puruShottama ity anenAbhidhAnenAbhigR^iNanti ||BhGS_15.18|| 

==============================

athedAnIm yathA-niruktam AtmAnam yo veda, tasyedam phalam ucyate - 

yo mAm evam asammUDho jAnAti puruShottamam |
sa sarva-vid bhajati mAm sarva-bhAvena bhArata ||BhG_15.19||

yo mAm Ishvaram yathokta-visheShaNam evam yathoktena prakAreNa asammUDhaH sammoha-varjitaH san jAnAty ayam aham asmIti puruShottamam, sa sarva-vit sarvAtmanA sarvam vettIti sarvaj~naH sarva-bhUta-stham bhajati mAm sarva-bhAvena sarvAtmatayA he bhArata ||BhGS_15.19|| 

==============================

asmin adhyAye bhagavat-tattva-j~nAnam mokSha-phalam uktvA, atha idAnIm tat stauti - 

iti guhyatamam shAstram idam uktam mayAnagha |
etad buddhvA buddhimAn syAt kR^ita-kR^ityash ca bhArata ||BhG_15.20||

iti etad guhyatamam gopyatamam, atyanta-rahasyam ity etat | kim tat ? shAstram | yady api gItAkhyam samastam shAstram ucyate, tathApy ayam evAdhyAya iha shAstram ity ucyate stuty-artham prakaraNAt | sarvo hi gItA-shAstrArtho 'smin adhyAye samAsena uktaH | na kevalam gItA-shAstrArtha eva, kimtu sarvash ca vedArtha iha parisamAptaH | yas tam veda sa veda-vit [GItA 15.1] vedaish ca sarvair aham eva vedyaH [GItA 15.15] iti coktam | idam uktam kathitam mayA he 'nagha apApa ! etac chAstram yathA-darshitArtham buddhvA buddhimAn syAt bhavet nAnyathA | kR^ita-kR^ityash ca bhArata kR^itam kR^ityam kartavyam yena sa kR^ita-kR^ityaH | vishiShTa-janma-prasUtena brAhmaNena yat kartavyam tat sarvam bhagavat-tattve vidite kR^itam bhaved ity arthaH | na cAnyathA kartavyam parisamApyate kasyacid ity abhiprAyaH | sarvam karmAkhilam pArtha j~nAne parisamApyate [GItA 4.33] iti coktam | 

etad dhi janma-sAmagryam brAhmaNasya visheShataH | 
prApyaitat kR^ita-kR^ityo hi dvijo bhavati nAnyathA || [Manu 12.93] 

iti ca mAnavam vacanam | yataH etat paramArthatattvam mattaH shrutavAn asi, ataH kR^itArthas tvam bhArateti ||BhGS_15.20|| 

iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrI-govinda-bhagavat-pUjya-pAda-
shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^itau shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye
paJNcadasho 'dhyAyaH ||

BhG 16

atha daivAsura-sampad-vibhAga-yogo nAma 
ShoDasho 'dhyAyaH

(shrI-shaN^karAcArya-bhagavat-pAda-kR^ita-bhAShyam)


daivI AsurI rAkShasI ceti prANiNAm prakR^itayo navame 'dhyAye sUcitAH | tAsAm vistareNa pradarshanAya abhayam sattva-samshuddhir ity Adir adhyAyaH Arabhyate | tatra samsAra-mokShAya daivI prakR^itiH, nibandhAyAsurI rAkShasI ceti daivyA AdAnAya pradarshanam kriyate | itarayoH parivarjanAya ca shrI-bhagavAn uvAca - 

abhayam sattva-samshuddhir j~nAna-yoga-vyavasthitiH |
dAnam damash ca yaj~nash ca svAdhyAyas tapa Arjavam ||BhG_16.1||

abhayam abhIrutA | sattva-samshuddhiH sattvasyAntaH-karaNasya samshuddhiH | samvyavahAreShu para-vaJNcanA-mAyAnR^itAdi-parivarjanam shuddha-sattva-bhAvena vyavahAra ity arthaH | j~nAna-yoga-vyavasthitir j~nAnam shAstrata AcAryatash ca AtmAdi-padArthAnAm avagamaH | avagatAnAm indriyAdy-upasamhAreNaikAgratayA svAtma-samvedyatApAdanam yogaH | tayor j~nAna-yogayor vyAvasthitiH vyavasthAnam tan-niShThatA | eShA pradhAnA daivI sAttvikI socyate | dAnam yathA-shakti samvibhAgo 'nnAdInAm | damash ca bAhya-karaNAnAm upashamaH | antaH-karaNasyopashamam shAntim vakShyati | yaj~nash ca shrauto 'gnihotrAdiH | smArtash ca deva-yaj~nAdiH | svAdhyAya R^ig-vedAdyadhyayanam adR^iShTArtham | tapo vakShyamANam shArIrAdi | Arjavam R^ijutvam sarvadA ||BhGS_16.1|| 

==============================

kim ca - 

ahimsA satyam akrodhas tyAgaH shAntir apaishunam |
dayA bhUteShv aloluptvam mArdavam hrIr acApalam ||BhG_16.2||

ahimsAhimsanam prANinAm pIDA-varjanam | satyam apriyAnR^ita-varjitam yathA-bhUtArtha-vacanam | akrodhaH parair AkruShTasyAbhihatasya vA prAptasya krodhasya upashamanam | tyAgaH samnyAsaH, pUrvam dAnasyoktatvAt | shAntir antaHkaraNasyopashamaH | apaishunam apishunatA | parasmai para-randhra-prakaTI-karaNam paishunam, tad-abhAvo 'paishunam | dayA kR^ipA bhUteShu duHkhiteShu | aloluptvam indriyANAm viShaya-samnidhAv avikriyA | mArdavam mR^idutAkrauryam | hrIr lajjA | acApalam asati prayojane vAk-pANi-pAdAdInAm avyApArayitR^itvam ||BhGS_16.2|| 

==============================
 
kim ca - 

tejaH kShamA dhR^itiH shaucam adroho nAtimAnitA |
bhavanti sampadam daivIm abhijAtasya bhArata ||BhG_16.3||

tejaH prAgalbhyam na tvag-gatA dIptiH | kShamA AkruShTasya tADitasya vAntar-vikriyAnutpattiH | utpannAyAm vikriyAyAm praashamanam akrodha ity avocAma | ittham kShamAyA akrodhasya ca visheShaH | dhR^itir dehendriyeShv avasAdam prApteShu tasya pratiShedhako 'ntaH-karaNa-vR^itti-visheShaH | yenottambhitAni karaNAni dehash ca nAvasIdanti | shaucam dvi-vidham mR^ij-jala-kR^itam bAhyam Abhyantaram ca mano-buddhayor nairmalyam mAyA-rAgAdi-kAluShyAbhAvaH | evam dvi-vidham shaucam | adrohaH para-jighAmsAbhAvo 'himsanam | nAtimAnitA atyartham mAno 'timAnaH, sa yasya vidyate so 'timAnI | tad-bhAvo 'timAnitA | tad-abhAvo nAtimAnitA AtmanaH pUjyatAtishaya-bhAvanAbhAva ity arthaH | bhavanty abhayAdIni etad-antAni sampadam abhijAtasya | kim-vishiShTam sampadam ? daivIm devAnAm yA sampat tAm abhilakShya jAtasya deva-vibhUty-arhasya bhAvi-kalyANasyety arthaH | he bhArata ! ||BhGS_16.3|| 

==============================
 
athedAnIm AsurI sampad ucyate - 

dambho darpo 'timAnash ca krodhaH pAruShyam eva ca |
aj~nAnam cAbhijAtasya pArtha sampadam AsurIm ||BhG_16.4||

dambho dharma-dhvajitvam | darpo vidyA-dhana-svajanAdi-nimitta utsekaH | atimAnaH pUrvoktaH | krodhash ca | pAruShyam eva ca paruSha-vacanam | yathA kANam cakShuShmAn, virUpam rUpavAn, hInAbhijanam uttamAbhijana ity Adi | aj~nAnam cAviveka-j~nAnam kartavyAkartavyAdi-viShaya-mithyA-pratyayaH | abhijAtasya pArtha | kim-abhijAtasyety Aha - sampadam AsurIm asurANAm sampat AsurI tAm abhijAtasya ity arthaH ||BhGS_16.4|| 

==============================

anayoH sampadoH kAryam ucyate - 

daivI sampad vimokShAya nibandhAyAsurI matA |
mA shucaH sampadam daivIm abhijAto 'si pANDava ||BhG_16.5||

daivI sampat yA sA vimokShAya samsAra-bandhanAt | nibandhAya niyato bandho nibandhas tad-artham AsurI sampat matA abhipretA | tathA rAkShasI ca | tatraivam ukte saty ar junasyAntar-gatam bhAvam kim aham Asura-sampad-yuktaH ? kim vA daiva-sampad-yuktaH ? ity evam AlocanA-rUpam AlakShya Aha bhagavAn - mA shucaH shokam mA kArShIH | sampadam daivIm abhijAto 'sy abhilakShya jAto 'si | bhAvi-kalyANas tvam asIty arthaH | he pANDAva ||BhGS_16.5|| 

==============================

dvau bhUta-sargau loke 'smin daiva Asura eva ca |
daivo vistarashaH prokta Asuram pArtha me shR^iNu ||BhG_16.6||

dvau dvi-samkhyAkau bhUta-sargau bhUtAnAm manuShyANAm sargau sR^iShTI bhUta-sargau sR^ijyeteti sargau bhUtAny eva sR^ijyamAnAni daivAsura-sampad-dvaya-yuktAnIti dvau bhUta-sargAv ity ucyate | dvayA ha vai prAjApatyA devAsh cAsurA ca [BAU 1.3.1] iti shruteH | loke 'smin, samsAra ity arthaH | sarveShAm dvaividhyopapatteH | kau tau bhUta-sargau ? ity ucyate - prakR^itAv eva daiva Asura eva ca | uktayor eva punar anuvAde prayojanam Aha - daivo bhUta-sargo 'bhayam sattva-samshuddhir ity AdinA vistarasho vistara-prakAraiH proktaH kathitaH, na tu Asuro vistarashaH | atas tat-parivarjanArtham Asuram pArtha me mama vacanAd ucyamAnam vistarashaH sR^iNu avadhAraya ||BhGS_16.6|| 

==============================
 
A adhyAya-parisamApter AsurI sampat prANi-visheShaNatvena pradarshyate, pratyakShI-karaNena ca shakyate tasyAH parivarjanam kartum iti -

pravR^ittim ca nivR^ittim ca janA na vidur AsurAH |
na shaucam nApi cAcAro na satyam teShu vidyate ||BhG_16.7||

pravR^ittim ca pravartanam yasmin puruShArtha-sAdhane kartavye pravR^ittis tAm, nivR^ittim ca etad-viparItAm yasmAt anartha-hetoH nivartitavyam sA nivR^ittis tAm ca, janA AsurA na vidur na jAnanti | na kevalam pravR^itti-nivR^ittI eva te na viduH, na shaucam nApi cAcAro na satyam teShu vidyate | ashaucA anAcArA mAyAvino 'nR^ita-vAdino hy AsurAH ||BhGS_16.7|| 

==============================

kim ca - 
asatyam apratiShTham te jagad Ahur anIshvaram |
aparaspara-sambhUtam kim anyat kAma-haitukam ||BhG_16.8||

asatyam yathA vayam anR^ita-prAyAs tathedam jagat sarvam asatyam | apratiShTham ca nAsya dharmAdharmau pratiShThAto 'pratiShTham ceti | te AsurAH janAH jagad Ahur anIshvaram na ca dharmAdharma-sa-vyapekShako 'sya shAsiteshvaro vidyata ity ato 'nIshvaram jagad AhuH | kim ca, aparaspara-sambhUtam kAma-prayuktayoH strI-puruShayor anyonya-samyogAj jagat sarvam sambhUtam | kim anyat kAma-haitukam | kAma-hetukam eva kAma-haitukam | kim anyaj jagataH kAraNam ? na kimcit adR^iShTam dharmAdharmAdi kAraNAntaram vidyate | jagataH kAma eva prANinAm kAraNam iti lokAyatika-dR^iShTir iyam ||BhGS_16.8|| 

==============================

etAm dR^iShTim avaShTabhya naShTAtmAno 'lpa-buddhayaH |
prabhavanty ugra-karmANaH kShayAya jagato 'hitAH ||BhG_16.9||

etAm dR^iShTim avaShTabhya Ashritya naShTatmAno naShTa-svabhAvA vibhraShTa-para-loka-sAdhanA alpa-buddhayo viShaya-viShayAlpaiva buddhir yeShAm te 'lpa-buddhayaH prabhavanti udbhavanti ugra-karmANaH krUra-karmANo himsAtmakAH | kShayAya jagataH prabhavantIti sambandhaH || jagato 'hitAH shatravaH ity arthaH ||BhGS_16.9|| 

==============================

te ca - 

kAmam Ashritya duShpUram dambha-mAna-madAnvitAH |
mohAd gR^ihItvAsad-grAhAn pravartante 'shucivratAH ||BhG_16.10||

kAmam icchA-visheSham Ashritya avaShTabhya duShpUram ashakya-pUraNam dambha-mAna-madAnvitA dambhash ca mAnash ca madash ca dambha-mAna-madAs tair anvitAH dambha-mAna-madAnvitA mohAd avivekato gR^ihItvA upAdAya asad-grAhAn ashubha-nishcayAn pravartante loke ashuci-vratAH ashucIni vratAni yeShAm te 'shuci-vratAH ||BhGS_16.10|| 

==============================

kim ca - 
cintAm aparimeyAm ca pralayAntAm upAshritAH |
kAmopabhoga-paramA etAvad iti nishcitAH ||BhG_16.11||

cintAm aparimeyAm ca, na parimAtum shakyate yasyAsh cintAyA iyattA sAparimeyA, tAm aparimeyAm, pralayAntAm maraNAntAm upAshritAH, sadA cintA-parA ity arthaH | kAmopabhoga-paramAH, kAmyante iti kAmA viShayAH shabdAdayas tad-upabhoga-paramA ayam eva paramaH puruShArtho yaH kAmopabhoga ity evam nishcitAtmAnaH | etAvat iti nishcitAH ||BhGS_16.11|| 

==============================

AshA-pAsha-shatair baddhAH kAma-krodha-parAyaNAH |
Ihante kAma-bhogArtham anyAyenArtha-samcayAn ||BhG_16.12||

AshA-pAsha-shatair Ashaiva pAshAs tac-chatair baddhAH niyantritAH santaH sarvata AkR^iShyamANAH, kAma-krodha-parAyaNAH kAma-krodhau param ayanam Ashrayo yeShAm te kAma-krodha-parAyaNAH | Ihante ceShTante kAma-bhogArtham kAma-bhoga-prayojanAya na dharmArtham | anyAyena para-svApaharaNAdinety arthaH | kim ? artha-samcayAn artha-pracayAn ||BhGS_16.12|| 

==============================

IdR^ishash ca teShAm abhiprAyaH - 

idam adya mayA labdham idam prApsye manoratham |
idam astIdam api me bhaviShyati punar dhanam ||BhG_16.13||

idam dravyam adya idAnIm mayA labdham | idam cAnyat prApsye manoratham manas-tuShTi-karam | idam cAstIdam api me bhaviShyati AgAmini samvatsare punar dhanam tenAham dhanI vikhyAto bhaviShyAmIti ||BhGS_16.13|| 

==============================

asau mayA hataH shatrur haniShye cAparAn api |
Ishvaro 'ham aham bhogI siddho 'ham balavAn sukhI ||BhG_16.14||

asau devadattanAmA mayA hato durjayaH shatruH | haniShye cAparAn anyAn varAkAn api | kim ete kariShyanti tapasvinaH | sarvathApi nAsti mattulyaH | katham ? Ishvaro 'ham, aham bhogI | sarva-prakAreNash ca siddho 'ham sampannaH putraiH naptR^ibhiH, na kevalam mAnuShaH, balavAn sukhI cAham eva | anye tu bhUmibhArAyAvitIrNAH ||BhGS_16.14||

==============================

ADhyo 'bhijanavAn asmi ko 'nyo 'sti sadR^isho mayA |
yakShye dAsyAmi modiShya ity aj~nAna-vimohitAH ||BhG_16.15||

ADhaDH dhanena, abhijanavAn saptapuruSham shrotriyatvAdisampannaH - tenApi na mama tulyo 'sti kashcit | ko 'nyo 'sti sadR^ishas tulyaH mayA ? kim ca, yakShye yAgenApy anyAn abhibhaviShyAmi, dAsyAmi naTAdibhyaH, modiShye harSham cAtishayam prApsyAmi, iti evam aj~nAnavimohitAH aj~nAnena vimohitAH vividham avivekabhAvam ApannAH ||BhGS_16.15||

==============================

aneka-citta-vibhrAntA moha-jAla-samAvR^itAH |
prasaktAH kAma-bhogeShu patanti narake 'shucau ||BhG_16.16||

aneka-citta-vibhrAntA ukta-prakArair anekaish cittaiH vividham bhrAntAH aneka-citta-vibhrAntAH, mohajAlasamAvR^itAH moho 'viveko 'j~nAnam tad eva jAlamiva AvaraNAtmakatvAt, tena samAvR^itAH | prasaktAH kAmabhogeShu tatraiva niShaNNAH santas tena upacita-kalmaShAH patanti narake 'shucau vaitaraNyAdau ||BhGS_16.16||

==============================

Atma-sambhAvitAH stabdhA dhana-mAna-madAnvitAH |
yajante nAma-yaj~nais te dambhenAvidhi-pUrvakam ||BhG_16.17||

AtmasambhAvittAH sarvaguNavishiShTatayA Atmanaiva sambhAvitAH AtmasambhAvitAH, na sAdhubhiH | stabdhAH apraNatAtmAnaH | dhanamAnamadAnvitAH dhananimittaH mAnaH madash ca, tAbhyAm dhanamAnamadAbhyAm anvitAH | yajante nAmayaj~naiH nAmamAtrair yaj~nais te dambhena dharmadhvajitayAvidhipUrvakam vidhivihitAN^getikartavyatArahitam ||BhGS_16.17|| 

==============================

ahamkAram balam darpam kAmam krodham ca samshritAH |
mAm Atma-para-deheShu pradviShanto 'bhyasUyakAH ||BhG_16.18||

ahamkAram ahamkaraNam ahamkAraH | vidyamAnair avidyamAnaish ca guNair Atmany adhyAropitair vishiShTam AtmAnam aham iti manyate, so 'hamkAro 'vidyAkhyaH kaShTatamaH sarva-doShANAm mUlam sarvAnartha-pravR^ittInAm ca, tam | tathA balam parAbhibhava-nimittam kAma-rAgAnvitam | darpam darpo nAma yasya udbhave dharmam atikrAmati so 'yam antaHkaraNAshrayo doSha-visheShaH | kAmam stry-Adi-viShayam | krodham aniShTa-viShayam | etAn anyAmsh ca mahato doShAn samshritAH | kim ca te mAm Ishvaram Atma-para-deheShu sva-dehe para-deheShu ca tad-buddhi-karma-sAkShi-bhUtam mAm pradviShantaH, mac-chAsanAtivartitvam pradveShaH, tam kurvanto 'bhyasUyakAH san-mArga-sthAnAm guNeShu asahamAnAH ||BhGS_16.18|| 

==============================

tAn aham dviShataH krUrAn samsAreShu narAdhamAn |
kShipAmy ajasram ashubhAn AsurIShv eva yoniShu ||BhG_16.19||

tAn aham sanmArgapratipakShabhUtAn sAdhudveShiNo dviShatash ca mAm krUrAn samsAreShu evAnekanarakasamsaraNamArgeShu narAdhamAn adharmadoShavattvAt kShipAmi prakShipAmy ajasram samtatam ashubhAn ashubhakarmakAriNaH AsurIShveva krUra-karma-prAyAsu vyAghra×sahAdiyoniShu kShipAmItyanena sambandhaH ||BhGS_16.19|| 

==============================

AsurIm yonim ApannA mUDhA janmani janmani |
mAm aprApyaiva kaunteya tato yAnty adhamAm gatim ||BhG_16.20||

AsurIm yonim ApannAH pratipannAH mUDhAH avivekino janmani janmani pratijanma tamobahulAsveva yoniShu jAyamAnAH adho gacchanto mUDhAH mAm Ishvaram aprApyAnAsAdya eva he kaunteya, tatas tasmAdapi yAnty adhamAm gatim nikR^iShTatamAm gatim | mAm aprApyaiveti na mat-prAptau kAcid api AshaN^kAsti, ataH macchiShTasAdhumArgam aprApya ity arthaH ||BhGS_16.20|| 

==============================

sarvasyA AsuryAH sampadaH samkShepo 'yam ucyate, yasmin trividhe sarvaH AsurIsampadbhedo 'nanto 'py antarbhavati | yatparihAreNa parihR^itash ca bhavati, yat mUlam sarvasyAnarthasya, tat etad ucyate - 

tri-vidham narakasyedam dvAram nAshanam AtmanaH |
kAmaH krodhas tathA lobhas tasmAd etat trayam tyajet ||BhG_16.21||

trividham triprakAram narakasya prAptAv idam dvAram nAshanam AtmanaH, yat dvAram pravishanneva nashyati AtmA | kasmaicit puruShArthAya yogyo na bhavatItyetat, atar ucyate dvAram nAshanam AtmanaH iti | kim tat ? kAmaH krodhas tathA lobhaH | tasmAt etat trayam tyajet | yataH etat dvAram nAshanam Atmanas tasmAt kAmAditrayametat tyajet ||BhGS_16.21|| 

==============================

tyAga-stutir iyam - 

etair vimuktaH kaunteya tamo-dvArais tribhir naraH |
Acaraty AtmanaH shreyas tato yAti parAm gatim ||BhG_16.22||

etaiH vimuktaH kaunteya tamo-dvArais tamaso narakasya duHkha-mohAtmakasya dvArANi kAmAdayas taiH, etais tribhiH vimukto nara Acaraty anutiShThati | kim ? AtmanaH shreyaH | yat-pratibaddhaH pUrvam nAcacAra, tad-apagamAd Acarati | tatas tad-AcaraNAt yAti parAm gatim mokSham apIti ||BhGS_16.22|| 

==============================

sarvasya etasya AsurI-sampat-parivarjanasya shreya-AcaraNasya ca shAstram kAraNam | shAstra-pramANAd ubhayam shakyam kartum, nAnyathA | ataH - 

yaH shAstra-vidhim utsR^ijya vartate kAma-kArataH |
na sa siddhim avApnoti na sukham na parAm gatim ||BhG_16.23||

yaH shAstra-vidhim shAstram vedas tasya vidhim kartavyAkartavya-j~nAna-kAraNam vidhi-pratiShedhAkhyam utsR^ijya tyaktvA vartate kAma-kArataH kAma-prayuktaH san, na sa siddhim puruShArtha-yogyatAm avApnoti, nApy asmin loke sukham nApi parAm prakR^iShTAm gatim svargam mokSham vA ||BhGS_16.23|| 


==============================

tasmAc chAstram pramANam te kAryAkArya-vyavasthitau |
j~nAtvA shAstra-vidhAnoktam karma kartum ihArhasi ||BhG_16.24||

tasmAt shAstram pramANam j~nAna-sAdhanam te tava kAryAkArya-vyavasthitau kartavyAkartavya-vyavasthAyAm | ato j~nAtvA buddhvA shAstra-vidhAnoktam -- vidhir vidhAnam shAstram eva vidhAnam shAstra-vidhAnam kuryAn na kuryAd ity evam-lakShaNam, tena uktam sva-karma yat tat kartum ihArhasi | iheti karmAdhikAra-bhUmi-pradarshanArtham iti ||BhGS_16.24|| 

iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrI-govinda-bhagavat-pUjya-pAda-
shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^itau shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye
ShoDAsho 'dhyAyaH ||


__________________________________________________________

BhG 17

atha shraddhA-traya-vibhAga-yogaH
saptadasho 'dhyAyaH

tasmAc chAstram pramANam ta [GItA 16.24] iti bhagavad-vAkyAl labdha-prashna-bIjo 'rjuna uvAca - 

ye shAstra-vidhim utsR^ijya yajante shraddhayAnvitAH |
teShAm niShThA tu kA kR^iShNa sattvam Aho rajas tamaH ||BhG_17.1||

ye kecid avisheShitAH shAstra-vidhim shAstra-vidhAnam shruti-smR^iti-shAstra-codanAm utsR^ijya parityajya yajante devAdIn pUjayanti shraddhayAnvitAH shraddhayAstikya-buddhyAnvitAH samyuktAH santaH | shruti-lakShaNam smR^iti-lakShaNam vA kamcit shAstra-vidhim apashyanto vR^iddha-vyavahAra-darshanAd eva shraddadhAnatayA ye devAdIn pUjayanti | te iha ye shAstra-vidhim utsR^ijya yajante shraddhayAnvitA ity evam gR^ihyante | ye punaH kamcit shAstra-vidhim upalabhamAnaiva tam utsR^ijyAyathA-vidhi devAdIn pUjayanti | ta iha ye shAstra-vidhim utsR^ijya yajanta iti na parigR^ihyante | kasmAt ? shraddhayAnvitatva-visheShaNAt | devAdi-pUjA-vidhi-param kimcit shAstram pashyanta eva tad utsR^ijyAshraddadhAnatayA tad-vihitAyAm devAdi-pUjAyAm shraddhayAnvitAH pravartanta iti na shakyam kalpayitum yasmAt, tasmAt pUrvoktaiva ye shAstra-vidhim utsR^ijya yajante shraddhayAnvitA ity atra gR^ihyante | teShAm evam-bhUtAnAm niShThA tu kA kR^iShNa sattvam Aho rajas tamaH, kim sattvam niShThAvasthAnam, Aho svit rajaH, athavA tama iti | etad uktam bhavati - yA teShAm devAdi-viShayA pUjA, sA kim sAttvikI, Aho svit rAjasI, uta tAmasIti ||BhGS_17.1||

==============================

sAmAnya-viShayo 'yam prashno nApravibhajrya prativacanam arhatIti shrIbhagavAnuvAca - 

tri-vidhA bhavati shraddhA dehinAm sA svabhAva-jA |
sAttvikI rAjasI caiva tAmasI ceti tAm shR^iNu ||BhG_17.2||

tri-vidhA tri-prakArA bhavati shraddhA | yasyAm niShThAyAm tvam pR^icchasi | dehinAm sharIriNAm sA svabhAva-jA | janmAntara-kR^ito dharmAdi-samskAro maraNa-kAle 'bhivyaktaH svabhAva ucyate, tato jAtA svabhAva-jA | sAttvikI sattva-nirvR^ittA deva-pUjAdi-viShayA | rAjasI rajo-nirvR^ittA yakSha-rakShaH-pUjAdi-viShayA | tAmasI tamo-nirvR^ittA preta-pishAcAdi-pUjA-viShayA | evam tri-vidhAm tAm ucyamAnAm shraddhAm shR^iNv avadhAraya ||BhGS_17.2|| 

==============================

sA iyam trividhA bhavati - 

sattvAnurUpA sarvasya shraddhA bhavati bhArata |
shraddhA-mayo 'yam puruSho yo yac-chraddhaH sa eva saH ||BhG_17.3||

sattvAnurUpA vishiShTa-samskAropetAntaH-karaNAnurUpA sarvasya prANi-jAtasya shraddhA bhavati bhArata | yady evam tataH kim syAt ? ity ucyate - shraddhA-mayo 'yam shraddhA-prAyaH puruShaH samsArI jIvaH | katham ? yo yac-chraddho yA shraddhA yasya jIvasya sa yac-chraddhaH sa eva tac-chraddhAnurUpa eva sa jIvaH ||BhGS_17.3|| 

==============================

tatash ca kAryeNa liN^gena devAdipUjayA sattvAdiniShThAnumeyA ity Aha - 

yajante sAttvikA devAn yakSha-rakShAmsi rAjasAH |
pretAn bhUta-gaNAmsh cAnye yajante tAmasA janAH ||BhG_17.4||

yajante pUjayanti sAttvikAH sattva-niShThA devAn, yakSha-rakShAmsi rAjasAH, pretAn bhUta-gaNAmsh ca sapta-mAtR^ikAdImsh cAnye yajante tAmasAH janAH ||BhGS_17.4|| 

==============================

evam kAryato nirNItAH sattvAdi-niShThAH shAstra-vidhy-utsarge | tatra kashcid eva sahasreShu deva-pUjAdi-paraH sattva-niShTho bhavati, bAhulyena tu rajo-niShThAs tamo-niShThAsh caiva prANino bhavanti | katham ? - 

ashAstra-vihitam ghoram tapyante ye tapo janAH |
dambhAhamkAra-samyuktAH kAma-rAga-balAnvitAH ||BhG_17.5||

ashAstra-vihitam na shAstra-vihitam ashAstra-vihitam ghoram pIDA-karam prANinAm Atmanash ca tapas tapyante nirvartayanti ye janAs te ca dambhAhamkAra-samyuktAH | dambhash cAhamkArash ca dambhAhamkArau, tAbhyAm samyuktAH dambhAhamkAra-samyuktAH, kAma-rAga-balAnvitAH kAmash ca rAgash ca kAma-rAgau tat-kR^itam balam kAma-rAga-balam tenAnvitAH kAma-rAga-balAnvitAH ||BhGS_17.5|| 

==============================

karshayantaH sharIra-stham bhUta-grAmam acetasaH |
mAm caivAntaH-sharIra-stham tAn viddhy Asura-nishcayAn ||BhG_17.6||

karshayantaH kR^ishI-kurvantaH sharIra-stham bhUta-grAmam karaNa-samudAyam acetaso 'vivekinaH mAm caiva tat-karma-buddhi-sAkShi-bhUtam antaH-sharIra-stham nArAyaNam karshayantaH, mad-anushAsanAkaraNam eva mat-karshanam | tAn viddhy Asura-nishcayAn Asuro nishcayo yeShAm te Asura-nishcayAs tAn pariharaNArtham viddhIti upadeshaH ||BhGS_17.6|| 

==============================

AhArANAm ca rasya-snigdhAdi-varga-traya-rUpeNa bhinnAnAm yathA-kramam sAttvika-rAjasa-tAmasa-puruSha-priyatva-darshanam iha kriyate rasya-snigdhAdiShu AhAra-visheSheShv AtmanaH prIty-atirekeNa liN^gena sAttvikatvam rAjasatvam tAmasatvam ca buddhvA rajas-tamo-liN^gAnAm AhArANAm parivarjanArtham sattva-liN^gAnAm copAdAnArtham | tathA yaj~nAdInAm api sattvAdi-guNa-bhedena tri-vidhatva-pratipAdanam iha rAjasa-tAmasAn buddhvA katham nu nAma parityajet, sAttvikAn evAnutiShThed ity evam artham Aha - 

AhAras tv api sarvasya trividho bhavati priyaH |
yaj~nas tapas tathA dAnam teShAm bhedam imam shR^iNu ||BhG_17.7||

AhAras tv api sarvasya bhoktuH prANinas tri-vidho bhavati priyaH iShTaH | tathA yaj~nas tathA tapas tathA dAnam | teShAm AhArAdInAm bhedam imam vakShyamANam sR^iNu ||BhGS_17.7|| 

==============================

AyuH-sattva-balArogya-sukha-prIti-vivardhanAH |
rasyAH snigdhAH sthirA hR^idyA AhArAH sAttvika-priyAH ||BhG_17.8||

Ayush ca sattvam ca balam ca Arogyam ca sukham ca prItish ca AyuH-sattva-balArogya-sukha-prItayas tAsAm vivardhanAH AyuH-sattva-balArogya-sukha-prIti-vivardhanAH | te ca rasyA rasopetAH, snigdhAH snehavantaH, sthirAsh cira-kAla-sthAyino dehe, hR^idyAH hR^idaya-priyAH, AhArAH sAttvika-priyAH sAttvikasyeShTAH ||BhGS_17.8|| 

==============================

kaTv-amla-lavaNAtyuShNa-tIkShNa-rUkSha-vidAhinaH |
AhArA rAjasasyeShTA duHkha-shokAmaya-pradAH ||BhG_17.9||

kaTv-amla-lavaNAtyuShNa-tIkShNa-rUkSha-vidAhina ity atrAti-shabdaH kaTvAdiShu sarvatra yojyaH | atikaTuH atitIkShNaH ity evam | kaTush cAmlash ca lavaNash cAtyuShNash ca tIkShNash ca rUkShash ca vidAhI ca te AhArA rAjasasyeShTA duHkha-shokAmaya-pradAH duHkham ca shokam cAmayam ca prayacchantIti duHkha-shokAmaya-pradAH ||BhGS_17.9|| 

==============================

yAta-yAmam gata-rasam pUti paryuShitam ca yat |
ucchiShTam api cAmedhyam bhojanam tAmasa-priyam ||BhG_17.10||

yAta-yAmam manda-pakvam, nirvIryasya gata-rasa-shabdenoktatvAt | gata-rasam rasa-viyuktam, pUti durgandhi, paryuShitam ca pakvam sad rAtry-antaritam ca yat, ucchiShTam api bhukta-shiShTam ucchiShTam, amedhyam ayaj~nArham bhojanam IdR^isham tAmasa-priyam ||BhGS_17.10|| 

==============================

athedAnIm yaj~nas trividha ucyate - 

aphalAkAN^kShibhir yaj~no vidhi-dR^iShTo ya ijyate |
yaShTavyam eveti manaH samAdhAya sa sAttvikaH ||BhG_17.11||

aphalAkAN^kShibhir aphalArthibhir yaj~no vidhi-dR^iShTaH shAstra-codanAdR^iShTau yo yaj~na ijyate nirvartyate, yaShTavyam eveti yaj~na-svarUpa-nirvartanam eva kAryam iti manaH samAdhAya, nAnena puruShArtho mama kartavya ity evam nishcitya, sa sAttviko yaj~na ucyate ||BhGS_17.11|| 

==============================

abhisamdhAya tu phalam dambhArtham api caiva yat |
ijyate bharata-shreShTha tam yaj~nam viddhi rAjasam ||BhG_17.12||

abhisandhAya tu uddishya phalam dambhArtham api caiva yad ijyate bharata-shreShTha tam yaj~nam viddhi rAjasam ||BhGS_17.12|| 

==============================

vidhi-hInam asR^iShTAnnam mantra-hInam adakShiNam |
shraddhA-virahitam yaj~nam tAmasam paricakShate ||BhG_17.13||

vidhi-hInam yathA-codita-viparItam, asR^iShTAnnam brAhmaNebhyo na sR^iShTam na dattam, annam yasmin yaj~ne so 'sR^iShTAnnas tam asR^iShTAnnam | mantra-hInam mantrataH svarato varNato vA viyuktam mantra-hInam, adakShiNam ukta-dakShiNA-rahitam, shraddhA-virahitam yaj~nam tAmasam paricakShate tamo-nirvR^ittam kathayanti ||BhGS_17.13|| 

==============================

atha idAnIm tapas tri-vidham ucyate -

deva-dvija-guru-prAj~na-pUjanam shaucam Arjavam |
brahmacaryam ahimsA ca shArIram tapa ucyate ||BhG_17.14||

devA ca dvijA ca guravash ca prAj~nAsh ca deva-dvija-guru-prAj~nAs teShAm pUjanam deva-dvija-guru-prAj~na-pUjanam | shaucam | Arjavam R^ijutvam | brahmacaryam ahimsA ca sharIra-nirvartyam shArIram sharIra-pradhAnaiH sarvair eva kArya-karaNaiH kartrAdibhiH sAdhyam shArIram tapa ucyate | paJNcaite tasya hetavaH [GItA 18.15] iti hi vakShyati ||BhGS_17.14|| 

==============================

anudvega-karam vAkyam satyam priya-hitam ca yat |
svAdhyAyAbhyasanam caiva vAN^-mayam tapa ucyate ||BhG_17.15||

anudvega-karam prANinAm aduHkha-karam vAkyam satyam priya-hitam ca yat priya-hite dR^iShTAdR^iShTArthe | anudvega-karatvAdibhir dharmair vAkyam visheShyate | visheShaNa-dharma-samucayArthash ca-shabdaH | para-pratyayArtham prayuktasya vAkyasya satya-priya-hitAnudvega-karatvAnAm anyatamena dvAbhyAm tribhir vA hInatA syAd yadi, na tad vAN^-mayam tapaH | tathA satya-vAkyasya itareShAm anyatamena dvAbhyAm tribhir vA vihInatAyAm na vAN^-maya-tapastvam | tathA priya-vAkyasyApItareShAm anyatamena dvAbhyAm tribhir vA vihInasya na vAN^-maya-tapastvam | tathA hita-vAkyasyApItareShAm anyatamena dvAbhyAm tribhir vA vihInasya na vAN^-maya-tapastvam | kim punas tat tapaH ? yat satyam vAkyam anudvega-karam priyam hitam ca, tat tapo vAN^-mayam | yathA shAnto bhava vatsa, svAdhyAyam yogam cAnutiShTha, tathA te shreyo bhaviShyatIti | svAdhyAyAbhyasanam caiva yathA-vidhi vAN^-mayam tapa ucyate ||BhGS_17.15|| 

==============================

manaH-prasAdaH saumyatvam maunam Atma-vinigrahaH |
bhAva-samshuddhir ity etat tapo mAnasam ucyate ||BhG_17.16||

manaH-prasAdaH manasaH prashAntiH svacchatApAdanam prasAdaH | saumyatvam yat saumanasyam AhuH | mukhAdi-prasAdAdi-kAryonneyAntaH-karaNasya vR^ittiH | maunam vAN^-niyamo 'pi manaH-samyama-pUrvako bhavatIti kAryeNa kAraNam ucyate manaH-samyamo maunam iti | Atma-vinigraho mano-nirodhaH sarvataH sAmAnya-rUpa Atma-vinigrahaH | vAg-viShayasyaiva manasaH samyamaH maunam iti visheShaH | bhAva-samshuddhiH paraiH vyavahAra-kAle 'mAyAvitvam bhAva-samshuddhiH | ity etat tapo mAnasam ucyate ||BhGS_17.16|| 

==============================

yathoktam kAyikam vAcikam mAnasam ca tapas taptam naraiH sattvAdi-guNa-bhedena katham tri-vidham bhavatIti, ucyate - 

shraddhayA parayA taptam tapas tat trividham naraiH |
aphalAkAN^kShibhir yuktaiH sAttvikam paricakShate ||BhG_17.17||

shraddhayA Astikya-buddhyA parayA prakR^iShTayA taptam anuShThitam tapas tat prakR^itam tri-vidham tri-prakAram try-adhiShThAnam narair anuShThAtR^ibhir aphalAkAN^kShibhiH phalAkAN^kShA-rahitair yuktaiH samAhitair yad IdR^isham tapaH, tat sAttvikam sattva-nirvR^ittam paricakShate kathayanti shiShTAH ||BhGS_17.17|| 

==============================

satkAra-mAna-pUjArtham tapo dambhena caiva yat |
kriyate tad iha proktam rAjasam calam adhruvam ||BhG_17.18||

satkAraH sAdhu-kAraH sAdhu ayam tapasvI brAhmaNa ity evam artham | mAno mAnanam pratyutthAnAbhivAdanAdis tad-artham | pUjA pAda-prakShAlanArcanAshayitR^itvAdis tad-artham ca tapaH satkAra-mAna-pUjArtham | dambhena caiva yat kriyate tapas tad iha proktam kathitam rAjasam calam kAdAcitka-phalatvena adhruvam ||BhGS_17.18|| 

==============================

mUDha-grAheNAtmano yat pIDayA kriyate tapaH |
parasyotsAdanArtham vA tat tAmasam udAhR^itam ||BhG_17.19||

mUDha-grAheNa aviveka-nishcayena AtmanaH pIDayA yat kriyate tapaH parasya utsAdanArtham vinAshArtham vA, tat tAmasam tapa udAhR^itam ||BhGS_17.19|| 

==============================

idAnIm dAna-traividhyam ucyate - 

dAtavyam iti yad dAnam dIyate 'nupakAriNe |
deshe kAle ca pAtre ca tad dAnam sAttvikam smR^itam ||BhG_17.20||

dAtavyam iti evam manaH kR^itvA yad dAnam dIyate 'nupakAriNe pratyupakArAsamarthAya, samarthAyApi nirapekSham dIyate | deshe puNye kurukShetrAdau | kAle samkrAnty-Adau | pAtre ca ShaD-aN^ga-vid veda-pAraga ity Adau | tad dAnam sAttvikam smR^itam ||BhGS_17.20|| 

==============================

yat tu pratyupakArArtham phalam uddishya vA punaH |
dIyate ca parikliShTam tad dAnam rAjasam smR^itam ||BhG_17.21||

yat tu dAnam pratyupakArArtham kAle tv ayam mAm pratyupakariShyatIty evam artham, phalam vAsya dAnasya me bhaviShyaty adR^iShTam iti | tad uddishya punar dIyate ca parikliShTam kheda-samyuktam, tad dAnam rAjasam smR^itam ||BhGS_17.21|| 

==============================

adesha-kAle yad dAnam apAtrebhyash ca dIyate |
asatkR^itam avaj~nAtam tat tAmasam udAhR^itam ||BhG_17.22||

adesha-kAle 'deshe 'puNye deshe mlecchAshucy-Adi-samkIrNe | akAle puNya-hetutvenAprakhyAte samkrAnty-Adi-visheSha-rahite 'pAtrebhyash ca mUrkha-taskarAdibhyaH | deshAdi-sampattau vA asatkR^itam priya-vacana-pAda-prakShAlana-pUjAdi-rahitam avaj~nAtam pAtra-paribhava-yuktam ca yad dAnam, tat tAmasam udAhR^itam ||BhGS_17.22|| 

==============================

yaj~na-dAna-tapaH-prabhR^itInAm sAdguNya-karaNAyAyam upadesha ucyate - 

om tat sad iti nirdesho brahmaNas trividhaH smR^itaH |
brAhmaNAs tena vedAsh ca yaj~nAsh ca vihitAH purA ||BhG_17.23||

om tat sad iti evam nirdeshaH, nirdishyate 'neneti nirdeshaH | trividho nAma nirdesho brahmaNaH smR^itash cintito vedAnteShu brahma-vidbhiH | brAhmaNAs tena nirdeshena trividhena vedAsh ca yaj~nAsh ca vihitAH nirmitAH purA pUrvam iti nirdesha-stuty-artham ucyate ||BhGS_17.23|| 

==============================

tasmAd om ity udAhR^itya yaj~na-dAna-tapaH-kriyAH |
pravartante vidhAnoktAH satatam brahma-vAdinAm ||BhG_17.24||

tasmAt om ity udAhR^itya uccArya yaj~na-dAna-tapaH-kriyA yaj~nAdi-svarUpAH kriyAH pravartante vidhAnoktAH shAstra-coditAH satatam sarvadA brahma-vAdinAm brahma-vadana-shIlAnAm ||BhGS_17.24|| 

==============================

tad ity anabhisamdhAya phalam yaj~na-tapaH-kriyAH |
dAna-kriyAsh ca vividhAH kriyante mokSha-kAN^kShibhiH ||BhG_17.25||

tad ity anabhisamdhAya | tad iti brahmAbhidhAnam uccAryAnabhisamdhAyash ca yaj~nAdi-karmaNaH phalam yaj~na-tapaH-kriyA yaj~na-kriyAsh ca tapaH-kriyAsh ca yaj~na-tapaH-kriyA dAna-kriyAsh ca vividhAH kShetra-hiraNya-pradAnAdi-lakShaNAH kriyante nirvartyante mokSha-kAN^kShibhir mokShArthibhir mumukShubhiH ||BhGS_17.25|| 

==============================

om-tac-chabdayor viniyoga uktaH | athedAnIm sac-chabdasya viniyogaH kathyate - 

sad-bhAve sAdhu-bhAve ca sad ity etat prayujyate |
prashaste karmaNi tathA sac-chabdaH pArtha yujyate ||BhG_17.26||

sad-bhAve | asataH sad-bhAve yathA-vidyamAnasya putrasya janmani | tathA sAdhu-bhAve cAsad-vR^ittasyAsAdhoH sad-vR^ittatA sAdhu-bhAvas tasmin sAdhu-bhAve ca | sad ity etad abhidhAnam brahmaNaH prayujyate 'bhidhIyate | prashaste karmaNi vivAhAdau ca tathA sac-chabdaH pArtha yujyate prayujyata ity etat ||BhGS_17.26|| 

==============================

yaj~ne tapasi dAne ca sthitiH sad iti cocyate |
karma caiva tad-arthIyam sad ity evAbhidhIyate ||BhG_17.27||

yaj~ne yaj~na-karmaNi yA sthitiH, tapasi ca yA sthitiH, dAne ca yA sthitiH, sA sad iti cocyate vidvadbhiH | karma caiva tad-arthIyam yaj~na-dAna-tapo 'rthIyam | athavA, yasyAbhidhAna-trayam prakR^itam tad-arthIyam yaj~na-dAna-tapo 'rthIyam IshvarArthIyam ity etat | sad ity evAbhidhIyate | tad etad yaj~na-dAna-tapa-Adi-karmAsAttvikam viguNam api shraddhA-pUrvakam brahmaNo 'bhidhAna-traya-prayogeNa sa-guNam sAttvikam sampAditam bhavati ||BhGS_17.27|| 

==============================

tatra ca sarvatra shraddhA-pradhAnatayA sarvam sampAdyate yasmAt, tasmAt - 

ashraddhayA hutam dattam tapas taptam kR^itam ca yat |
asad ity ucyate pArtha na ca tat pretya no iha ||BhG_17.28||

ashraddhayA hutam havanam kR^itam | ashraddhayA dattam brAhmaNebhyaH | ashraddhayA tapas taptam anuShThitam | tathAshraddhayaiva kR^itam yat stuti-namaskArAdi, tat sarvam asad ity ucyate mat-prApti-sAdhana-mArga-bAhyatvAt pArtha | na ca tad bahulAyAsam api pretya phalAya no apIhArtham, sAdhubhir ninditatvAd iti ||BhGS_17.28|| 

iti shrImat-paramahamsa-parivrAjakAcAryasya shrI-govinda-bhagavat-pUjya-pAda-
shiShyasya shrImac-chamkara-bhagavataH kR^itau shrImad-bhagavad-gItA-bhAShye
saptadasho 'dhyAyaH |


__________________________________________________________

[*NOTE: BhG 18 not included!]
